     7	import { useClientT } from '@/components/client/ClientI18nProvider'
     8	import { getNutritionProgressMeta, type NutritionProgressState } from '@/lib/nutrition/progress'
     9	import { NUTRITION_UI_COLORS } from '@/lib/nutrition/ui-colors'
    10	
    11	export type NutritionMacros = {
    12	  kcal: number
    13	  protein_g: number
    14	  carbs_g: number
    15	  fat_g: number
    16	  water_ml: number
    17	  caffeine_mg?: number
    18	}
    19	
    20	export type SmartNutritionWidgetProps = {
    21	  consumed: NutritionMacros
    22	  target: NutritionMacros
    23	  proteinStreakDays?: number
    24	}
    25	
    26	function formatOverflow(value: number, unit: 'g' | 'L'): string | null {
    27	  if (value <= 0) return null
    28	  return unit === 'L'
    29	    ? `+${value.toFixed(1)} ${unit} au-dessus`
    30	    : `+${Math.round(value)}${unit} au-dessus`
    31	}
    32	
    33	export default function SmartNutritionWidget({ consumed, target, proteinStreakDays }: SmartNutritionWidgetProps) {
    34	  const { t } = useClientT()
    35	  const MACROS = [
    36	    { key: 'protein_g' as const, label: t('smart.nutrition.protein'), color: NUTRITION_UI_COLORS.protein },
    37	    { key: 'carbs_g'   as const, label: t('smart.nutrition.carbs'),   color: NUTRITION_UI_COLORS.carbs },
    38	    { key: 'fat_g'     as const, label: t('smart.nutrition.fat'),     color: NUTRITION_UI_COLORS.fat },
    39	  ]
    40	  const [waterOpen, setWaterOpen] = useState(false)
    41	  const [waterDelta, setWaterDelta] = useState(0)
    42	  const effectiveWaterMl = consumed.water_ml + waterDelta
    43	
    44	  function getStateColor(state: NutritionProgressState, baseColor: string): string {
    45	    if (state === 'over')       return '#ef4444'
    46	    if (state === 'near_limit') return '#f59e0b'
    47	    return baseColor
    48	  }
    49	
    50	  const kcalMeta = getNutritionProgressMeta(consumed.kcal, target.kcal)
    51	  const waterMeta = getNutritionProgressMeta(effectiveWaterMl, target.water_ml)
    52	  const waterOverflowLabel = formatOverflow((effectiveWaterMl - target.water_ml) / 1000, 'L')
    53	  const kcalPct = Math.min(kcalMeta.ratio, 1)
    54	  const r = 80
    55	  const arcTotal = Math.PI * r
    56	  const arcOffset = arcTotal * (1 - kcalPct)
    57	  const kcalStroke = getStateColor(kcalMeta.state, NUTRITION_UI_COLORS.calories)
    58	
    59	  return (
    60	    <>
    61	      <QuickWaterModal
    62	        open={waterOpen}
    63	        onClose={() => setWaterOpen(false)}
    64	        onLogged={ml => setWaterDelta(d => d + ml)}
    65	        onDeleted={ml => setWaterDelta(d => d - ml)}
    66	      />
    67	      <Link
    68	        href="/client/nutrition"
    69	        className="block bg-[#111111] rounded-2xl p-5 active:scale-[0.99] transition-transform"
    70	      >
    71	        <div className="flex items-baseline justify-between mb-3">
    72	          <span className="font-barlow-condensed font-bold uppercase tracking-[0.18em] text-[11px] text-white/30">Nutrition</span>
    73	          <span className="text-[10px] font-semibold text-[#f2f2f2]">→</span>
    74	        </div>
    75	
    76	        {/* Arc demi-cercle */}
    77	        <div className="relative" style={{ height: 110 }}>
    78	          <svg viewBox="0 0 200 110" className="w-full h-full">
    79	            <path
    80	              d={`M ${100 - r} 100 A ${r} ${r} 0 0 1 ${100 + r} 100`}
    81	              fill="none"
    82	              stroke="rgba(255,255,255,0.08)"
    83	              strokeWidth={12}
    84	              strokeLinecap="round"
    85	            />
    86	            <path
    87	              d={`M ${100 - r} 100 A ${r} ${r} 0 0 1 ${100 + r} 100`}
    88	              fill="none"
    89	              stroke={kcalStroke}
    90	              strokeWidth={12}
    91	              strokeLinecap="round"
    92	              strokeDasharray={arcTotal}
    93	              strokeDashoffset={arcOffset}
    94	              style={{ transition: 'stroke-dashoffset 0.6s ease' }}
    95	            />
    96	          </svg>
    97	          <div className="absolute inset-0 flex flex-col items-center justify-end pb-1">
    98	            <div className="font-black leading-none text-white tabular-nums text-[28px]">
    99	              {Math.round(consumed.kcal)}
   100	            </div>
   101	            <div className="text-[9px] uppercase tracking-[0.12em] text-white/35 mt-1">Calories consommées</div>
   102	            <div className="text-[10px] text-white/50 tabular-nums">/ {target.kcal} kcal</div>
   103	          </div>
   104	        </div>
   105	
   106	        {/* Barres macros */}
   107	        <div className="flex flex-col gap-2 mt-3">
   108	          {MACROS.map(m => {
   109	            const c = (consumed[m.key] as number) ?? 0
   110	            const tg = (target[m.key] as number) ?? 0
   111	            const meta = getNutritionProgressMeta(c, tg)
   112	            const fillColor = getStateColor(meta.state, m.color)
   113	            const overflowLabel = formatOverflow(c - tg, 'g')
   114	            return (
   115	              <div key={m.key}>
   116	                <div className="flex justify-between text-[10px] mb-1">
   117	                  <span className="text-white/50 uppercase tracking-[0.1em] font-bold">{m.label}</span>
   118	                  <span className="font-bold tabular-nums" style={{ color: fillColor }}>
   119	                    {Math.round(c)}/{tg}g
   120	                  </span>
   121	                </div>
   122	                <div className="h-1.5 bg-white/[0.06] rounded-full overflow-hidden">
   123	                  <div
   124	                    className="h-full rounded-full"
   125	                    style={{
   126	                      width: `${meta.clampedPercent}%`,
   127	                      background: fillColor,
   128	                      transition: 'width 0.4s ease',
   129	                    }}
   130	                  />
   131	                </div>
   132	                <div className="mt-1 min-h-[14px] text-[9px] font-bold tabular-nums" style={{ color: meta.state === 'over' ? '#ef4444' : 'rgba(255,255,255,0.28)' }}>
   133	                  {overflowLabel ?? '\u00A0'}
   134	                </div>
   135	              </div>
   136	            )
   137	          })}
   138	        </div>
   139	
   140	        {/* Eau */}
   141	        <div className="flex items-center gap-3 mt-4 pt-3">
   142	          <div className="flex-1">
   143	            <div className="flex justify-between text-[10px] mb-1">
   144	              <span className="text-white/50 uppercase tracking-[0.1em] font-bold">Hydratation</span>
   145	              <span className="text-white font-bold tabular-nums">
   146	                {(effectiveWaterMl / 1000).toFixed(1)} / {(target.water_ml / 1000).toFixed(1)} L
   147	              </span>
   148	            </div>
   149	            <div className="h-1.5 bg-white/[0.06] rounded-full overflow-hidden">
   150	              <div
   151	                className="h-full rounded-full"
   152	                style={{
   153	                  width: `${waterMeta.clampedPercent}%`,
   154	                  background: getStateColor(waterMeta.state, NUTRITION_UI_COLORS.water),
   155	                  transition: 'width 0.4s ease',
   156	                }}
   157	              />
   158	            </div>
   159	            <div className="mt-1 min-h-[14px] text-[9px] font-bold tabular-nums" style={{ color: waterMeta.state === 'over' ? '#ef4444' : 'rgba(255,255,255,0.28)' }}>
   160	              {waterOverflowLabel ?? '\u00A0'}
   161	            </div>
   162	          </div>
   163	          <button
   164	            onClick={e => { e.preventDefault(); setWaterOpen(true) }}
   165	            className="w-9 h-9 rounded-xl bg-[#f2f2f2] flex items-center justify-center text-[#080808] active:scale-95 transition-transform shrink-0"
   166	          >
   167	            <Plus size={16} strokeWidth={2.5} />
   168	          </button>
   169	        </div>
   170	
   171	        {consumed.caffeine_mg != null && consumed.caffeine_mg > 0 && (
   172	          <div className="mt-2 flex items-center justify-between rounded-xl bg-white/[0.03] px-3 py-2 text-[10px]">
   173	            <span className="text-white/40 uppercase tracking-[0.1em] font-bold">Caféine / théine</span>
   174	            <span className="text-white font-bold tabular-nums">{Math.round(consumed.caffeine_mg)} mg</span>
   175	          </div>
   176	        )}
   177	
   178	        {/* Régularité protéines */}
   179	        {proteinStreakDays !== undefined && target.protein_g > 0 && (
   180	          <div className="mt-3 pt-3">
   181	            <div className="flex justify-between text-[10px] mb-1.5">
   182	              <span className="text-white/40 uppercase tracking-[0.1em] font-bold">{t('nutrition.consistency')}</span>
   183	              <span className="text-white/60 tabular-nums font-bold">{proteinStreakDays}/7j</span>
   184	            </div>
   185	            <div className="h-1 bg-white/[0.06] rounded-full overflow-hidden">
   186	              <div
   187	                className="h-full rounded-full bg-[#f2f2f2]"
   188	                style={{ width: `${(proteinStreakDays / 7) * 100}%`, transition: 'width 0.6s ease' }}
   189	              />
   190	            </div>
   191	          </div>
   192	        )}
   193	      </Link>
   194	    </>
   195	  )
   196	}

FILE: ./components/client/QuickLogSheet.tsx

     1	"use client";
     2	
     3	import { useEffect, useState } from "react";
     4	import { motion, AnimatePresence } from "framer-motion";
     5	import { X, Drop, ForkKnife, Lightning } from "@phosphor-icons/react";
     6	import dynamic from "next/dynamic";
     7	import type { CycleState } from "@/lib/cycle/cycleEngine";
     8	import type { NutritionMacros } from "@/components/client/smart/SmartNutritionWidget";
     9	import { CaffeineGlyph } from "@/components/client/CaffeineGlyph";
    10	
    11	const QuickWaterModal   = dynamic(() => import("@/components/client/QuickWaterModal"),           { ssr: false });
    12	const QuickCaffeineModal = dynamic(() => import("@/components/client/QuickCaffeineModal"),       { ssr: false });
    13	const FreeActivitySheet = dynamic(() => import("@/components/client/smart/FreeActivitySheet"),   { ssr: false });
    14	const LogPeriodSheet    = dynamic(() => import("@/components/client/cycle/LogPeriodSheet"),      { ssr: false });
    15	const MealLogSheet      = dynamic(() => import("@/components/client/smart/MealLogSheet"),        { ssr: false });
    16	const VoiceLogSheet     = dynamic(() => import("@/components/client/smart/VoiceLogSheet"),       { ssr: false });
    17	
    18	interface Props {
    19	  open: boolean;
    20	  onClose: () => void;
    21	}
    22	
    23	type BalanceContext = {
    24	  consumed: NutritionMacros
    25	  target: NutritionMacros
    26	}
    27	
    28	type SubSheet = "water" | "caffeine" | "activity" | "cycle" | "meal" | "meal-voice" | null;
    29	
    30	const BASE_ACTIONS = [
    31	  {
    32	    key: "water" as const,
    33	    Icon: Drop,
    34	    label: "Eau",
    35	    sub: "Logger ma consommation d'eau",
    36	  },
    37	  {
    38	    key: "caffeine" as const,
    39	    Icon: Drop,
    40	    label: "Café & thé",
    41	    sub: "Espresso, normal, lungo",
    42	  },
    43	  {
    44	    key: "meal" as const,
    45	    Icon: ForkKnife,
    46	    label: "Repas",
    47	    sub: "Ajouter un repas ou aliment",
    48	  },
    49	  {
    50	    key: "activity" as const,
    51	    Icon: Lightning,
    52	    label: "Activité",
    53	    sub: "Course, marche, sport libre…",
    54	  },
    55	];
    56	
    57	export default function QuickLogSheet({ open, onClose }: Props) {
    58	  const [sub, setSub] = useState<SubSheet>(null);
    59	  const [cycleState, setCycleState] = useState<CycleState | null>(null);
    60	  const [balanceContext, setBalanceContext] = useState<BalanceContext | null>(null);
    61	
    62	  useEffect(() => {
    63	    if (!open) return;
    64	    // Cycle state
    65	    fetch("/api/client/cycle/status")
    66	      .then(r => r.ok ? r.json() : null)
    67	      .then(data => { if (data?.cycleState) setCycleState(data.cycleState); })
    68	      .catch(() => {});
    69	    // Nutrition balance du jour pour les jauges live
    70	    fetch("/api/client/nutrition/today-progress")
    71	      .then(r => r.ok ? r.json() : null)
    72	      .then(data => {
    73	        if (!data?.target) return;
    74	        const toMacros = (d: { calories: number; protein_g: number; carbs_g: number; fat_g: number }): NutritionMacros => ({
    75	          kcal: d.calories,
    76	          protein_g: d.protein_g,
    77	          carbs_g: d.carbs_g,
    78	          fat_g: d.fat_g,
    79	          water_ml: 0,
    80	        });
    81	        setBalanceContext({ consumed: toMacros(data.consumed), target: toMacros(data.target) });
    82	      })
    83	      .catch(() => {});
    84	  }, [open]);
    85	
    86	  function handleClose() {
    87	    setSub(null);
    88	    onClose();
    89	  }
    90	
    91	  function handleAction(key: string) {
    92	    if (key === "water")    { setSub("water"); return; }
    93	    if (key === "caffeine") { setSub("caffeine"); return; }
    94	    if (key === "activity") { setSub("activity"); return; }
    95	    if (key === "cycle")    { setSub("cycle"); return; }
    96	    // "meal" → ouvrir directement MealLogSheet standard, pas de sélecteur intermédiaire
    97	    if (key === "meal")     { setSub("meal"); return; }
    98	  }
    99	
   100	  const actions = [
   101	    ...BASE_ACTIONS,
   102	    ...(cycleState?.hasActiveCycle ? [{
   103	      key: "cycle" as const,
   104	      Icon: Drop,
   105	      label: "Cycle",
   106	      sub: "Début ou fin de règles",
   107	    }] : []),
   108	  ];
   109	
   110	  return (
   111	    <>
   112	      {/* Main quick-log sheet */}
   113	      <AnimatePresence>
   114	        {open && sub === null && (
   115	          <>
   116	            <motion.div
   117	              key="overlay"
   118	              className="fixed inset-0 z-[60] bg-black/60 backdrop-blur-[2px]"
   119	              initial={{ opacity: 0 }}
   120	              animate={{ opacity: 1 }}
   121	              exit={{ opacity: 0 }}
   122	              onClick={handleClose}
   123	            />
   124	            <motion.div
   125	              key="sheet"
   126	              className="fixed left-0 right-0 bottom-0 z-[70] rounded-t-2xl"
   127	              style={{ background: '#0d0d0d', maxHeight: '88vh', display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', paddingBottom: "max(env(safe-area-inset-bottom), 16px)" }}
   128	              initial={{ y: "100%" }}
   129	              animate={{ y: 0 }}
   130	              exit={{ y: "100%" }}
   131	              transition={{ type: "spring", stiffness: 300, damping: 30 }}
   132	            >
   133	              {/* Header */}
   134	              <div className="relative flex items-center justify-between px-5 pt-5 pb-4 shrink-0">
   135	                <div className="absolute top-2.5 left-1/2 -translate-x-1/2 w-10 h-1 rounded-full bg-white/[0.10]" />
   136	                <p className="text-[15px] font-barlow-condensed font-bold uppercase tracking-[0.12em] text-white">
   137	                  Logger
   138	                </p>
   139	                <button
   140	                  onClick={handleClose}
   141	                  className="w-8 h-8 flex items-center justify-center rounded-xl bg-white/[0.06] text-white/40 active:bg-white/[0.08]"
   142	                >
   143	                  <X size={15} />
   144	                </button>
   145	              </div>
   146	
   147	              {/* Actions */}
   148	              <div className="px-4 pb-4 flex flex-col gap-2">
   149	                <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-2">
   150	                  {actions.filter(action => action.key === "water" || action.key === "caffeine").map(({ key, Icon, label, sub: subLabel }) => (
   151	                    <button
   152	                      key={key}
   153	                      onClick={() => handleAction(key)}
   154	                      className="flex items-center gap-3 px-3 h-[64px] rounded-xl bg-white/[0.03] active:bg-white/[0.06] transition-colors text-left"
   155	                    >
   156	                      <div className="w-10 h-10 rounded-xl flex items-center justify-center shrink-0 bg-white/[0.06]">
   157	                        {key === "caffeine" ? <CaffeineGlyph drinkType="coffee" active size="sm" color="#111111" /> : <Icon size={18} className="text-white/70" />}
   158	                      </div>
   159	                      <div className="flex flex-col min-w-0">
   160	                        <span className="text-[13px] font-barlow font-semibold text-[#e0e0e0] leading-tight">
   161	                          {label}
   162	                        </span>
   163	                        <span className="text-[10px] font-barlow text-white/40 leading-tight truncate">
   164	                          {subLabel}
   165	                        </span>
   166	                      </div>
   167	                    </button>
   168	                  ))}
   169	                </div>
   170	                <div className="flex flex-col gap-2">
   171	                  {actions.filter(action => action.key !== "water" && action.key !== "caffeine").map(({ key, Icon, label, sub: subLabel }) => (
   172	                    <button
   173	                      key={key}
   174	                      onClick={() => handleAction(key)}
   175	                      className="flex items-center gap-4 px-4 h-[60px] rounded-xl bg-white/[0.03] active:bg-white/[0.06] transition-colors text-left"
   176	                    >
   177	                      <div className="w-9 h-9 rounded-lg flex items-center justify-center shrink-0 bg-white/[0.06]">
   178	                        <Icon size={18} className="text-white/70" />
   179	                      </div>
   180	                      <div className="flex flex-col min-w-0">
   181	                        <span className="text-[14px] font-barlow font-semibold text-[#e0e0e0] leading-tight">
   182	                          {label}
   183	                        </span>
   184	                        <span className="text-[11px] font-barlow text-white/40 leading-tight truncate">
   185	                          {subLabel}
   186	                        </span>
   187	                      </div>
   188	                    </button>
   189	                  ))}
   190	                </div>
   191	              </div>
   192	            </motion.div>
   193	          </>
   194	        )}
   195	      </AnimatePresence>
   196	
   197	      {/* Sub-sheets */}
   198	      <QuickWaterModal
   199	        open={sub === "water"}
   200	        onClose={() => { setSub(null); onClose(); }}
   201	      />
   202	      <QuickCaffeineModal
   203	        open={sub === "caffeine"}
   204	        onClose={() => { setSub(null); onClose(); }}
   205	      />
   206	      <FreeActivitySheet
   207	        open={sub === "activity"}
   208	        onClose={() => { setSub(null); onClose(); }}
   209	        onSaved={() => { setSub(null); onClose(); }}
   210	      />
   211	      <LogPeriodSheet
   212	        open={sub === "cycle"}
   213	        cycleState={cycleState}
   214	        onClose={() => { setSub(null); onClose(); }}
   215	        onUpdated={(newState) => { setCycleState(newState); setSub(null); onClose(); }}
   216	      />
   217	      {/* Repas → surface unifiée avec jauges live */}
   218	      <MealLogSheet
   219	        open={sub === "meal"}
   220	        composerMode="standard"
   221	        intent="track"
   222	        balanceContext={balanceContext ?? undefined}
   223	        onClose={() => { setSub(null); onClose(); }}
   224	        onSuccess={() => { setSub(null); onClose(); }}
   225	      />
   226	      <VoiceLogSheet
   227	        open={sub === "meal-voice"}
   228	        onClose={() => { setSub(null); onClose(); }}
   229	        onSuccess={() => { setSub(null); onClose(); }}
   230	        initialInputMode="voice"
   231	      />
   232	    </>
   233	  );
   234	}

FILE: ./components/client/QuickCaffeineModal.tsx
------------------------------------------------------------
     1	"use client"
     2	
     3	import { useEffect, useMemo, useState } from "react"
     4	import { useRouter } from "next/navigation"
     5	import { motion, AnimatePresence } from "framer-motion"
     6	import { Minus, Plus, Trash2, X } from "lucide-react"
     7	import { DRINK_PRESETS, estimateCaffeineMg, type DrinkType } from "@/lib/client/nutrition/drinks"
     8	import { CaffeineGlyph } from "@/components/client/CaffeineGlyph"
     9	
    10	type CaffeineLog = {
    11	  id: string
    12	  amount_ml: number
    13	  caffeine_mg: number
    14	  drink_type: DrinkType
    15	  logged_at: string
    16	}
    17	
    18	interface Props {
    19	  open: boolean
    20	  onClose: () => void
    21	  date?: string
    22	  onLogged?: (mg: number) => void
    23	  onDeleted?: (mg: number) => void
    24	}
    25	
    26	function formatTime(iso: string): string {
    27	  return new Date(iso).toLocaleTimeString("fr-FR", { hour: "2-digit", minute: "2-digit" })
    28	}
    29	
    30	export default function QuickCaffeineModal({ open, onClose, date, onLogged, onDeleted }: Props) {
    31	  const router = useRouter()
    32	  const [drinkType, setDrinkType] = useState<DrinkType>("coffee")
    33	  const [ml, setMl] = useState(DRINK_PRESETS.coffee.baseAmountMl)
    34	  const [saving, setSaving] = useState(false)
    35	  const [done, setDone] = useState(false)
    36	  const [error, setError] = useState<string | null>(null)
    37	  const [logs, setLogs] = useState<CaffeineLog[]>([])
    38	  const [deletingId, setDeletingId] = useState<string | null>(null)
    39	
    40	  useEffect(() => {
    41	    if (!open) return
    42	    const url = new URL("/api/client/water", window.location.origin)
    43	    url.searchParams.set("kind", "caffeine")
    44	    if (date) url.searchParams.set("date", date)
    45	    fetch(url)
    46	      .then(r => r.json())
    47	      .then(d => setLogs(d.logs ?? []))
    48	      .catch(() => {})
    49	  }, [open, date])
    50	
    51	  useEffect(() => {
    52	    if (!open) return
    53	    const preset = DRINK_PRESETS[drinkType]
    54	    setMl(preset.baseAmountMl)
    55	  }, [drinkType, open])
    56	
    57	  const caffeineMg = useMemo(() => estimateCaffeineMg(drinkType, ml), [drinkType, ml])
    58	  const totalMl = logs.reduce((s, l) => s + l.amount_ml, 0)
    59	  const totalMg = logs.reduce((s, l) => s + l.caffeine_mg, 0)
    60	
    61	  async function log() {
    62	    if (saving) return
    63	    setSaving(true)
    64	    setError(null)
    65	    onLogged?.(caffeineMg)
    66	
    67	    try {
    68	      const res = await fetch("/api/client/water", {
    69	        method: "POST",
    70	        headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
    71	        body: JSON.stringify({
    72	          amount_ml: ml,
    73	          caffeine_mg: caffeineMg,
    74	          drink_type: drinkType,
    75	          date,
    76	        }),
    77	      })
    78	
    79	      if (!res.ok) {
    80	        const json = await res.json().catch(() => ({}))
    81	        setError(json.error ?? "Impossible d'enregistrer la boisson.")
    82	        setSaving(false)
    83	        return
    84	      }
    85	
    86	      const payload = await res.json().catch(() => ({}))
    87	      const newLog: CaffeineLog = {
    88	        id: payload.id ?? crypto.randomUUID(),
    89	        amount_ml: ml,
    90	        caffeine_mg: caffeineMg,
    91	        drink_type: drinkType,
    92	        logged_at: payload.logged_at ?? new Date().toISOString(),
    93	      }
    94	      setLogs(prev => [...prev, newLog])
    95	      setDone(true)
    96	      setTimeout(() => {
    97	        setDone(false)
    98	        setSaving(false)
    99	        router.refresh()
   100	      }, 700)
   101	    } catch {
   102	      setError("Impossible d'enregistrer la boisson.")
   103	      setSaving(false)
   104	    }
   105	  }
   106	
   107	  async function deleteLog(log: CaffeineLog) {
   108	    setDeletingId(log.id)
   109	    try {
   110	      const res = await fetch(`/api/client/water/${log.id}`, { method: "DELETE" })
   111	      if (res.ok) {
   112	        setLogs(prev => prev.filter(l => l.id !== log.id))
   113	        onDeleted?.(log.caffeine_mg)
   114	        router.refresh()
   115	      }
   116	    } finally {
   117	      setDeletingId(null)
   118	    }
   119	  }
   120	
   121	  const options: DrinkType[] = ["espresso", "coffee", "lungo", "tea"]
   122	
   123	  return (
   124	    <AnimatePresence>
   125	      {open && (
   126	        <>
   127	          <motion.div
   128	            initial={{ opacity: 0 }}
   129	            animate={{ opacity: 1 }}
   130	            exit={{ opacity: 0 }}
   131	            onClick={onClose}
   132	            className="fixed inset-0 z-[80] bg-black/60 backdrop-blur-[2px]"
   133	          />
   134	          <motion.div
   135	            initial={{ y: "100%" }}
   136	            animate={{ y: 0, transition: { type: "spring", stiffness: 300, damping: 30 } }}
   137	            exit={{ y: "100%", transition: { duration: 0.2, ease: "easeIn" } }}
   138	            className="fixed bottom-0 left-0 right-0 z-[90] rounded-t-2xl"
   139	            style={{ background: "#0d0d0d", maxHeight: "88vh", display: "flex", flexDirection: "column" }}
   140	          >
   141	            <div className="relative flex items-center justify-between px-5 pt-5 pb-4 shrink-0">
   142	              <div className="absolute top-2.5 left-1/2 -translate-x-1/2 w-10 h-1 rounded-full bg-white/[0.10]" />
   143	              <p className="text-[15px] font-barlow-condensed font-bold uppercase tracking-[0.12em] text-white">
   144	                Café & thé
   145	              </p>
   146	              <button
   147	                onClick={onClose}
   148	                className="h-8 w-8 flex items-center justify-center rounded-xl bg-white/[0.06] text-white/40 hover:text-white/70 transition-colors"
   149	              >
   150	                <X size={14} />
   151	              </button>
   152	            </div>
   153	
   154	            <div className="flex-1 overflow-y-auto min-h-0 px-5 pb-8">
   155	              {logs.length > 0 && (
   156	                <div className="mb-4">
   157	                  <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-2">
   158	                    <p className="text-[9px] font-barlow-condensed font-bold uppercase tracking-[0.14em] text-white/30">Aujourd'hui</p>
   159	                    <p className="text-[11px] font-bold tabular-nums" style={{ color: DRINK_PRESETS[drinkType].accent }}>
   160	                      {totalMg}mg cumulés · {totalMl}ml
   161	                    </p>
   162	                  </div>
   163	                  <div className="space-y-1.5 max-h-[160px] overflow-y-auto">
   164	                    {logs.map(log => {
   165	                      const label = DRINK_PRESETS[log.drink_type]?.label ?? "Boisson"
   166	                      const entryUnit = log.drink_type === "tea" ? "théine" : "caféine"
   167	                      return (
   168	                        <div
   169	                          key={log.id}
   170	                          className="flex items-center justify-between bg-white/[0.03] rounded-xl px-3 py-2"
   171	                        >
   172	                          <div className="flex items-center gap-2 min-w-0">
   173	                            <CaffeineGlyph drinkType={log.drink_type} active={false} size="sm" color={DRINK_PRESETS[log.drink_type]?.accent ?? "#c08457"} className="shrink-0" />
   174	                            <span className="text-[13px] font-bold text-white tabular-nums">{log.amount_ml} ml</span>
   175	                            <span className="text-[10px] text-white/25 truncate">{label} · {log.caffeine_mg}mg {entryUnit}</span>
   176	                            <span className="text-[10px] text-white/20 shrink-0">{formatTime(log.logged_at)}</span>
   177	                          </div>
   178	                          <button
   179	                            onClick={() => deleteLog(log)}
   180	                            disabled={deletingId === log.id}
   181	                            className="h-7 w-7 flex items-center justify-center rounded-lg bg-white/[0.06] text-white/40 hover:text-white/70 active:scale-95 transition-all disabled:opacity-40"
   182	                          >
   183	                            <Trash2 size={12} />
   184	                          </button>
   185	                        </div>
   186	                      )
   187	                    })}
   188	                  </div>
   189	                  <div className="h-px bg-white/[0.06] mt-3 mb-4" />
   190	                </div>
   191	              )}
   192	
   193	              <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-2 mb-4">
   194	                {options.map((type) => {
   195	                  const preset = DRINK_PRESETS[type]
   196	                  const active = drinkType === type
   197	                  const density = Math.round((preset.baseCaffeineMg / preset.baseAmountMl) * 100)
   198	                  return (
   199	                    <button
   200	                      key={type}
   201	                      onClick={() => setDrinkType(type)}
   202	                      className={`rounded-2xl px-3 py-3 text-left transition-all active:scale-[0.98] ${
   203	                        active ? "bg-white/[0.08] border border-white/10" : "bg-white/[0.03]"
   204	                      }`}
   205	                      style={active ? { boxShadow: `0 0 0 1px ${preset.accent}22 inset` } : undefined}
   206	                    >
   207	                      <CaffeineGlyph drinkType={type} active={active} size="lg" className="mx-auto" color={active ? "#111111" : preset.accent} />
   208	                      <div className="mt-2 flex items-center justify-between">
   209	                        <span className="text-[12px] font-bold text-white">{preset.label}</span>
   210	                        <span className="text-[10px] text-white/30 tabular-nums">{preset.baseAmountMl}ml</span>
   211	                      </div>
   212	                      <p className="text-[10px] text-white/35 leading-tight mt-1">
   213	                        {preset.baseCaffeineMg}mg · {density}mg/100ml · {preset.strengthLabel}
   214	                      </p>
   215	                    </button>
   216	                  )
   217	                })}
   218	              </div>
   219	
   220	              <div className="flex items-center gap-3 mb-5">
   221	                <button
   222	                  onClick={() => setMl(m => Math.max(20, m - 20))}
   223	                  className="h-10 w-10 flex items-center justify-center bg-white/[0.06] rounded-xl text-white active:scale-95 shrink-0"
   224	                >
   225	                  <Minus size={15} />
   226	                </button>
   227	                <div className="flex-1 text-center">
   228	                  <p className="text-[28px] font-black text-white leading-none tabular-nums">{ml}</p>
   229	                  <p className="text-[10px] text-white/30 font-barlow-condensed uppercase tracking-wider mt-0.5">millilitres</p>
   230	                </div>
   231	                <button
   232	                  onClick={() => setMl(m => Math.min(600, m + 20))}
   233	                  className="h-10 w-10 flex items-center justify-center bg-white/[0.06] rounded-xl text-white active:scale-95 shrink-0"
   234	                >
   235	                  <Plus size={15} />
   236	                </button>
   237	              </div>
   238	
   239	              <div className="mb-4 rounded-2xl bg-white/[0.03] px-4 py-3">
   240	                <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
   241	                  <span className="text-[10px] uppercase tracking-[0.14em] text-white/35 font-bold">Charge active</span>
   242	                  <span className="text-[14px] font-black text-white tabular-nums">{caffeineMg} mg</span>
   243	                </div>
   244	                <div className="mt-2 h-1.5 bg-white/[0.06] rounded-full overflow-hidden">
   245	                  <div
   246	                    className="h-full rounded-full"
   247	                    style={{
   248	                      width: `${Math.min(100, (caffeineMg / 160) * 100)}%`,
   249	                      background: DRINK_PRESETS[drinkType].accent,
   250	                      transition: "width 0.25s ease",
   251	                    }}
   252	                  />
   253	                </div>
   254	                <p className="mt-2 text-[10px] text-white/30">
   255	                  {drinkType === "tea" ? "théine estimée" : "caféine estimée"} à partir du volume choisi.
   256	                </p>
   257	              </div>
   258	
   259	              {error && <p className="text-[11px] text-red-400 text-center mb-3">{error}</p>}
   260	
   261	              <button
   262	                onClick={log}
   263	                disabled={saving && !done}
   264	                className={`w-full h-12 flex items-center justify-center gap-2 rounded-xl font-barlow-condensed font-bold uppercase tracking-[0.14em] text-[12px] transition-all active:scale-[0.98] ${
   265	                  done ? "bg-white/[0.06] text-white/50" : "disabled:opacity-60"
   266	                }`}
   267	                style={done ? undefined : { background: DRINK_PRESETS[drinkType].accent, color: "#080808" }}
   268	              >
   269	                {done ? "Boisson loguée" : saving ? "Enregistrement..." : `Loguer ${DRINK_PRESETS[drinkType].label}`}
   270	              </button>
   271	            </div>
   272	          </motion.div>
   273	        </>
   274	      )}
   275	    </AnimatePresence>
   276	  )
   277	}

FILE: ./lib/client/ai-coach/patternDetector.ts

     1	import { SupabaseClient } from '@supabase/supabase-js'
     2	import { computePhysiologicalDate } from '@/lib/nutrition/physiological-date'
     3	import { resolveClientTimezone } from '@/lib/client/checkin/resolveClientTimezone'
     4	import { utcRangeForPhysiologicalDate } from '@/lib/client/checkin/timeWindows'
     5	import { resolveProtocolDayByDate } from '@/lib/nutrition/protocol-schedule'
     6	
     7	export interface PatternResult {
     8	  code: string
     9	  statement: string
    10	  question: string
    11	  options: { label: string; value: number }[]
    12	}
    13	
    14	/**
    15	 * Returns a date string YYYY-MM-DD offset by X days
    16	 */
    17	function getOffsetDateStr(dateStr: string, offsetDays: number): string {
    18	  const d = new Date(dateStr)
    19	  d.setDate(d.getDate() + offsetDays)
    20	  return d.toISOString().split('T')[0]
    21	}
    22	
    23	export async function evaluateClientPatterns(clientId: string, db: SupabaseClient): Promise<PatternResult | null> {
    24	  const timezone = await resolveClientTimezone(db as any, clientId)
    25	  const today = computePhysiologicalDate(new Date(), timezone)
    26	  const todayDateObj = new Date(today)
    27	  const sevenDaysAgoObj = new Date(today)
    28	  sevenDaysAgoObj.setDate(sevenDaysAgoObj.getDate() - 7)
    29	  const sevenDaysAgo = sevenDaysAgoObj.toISOString().split('T')[0]
    30	  const { start: sevenDaysAgoStart } = utcRangeForPhysiologicalDate(sevenDaysAgo, timezone)
    31	  const { start: todayStart } = utcRangeForPhysiologicalDate(today, timezone)
    32	
    33	  // 1. Fetch data
    34	  const [
    35	    { data: protocol },
    36	    { data: meals },
    37	    { data: legacyMeals },
    38	    { data: checkins },
    39	    { data: waterLogs },
    40	    { data: activeProgram },
    41	    { data: sessionLogs },
    42	  ] = await Promise.all([
    43	    db.from('nutrition_protocols')
    44	      .select('schedule_start_date, nutrition_protocol_days(position, calories, protein_g, carbs_g, fat_g, hydration_ml), nutrition_protocol_schedule_slots(week_index, dow, protocol_day_position)')
    45	      .eq('client_id', clientId)
    46	      .eq('status', 'shared')
    47	      .order('updated_at', { ascending: false })
    48	      .limit(1)
    49	      .maybeSingle(),
    50	    db.from('nutrition_meals')
    51	      .select('physiological_date, total_calories, total_protein_g, total_carbs_g, total_fat_g')
    52	      .eq('client_id', clientId)
    53	      .gte('physiological_date', sevenDaysAgo)
    54	      .lt('physiological_date', today),
    55	    db.from('meal_logs')
    56	      .select('logged_at, estimated_macros')
    57	      .eq('client_id', clientId)
    58	      .gte('logged_at', sevenDaysAgoStart.toISOString())
    59	      .lt('logged_at', todayStart.toISOString())
    60	      .eq('ai_status', 'done'),
    61	    db.from('client_daily_checkins')
    62	      .select('date, flow_type, sleep_hours, energy_level, stress_level')
    63	      .eq('client_id', clientId)
    64	      .gte('date', sevenDaysAgo)
    65	      .lte('date', today), // we include today for check-ins (e.g., morning checkin already done)
    66	    db.from('client_water_logs')
    67	      .select('logged_at, amount_ml')
    68	      .eq('client_id', clientId)
    69	      .gte('logged_at', `${sevenDaysAgo}T00:00:00.000Z`),
    70	    db.from('programs')
    71	      .select('id, name, weeks, frequency, program_sessions(id, name, day_of_week, days_of_week)')
    72	      .eq('client_id', clientId)
    73	      .eq('status', 'active')
    74	      .order('created_at', { ascending: false })
    75	      .limit(1)
    76	      .maybeSingle(),
    77	    db.from('client_session_logs')
    78	      .select('completed_at')
    79	      .eq('client_id', clientId)
    80	      .not('completed_at', 'is', null)
    81	      .gte('completed_at', `${sevenDaysAgo}T00:00:00.000Z`)
    82	      .order('completed_at', { ascending: false }),
    83	  ])
    84	
    85	  // 2. Aggregate Data per day
    86	  const dailyStats: Record<string, any> = {}
    87	  for (let i = 1; i <= 7; i++) {
    88	    const d = getOffsetDateStr(today, -i)
    89	    dailyStats[d] = {
    90	      target: null, consumedKcal: 0, consumedProt: 0, consumedCarbs: 0, consumedFat: 0, consumedWater: 0,
    91	      sleep: null, energy: null, stress: null,
    92	    }
    93	  }
    94	
    95	  // Assign targets
    96	  const pDays = (protocol as any)?.nutrition_protocol_days ?? []
    97	  const pSlots = (protocol as any)?.nutrition_protocol_schedule_slots ?? []
    98	  const startDate = (protocol as any)?.schedule_start_date ?? null
    99	
   100	  for (const d of Object.keys(dailyStats)) {
   101	    const dayProtocol = resolveProtocolDayByDate(d, startDate, pDays, pSlots) as any
   102	    if (dayProtocol) {
   103	      dailyStats[d].target = {
   104	        kcal: Number(dayProtocol.calories ?? 0),
   105	        prot: Number(dayProtocol.protein_g ?? 0),
   106	        carbs: Number(dayProtocol.carbs_g ?? 0),
   107	        fat: Number(dayProtocol.fat_g ?? 0),
   108	        water: Number(dayProtocol.hydration_ml ?? 2500)
   109	      }
   110	    }
   111	  }
   112	
   113	  // Aggregate macros
   114	  for (const m of (meals ?? [])) {
   115	    const d = m.physiological_date
   116	    if (dailyStats[d]) {
   117	      dailyStats[d].consumedKcal += Number(m.total_calories ?? 0)
   118	      dailyStats[d].consumedProt += Number(m.total_protein_g ?? 0)
   119	      dailyStats[d].consumedCarbs += Number(m.total_carbs_g ?? 0)
   120	      dailyStats[d].consumedFat += Number(m.total_fat_g ?? 0)
   121	    }
   122	  }
   123	  for (const m of (legacyMeals ?? [])) {
   124	    const d = computePhysiologicalDate(new Date(m.logged_at), timezone)
   125	    if (dailyStats[d]) {
   126	      const em = (m.estimated_macros ?? {}) as any
   127	      dailyStats[d].consumedKcal += Number(em.calories ?? 0)
   128	      dailyStats[d].consumedProt += Number(em.protein_g ?? 0)
   129	      dailyStats[d].consumedCarbs += Number(em.carbs_g ?? 0)
   130	      dailyStats[d].consumedFat += Number(em.fats_g ?? em.fat_g ?? 0)
   131	    }
   132	  }
   133	  for (const w of (waterLogs ?? [])) {
   134	    const d = computePhysiologicalDate(new Date(w.logged_at))
   135	    if (dailyStats[d]) {
   136	      dailyStats[d].consumedWater += Number(w.amount_ml ?? 0)
   137	    }
   138	  }
   139	  for (const c of (checkins ?? [])) {
   140	    const d = c.date
   141	    if (dailyStats[d] || d === today) {
   142	      const target = dailyStats[d] || {}
   143	      if (c.flow_type === 'morning') {
   144	        if (c.sleep_hours != null) target.sleep = c.sleep_hours
   145	        if (c.energy_level != null) target.energy = c.energy_level
   146	      } else if (c.flow_type === 'evening') {
   147	        if (c.stress_level != null) target.stress = c.stress_level
   148	      }
   149	    }
   150	  }
   151	
   152	  // 3. Evaluate Patterns
   153	  const daysDesc = Array.from({ length: 7 }, (_, i) => getOffsetDateStr(today, -(i + 1)))
   154	
   155	  const checkSequence = (count: number, condition: (stats: any) => boolean) => {
   156	    for (let i = 0; i < count; i++) {
   157	      const d = daysDesc[i]
   158	      const st = dailyStats[d]
   159	      if (!st || !st.target) return false // Missing data prevents triggering
   160	      if (!condition(st)) return false
   161	    }
   162	    return true
   163	  }
   164	
   165	  const checkCheckinsSequence = (count: number, flow: 'morning'|'evening', condition: (c: any) => boolean) => {
   166	    // Collect the last `count` days where checkin was supposed to happen, we look at the last `count` days chronologically ending today or yesterday.
   167	    const relevantDates = [today, ...daysDesc].slice(0, count + 1)
   168	    let validDays = 0
   169	    let matchDays = 0
   170	    for (const d of relevantDates) {
   171	      const st = dailyStats[d] || {}
   172	      const c = checkins?.find(x => x.date === d && x.flow_type === flow)
   173	      if (c) {
   174	        validDays++
   175	        if (condition(c)) matchDays++
   176	      }
   177	    }
   178	    return validDays >= count && matchDays >= count
   179	  }
   180	
   181	  // 1. Calories dépassées > 110% (3j)
   182	  if (checkSequence(3, s => s.consumedKcal > s.target.kcal * 1.1)) {
   183	    return {
   184	      code: 'calories_high', statement: "J'ai vu que tes calories dépassaient ta cible ces 3 derniers jours.",
   185	      question: "Qu'est-ce qui se passe en ce moment ?",
   186	      options: [
   187	        { label: "Beaucoup de restos/sorties", value: 1 },
   188	        { label: "J'ai souvent faim", value: 2 },
   189	        { label: "Du mal à peser/logger", value: 3 },
   190	        { label: "Autre (écrire)", value: 99 }
   191	      ]
   192	    }
   193	  }
   194	
   195	  // 2. Calories en deçà < 80% (3j)
   196	  if (checkSequence(3, s => s.target.kcal > 0 && s.consumedKcal > 0 && s.consumedKcal < s.target.kcal * 0.8)) {
   197	    return {
   198	      code: 'calories_low', statement: "J'ai vu que tu étais bien en dessous de tes calories cibles ces 3 derniers jours.",
   199	      question: "Quelle en est la raison principale ?",
   200	      options: [
   201	        { label: "Pas très faim", value: 1 },
   202	        { label: "Pas le temps de manger", value: 2 },
   203	        { label: "J'oublie de logger", value: 3 },
   204	        { label: "Autre (écrire)", value: 99 }
   205	      ]
   206	    }
   207	  }
   208	
   209	  // 3. Protéines en deçà < 85% (5j)
   210	  if (checkSequence(5, s => s.target.prot > 0 && s.consumedProt > 0 && s.consumedProt < s.target.prot * 0.85)) {
   211	    return {
   212	      code: 'protein_low', statement: "Tes protéines sont en dessous de la cible depuis 5 jours.",
   213	      question: "Est-ce qu'on peut t'aider là-dessus ?",
   214	      options: [
   215	        { label: "Manque d'inspiration repas", value: 1 },
   216	        { label: "Trop compliqué à cuisiner", value: 2 },
   217	        { label: "Budget serré en ce moment", value: 3 },
   218	        { label: "Autre (écrire)", value: 99 }
   219	      ]
   220	    }
   221	  }
   222	
   223	  // 4. Glucides dépassés > 115% (3j)
   224	  if (checkSequence(3, s => s.target.carbs > 0 && s.consumedCarbs > s.target.carbs * 1.15)) {
   225	    return {
   226	      code: 'carbs_high', statement: "Tu as consommé pas mal de glucides au-dessus de la cible ces 3 derniers jours.",
   227	      question: "Une idée de ce qui bloque ?",
   228	      options: [
   229	        { label: "Envies de sucre fréquentes", value: 1 },
   230	        { label: "Repas imprévus", value: 2 },
   231	        { label: "Autre (écrire)", value: 99 }
   232	      ]
   233	    }
   234	  }
   235	
   236	  // 6. Lipides dépassés > 115% (3j)
   237	  if (checkSequence(3, s => s.target.fat > 0 && s.consumedFat > s.target.fat * 1.15)) {
   238	    return {
   239	      code: 'fat_high', statement: "J'ai vu que tes lipides étaient au-dessus de la cible ces 3 derniers jours.",
   240	      question: "Qu'est-ce qui explique cela ?",
   241	      options: [
   242	        { label: "Je mange souvent dehors", value: 1 },
   243	        { label: "Des craquages récents", value: 2 },
   244	        { label: "Repas habituels trop riches", value: 3 },
   245	        { label: "Autre (écrire)", value: 99 }
   246	      ]
   247	    }
   248	  }
   249	
   250	  // 7. Hydratation < 70% (5j)
   251	  if (checkSequence(5, s => s.target.water > 0 && s.consumedWater > 0 && s.consumedWater < s.target.water * 0.7)) {
   252	    return {
   253	      code: 'hydration_low', statement: "Tu n'as pas atteint tes objectifs d'hydratation ces 5 derniers jours.",
   254	      question: "Qu'est-ce qui t'empêche de boire plus ?",
   255	      options: [
   256	        { label: "J'y pense pas", value: 1 },
   257	        { label: "Pas de gourde sous la main", value: 2 },
   258	        { label: "J'oublie de logger", value: 3 },
   259	        { label: "Autre (écrire)", value: 99 }
   260	      ]
   261	    }
   262	  }
   263	
   264	  // 8. Sommeil < 6h (3j)
   265	  if (checkCheckinsSequence(3, 'morning', c => c.sleep_hours != null && c.sleep_hours < 6)) {
   266	    return {
   267	      code: 'sleep_low', statement: "Tu as dormi moins de 6 heures sur tes 3 dernières nuits.",
   268	      question: "Qu'est-ce qui perturbe ton sommeil ?",
   269	      options: [
   270	        { label: "Beaucoup de travail/stress", value: 1 },
   271	        { label: "Je me couche trop tard", value: 2 },
   272	        { label: "Insomnies/Réveils", value: 3 },
   273	        { label: "Autre (écrire)", value: 99 }
   274	      ]
   275	    }
   276	  }
   277	
   278	  // 9. Sommeil > 9h (3j)
   279	  if (checkCheckinsSequence(3, 'morning', c => c.sleep_hours != null && c.sleep_hours > 9)) {
   280	    return {
   281	      code: 'sleep_high', statement: "Tu dors plus de 9 heures depuis 3 jours, c'est pas dans tes habitudes.",
   282	      question: "Tu te sens fatigué(e) en ce moment ?",
   283	      options: [
   284	        { label: "Oui, très fatigué(e)", value: 1 },
   285	        { label: "Non, je récupère de ma semaine", value: 2 },
   286	        { label: "Autre (écrire)", value: 99 }
   287	      ]
   288	    }
   289	  }
   290	
   291	  // 10. Energie <= 2/5 (3j)
   292	  if (checkCheckinsSequence(3, 'morning', c => c.energy_level != null && c.energy_level <= 2)) {
   293	    return {
   294	      code: 'energy_low', statement: "Ton niveau d'énergie est au plus bas depuis 3 jours.",
   295	      question: "Comment on peut t'aider ?",
   296	      options: [
   297	        { label: "J'ai besoin de repos", value: 1 },
   298	        { label: "Je mange peut-être pas assez", value: 2 },
   299	        { label: "Trop de stress externe", value: 3 },
   300	        { label: "Autre (écrire)", value: 99 }
   301	      ]
   302	    }
   303	  }
   304	
   305	  // 11. Stress >= 4/5 (3j)
   306	  if (checkCheckinsSequence(3, 'evening', c => c.stress_level != null && c.stress_level >= 4)) {
   307	    return {
   308	      code: 'stress_high', statement: "Tu as signalé un niveau de stress élevé ces 3 derniers jours.",
   309	      question: "Est-ce que ça impacte ta récupération ?",
   310	      options: [
   311	        { label: "Oui, je dors mal", value: 1 },
   312	        { label: "Oui, mon appétit change", value: 2 },
   313	        { label: "Non, je gère", value: 3 },
   314	        { label: "Autre (écrire)", value: 99 }
   315	      ]
   316	    }
   317	  }
   318	
   319	  // 12. Séance manquée (on regarde si hier il y avait une séance, et si elle a été loggée)
   320	  // Simplification: si hier était un jour de séance (selon le protocole) et pas de log hier.

------------------------------------------------------------
FILE: ./lib/client/ai-coach/loadDailyFacts.ts
------------------------------------------------------------
     1	import type { SupabaseClient } from '@supabase/supabase-js'
     2	import { computeDailyFacts, computeDayKind, type DailyFacts, type CheckinSignals } from '@/lib/client/ai-coach/dailyFacts'
     3	import { resolveTone, type Tone } from '@/lib/client/ai-coach/resolveTone'
     4	import type { Freedom, AdviceTrend } from '@/lib/client/ai-coach/adviceRules'
     5	import { resolveProtocolDayByDate, resolveRestProtocolDay } from '@/lib/nutrition/protocol-schedule'
     6	import { fetchClientDayOverride } from '@/lib/client/day-kind'
     7	import { utcRangeForPhysiologicalDate, addDaysToDateKey, getLocalWeekday } from '@/lib/client/checkin/timeWindows'
     8	import { filterSessionsForJsWeekday } from '@/lib/client/plannedSessions'
     9	
    10	const OVER_KCAL = 200
    11	const PROTEIN_SHORT_RATIO = 0.8
    12	
    13	export type DailyCoachContext = {
    14	  facts: DailyFacts
    15	  trend: AdviceTrend
    16	  tone: Tone
    17	  freedom: Freedom
    18	  enabledMorningFields: string[]
    19	  coachId: string | null
    20	}
    21	
    22	/**
    23	 * Single loader: assembles the deterministic DailyFacts + trend + tone + freedom for a client/day.
    24	 * Pure cores (computeDailyFacts/computeDayKind) do the logic; this only fetches.
    25	 */
    26	export async function loadDailyCoachContext(
    27	  db: SupabaseClient,
    28	  clientId: string,
    29	  date: string,
    30	  timezone: string,
    31	  submittedCheckin?: CheckinSignals,
    32	  steps?: number | null,
    33	): Promise<DailyCoachContext> {
    34	  const { start, end } = utcRangeForPhysiologicalDate(date, timezone)
    35	  const dayDate = new Date(`${date}T12:00:00.000Z`)
    36	  const weekday = getLocalWeekday(dayDate, timezone)
    37	  const threeDaysAgo = addDaysToDateKey(date, -3)
    38	  const yesterday = addDaysToDateKey(date, -1)
    39	
    40	  const [
    41	    { data: composerMeals },
    42	    { data: legacyMeals },
    43	    { data: waterRows },
    44	    { data: protocol },
    45	    { data: plannedSessions },
    46	    { data: completedSessions },
    47	    { data: skips },
    48	    { data: trendMeals },
    49	    { data: perClientAi },
    50	    { data: cfgRow },
    51	  ] = await Promise.all([
    52	    db.from('nutrition_meals').select('total_calories, total_protein_g').eq('client_id', clientId).eq('physiological_date', date),
    53	    db.from('meal_logs').select('estimated_macros').eq('client_id', clientId).gte('logged_at', start.toISOString()).lt('logged_at', new Date(end.getTime() + 1).toISOString()).eq('ai_status', 'done'),
    54	    db.from('client_water_logs').select('amount_ml, caffeine_mg').eq('client_id', clientId).gte('logged_at', start.toISOString()).lte('logged_at', end.toISOString()),
    55	    db.from('nutrition_protocols').select('schedule_start_date, nutrition_protocol_days(position, calories, protein_g, hydration_ml, name, carb_cycle_type), nutrition_protocol_schedule_slots(week_index, dow, protocol_day_position)').eq('client_id', clientId).eq('status', 'shared').order('updated_at', { ascending: false }).limit(1).maybeSingle(),
    56	    db.from('program_sessions').select('id, name, day_of_week, days_of_week, programs!inner(status, client_id)').eq('programs.client_id', clientId).eq('programs.status', 'active'),
    57	    db.from('client_session_logs').select('id').eq('client_id', clientId).not('completed_at', 'is', null).gte('completed_at', start.toISOString()).lte('completed_at', end.toISOString()).limit(1),
    58	    db.from('client_workout_skips').select('program_session_id').eq('client_id', clientId).eq('scheduled_date', date),
    59	    db.from('nutrition_meals').select('physiological_date, total_calories, total_protein_g').eq('client_id', clientId).gte('physiological_date', threeDaysAgo).lte('physiological_date', yesterday),
    60	    db.from('coach_ai_settings_per_client').select('ai_tone, coach_id, coaching_freedom').eq('client_id', clientId).maybeSingle(),
    61	    db.from('daily_checkin_configs').select('moments').eq('client_id', clientId).maybeSingle(),
    62	  ])
    63	
    64	  // Global tone needs coach_id (from per-client settings row)
    65	  const coachId = (perClientAi as { coach_id?: string } | null)?.coach_id ?? null
    66	  const { data: coachProfile } = coachId
    67	    ? await db.from('coach_profiles').select('ai_tone').eq('coach_id', coachId).maybeSingle()
    68	    : { data: null }
    69	
    70	  // ── Nutrition ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    71	  const kcalLogged =
    72	    (composerMeals ?? []).reduce((s: number, m: any) => s + Number(m.total_calories ?? 0), 0) +
    73	    (legacyMeals ?? []).reduce((s: number, m: any) => s + Number((m.estimated_macros as any)?.calories_kcal ?? 0), 0)
    74	  const proteinLogged =
    75	    (composerMeals ?? []).reduce((s: number, m: any) => s + Number(m.total_protein_g ?? 0), 0) +
    76	    (legacyMeals ?? []).reduce((s: number, m: any) => s + Number((m.estimated_macros as any)?.protein_g ?? 0), 0)
    77	  const hydrationMl = (waterRows ?? []).reduce((s: number, w: any) => s + Number(w.amount_ml ?? 0), 0)
    78	  const caffeineMg = (waterRows ?? []).reduce((s: number, w: any) => s + Number(w.caffeine_mg ?? 0), 0)
    79	
    80	  // ── Day kind / session ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    81	  const dayOverride = await fetchClientDayOverride(db, clientId, date)
    82	  const protocolDays = (protocol as any)?.nutrition_protocol_days ?? []
    83	  const rawProtocolDay = resolveProtocolDayByDate(
    84	    date,
    85	    (protocol as any)?.schedule_start_date ?? null,
    86	    protocolDays,
    87	    (protocol as any)?.nutrition_protocol_schedule_slots ?? [],
    88	  ) as any
    89	  const isOff = dayOverride?.kind === 'off'
    90	  const protocolDay = isOff ? (resolveRestProtocolDay(protocolDays) ?? rawProtocolDay) : rawProtocolDay
    91	
    92	  const kcalTarget = Number(protocolDay?.calories ?? 0)
    93	  const proteinTarget = Number(protocolDay?.protein_g ?? 0)
    94	  const hydrationTargetMl = Number(protocolDay?.hydration_ml ?? 2500)
    95	
    96	  const plannedList = filterSessionsForJsWeekday(
    97	    (plannedSessions ?? []) as Array<{ id: string; name?: string | null; day_of_week?: number | null; days_of_week?: number[] | null }>,
    98	    weekday,
    99	  )
   100	  const plannedSessionName = plannedList[0]?.name ?? null
   101	  const completed = ((completedSessions ?? []) as any[]).length > 0
   102	  const skipped = ((skips ?? []) as any[]).length > 0
   103	  const { dayKind, sessionStatus } = computeDayKind({
   104	    plannedSessionName,
   105	    completed,
   106	    skipped,
   107	    overrideOff: isOff,
   108	  })
   109	
   110	  // ── Trend (3 days) ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   111	  const byDay = new Map<string, { kcal: number; protein: number }>()
   112	  for (const m of (trendMeals ?? []) as any[]) {
   113	    const d = m.physiological_date as string
   114	    const cur = byDay.get(d) ?? { kcal: 0, protein: 0 }
   115	    cur.kcal += Number(m.total_calories ?? 0)
   116	    cur.protein += Number(m.total_protein_g ?? 0)
   117	    byDay.set(d, cur)
   118	  }
   119	  let kcalOverDays = 0
   120	  let proteinShortDays = 0
   121	  for (const { kcal, protein } of Array.from(byDay.values())) {
   122	    if (kcalTarget > 0 && kcal - kcalTarget > OVER_KCAL) kcalOverDays++
   123	    if (proteinTarget > 0 && protein < proteinTarget * PROTEIN_SHORT_RATIO) proteinShortDays++
   124	  }
   125	
   126	  // ── Tone / fields ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   127	  const tone = resolveTone(
   128	    (perClientAi as { ai_tone?: string | null } | null)?.ai_tone ?? null,
   129	    (coachProfile as { ai_tone?: string | null } | null)?.ai_tone ?? null,
   130	  )
   131	  const cfgMoments = ((cfgRow as { moments?: Array<{ moment?: string; fields?: string[] }> } | null)?.moments) ?? []
   132	  const enabledMorningFields = cfgMoments.find((m) => m.moment === 'morning')?.fields ?? []
   133	
   134	  const rawFreedom = (perClientAi as { coaching_freedom?: string | null } | null)?.coaching_freedom ?? 'safe'
   135	  const freedom: Freedom = rawFreedom === 'none' || rawFreedom === 'extended' ? rawFreedom : 'safe'
   136	
   137	  const facts = computeDailyFacts({
   138	    dayKind,
   139	    sessionStatus,
   140	    plannedSessionName,
   141	    kcalLogged,
   142	    kcalTarget,
   143	    proteinLogged,
   144	    proteinTarget,
   145	    hydrationMl,
   146	    hydrationTargetMl,
   147	    caffeineMg,
   148	    steps: steps ?? null,
   149	    checkin: submittedCheckin ?? {},
   150	  })
   151	
   152	  return {
   153	    facts,
   154	    trend: { kcalOverDays, proteinShortDays },
   155	    tone,
   156	    freedom,
   157	    enabledMorningFields,
   158	    coachId,
   159	  }
   160	}

FILE: ./lib/client/ai-coach/buildSystemPrompt.ts

     1	import { createClient as createServiceClient } from '@supabase/supabase-js'
     2	import { computePhysiologicalDate } from '@/lib/nutrition/physiological-date'
     3	import { resolveClientTimezone } from '@/lib/client/checkin/resolveClientTimezone'
     4	import { utcRangeForPhysiologicalDate } from '@/lib/client/checkin/timeWindows'
     5	import { computeDailySignals } from '@/lib/client/ai-coach/chatSignals'
     6	import { resolveTone } from '@/lib/client/ai-coach/resolveTone'
     7	
     8	function svc() {
     9	  return createServiceClient(
    10	    process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_URL!,
    11	    process.env.SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY!
    12	  )
    13	}
    14	
    15	function pct(val: number, total: number): string {
    16	  if (!total) return '0%'
    17	  return `${Math.round((val / total) * 100)}%`
    18	}
    19	
    20	function fmtDate(date: string): string {
    21	  const [, m, d] = date.split('-')
    22	  const months = ['jan', 'fév', 'mar', 'avr', 'mai', 'jun', 'jul', 'aoû', 'sep', 'oct', 'nov', 'déc']
    23	  return `${parseInt(d)} ${months[parseInt(m) - 1]}`
    24	}
    25	
    26	export async function buildSystemPrompt(clientId: string): Promise<string> {
    27	  const db = svc()
    28	  const timezone = await resolveClientTimezone(db, clientId)
    29	  const today = computePhysiologicalDate(new Date(), timezone)
    30	  const { start: physiologicalStart, end: physiologicalEnd } = utcRangeForPhysiologicalDate(today, timezone)
    31	  const dayStart = physiologicalStart.toISOString()
    32	  const dayEnd   = physiologicalEnd.toISOString()
    33	  const nowTime  = new Date().toLocaleTimeString('fr-FR', { hour: '2-digit', minute: '2-digit' })
    34	  const nextPhysioStart = new Date(physiologicalEnd.getTime() + 1).toISOString()
    35	
    36	  const threeDaysAgo = (() => {
    37	    const d = new Date(`${today}T00:00:00`)
    38	    d.setDate(d.getDate() - 3)
    39	    return d.toISOString().split('T')[0]
    40	  })()
    41	
    42	  // Sequential first: need coach_id before running parallel queries
    43	  const { data: profileData } = await db
    44	    .from('coach_clients')
    45	    .select('first_name, goal, tdee, fitness_level, coach_id, display_lang')
    46	    .eq('id', clientId)
    47	    .single()
    48	
    49	  const firstName    = profileData?.first_name   ?? 'le client'
    50	  const goal         = profileData?.goal          ?? 'non renseigné'
    51	  const tdee         = profileData?.tdee          ?? 0
    52	  const fitnessLevel = profileData?.fitness_level ?? 'intermédiaire'
    53	  const coachId      = profileData?.coach_id      ?? null
    54	  const clientDisplayLang = (profileData?.display_lang ?? 'fr') as 'fr' | 'es' | 'en'
    55	
    56	  const [
    57	    coachProfileResult,
    58	    nutritionProtocol,
    59	    mealsResult,
    60	    legacyMealsResult,
    61	    waterResult,
    62	    sessionResult,
    63	    activitiesResult,
    64	    restrictionsResult,
    65	    bodyCompResult,
    66	    nutritionTrendsResult,
    67	    checkinsResult,
    68	    activeProgramResult,
    69	    perClientToneResult,
    70	    globalToneResult,
    71	    plannedPrepsResult,
    72	  ] = await Promise.allSettled([
    73	    coachId
    74	      ? db.from('user_profiles').select('first_name, last_name').eq('id', coachId).single()
    75	      : Promise.resolve({ data: null }),
    76	    db.from('nutrition_protocols')
    77	      .select('name, nutrition_protocol_days(calories, protein_g, fat_g, carbs_g, hydration_ml)')
    78	      .eq('client_id', clientId)
    79	      .eq('status', 'shared')
    80	      .order('created_at', { ascending: false })
    81	      .limit(1)
    82	      .maybeSingle(),
    83	    // Nutrition Composer meals (correct columns)
    84	    db.from('nutrition_meals')
    85	      .select('total_calories, total_protein_g, total_fat_g, total_carbs_g, meal_type, title, logged_at')
    86	      .eq('client_id', clientId)
    87	      .eq('physiological_date', today)
    88	      .order('logged_at', { ascending: true }),
    89	    // Legacy meal_logs
    90	    db.from('meal_logs')
    91	      .select('estimated_macros, logged_at, meal_name')
    92	      .eq('client_id', clientId)
    93	      .gte('logged_at', physiologicalStart.toISOString())
    94	      .lt('logged_at', nextPhysioStart)
    95	      .eq('ai_status', 'done'),
    96	    db.from('client_water_logs')
    97	      .select('amount_ml, caffeine_mg')
    98	      .eq('client_id', clientId)
    99	      .gte('logged_at', dayStart)
   100	      .lte('logged_at', dayEnd),
   101	    db.from('client_session_logs')
   102	      .select('id, completed_at')
   103	      .eq('client_id', clientId)
   104	      .not('completed_at', 'is', null)
   105	      .gte('completed_at', dayStart)
   106	      .lte('completed_at', dayEnd)
   107	      .order('completed_at', { ascending: false })
   108	      .limit(1)
   109	      .maybeSingle(),
   110	    db.from('client_activity_logs')
   111	      .select('activity_type, custom_label, duration_min')
   112	      .eq('client_id', clientId)
   113	      .gte('started_at', dayStart)
   114	      .lte('started_at', dayEnd),
   115	    db.from('metric_annotations')
   116	      .select('label, body_part, severity')
   117	      .eq('client_id', clientId)
   118	      .eq('event_type', 'injury')
   119	      .not('body_part', 'is', null),
   120	    // Full bilan history — ascending (oldest first) for correct progression delta
   121	    db.from('assessment_submissions')
   122	      .select('bilan_date, assessment_responses(field_key, value_number)')
   123	      .eq('client_id', clientId)
   124	      .eq('status', 'completed')
   125	      .order('bilan_date', { ascending: true })
   126	      .limit(10),
   127	    // 3-day nutrition trends
   128	    db.from('nutrition_meals')
   129	      .select('physiological_date, total_calories, total_protein_g')
   130	      .eq('client_id', clientId)
   131	      .gte('physiological_date', threeDaysAgo)
   132	      .lt('physiological_date', today)
   133	      .order('physiological_date', { ascending: false }),
   134	    // Check-ins of the past 3 days
   135	    db.from('client_daily_checkins')
   136	      .select('date, flow_type, sleep_hours, sleep_quality, energy_level, stress_level, weight_kg, hunger_level, muscle_soreness')
   137	      .eq('client_id', clientId)
   138	      .gte('date', threeDaysAgo)
   139	      .lte('date', today),
   140	    // Active program with sessions
   141	    db.from('programs')
   142	      .select('name, weeks, frequency, program_sessions(id, name, day_of_week, days_of_week)')
   143	      .eq('client_id', clientId)
   144	      .eq('status', 'active')
   145	      .order('created_at', { ascending: false })
   146	      .limit(1)
   147	      .maybeSingle(),
   148	    // Tone — per-client override + coach global
   149	    db.from('coach_ai_settings_per_client').select('ai_tone, ai_chat_lang').eq('client_id', clientId).maybeSingle(),
   150	    coachId
   151	      ? db.from('coach_profiles').select('ai_tone').eq('coach_id', coachId).maybeSingle()
   152	      : Promise.resolve({ data: null }),
   153	    // Planned preps for today
   154	    db.from('client_nutrition_preps')
   155	      .select('meal_slot, total_calories, total_protein_g, scenario_label, title')
   156	      .eq('client_id', clientId)
   157	      .eq('physiological_date', today)
   158	      .eq('status', 'planned'),
   159	  ])
   160	
   161	  // ── Tone (D5) ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   162	  const perClientTone = perClientToneResult.status === 'fulfilled' ? (perClientToneResult.value as any)?.data?.ai_tone ?? null : null
   163	  const globalTone = globalToneResult.status === 'fulfilled' ? (globalToneResult.value as any)?.data?.ai_tone ?? null : null
   164	  const tone = resolveTone(perClientTone, globalTone)
   165	  const TONE_DIRECTIVE: Record<typeof tone, string> = {
   166	    strict: 'Ton strict, direct, sans complaisance. Pas de flatterie.',
   167	    bienveillant: 'Ton bienveillant et direct. Encourageant sans flatterie.',
   168	    motivant: 'Ton motivant et énergique. Pas de flatterie creuse.',
   169	    neutre: 'Ton neutre et factuel. Sobre.',
   170	  }
   171	
   172	  // ── Chat language ─────────────────────────────────────
   173	  const perClientSettings = perClientToneResult.status === 'fulfilled' ? (perClientToneResult.value as any)?.data : null
   174	  const coachLangOverride = perClientSettings?.ai_chat_lang as 'fr' | 'es' | 'en' | null ?? null
   175	  const chatLang: 'fr' | 'es' | 'en' = coachLangOverride ?? clientDisplayLang
   176	
   177	  const LANG_DIRECTIVE: Record<'fr' | 'es' | 'en', string> = {
   178	    fr: "Tu réponds TOUJOURS en français, quelle que soit la langue utilisée par le client.",
   179	    es: "Respondes SIEMPRE en español, sin importar el idioma que use el cliente.",
   180	    en: "You ALWAYS reply in English, regardless of the language used by the client.",
   181	  }
   182	
   183	  // ── Coach identity ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   184	  const coachProfile = coachProfileResult.status === 'fulfilled' ? (coachProfileResult.value as any)?.data : null
   185	  const coachFirstName = coachProfile?.first_name ?? null
   186	  const coachLastName  = coachProfile?.last_name  ?? null
   187	  const coachName = coachFirstName
   188	    ? [coachFirstName, coachLastName].filter(Boolean).join(' ')
   189	    : 'ton coach'
   190	
   191	  // ── Macros targets ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   192	  const protocol = nutritionProtocol.status === 'fulfilled' ? nutritionProtocol.value.data : null
   193	  const protocolDay = (protocol as any)?.nutrition_protocol_days?.[0]
   194	  const targetKcal: number     = protocolDay?.calories     ?? tdee
   195	  const targetProtein: number  = protocolDay?.protein_g    ?? 0
   196	  const targetFat: number      = protocolDay?.fat_g        ?? 0
   197	  const targetCarbs: number    = protocolDay?.carbs_g      ?? 0
   198	  const targetWaterMl: number  = protocolDay?.hydration_ml ?? 2500
   199	
   200	  // ── Today nutrition (both sources) ────────────────────────────────────────
   201	  const composerMeals    = mealsResult.status       === 'fulfilled' ? (mealsResult.value.data       ?? []) : []
   202	  const legacyMealsData  = legacyMealsResult.status === 'fulfilled' ? (legacyMealsResult.value.data ?? []) : []
   203	
   204	  const totalKcal =
   205	    composerMeals.reduce((s, m) => s + Number((m as any).total_calories ?? 0), 0) +
   206	    legacyMealsData.reduce((s: number, m: any) => s + Number(m.estimated_macros?.calories_kcal ?? 0), 0)
   207	
   208	  const totalProtein =
   209	    composerMeals.reduce((s, m) => s + Number((m as any).total_protein_g ?? 0), 0) +
   210	    legacyMealsData.reduce((s: number, m: any) => s + Number(m.estimated_macros?.protein_g ?? 0), 0)
   211	
   212	  const totalFat =
   213	    composerMeals.reduce((s, m) => s + Number((m as any).total_fat_g ?? 0), 0) +
   214	    legacyMealsData.reduce((s: number, m: any) => s + Number(m.estimated_macros?.fat_g ?? 0), 0)
   215	
   216	  const totalCarbs =
   217	    composerMeals.reduce((s, m) => s + Number((m as any).total_carbs_g ?? 0), 0) +
   218	    legacyMealsData.reduce((s: number, m: any) => s + Number(m.estimated_macros?.carbs_g ?? 0), 0)
   219	
   220	  const MEAL_LABELS: Record<string, string> = {
   221	    breakfast: 'Petit-déjeuner', lunch: 'Déjeuner',
   222	    dinner: 'Dîner', snack: 'Collation',
   223	  }
   224	
   225	  const mealsLines = composerMeals.length > 0 || legacyMealsData.length > 0
   226	    ? [
   227	        ...composerMeals.map((m: any) => {
   228	          const time  = new Date(m.logged_at).toLocaleTimeString('fr-FR', { hour: '2-digit', minute: '2-digit' })
   229	          const label = m.title ?? MEAL_LABELS[m.meal_type as string] ?? 'Repas'
   230	          return `  - ${time} ${label}: ${Math.round(Number(m.total_calories ?? 0))} kcal`
   231	        }),
   232	        ...legacyMealsData.map((m: any) => {
   233	          const time = new Date(m.logged_at).toLocaleTimeString('fr-FR', { hour: '2-digit', minute: '2-digit' })
   234	          return `  - ${time} ${m.meal_name ?? 'Repas'}: ${Math.round(Number(m.estimated_macros?.calories_kcal ?? 0))} kcal`
   235	        }),
   236	      ].join('\n')
   237	    : '  - Aucun repas loggé'
   238	
   239	  // ── Water ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   240	  const water        = waterResult.status === 'fulfilled' ? (waterResult.value.data ?? []) : []
   241	  const totalWaterMl = water.reduce((s, w) => s + Number(w.amount_ml ?? 0), 0)
   242	  const totalCaffeineMg = water.reduce((s, w) => s + Number(w.caffeine_mg ?? 0), 0)
   243	
   244	  // ── Session (completed today) ─────────────────────────────────────────────
   245	  const session     = sessionResult.status === 'fulfilled' ? sessionResult.value.data : null
   246	  const sessionLine = session
   247	    ? `Séance complétée à ${new Date(session.completed_at as string).toLocaleTimeString('fr-FR', { hour: '2-digit', minute: '2-digit' })}`
   248	    : "Aucune séance complétée aujourd'hui"
   249	
   250	  // ── Activities ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   251	  const activities      = activitiesResult.status === 'fulfilled' ? (activitiesResult.value.data ?? []) : []
   252	  const activitiesLine  = activities.length > 0
   253	    ? activities.map(a => `  - ${a.custom_label ?? a.activity_type} ${a.duration_min}min`).join('\n')
   254	    : '  Aucune'
   255	
   256	  // ── Restrictions ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   257	  const restrictions     = restrictionsResult.status === 'fulfilled' ? (restrictionsResult.value.data ?? []) : []
   258	  const restrictionsLine = restrictions.length > 0
   259	    ? restrictions.map(r => `${r.label ?? r.body_part} (${r.severity})`).join(', ')
   260	    : 'aucune'
   261	
   262	  // ── Body composition — full history ───────────────────────────────────────
   263	  const bilans = bodyCompResult.status === 'fulfilled' ? (bodyCompResult.value.data ?? []) : []
   264	  type AssessmentResponse = { field_key: string; value_number: number | null }
   265	  const extractValues = (bilan: any): Record<string, number> => {
   266	    const out: Record<string, number> = {}
   267	    for (const r of (bilan?.assessment_responses ?? []) as AssessmentResponse[]) {
   268	      if (r.value_number != null) out[r.field_key] = r.value_number
   269	    }
   270	    return out
   271	  }
   272	
   273	  const firstBilanData  = bilans[0]     ? extractValues(bilans[0])                : {}
   274	  const latestBilanData = bilans.length ? extractValues(bilans[bilans.length - 1]) : {}
   275	
   276	  const firstWeight  = firstBilanData['weight_kg']    ?? null
   277	  const firstBF      = firstBilanData['body_fat_pct'] ?? null
   278	  const latestWeight = latestBilanData['weight_kg']    ?? null
   279	  const latestBF     = latestBilanData['body_fat_pct'] ?? null
   280	  const latestLBM    = latestBilanData['lean_mass_kg'] ?? null
   281	
   282	  const totalWeightDelta = latestWeight != null && firstWeight != null
   283	    ? +(latestWeight - firstWeight).toFixed(1) : null
   284	  const totalBFDelta     = latestBF != null && firstBF != null
   285	    ? +(latestBF - firstBF).toFixed(1) : null
   286	
   287	  let bodyCompLines: string
   288	  if (latestWeight == null) {
   289	    bodyCompLines = 'Aucun bilan corporel enregistré'
   290	  } else {
   291	    const lines: string[] = []
   292	    if (bilans[0]?.bilan_date && bilans.length > 1) {
   293	      lines.push(`Début du suivi (${fmtDate(bilans[0].bilan_date)}): ${firstWeight ?? '?'}kg${firstBF != null ? ` | MG ${firstBF}%` : ''}`)
   294	    }
   295	    // Intermediate bilans
   296	    if (bilans.length > 2) {
   297	      bilans.slice(1, -1).forEach((b: any) => {
   298	        const v  = extractValues(b)
   299	        const w  = v['weight_kg'] ?? '?'
   300	        const bf = v['body_fat_pct']
   301	        lines.push(`  ${fmtDate(b.bilan_date)}: ${w}kg${bf != null ? ` | MG ${bf}%` : ''}`)
   302	      })
   303	    }
   304	    const lastBilan = bilans[bilans.length - 1]
   305	    lines.push(`Actuel (${fmtDate(lastBilan.bilan_date)}): ${latestWeight}kg${latestBF != null ? ` | MG ${latestBF}%` : ''}${latestLBM != null ? ` | MM ${latestLBM}kg` : ''}`)
   306	    if (totalWeightDelta !== null) {
   307	      const sign = totalWeightDelta > 0 ? '+' : ''
   308	      lines.push(`PROGRESSION TOTALE: ${sign}${totalWeightDelta}kg poids${totalBFDelta !== null ? ` | ${totalBFDelta > 0 ? '+' : ''}${totalBFDelta}% MG` : ''}`)
   309	    }
   310	    bodyCompLines = lines.join('\n')
   311	  }
   312	
   313	  // ── Nutrition trends (3 derniers jours) ───────────────────────────────────
   314	  const trendRows = nutritionTrendsResult.status === 'fulfilled'
   315	    ? (nutritionTrendsResult.value.data ?? [])
   316	    : []
   317	
   318	  const trendBlock = trendRows.length > 0
   319	    ? trendRows.map((row: any) => {
   320	        const kcal      = Math.round(Number(row.total_calories ?? 0))

FILE: ./lib/client/smart/nutritionAlerts.ts
------------------------------------------------------------
     1	export type NutritionAlertCode =
     2	  | 'protein_low'
     3	  | 'carbs_limit'
     4	  | 'hydration_low'
     5	  | 'lunch_missing'
     6	
     7	export type NutritionAlertSeverity = 'info' | 'warning' | 'critical'
     8	
     9	export type NutritionAlert = {
    10	  code: NutritionAlertCode
    11	  severity: NutritionAlertSeverity
    12	  title: string
    13	  body?: string
    14	  delta?: number
    15	}
    16	
    17	export type NutritionConsumed = {
    18	  kcal: number
    19	  protein_g: number
    20	  carbs_g: number
    21	  fat_g: number
    22	  water_ml: number
    23	  caffeine_mg?: number
    24	}
    25	
    26	export type NutritionInput = {
    27	  consumed: NutritionConsumed
    28	  target: NutritionConsumed
    29	  currentHour: number
    30	  hasLunchLog: boolean
    31	}
    32	
    33	export function computeNutritionAlerts(input: NutritionInput): NutritionAlert[] {
    34	  const alerts: NutritionAlert[] = []
    35	  const { consumed, target, currentHour, hasLunchLog } = input
    36	
    37	  // Rule 1: protein_low (warning) — after 14h, behind schedule
    38	  if (currentHour >= 14) {
    39	    const expected = target.protein_g * (currentHour / 22)
    40	    const threshold = expected * 0.8
    41	    if (consumed.protein_g < threshold) {
    42	      const delta = Math.round(target.protein_g - consumed.protein_g)
    43	      alerts.push({
    44	        code: 'protein_low',
    45	        severity: 'warning',
    46	        title: 'PROTÉINES EN RETARD',
    47	        body: `il te reste ${delta}g pour atteindre ${target.protein_g}g`,
    48	        delta,
    49	      })
    50	    }
    51	  }
    52	
    53	  // Rule 2: carbs_limit (critical) — over target
    54	  if (consumed.carbs_g > target.carbs_g) {
    55	    const delta = Math.round(consumed.carbs_g - target.carbs_g)
    56	    alerts.push({
    57	      code: 'carbs_limit',
    58	      severity: 'critical',
    59	      title: 'LIMITE GLUCIDES ATTEINTE',
    60	      body: `-${delta}g sur ta cible`,
    61	      delta,
    62	    })
    63	  }
    64	
    65	  // Rule 3: hydration_low (warning) — after 14h, <50% of target
    66	  if (currentHour >= 14) {
    67	    const ratio = target.water_ml > 0 ? consumed.water_ml / target.water_ml : 1
    68	    if (ratio < 0.5) {
    69	      const deltaMl = target.water_ml - consumed.water_ml
    70	      const deltaL = (deltaMl / 1000).toFixed(1)
    71	      alerts.push({
    72	        code: 'hydration_low',
    73	        severity: 'warning',
    74	        title: 'HYDRATATION FAIBLE',
    75	        body: `il manque ${deltaL}L`,
    76	        delta: deltaMl,
    77	      })
    78	    }
    79	  }
    80	
    81	  // Rule 4: lunch_missing (info) — between 13-14h, no lunch log
    82	  if (currentHour >= 13 && currentHour < 15 && !hasLunchLog) {
    83	    alerts.push({
    84	      code: 'lunch_missing',
    85	      severity: 'info',
    86	      title: 'PAS DE DÉJEUNER LOGUÉ',
    87	    })
    88	  }
    89	
    90	  return alerts
    91	}
