     1	export type DrinkType = "water" | "espresso" | "coffee" | "lungo" | "tea"
     2	export type DrinkLogKind = "all" | "water" | "caffeine"
     3	
     4	export type DrinkPreset = {
     5	  drinkType: DrinkType
     6	  label: string
     7	  shortLabel: string
     8	  baseAmountMl: number
     9	  baseCaffeineMg: number
    10	  accent: string
    11	  cupCount: 1 | 2 | 3
    12	  strengthLabel: string
    13	}
    14	
    15	export const DRINK_PRESETS: Record<DrinkType, DrinkPreset> = {
    16	  water: {
    17	    drinkType: "water",
    18	    label: "Eau",
    19	    shortLabel: "Eau",
    20	    baseAmountMl: 250,
    21	    baseCaffeineMg: 0,
    22	    accent: "#60a5fa",
    23	    cupCount: 1,
    24	    strengthLabel: "hydratation",
    25	  },
    26	  espresso: {
    27	    drinkType: "espresso",
    28	    label: "Espresso",
    29	    shortLabel: "Espresso",
    30	    baseAmountMl: 40,
    31	    baseCaffeineMg: 80,
    32	    accent: "#c08457",
    33	    cupCount: 1,
    34	    strengthLabel: "concentré",
    35	  },
    36	  coffee: {
    37	    drinkType: "coffee",
    38	    label: "Café",
    39	    shortLabel: "Café",
    40	    baseAmountMl: 180,
    41	    baseCaffeineMg: 95,
    42	    accent: "#c08457",
    43	    cupCount: 2,
    44	    strengthLabel: "classique",
    45	  },
    46	  lungo: {
    47	    drinkType: "lungo",
    48	    label: "Lungo",
    49	    shortLabel: "Lungo",
    50	    baseAmountMl: 120,
    51	    baseCaffeineMg: 110,
    52	    accent: "#c08457",
    53	    cupCount: 3,
    54	    strengthLabel: "allongé",
    55	  },
    56	  tea: {
    57	    drinkType: "tea",
    58	    label: "Thé",
    59	    shortLabel: "Thé",
    60	    baseAmountMl: 250,
    61	    baseCaffeineMg: 35,
    62	    accent: "#34d399",
    63	    cupCount: 1,
    64	    strengthLabel: "infusé",
    65	  },
    66	}
    67	
    68	const CAFFEINATED_TYPES: Exclude<DrinkType, "water">[] = ["espresso", "coffee", "lungo", "tea"]
    69	
    70	export function isCaffeinatedDrinkType(type: DrinkType): type is Exclude<DrinkType, "water"> {
    71	  return CAFFEINATED_TYPES.includes(type as Exclude<DrinkType, "water">)
    72	}
    73	
    74	export function getDrinkPreset(drinkType: DrinkType): DrinkPreset {
    75	  return DRINK_PRESETS[drinkType]
    76	}
    77	
    78	export function estimateCaffeineMg(drinkType: DrinkType, amountMl: number): number {
    79	  if (drinkType === "water") return 0
    80	  const preset = DRINK_PRESETS[drinkType]
    81	  const safeAmount = Math.max(1, amountMl)
    82	  return Math.max(0, Math.round(preset.baseCaffeineMg * (safeAmount / preset.baseAmountMl)))
    83	}
    84	
    85	export function inferDrinkTypeFromFoodItem(input: { name_fr: string; category_l1: string; category_l2: string | null }): DrinkType {
    86	  const name = input.name_fr.toLowerCase()
    87	  const category = `${input.category_l1 ?? ""} ${input.category_l2 ?? ""}`.toLowerCase()
    88	
    89	  if (input.category_l1 !== "drinks") return "water"
    90	  if (/espresso|expresso/.test(name)) return "espresso"
    91	  if (/lungo/.test(name)) return "lungo"
    92	  if (/(th[eé]|tisane|infusion|rooibos|camomille)/.test(name) || /(th[eé]|tisane|infusion|rooibos|camomille)/.test(category)) return "tea"
    93	  if (/cafe|coffee|cappuccino|latte|macchiato|ristretto/.test(name)) return "coffee"
    94	  if (/chauds?/.test(category)) return "coffee"
    95	  return "water"
    96	}

------------------------------------------------------------
UI CANDIDATE: ./app/api/client/activity-logs/route.ts
------------------------------------------------------------
     1	import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from 'next/server'
     2	import { z } from 'zod'
     3	import { createClient } from '@/utils/supabase/server'
     4	import { createClient as createServiceClient } from '@supabase/supabase-js'
     5	
     6	const bodySchema = z.object({
     7	  activity_type: z.enum(['running', 'cycling', 'swimming', 'walking', 'team_sport', 'other']),
     8	  custom_label: z.string().max(80).optional(),
     9	  started_at: z.string().datetime(),
    10	  duration_min: z.number().int().min(1).max(360),
    11	  intensity: z.number().int().min(1).max(10),
    12	  notes: z.string().max(500).optional(),
    13	})
    14	
    15	function svc() {
    16	  return createServiceClient(
    17	    process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_URL!,
    18	    process.env.SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY!,
    19	  )
    20	}
    21	
    22	async function getClientId(): Promise<string | null> {
    23	  const supabase = createClient()
    24	  const { data: { user } } = await supabase.auth.getUser()
    25	  if (!user) return null
    26	  const { data: cc } = await svc().from('coach_clients').select('id').eq('user_id', user.id).single()
    27	  return cc?.id ?? null
    28	}
    29	
    30	export async function GET(req: NextRequest) {
    31	  const clientId = await getClientId()
    32	  if (!clientId) return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Unauthorized' }, { status: 401 })
    33	
    34	  const url = new URL(req.url)
    35	  const date = url.searchParams.get('date')
    36	
    37	  let q = svc()
    38	    .from('client_activity_logs')
    39	    .select('id, activity_type, custom_label, started_at, duration_min, intensity, notes')
    40	    .eq('client_id', clientId)
    41	    .order('started_at', { ascending: false })
    42	    .limit(50)
    43	
    44	  if (date) {
    45	    q = q.gte('started_at', `${date}T00:00:00Z`).lte('started_at', `${date}T23:59:59Z`)
    46	  }
    47	
    48	  const { data, error } = await q
    49	  if (error) return NextResponse.json({ error: error.message }, { status: 500 })
    50	  return NextResponse.json({ logs: data ?? [] })
    51	}
    52	
    53	export async function POST(req: NextRequest) {
    54	  const clientId = await getClientId()
    55	  if (!clientId) return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Unauthorized' }, { status: 401 })
    56	
    57	  const parsed = bodySchema.safeParse(await req.json())
    58	  if (!parsed.success) {
    59	    return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Invalid body', issues: parsed.error.issues }, { status: 400 })
    60	  }
    61	
    62	  const { data, error } = await svc()
    63	    .from('client_activity_logs')
    64	    .insert({ ...parsed.data, client_id: clientId })
    65	    .select('id')
    66	    .single()
    67	
    68	  if (error) return NextResponse.json({ error: error.message }, { status: 500 })
    69	  return NextResponse.json({ id: data.id }, { status: 201 })
    70	}

------------------------------------------------------------
UI CANDIDATE: ./app/api/client/nutrition-alerts/route.ts
------------------------------------------------------------
     1	import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from 'next/server'
     2	import { createClient } from '@/utils/supabase/server'
     3	import { createClient as createServiceClient } from '@supabase/supabase-js'
     4	import { computeNutritionAlerts } from '@/lib/client/smart/nutritionAlerts'
     5	import { computeMacroEnergy } from '@/lib/nutrition/energy'
     6	import { computePhysiologicalDate } from '@/lib/nutrition/physiological-date'
     7	import { resolveProtocolDayByDate } from '@/lib/nutrition/protocol-schedule'
     8	import { resolveClientTimezone } from '@/lib/client/checkin/resolveClientTimezone'
     9	import { utcRangeForPhysiologicalDate } from '@/lib/client/checkin/timeWindows'
    10	
    11	function svc() {
    12	  return createServiceClient(
    13	    process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_URL!,
    14	    process.env.SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY!,
    15	  )
    16	}
    17	
    18	export async function GET(_req: NextRequest) {
    19	  const supabase = createClient()
    20	  const { data: { user } } = await supabase.auth.getUser()
    21	  if (!user) return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Unauthorized' }, { status: 401 })
    22	
    23	  const { data: cc } = await svc().from('coach_clients').select('id').eq('user_id', user.id).single()
    24	  if (!cc) return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Unauthorized' }, { status: 401 })
    25	
    26	  const timezone = await resolveClientTimezone(svc(), cc.id)
    27	  const date = computePhysiologicalDate(new Date(), timezone)
    28	  const { start: physiologicalStart, end: physiologicalEnd } = utcRangeForPhysiologicalDate(date, timezone)
    29	
    30	  const { data: proto } = await svc()
    31	    .from('nutrition_protocols')
    32	    .select('schedule_start_date, nutrition_protocol_days(position, calories, protein_g, carbs_g, fat_g, hydration_ml, carb_cycle_type), nutrition_protocol_schedule_slots(week_index, dow, protocol_day_position)')
    33	    .eq('client_id', cc.id)
    34	    .eq('status', 'shared')
    35	    .order('created_at', { ascending: false })
    36	    .limit(1)
    37	    .maybeSingle()
    38	
    39	  const td = resolveProtocolDayByDate(
    40	    date,
    41	    (proto as any)?.schedule_start_date ?? null,
    42	    (proto?.nutrition_protocol_days as any) ?? [],
    43	    (proto?.nutrition_protocol_schedule_slots as any) ?? [],
    44	  )
    45	  const target = {
    46	    kcal: Number(td?.calories ?? 0),
    47	    protein_g: Number(td?.protein_g ?? 0),
    48	    carbs_g: Number(td?.carbs_g ?? 0),
    49	    fat_g: Number(td?.fat_g ?? 0),
    50	    water_ml: Number(td?.hydration_ml ?? 2500),
    51	  }
    52	
    53	  const { data: meals } = await svc()
    54	    .from('nutrition_meals')
    55	    .select('meal_type, total_calories, total_protein_g, total_carbs_g, total_fat_g, total_fiber_g')
    56	    .eq('client_id', cc.id)
    57	    .eq('physiological_date', date)
    58	
    59	  const consumed = (meals ?? []).reduce(
    60	    (acc, m) => ({
    61	      kcal: acc.kcal + computeMacroEnergy({
    62	        protein_g: Number(m.total_protein_g ?? 0),
    63	        carbs_g: Number(m.total_carbs_g ?? 0),
    64	        fat_g: Number(m.total_fat_g ?? 0),
    65	        fiber_g: Number(m.total_fiber_g ?? 0),
    66	      }),
    67	      protein_g: acc.protein_g + Number(m.total_protein_g ?? 0),
    68	      carbs_g: acc.carbs_g + Number(m.total_carbs_g ?? 0),
    69	      fat_g: acc.fat_g + Number(m.total_fat_g ?? 0),
    70	    }),
    71	    { kcal: 0, protein_g: 0, carbs_g: 0, fat_g: 0 },
    72	  )
    73	
    74	  const { data: water } = await svc()
    75	    .from('client_water_logs')
    76	    .select('amount_ml, caffeine_mg')
    77	    .eq('client_id', cc.id)
    78	    .gte('logged_at', physiologicalStart.toISOString())
    79	    .lte('logged_at', physiologicalEnd.toISOString())
    80	
    81	  const water_ml = (water ?? []).reduce((s, w) => s + Number(w.amount_ml ?? 0), 0)
    82	  const caffeine_mg = (water ?? []).reduce((s, w) => s + Number(w.caffeine_mg ?? 0), 0)
    83	  const hasLunchLog = (meals ?? []).some(m => m.meal_type === 'lunch')
    84	  const currentHour = new Date().getHours()
    85	
    86	  const alerts = computeNutritionAlerts({
    87	    consumed: { ...consumed, water_ml, caffeine_mg },
    88	    target,
    89	    currentHour,
    90	    hasLunchLog,
    91	  })
    92	
    93	  // Engine triggers — best-effort, never block daily alerts
    94	  let engineTriggers: import('@/lib/nutrition/engine/types').TriggerRecommendation[] = []
    95	  try {
    96	    const { computeTriggers } = await import('@/lib/nutrition/engine/triggers')
    97	    const { data: recentCheckins } = await svc()
    98	      .from('client_daily_checkins')
    99	      .select('flow_type, sleep_hours, energy_level, stress_level, hunger_level, muscle_soreness')
   100	      .eq('client_id', cc.id)
   101	      .gte('date', new Date(Date.now() - 7 * 86400000).toISOString().slice(0, 10))
   102	    const morning = (recentCheckins ?? []).filter(r => r.flow_type === 'morning')
   103	    const evening = (recentCheckins ?? []).filter(r => r.flow_type === 'evening')
   104	    const avgOf = (arr: (number | null)[]): number | null => {
   105	      const vals = arr.filter((v): v is number => v !== null)
   106	      return vals.length > 0 ? vals.reduce((s, v) => s + v, 0) / vals.length : null
   107	    }
   108	    engineTriggers = computeTriggers({
   109	      avgSleepH: avgOf(morning.map(r => r.sleep_hours !== null ? Number(r.sleep_hours) : null)),
   110	      avgEnergyLevel: avgOf(morning.map(r => r.energy_level)),
   111	      avgStressLevel: avgOf(morning.map(r => r.stress_level)),
   112	      avgHungerLevel: avgOf(evening.map(r => r.hunger_level)),
   113	      avgMuscleSoreness: avgOf(evening.map(r => r.muscle_soreness)),
   114	      isLowCarbDay: (td as { carb_cycle_type?: string } | null)?.carb_cycle_type === 'low',
   115	      rpeLastSession: null,
   116	      performanceTrend: null,
   117	    })
   118	  } catch { /* never block daily alerts */ }
   119	
   120	  return NextResponse.json({ alerts, triggers: engineTriggers })
   121	}

------------------------------------------------------------
UI CANDIDATE: ./app/api/client/nutrition/hydration/route.ts
------------------------------------------------------------
     1	import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from "next/server"
     2	import { createClient } from "@/utils/supabase/server"
     3	import { createClient as createServiceClient } from "@supabase/supabase-js"
     4	import { z } from "zod"
     5	import { computePhysiologicalDate } from "@/lib/nutrition/physiological-date"
     6	import { calcEntryMacros } from "@/lib/nutrition/food-items"
     7	import { computeMacroEnergy } from "@/lib/nutrition/energy"
     8	import { resolveClientTimezone } from "@/lib/client/checkin/resolveClientTimezone"
     9	import { estimateCaffeineMg, inferDrinkTypeFromFoodItem } from "@/lib/client/nutrition/drinks"
    10	
    11	function service() {
    12	  return createServiceClient(
    13	    process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_URL!,
    14	    process.env.SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY!
    15	  )
    16	}
    17	
    18	async function resolveClientId(userId: string): Promise<string | null> {
    19	  const { data } = await service().from("coach_clients").select("id").eq("user_id", userId).single()
    20	  return data?.id ?? null
    21	}
    22	
    23	const schema = z.object({
    24	  food_item_id: z.string().uuid(),
    25	  quantity_g: z.number().positive().max(5000),
    26	})
    27	
    28	/**
    29	 * POST /api/client/nutrition/hydration
    30	 * Loguer une boisson (eau, café...) sans créer une carte repas visible dans le journal.
    31	 * Crée ou réutilise un seul repas "Boissons" par jour physiologique.
    32	 * Ce repas n'apparaît PAS dans la liste des repas du journal (meal_type = "drinks").
    33	 * Les macros sont quand même comptabilisées dans le total du jour.
    34	 */
    35	export async function POST(req: NextRequest) {
    36	  const supabase = createClient()
    37	  const { data: { user } } = await supabase.auth.getUser()
    38	  if (!user) return NextResponse.json({ error: "Unauthorized" }, { status: 401 })
    39	
    40	  const clientId = await resolveClientId(user.id)
    41	  if (!clientId) return NextResponse.json({ error: "Client not found" }, { status: 404 })
    42	
    43	  const body = schema.safeParse(await req.json())
    44	  if (!body.success) return NextResponse.json({ error: body.error }, { status: 400 })
    45	
    46	  const { food_item_id, quantity_g } = body.data
    47	  const db = service()
    48	  const timezone = await resolveClientTimezone(db, clientId)
    49	  const loggedAt = new Date()
    50	  const today = computePhysiologicalDate(loggedAt, timezone)
    51	
    52	  // Fetch food item
    53	  const { data: item } = await db
    54	    .from("food_items")
    55	    .select("id, name_fr, category_l1, category_l2, kcal_per_100g, protein_per_100g, carbs_per_100g, fat_per_100g, fiber_per_100g")
    56	    .eq("id", food_item_id)
    57	    .single()
    58	  if (!item) return NextResponse.json({ error: "Food item not found" }, { status: 404 })
    59	
    60	  const macros = calcEntryMacros(
    61	    { ...item, name_fr: "", category_l1: "drinks", category_l2: "eau", item_key: "", source: "internal", is_verified: true },
    62	    quantity_g
    63	  )
    64	
    65	  // Trouver ou créer un repas "drinks" pour aujourd'hui
    66	  let mealId: string
    67	  const { data: existing } = await db
    68	    .from("nutrition_meals")
    69	    .select("id, total_calories, total_protein_g, total_carbs_g, total_fat_g, total_fiber_g")
    70	    .eq("client_id", clientId)
    71	    .eq("physiological_date", today)
    72	    .eq("meal_type", "drinks" as any)
    73	    .maybeSingle()
    74	
    75	  if (existing) {
    76	    mealId = existing.id
    77	    // Mettre à jour les totaux
    78	    const nextTotals = {
    79	      total_protein_g: Math.round((Number(existing.total_protein_g) + macros.protein_g) * 10) / 10,
    80	      total_carbs_g: Math.round((Number(existing.total_carbs_g) + macros.carbs_g) * 10) / 10,
    81	      total_fat_g: Math.round((Number(existing.total_fat_g) + macros.fat_g) * 10) / 10,
    82	      total_fiber_g: Math.round((Number(existing.total_fiber_g) + macros.fiber_g) * 10) / 10,
    83	    }
    84	    await db.from("nutrition_meals").update({
    85	      ...nextTotals,
    86	      total_calories: computeMacroEnergy({
    87	        protein_g: nextTotals.total_protein_g,
    88	        carbs_g: nextTotals.total_carbs_g,
    89	        fat_g: nextTotals.total_fat_g,
    90	        fiber_g: nextTotals.total_fiber_g,
    91	      }),
    92	    }).eq("id", mealId)
    93	  } else {
    94	    const { data: newMeal, error: mealError } = await db
    95	      .from("nutrition_meals")
    96	      .insert({
    97	        client_id: clientId,
    98	        physiological_date: today,
    99	        meal_type: "drinks" as any,
   100	        logged_at: loggedAt.toISOString(),
   101	        total_calories:  macros.calories_kcal,
   102	        total_protein_g: macros.protein_g,
   103	        total_carbs_g:   macros.carbs_g,
   104	        total_fat_g:     macros.fat_g,
   105	        total_fiber_g:   macros.fiber_g,
   106	      })
   107	      .select("id")
   108	      .single()
   109	    if (mealError || !newMeal) return NextResponse.json({ error: mealError?.message }, { status: 500 })
   110	    mealId = newMeal.id
   111	  }
   112	
   113	  // Insérer l'entrée
   114	  await db.from("nutrition_entries").insert({
   115	    meal_id: mealId,
   116	    client_id: clientId,
   117	    food_item_id,
   118	    physiological_date: today,
   119	    quantity_g,
   120	    calories_kcal: macros.calories_kcal,
   121	    protein_g: macros.protein_g,
   122	    carbs_g: macros.carbs_g,
   123	    fat_g: macros.fat_g,
   124	    fiber_g: macros.fiber_g,
   125	    input_mode: "composer",
   126	    confidence_score: 0.85,
   127	  })
   128	
   129	  // Sync client_water_logs — source lue par home page et nutrition page
   130	  const drinkType = inferDrinkTypeFromFoodItem({
   131	    name_fr: item.name_fr ?? "",
   132	    category_l1: item.category_l1 ?? "drinks",
   133	    category_l2: item.category_l2 ?? null,
   134	  })
   135	  await db.from("client_water_logs").insert({
   136	    client_id: clientId,
   137	    amount_ml: quantity_g,
   138	    drink_type: drinkType,
   139	    caffeine_mg: estimateCaffeineMg(drinkType, quantity_g),
   140	    logged_at: loggedAt.toISOString(),
   141	  })
   142	
   143	  return NextResponse.json({ ok: true, meal_id: mealId, quantity_ml: quantity_g })
   144	}

------------------------------------------------------------
UI CANDIDATE: ./app/api/client/nutrition/today-progress/route.ts
------------------------------------------------------------
     1	import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from 'next/server'
     2	import { createClient } from '@/utils/supabase/server'
     3	import { createClient as createServiceClient } from '@supabase/supabase-js'
     4	import { computePhysiologicalDate } from '@/lib/nutrition/physiological-date'
     5	import { computeMacroEnergy } from '@/lib/nutrition/energy'
     6	import { resolveProtocolDayByDate } from '@/lib/nutrition/protocol-schedule'
     7	import { resolveClientTimezone } from '@/lib/client/checkin/resolveClientTimezone'
     8	import { utcRangeForPhysiologicalDate } from '@/lib/client/checkin/timeWindows'
     9	
    10	function service() {
    11	  return createServiceClient(
    12	    process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_URL!,
    13	    process.env.SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY!
    14	  )
    15	}
    16	
    17	// GET /api/client/nutrition/today-progress
    18	export async function GET(_req: NextRequest) {
    19	  const supabase = createClient()
    20	  const { data: { user } } = await supabase.auth.getUser()
    21	  if (!user) return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Unauthorized' }, { status: 401 })
    22	
    23	  const { data: cc } = await service()
    24	    .from('coach_clients')
    25	    .select('id')
    26	    .eq('user_id', user.id)
    27	    .single()
    28	  if (!cc) return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Client not found' }, { status: 404 })
    29	
    30	  const db = service()
    31	  const timezone = await resolveClientTimezone(db, cc.id)
    32	  const today = computePhysiologicalDate(new Date(), timezone)
    33	  const { start: physiologicalStart, end: physiologicalEnd } = utcRangeForPhysiologicalDate(today, timezone)
    34	
    35	  const [{ data: protocol }, { data: composerMeals }, { data: legacyMeals }, { data: waterLogs }] = await Promise.all([
    36	    db.from('nutrition_protocols')
    37	      .select('id, schedule_start_date, nutrition_protocol_days(*), nutrition_protocol_schedule_slots(week_index, dow, protocol_day_position)')
    38	      .eq('client_id', cc.id)
    39	      .eq('status', 'shared')
    40	      .order('updated_at', { ascending: false })
    41	      .limit(1)
    42	      .maybeSingle(),
    43	    // Composer meals — high confidence (0.85)
    44	    db.from('nutrition_meals')
    45	      .select('total_calories, total_protein_g, total_carbs_g, total_fat_g')
    46	      .eq('client_id', cc.id)
    47	      .eq('physiological_date', today),
    48	    // Legacy AI meals — lower confidence (0.55), fallback
    49	    db.from('meal_logs')
    50	      .select('estimated_macros, ai_status')
    51	      .eq('client_id', cc.id)
    52	      .gte('logged_at', physiologicalStart.toISOString())
    53	      .lt('logged_at', new Date(physiologicalEnd.getTime() + 1).toISOString())
    54	      .eq('ai_status', 'done'),
    55	    db.from('client_water_logs')
    56	      .select('amount_ml, caffeine_mg')
    57	      .eq('client_id', cc.id)
    58	      .gte('logged_at', physiologicalStart.toISOString())
    59	      .lte('logged_at', physiologicalEnd.toISOString()),
    60	  ])
    61	
    62	  const fromComposer = (composerMeals ?? []).reduce(
    63	    (acc, m: any) => ({
    64	      calories:  acc.calories  + computeMacroEnergy({
    65	        protein_g: Number(m.total_protein_g ?? 0),
    66	        carbs_g: Number(m.total_carbs_g ?? 0),
    67	        fat_g: Number(m.total_fat_g ?? 0),
    68	      }),
    69	      protein_g: acc.protein_g + (Number(m.total_protein_g) || 0),
    70	      carbs_g:   acc.carbs_g   + (Number(m.total_carbs_g)   || 0),
    71	      fat_g:     acc.fat_g     + (Number(m.total_fat_g)     || 0),
    72	    }),
    73	    { calories: 0, protein_g: 0, carbs_g: 0, fat_g: 0 }
    74	  )
    75	
    76	  const fromLegacy = (legacyMeals ?? []).reduce(
    77	    (acc, m: any) => {
    78	      const em = m.estimated_macros as Record<string, number> | null
    79	      if (!em) return acc
    80	      return {
    81	        calories:  acc.calories  + computeMacroEnergy({
    82	          protein_g: Number(em.protein_g ?? 0),
    83	          carbs_g: Number(em.carbs_g ?? 0),
    84	          fat_g: Number(em.fats_g ?? em.fat_g ?? 0),
    85	        }),
    86	        protein_g: acc.protein_g + (em.protein_g ?? 0),
    87	        carbs_g:   acc.carbs_g   + (em.carbs_g ?? 0),
    88	        fat_g:     acc.fat_g     + (em.fats_g ?? em.fat_g ?? 0),
    89	      }
    90	    },
    91	    { calories: 0, protein_g: 0, carbs_g: 0, fat_g: 0 }
    92	  )
    93	
    94	  const consumed = {
    95	    calories:  fromComposer.calories  + fromLegacy.calories,
    96	    protein_g: fromComposer.protein_g + fromLegacy.protein_g,
    97	    carbs_g:   fromComposer.carbs_g   + fromLegacy.carbs_g,
    98	    fat_g:     fromComposer.fat_g     + fromLegacy.fat_g,
    99	    water_ml: (waterLogs ?? []).reduce((s, w: any) => s + Number(w.amount_ml ?? 0), 0),
   100	    caffeine_mg: (waterLogs ?? []).reduce((s, w: any) => s + Number(w.caffeine_mg ?? 0), 0),
   101	  }
   102	
   103	  const days = (protocol as any)?.nutrition_protocol_days ?? []
   104	  const slots = (protocol as any)?.nutrition_protocol_schedule_slots ?? []
   105	  const targetDay = resolveProtocolDayByDate(
   106	    today,
   107	    (protocol as any)?.schedule_start_date ?? null,
   108	    days,
   109	    slots,
   110	  )
   111	
   112	  const target = targetDay
   113	    ? {
   114	        calories:  Number(targetDay.calories  ?? 0),
   115	        protein_g: Number(targetDay.protein_g ?? 0),
   116	        carbs_g:   Number(targetDay.carbs_g   ?? 0),
   117	        fat_g:     Number(targetDay.fat_g     ?? 0),
   118	      }
   119	    : null
   120	
   121	  return NextResponse.json({
   122	    consumed,
   123	    target,
   124	    hasProtocol: !!protocol,
   125	    mealCount: (composerMeals ?? []).length + (legacyMeals ?? []).length,
   126	  })
   127	}

UI CANDIDATE: ./app/api/client/nutrition/today/route.ts
------------------------------------------------------------
     1	import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from 'next/server'
     2	import { createClient } from '@/utils/supabase/server'
     3	import { createClient as createServiceClient } from '@supabase/supabase-js'
     4	import { computeMacroEnergy } from '@/lib/nutrition/energy'
     5	import { computePhysiologicalDate } from '@/lib/nutrition/physiological-date'
     6	import { resolveProtocolDayByDate, resolveRestProtocolDay } from '@/lib/nutrition/protocol-schedule'
     7	import { utcRangeForPhysiologicalDate } from '@/lib/client/checkin/timeWindows'
     8	import { fetchClientDayOverride } from '@/lib/client/day-kind'
     9	
    10	function svc() {
    11	  return createServiceClient(
    12	    process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_URL!,
    13	    process.env.SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY!,
    14	  )
    15	}
    16	
    17	export async function GET(req: NextRequest) {
    18	  const supabase = createClient()
    19	  const { data: { user } } = await supabase.auth.getUser()
    20	  if (!user) return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Unauthorized' }, { status: 401 })
    21	
    22	  const { data: cc } = await svc().from('coach_clients').select('id, timezone').eq('user_id', user.id).single()
    23	  if (!cc) return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Unauthorized' }, { status: 401 })
    24	
    25	  const url = new URL(req.url)
    26	  const dateParam = url.searchParams.get('date')
    27	  const date = dateParam ?? computePhysiologicalDate(new Date(), cc.timezone)
    28	  const { start: physiologicalStart, end: physiologicalEnd } = utcRangeForPhysiologicalDate(date, cc.timezone ?? 'Europe/Paris')
    29	
    30	  const { data: proto } = await svc()
    31	    .from('nutrition_protocols')
    32	    .select('schedule_start_date, nutrition_protocol_days(position, calories, protein_g, carbs_g, fat_g, hydration_ml), nutrition_protocol_schedule_slots(week_index, dow, protocol_day_position)')
    33	    .eq('client_id', cc.id)
    34	    .eq('status', 'shared')
    35	    .order('updated_at', { ascending: false })
    36	    .limit(1)
    37	    .maybeSingle()
    38	
    39	  const days = (proto?.nutrition_protocol_days as any) ?? []
    40	  const slots = (proto?.nutrition_protocol_schedule_slots as any) ?? []
    41	  const dayOverride = await fetchClientDayOverride(svc(), cc.id, date)
    42	  const baseProtocolDay = resolveProtocolDayByDate(
    43	    date,
    44	    (proto as any)?.schedule_start_date ?? null,
    45	    days,
    46	    slots,
    47	  )
    48	  const td = dayOverride?.kind === 'off'
    49	    ? resolveRestProtocolDay(days) ?? baseProtocolDay
    50	    : baseProtocolDay
    51	  const target = {
    52	    kcal: Number(td?.calories ?? 0),
    53	    protein_g: Number(td?.protein_g ?? 0),
    54	    carbs_g: Number(td?.carbs_g ?? 0),
    55	    fat_g: Number(td?.fat_g ?? 0),
    56	    water_ml: Number(td?.hydration_ml ?? 2500),
    57	  }
    58	
    59	  const { data: meals } = await svc()
    60	    .from('nutrition_meals')
    61	    .select('id, meal_type, title, logged_at, total_calories, total_protein_g, total_carbs_g, total_fat_g, total_fiber_g')
    62	    .eq('client_id', cc.id)
    63	    .eq('physiological_date', date)
    64	    .order('logged_at', { ascending: true })
    65	
    66	  const consumed = (meals ?? []).reduce(
    67	    (acc, m) => ({
    68	      kcal: acc.kcal + computeMacroEnergy({
    69	        protein_g: Number(m.total_protein_g ?? 0),
    70	        carbs_g: Number(m.total_carbs_g ?? 0),
    71	        fat_g: Number(m.total_fat_g ?? 0),
    72	        fiber_g: Number(m.total_fiber_g ?? 0),
    73	      }),
    74	      protein_g: acc.protein_g + Number(m.total_protein_g ?? 0),
    75	      carbs_g: acc.carbs_g + Number(m.total_carbs_g ?? 0),
    76	      fat_g: acc.fat_g + Number(m.total_fat_g ?? 0),
    77	    }),
    78	    { kcal: 0, protein_g: 0, carbs_g: 0, fat_g: 0 },
    79	  )
    80	
    81	  const { data: water } = await svc()
    82	    .from('client_water_logs')
    83	    .select('amount_ml, caffeine_mg, logged_at')
    84	    .eq('client_id', cc.id)
    85	    .gte('logged_at', physiologicalStart.toISOString())
    86	    .lte('logged_at', physiologicalEnd.toISOString())
    87	
    88	  const water_ml = (water ?? []).reduce((s, w) => s + Number(w.amount_ml ?? 0), 0)
    89	  const caffeine_mg = (water ?? []).reduce((s, w) => s + Number(w.caffeine_mg ?? 0), 0)
    90	
    91	  return NextResponse.json({
    92	    date,
    93	    dayOverride,
    94	    target,
    95	    consumed: { ...consumed, water_ml, caffeine_mg },
    96	    meals: meals ?? [],
    97	    water_logs: water ?? [],
    98	  })
    99	}

     1	import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from "next/server"

     8	    process.env.SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY!
     9	  )

    12	async function resolveClientId(userId: string): Promise<string | null> {
    13	  const { data } = await service().from("coach_clients").select("id").eq("user_id", userId).single()
    14	  return data?.id ?? null
    15	}
    16	
    17	export async function DELETE(
    18	  req: NextRequest,
    19	  { params }: { params: { id: string } }
    20	) {
    21	  const supabase = createClient()
    22	  const { data: { user } } = await supabase.auth.getUser()
    23	  if (!user) return NextResponse.json({ error: "Unauthorized" }, { status: 401 })
    24	
    25	  const clientId = await resolveClientId(user.id)
    26	  if (!clientId) return NextResponse.json({ error: "Client not found" }, { status: 404 })
    27	
    28	  const { error } = await service()
    29	    .from("client_water_logs")
    30	    .delete()
    31	    .eq("id", params.id)
    32	    .eq("client_id", clientId)
    33	
    34	  if (error) return NextResponse.json({ error: error.message }, { status: 500 })
    35	
    36	  return NextResponse.json({ ok: true })
    37	}

UI CANDIDATE: ./app/api/client/water/route.ts
------------------------------------------------------------
     1	import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from "next/server"
     2	import { createClient } from "@/utils/supabase/server"
     3	import { createClient as createServiceClient } from "@supabase/supabase-js"
     4	import { z } from "zod"
     5	import { resolveClientTimezone } from "@/lib/client/checkin/resolveClientTimezone"
     6	import { addDaysToDateKey, findUtcForLocalTime, getLocalTimeParts, utcRangeForPhysiologicalDate } from "@/lib/client/checkin/timeWindows"
     7	import {
     8	  computePhysiologicalDate,
     9	  PHYSIOLOGICAL_DAY_CUTOFF_HOUR,
    10	  PHYSIOLOGICAL_DAY_CUTOFF_MINUTE,
    11	} from "@/lib/nutrition/physiological-date"
    12	import { estimateCaffeineMg, type DrinkType, type DrinkLogKind } from "@/lib/client/nutrition/drinks"
    13	
    14	function service() {
    15	  return createServiceClient(
    16	    process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_URL!,
    17	    process.env.SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY!
    18	  )
    19	}
    20	
    21	async function resolveClientId(userId: string): Promise<string | null> {
    22	  const { data } = await service().from("coach_clients").select("id").eq("user_id", userId).single()
    23	  return data?.id ?? null
    24	}
    25	
    26	const schema = z.object({
    27	  amount_ml: z.number().positive().max(5000),
    28	  caffeine_mg: z.number().int().min(0).max(2000).optional(),
    29	  drink_type: z.enum(["water", "espresso", "coffee", "lungo", "tea"]).optional(),
    30	  date: z.string().regex(/^\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2}$/).optional(),
    31	})
    32	
    33	function resolveLoggedAtForPhysiologicalDate(targetDate: string, timezone: string, reference: Date): Date {
    34	  const currentPhysiologicalDate = computePhysiologicalDate(reference, timezone)
    35	  if (targetDate === currentPhysiologicalDate) return reference
    36	
    37	  const { hour, minute } = getLocalTimeParts(reference, timezone)
    38	  const minutesSinceMidnight = hour * 60 + minute
    39	  const cutoffMinutes = PHYSIOLOGICAL_DAY_CUTOFF_HOUR * 60 + PHYSIOLOGICAL_DAY_CUTOFF_MINUTE
    40	  const calendarDate = minutesSinceMidnight < cutoffMinutes ? addDaysToDateKey(targetDate, 1) : targetDate
    41	  const exactMatch = findUtcForLocalTime(calendarDate, hour, minute, timezone)
    42	  if (exactMatch) return exactMatch
    43	
    44	  const { start } = utcRangeForPhysiologicalDate(targetDate, timezone)
    45	  return new Date(start.getTime() + 12 * 60 * 60 * 1000)
    46	}
    47	
    48	export async function GET(req: NextRequest) {
    49	  const supabase = createClient()
    50	  const { data: { user } } = await supabase.auth.getUser()
    51	  if (!user) return NextResponse.json({ error: "Unauthorized" }, { status: 401 })
    52	
    53	  const clientId = await resolveClientId(user.id)
    54	  if (!clientId) return NextResponse.json({ error: "Client not found" }, { status: 404 })
    55	
    56	  const { searchParams } = new URL(req.url)
    57	  const timezone = await resolveClientTimezone(service(), clientId)
    58	  const date = searchParams.get('date') ?? computePhysiologicalDate(new Date(), timezone)
    59	  const kind = searchParams.get("kind") as DrinkLogKind | null
    60	  const { start: physiologicalStart, end: physiologicalEnd } = utcRangeForPhysiologicalDate(date, timezone)
    61	
    62	  let query = service()
    63	    .from("client_water_logs")
    64	    .select("id, amount_ml, caffeine_mg, drink_type, logged_at")
    65	    .eq("client_id", clientId)
    66	    .gte("logged_at", physiologicalStart.toISOString())
    67	    .lte("logged_at", physiologicalEnd.toISOString())
    68	    .order("logged_at", { ascending: true })
    69	
    70	  if (kind === "water") {
    71	    query = query.or("drink_type.is.null,drink_type.eq.water")
    72	  } else if (kind === "caffeine") {
    73	    query = query.in("drink_type", ["espresso", "coffee", "lungo", "tea"])
    74	  }
    75	
    76	  const { data, error } = await query
    77	
    78	  if (error) return NextResponse.json({ error: error.message }, { status: 500 })
    79	
    80	  return NextResponse.json({ logs: data ?? [] })
    81	}
    82	
    83	export async function POST(req: NextRequest) {
    84	  const supabase = createClient()
    85	  const { data: { user } } = await supabase.auth.getUser()
    86	  if (!user) return NextResponse.json({ error: "Unauthorized" }, { status: 401 })
    87	
    88	  const clientId = await resolveClientId(user.id)
    89	  if (!clientId) return NextResponse.json({ error: "Client not found" }, { status: 404 })
    90	
    91	  const body = schema.safeParse(await req.json())
    92	  if (!body.success) return NextResponse.json({ error: body.error }, { status: 400 })
    93	
    94	  const { amount_ml } = body.data
    95	  const db = service()
    96	  const timezone = await resolveClientTimezone(db, clientId)
    97	  const reference = new Date()
    98	  const targetDate = body.data.date ?? computePhysiologicalDate(reference, timezone)
    99	  const loggedAt = resolveLoggedAtForPhysiologicalDate(targetDate, timezone, reference)
   100	  const drinkType: DrinkType = body.data.drink_type ?? "water"
   101	  const caffeineMg = body.data.caffeine_mg ?? estimateCaffeineMg(drinkType, amount_ml)
   102	
   103	  const { data, error } = await db.from("client_water_logs").insert({
   104	    client_id: clientId,
   105	    amount_ml,
   106	    drink_type: drinkType,
   107	    caffeine_mg: caffeineMg,
   108	    logged_at: loggedAt.toISOString(),
   109	  }).select("id, amount_ml, caffeine_mg, drink_type, logged_at").single()
   110	
   111	  if (error) return NextResponse.json({ error: error.message }, { status: 500 })
   112	
   113	  return NextResponse.json({ ok: true, ...data })
   114	}

UI CANDIDATE: ./app/api/clients/[clientId]/nutrition-hub/route.ts

     1	import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from "next/server";
     2	import { z } from "zod";
     3	import { createClient as createServerClient } from "@/utils/supabase/server";
     4	import { createClient as createServiceClient } from "@supabase/supabase-js";
     5	import {
     6	  addDaysToDateKey,
     7	  computePhysiologicalDateInTimezone,
     8	  utcRangeForPhysiologicalDate,
     9	} from "@/lib/client/checkin/timeWindows";
    10	import { computeMacroEnergy } from "@/lib/nutrition/energy";
    11	import { resolveProtocolDayByDate } from "@/lib/nutrition/protocol-schedule";
    12	import {
    13	  buildNutritionHubInsights,
    14	  buildNutritionHubSummary,
    15	  classifyNutritionAgendaDay,
    16	  computeNutritionAdherence,
    17	  computeNutritionDeltaPct,
    18	  type NutritionHubCompleteness,
    19	  type NutritionHubDayInput,
    20	  type NutritionHubDayKind,
    21	  type NutritionHubInsightInput,
    22	} from "@/lib/coach/nutritionHub";
    23	
    24	const querySchema = z.object({
    25	  window: z.enum(["3", "7", "14", "30"]).default("7"),
    26	});
    27	
    28	function serviceClient() {
    29	  return createServiceClient(
    30	    process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_URL!,
    31	    process.env.SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY!,
    32	  );
    33	}
    34	
    35	function inferTrainingDay(protocolDay: Record<string, unknown> | null): boolean {
    36	  if (!protocolDay) return false;
    37	  const name = String(protocolDay.name ?? "").toLowerCase();
    38	  const cycle = String(protocolDay.carb_cycle_type ?? "").toLowerCase();
    39	
    40	  return (
    41	    name.includes("entraînement") ||
    42	    name.includes("entrainement") ||
    43	    name.includes("training") ||
    44	    cycle.includes("high")
    45	  );
    46	}
    47	
    48	type ProtocolDayRecord = {
    49	  position: number;
    50	  name?: string | null;
    51	  calories?: number | null;
    52	  protein_g?: number | null;
    53	  carbs_g?: number | null;
    54	  fat_g?: number | null;
    55	  hydration_ml?: number | null;
    56	  carb_cycle_type?: string | null;
    57	};
    58	
    59	type ScheduleSlotRecord = {
    60	  week_index: number;
    61	  dow: number;
    62	  protocol_day_position: number;
    63	};
    64	
    65	export async function GET(
    66	  req: NextRequest,
    67	  { params }: { params: Promise<{ clientId: string }> },
    68	) {
    69	  const supabase = createServerClient();
    70	  const {
    71	    data: { user },
    72	  } = await supabase.auth.getUser();
    73	
    74	  if (!user) {
    75	    return NextResponse.json({ error: "Unauthorized" }, { status: 401 });
    76	  }
    77	
    78	  const parsed = querySchema.safeParse(
    79	    Object.fromEntries(new URL(req.url).searchParams),
    80	  );
    81	  if (!parsed.success) {
    82	    return NextResponse.json({ error: parsed.error.flatten() }, { status: 400 });
    83	  }
    84	
    85	  const { clientId } = await params;
    86	  const db = serviceClient();
    87	
    88	  const { data: ownedClient, error: clientError } = await db
    89	    .from("coach_clients")
    90	    .select("id, timezone")
    91	    .eq("id", clientId)
    92	    .eq("coach_id", user.id)
    93	    .maybeSingle();
    94	
    95	  if (clientError) {
    96	    return NextResponse.json({ error: clientError.message }, { status: 500 });
    97	  }
    98	
    99	  if (!ownedClient) {
   100	    return NextResponse.json({ error: "Not found" }, { status: 404 });
   101	  }
   102	
   103	  const timezone =
   104	    (ownedClient as { timezone?: string | null }).timezone || "Europe/Paris";
   105	  const windowDays = Number(parsed.data.window) as 3 | 7 | 14 | 30;
   106	  const today = computePhysiologicalDateInTimezone(new Date(), timezone);
   107	  // dateKeys includes today for the agenda ("Journées observées")
   108	  const dateKeys = Array.from({ length: windowDays }, (_, index) =>
   109	    addDaysToDateKey(today, -(windowDays - index - 1)),
   110	  );
   111	  // chartDateKeys excludes today — a partial day distorts charts and KPIs
   112	  const chartDateKeys = dateKeys.filter((key) => key !== today);
   113	  const earliestRange = utcRangeForPhysiologicalDate(dateKeys[0], timezone);
   114	  const latestRange = utcRangeForPhysiologicalDate(
   115	    dateKeys[dateKeys.length - 1],
   116	    timezone,
   117	  );
   118	
   119	  const [
   120	    { data: protocol, error: protocolError },
   121	    { data: meals, error: mealsError },
   122	    { data: waterLogs, error: waterError },
   123	    { data: tdeeHistory, error: tdeeError },
   124	  ] = await Promise.all([
   125	      db
   126	        .from("nutrition_protocols")
   127	        .select(
   128	          "schedule_start_date, tdee_adaptive, tdee_adaptive_at, tdee_data_source, nutrition_protocol_days(position, name, calories, protein_g, carbs_g, fat_g, hydration_ml, carb_cycle_type), nutrition_protocol_schedule_slots(week_index, dow, protocol_day_position)",
   129	        )
   130	        .eq("client_id", clientId)
   131	        .eq("status", "shared")
   132	        .order("updated_at", { ascending: false })
   133	        .limit(1)
   134	        .maybeSingle(),
   135	      db
   136	        .from("nutrition_meals")
   137	        .select(
   138	          "physiological_date, meal_type, total_protein_g, total_carbs_g, total_fat_g, total_fiber_g",
   139	        )
   140	        .eq("client_id", clientId)
   141	        .neq("meal_type", "drinks")
   142	        .in("physiological_date", dateKeys),
   143	      db
   144	        .from("client_water_logs")
   145	        .select("amount_ml, logged_at")
   146	        .eq("client_id", clientId)
   147	        .gte("logged_at", earliestRange.start.toISOString())
   148	        .lte("logged_at", latestRange.end.toISOString()),
   149	      db
   150	        .from("nutrition_tdee_history")
   151	        .select(
   152	          "calculated_at, tdee_adaptive, tdee_formula, delta_kcal, avg_intake_kcal, weight_delta_kg, weight_samples",
   153	        )
   154	        .eq("client_id", clientId)
   155	        .gte("calculated_at", earliestRange.start.toISOString())
   156	        .order("calculated_at", { ascending: true }),
   157	    ]);
   158	
   159	  if (protocolError || mealsError || waterError || tdeeError) {
   160	    return NextResponse.json(
   161	      {
   162	        error:
   163	          protocolError?.message ||
   164	          mealsError?.message ||
   165	          waterError?.message ||
   166	          tdeeError?.message ||
   167	          "Failed to load nutrition hub data",
   168	      },
   169	      { status: 500 },
   170	    );
   171	  }
   172	
   173	  const protocolDays = ((protocol as any)?.nutrition_protocol_days ??
   174	    []) as ProtocolDayRecord[];
   175	  const scheduleSlots = ((protocol as any)?.nutrition_protocol_schedule_slots ??
   176	    []) as ScheduleSlotRecord[];
   177	
   178	  const mealsByDate = new Map<
   179	    string,
   180	    {
   181	      mealCount: number;
   182	      calories: number;
   183	      protein_g: number;
   184	      carbs_g: number;
   185	      fat_g: number;
   186	    }
   187	  >();
   188	
   189	  for (const meal of (meals ?? []) as any[]) {
   190	    const key = meal.physiological_date as string;
   191	    const current = mealsByDate.get(key) ?? {
   192	      mealCount: 0,
   193	      calories: 0,
   194	      protein_g: 0,
   195	      carbs_g: 0,
   196	      fat_g: 0,
   197	    };
   198	
   199	    current.mealCount += 1;
   200	    current.protein_g += Number(meal.total_protein_g ?? 0);
   201	    current.carbs_g += Number(meal.total_carbs_g ?? 0);
   202	    current.fat_g += Number(meal.total_fat_g ?? 0);
   203	    current.calories += computeMacroEnergy({
   204	      protein_g: Number(meal.total_protein_g ?? 0),
   205	      carbs_g: Number(meal.total_carbs_g ?? 0),
   206	      fat_g: Number(meal.total_fat_g ?? 0),
   207	      fiber_g: Number(meal.total_fiber_g ?? 0),
   208	    });
   209	
   210	    mealsByDate.set(key, current);
   211	  }
   212	
   213	  const waterByDate = new Map<string, number>();
   214	  for (const dateKey of dateKeys) {
   215	    const range = utcRangeForPhysiologicalDate(dateKey, timezone);
   216	    const total = ((waterLogs ?? []) as Array<{ amount_ml: number | null; logged_at: string }>)
   217	      .filter((entry) => {
   218	        const timestamp = new Date(entry.logged_at).getTime();
   219	        return (
   220	          timestamp >= range.start.getTime() && timestamp <= range.end.getTime()
   221	        );
   222	      })
   223	      .reduce((sum, entry) => sum + Number(entry.amount_ml ?? 0), 0);
   224	    waterByDate.set(dateKey, total);
   225	  }
   226	
   227	  function buildDayEntry(dateKey: string) {
   228	    const protocolDay = resolveProtocolDayByDate(
   229	      dateKey,
   230	      (protocol as any)?.schedule_start_date ?? null,
   231	      protocolDays,
   232	      scheduleSlots,
   233	    ) as ProtocolDayRecord | null;
   234	    const mealsForDay = mealsByDate.get(dateKey) ?? {
   235	      mealCount: 0,
   236	      calories: 0,
   237	      protein_g: 0,
   238	      carbs_g: 0,
   239	      fat_g: 0,
   240	    };
   241	    const hydration_ml = waterByDate.get(dateKey) ?? 0;
   242	    const dayKind: NutritionHubDayKind = inferTrainingDay(protocolDay) ? "training" : protocolDay ? "off" : "unknown";
   243	    const completeness: NutritionHubCompleteness =
   244	      mealsForDay.mealCount === 0 && hydration_ml === 0
   245	        ? "missing"
   246	        : mealsForDay.mealCount === 0 || hydration_ml === 0
   247	          ? "partial"
   248	          : "complete";
   249	
   250	    const target = {
   251	      calories: protocolDay?.calories != null ? Number(protocolDay.calories) : null,
   252	      protein_g: protocolDay?.protein_g != null ? Number(protocolDay.protein_g) : null,
   253	      carbs_g: protocolDay?.carbs_g != null ? Number(protocolDay.carbs_g) : null,
   254	      fat_g: protocolDay?.fat_g != null ? Number(protocolDay.fat_g) : null,
   255	      hydration_ml:
   256	        protocolDay?.hydration_ml != null
   257	          ? Number(protocolDay.hydration_ml)
   258	          : null,
   259	    };
   260

     7	  return createServiceClient(
     8	    process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_URL!,
     9	    process.env.SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY!
    10	  )

    13	async function resolveProtocol(coachId: string, clientId: string, protocolId: string) {
    14	  const db = serviceClient()
    15	  const { data: cc } = await db
    16	    .from('coach_clients')
    17	    .select('id')
    18	    .eq('id', clientId)
    19	    .eq('coach_id', coachId)
    20	    .single()
    21	  if (!cc) return null
    22	
    23	  const { data } = await db
    24	    .from('nutrition_protocols')
    25	    .select(`*, days:nutrition_protocol_days(*), schedule_slots:nutrition_protocol_schedule_slots(*)`)
    26	    .eq('id', protocolId)
    27	    .eq('client_id', clientId)
    28	    .single()
    29	  if (!data) return null
    30	
    31	  return {
    32	    ...data,
    33	    days: (data.days ?? []).sort((a: { position: number }, b: { position: number }) => a.position - b.position),
    34	    schedule_slots: (data.schedule_slots ?? []).sort(
    35	      (a: { week_index: number; dow: number }, b: { week_index: number; dow: number }) =>
    36	        a.week_index - b.week_index || a.dow - b.dow,
    37	    ),
    38	  }
    39	}

    41	export async function GET(
    42	  _req: NextRequest,
    43	  { params }: { params: Promise<{ clientId: string; protocolId: string }> }
    44	) {
    45	  const { clientId, protocolId } = await params
    46	  const supabase = await createServerClient()
    47	  const { data: { user } } = await supabase.auth.getUser()
    48	  if (!user) return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Unauthorized' }, { status: 401 })
    49	
    50	  const protocol = await resolveProtocol(user.id, clientId, protocolId)
    51	  if (!protocol) return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Not found' }, { status: 404 })
    52	
    53	  return NextResponse.json({ protocol })
    54	}

    86	export async function PATCH(
    87	  req: NextRequest,
    88	  { params }: { params: Promise<{ clientId: string; protocolId: string }> }
    89	) {
    90	  const { clientId, protocolId } = await params
    91	  const supabase = await createServerClient()
    92	  const { data: { user } } = await supabase.auth.getUser()
    93	  if (!user) return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Unauthorized' }, { status: 401 })
    94	
    95	  const existing = await resolveProtocol(user.id, clientId, protocolId)
    96	  if (!existing) return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Not found' }, { status: 404 })
    97	
    98	  const body = updateSchema.safeParse(await req.json())
    99	  if (!body.success) return NextResponse.json({ error: body.error }, { status: 400 })
   100	
   101	  const db = serviceClient()
   102	
   103	  if (body.data.name !== undefined || body.data.notes !== undefined || body.data.schedule_start_date !== undefined || body.data.cycle_sync_enabled !== undefined || body.data.tdee_auto_enabled !== undefined || body.data.tdee_adaptive_active !== undefined || body.data.tdee_reference !== undefined) {
   104	    const updates: Record<string, unknown> = {}
   105	    if (body.data.name !== undefined) updates.name = body.data.name
   106	    if (body.data.notes !== undefined) updates.notes = body.data.notes
   107	    if (body.data.schedule_start_date !== undefined) updates.schedule_start_date = body.data.schedule_start_date
   108	    if (body.data.cycle_sync_enabled !== undefined) updates.cycle_sync_enabled = body.data.cycle_sync_enabled
   109	    if (body.data.tdee_auto_enabled !== undefined) updates.tdee_auto_enabled = body.data.tdee_auto_enabled
   110	    if (body.data.tdee_adaptive_active !== undefined) updates.tdee_adaptive_active = body.data.tdee_adaptive_active
   111	    if (body.data.tdee_reference !== undefined) updates.tdee_reference = body.data.tdee_reference
   112	    await db.from('nutrition_protocols').update(updates).eq('id', protocolId)
   113	  }
   114	
   115	    if (body.data.days !== undefined) {
   116	      const allDaysHaveIds =
   117	        body.data.days.length > 0 && body.data.days.every((d) => Boolean(d.id))
   118	
   119	      if (allDaysHaveIds) {
   120	        for (const d of body.data.days) {
   121	          const updates: Record<string, unknown> = {}
   122	
   123	          if (d.name !== undefined) updates.name = d.name
   124	          if (d.position !== undefined) updates.position = d.position
   125	          if (d.calories !== undefined) updates.calories = d.calories
   126	          if (d.protein_g !== undefined) updates.protein_g = d.protein_g
   127	          if (d.carbs_g !== undefined) updates.carbs_g = d.carbs_g
   128	          if (d.fat_g !== undefined) updates.fat_g = d.fat_g
   129	          if (d.hydration_ml !== undefined) updates.hydration_ml = d.hydration_ml
   130	          if (d.carb_cycle_type !== undefined) updates.carb_cycle_type = d.carb_cycle_type
   131	          if (d.cycle_sync_phase !== undefined) updates.cycle_sync_phase = d.cycle_sync_phase
   132	          if (d.recommendations !== undefined) updates.recommendations = d.recommendations
   133	
   134	          if (Object.keys(updates).length > 0) {
   135	            await db
   136	              .from('nutrition_protocol_days')
   137	              .update(updates)
   138	              .eq('protocol_id', protocolId)
   139	              .eq('id', d.id)
   140	          }
   141	        }
   142	      } else {
   143	        const invalidDay = body.data.days.find((d) => !d.name || d.position === undefined)
   144	
   145	        if (invalidDay) {
   146	          return NextResponse.json(
   147	            { error: 'Each protocol day requires name and position when replacing days.' },
   148	            { status: 400 },
   149	          )
   150	        }
   151	
   152	        await db.from('nutrition_protocol_days').delete().eq('protocol_id', protocolId)
   153	        const daysToInsert = body.data.days.map(d => ({
   154	          protocol_id: protocolId,
   155	          name: d.name!,
   156	          position: d.position!,
   157	          calories: d.calories ?? null,
   158	          protein_g: d.protein_g ?? null,
   159	          carbs_g: d.carbs_g ?? null,
   160	          fat_g: d.fat_g ?? null,
   161	          hydration_ml: d.hydration_ml ?? null,
   162	          carb_cycle_type: d.carb_cycle_type ?? null,
   163	          cycle_sync_phase: d.cycle_sync_phase ?? null,
   164	          recommendations: d.recommendations ?? null,
   165	        }))
   166	        await db.from('nutrition_protocol_days').insert(daysToInsert)
   167	      }
   168	    }
   169	
   170	  if (body.data.schedule_slots !== undefined) {
   171	    await db.from('nutrition_protocol_schedule_slots').delete().eq('protocol_id', protocolId)
   172	    if (body.data.schedule_slots.length > 0) {
   173	      const slotsToInsert = body.data.schedule_slots.map((slot) => ({
   174	        protocol_id: protocolId,
   175	        week_index: slot.week_index,
   176	        dow: slot.dow,
   177	        protocol_day_position: slot.protocol_day_position,
   178	      }))
   179	      await db.from('nutrition_protocol_schedule_slots').insert(slotsToInsert)
   180	    }
   181	  }
   182	
   183	  const updated = await resolveProtocol(user.id, clientId, protocolId)
   184	  return NextResponse.json({ protocol: updated })
   185	}

   187	export async function DELETE(
   188	  _req: NextRequest,
   189	  { params }: { params: Promise<{ clientId: string; protocolId: string }> }
   190	) {
   191	  const { clientId, protocolId } = await params
   192	  const supabase = await createServerClient()
   193	  const { data: { user } } = await supabase.auth.getUser()
   194	  if (!user) return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Unauthorized' }, { status: 401 })
   195	
   196	  const existing = await resolveProtocol(user.id, clientId, protocolId)
   197	  if (!existing) return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Not found' }, { status: 404 })
   198	
   199	  const db = serviceClient()
   200	
   201	  // Remove metric annotations created when this protocol was shared
   202	  await db
   203	    .from('metric_annotations')
   204	    .delete()
   205	    .eq('source_id', protocolId)
   206	    .eq('client_id', clientId)
   207	
   208	  await db.from('nutrition_protocols').delete().eq('id', protocolId)
   209	
   210	  return NextResponse.json({ success: true })
   211	}

    13	async function ownershipCheck(coachId: string, clientId: string) {
    14	  const db = serviceClient()
    15	  const { data } = await db
    16	    .from('coach_clients')
    17	    .select('id')
    18	    .eq('id', clientId)
    19	    .eq('coach_id', coachId)

    24	export async function GET(
    25	  _req: NextRequest,
    26	  { params }: { params: Promise<{ clientId: string }> }
    27	) {
    28	  const { clientId } = await params
    29	  const supabase = await createServerClient()
    30	  const { data: { user } } = await supabase.auth.getUser()
    31	  if (!user) return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Unauthorized' }, { status: 401 })
    32	
    33	  if (!(await ownershipCheck(user.id, clientId))) {
    34	    return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Not found' }, { status: 404 })
    35	  }
    36	
    37	  const db = serviceClient()
    38	  const { data, error } = await db
    39	    .from('nutrition_protocols')
    40	    .select(`*, days:nutrition_protocol_days(*), schedule_slots:nutrition_protocol_schedule_slots(*)`)
    41	    .eq('client_id', clientId)
    42	    .order('created_at', { ascending: false })
    43	
    44	  if (error) return NextResponse.json({ error: error.message }, { status: 500 })
    45	
    46	  const protocols = (data ?? []).map(p => ({
    47	    ...p,
    48	    days: (p.days ?? []).sort((a: { position: number }, b: { position: number }) => a.position - b.position),
    49	    schedule_slots: (p.schedule_slots ?? []).sort(
    50	      (a: { week_index: number; dow: number }, b: { week_index: number; dow: number }) =>
    51	        a.week_index - b.week_index || a.dow - b.dow,
    52	    ),
    53	  }))
    54	
    55	  return NextResponse.json({ protocols })
    56	}

    58	const daySchema = z.object({

    86	export async function POST(
    87	  req: NextRequest,
    88	  { params }: { params: Promise<{ clientId: string }> }
    89	) {
    90	  const { clientId } = await params
    91	  const supabase = await createServerClient()
    92	  const { data: { user } } = await supabase.auth.getUser()
    93	  if (!user) return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Unauthorized' }, { status: 401 })
    94	
    95	  if (!(await ownershipCheck(user.id, clientId))) {
    96	    return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Not found' }, { status: 404 })
    97	  }
    98	
    99	  const body = createSchema.safeParse(await req.json())
   100	  if (!body.success) return NextResponse.json({ error: body.error }, { status: 400 })
   101	
   102	  const db = serviceClient()
   103	
   104	  const { data: protocol, error: protoError } = await db
   105	    .from('nutrition_protocols')
   106	    .insert({
   107	      client_id: clientId,
   108	      coach_id: user.id,
   109	      name: body.data.name,
   110	      notes: body.data.notes ?? null,
   111	      schedule_start_date: body.data.schedule_start_date ?? new Date().toISOString().slice(0, 10),
   112	      cycle_sync_enabled: body.data.cycle_sync_enabled ?? false,
   113	    })
   114	    .select('*')
   115	    .single()
   116	
   117	  if (protoError || !protocol) {
   118	    return NextResponse.json({ error: protoError?.message ?? 'Failed to create protocol' }, { status: 500 })
   119	  }
   120	
   121	  const daysToInsert = body.data.days.map(d => ({
   122	    protocol_id: protocol.id,
   123	    name: d.name,
   124	    position: d.position,
   125	    calories: d.calories ?? null,
   126	    protein_g: d.protein_g ?? null,
   127	    carbs_g: d.carbs_g ?? null,
   128	    fat_g: d.fat_g ?? null,
   129	    hydration_ml: d.hydration_ml ?? null,
   130	    carb_cycle_type: d.carb_cycle_type ?? null,
   131	    cycle_sync_phase: d.cycle_sync_phase ?? null,
   132	    recommendations: d.recommendations ?? null,
   133	  }))
   134	
   135	  const { data: days, error: daysError } = await db
   136	    .from('nutrition_protocol_days')
   137	    .insert(daysToInsert)
   138	    .select('*')
   139	
   140	  if (daysError) {
   141	    return NextResponse.json({ error: daysError.message }, { status: 500 })
   142	  }
   143	
   144	  let slots: unknown[] = []
   145	  if (body.data.schedule_slots.length > 0) {
   146	    const { data: insertedSlots, error: slotsError } = await db
   147	      .from('nutrition_protocol_schedule_slots')
   148	      .insert(
   149	        body.data.schedule_slots.map((slot) => ({
   150	          protocol_id: protocol.id,
   151	          week_index: slot.week_index,
   152	          dow: slot.dow,
   153	          protocol_day_position: slot.protocol_day_position,
   154	        })),
   155	      )
   156	      .select('*')
   157	    if (slotsError) return NextResponse.json({ error: slotsError.message }, { status: 500 })
   158	    slots = insertedSlots ?? []
   159	  }
   160	
   161	  return NextResponse.json({ protocol: { ...protocol, days: days ?? [], schedule_slots: slots } }, { status: 201 })
   162	}

UI CANDIDATE: ./app/client/login/page.tsx

     1	'use client'

    11	export default function ClientLoginPage() {
    12	  const router = useRouter()
    13	  const { t } = useClientT()
    14	  const [showPassword, setShowPassword] = useState(false)
    15	  const [error, setError] = useState('')
    16	  const [isPending, startTransition] = useTransition()
    17	  const [hashError, setHashError] = useState<string | null>(null)
    18	
    19	  useEffect(() => {
    20	    if (typeof window === 'undefined') return
    21	
    22	    // If an invite/magiclink token lands here (misconfigured redirect URL),
    23	    // forward to the correct onboarding page instead of staying on login.
    24	    const hash = window.location.hash
    25	    if (hash && hash.includes('access_token=')) {
    26	      window.location.replace('/client/onboarding' + hash)
    27	      return
    28	    }
    29	
    30	    const queryParams = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search)
    31	    if (queryParams.get('error') === 'link_expired') {
    32	      setHashError(t('login.error.expired'))
    33	      return
    34	    }
    35	
    36	    const hashParams = new URLSearchParams((hash ?? '').replace(/^#/, ''))
    37	    const errorCode = hashParams.get('error_code')
    38	    if (!errorCode) return
    39	    if (errorCode === 'otp_expired') {
    40	      setHashError(t('login.error.otpExpired'))
    41	    } else {
    42	      setHashError(t('login.error.invalid'))
    43	    }
    44	  }, []) // eslint-disable-line react-hooks/exhaustive-deps
    45	
    46	  function handleSubmit(e: React.FormEvent<HTMLFormElement>) {
    47	    e.preventDefault()
    48	    setError('')
    49	    const formData = new FormData(e.currentTarget)
    50	    startTransition(async () => {
    51	      const result = await clientLogin(formData)
    52	      if (result.error) {
    53	        setError(result.error)
    54	      } else {
    55	        router.push('/client')
    56	      }
    57	    })
    58	  }
    59	
    60	  function handleDemoLogin() {
    61	    setError('')
    62	    startTransition(async () => {
    63	      const result = await clientDemoLogin()
    64	      if (result.error) {
    65	        setError(result.error)
    66	      } else {
    67	        router.push('/client')
    68	      }
    69	    })
    70	  }
    71	
    72	  return (
    73	    <div className="min-h-screen bg-[#0d0d0d] flex flex-col items-center justify-center p-6">
    74	
    75	      {/* Logo */}
    76	      <div className="mb-10 flex flex-col items-center gap-3">
    77	        <img src="/logo/logo-stryvr-silver.png" alt="STRYVR" className="w-12 h-12 object-contain" />
    78	        <div className="text-center">
    79	          <p className="text-[11px] text-white/30 mt-1.5">{t('login.mySpace')}</p>
    80	        </div>
    81	      </div>
    82	
    83	      {/* Erreur lien */}
    84	      {hashError && (
    85	        <div className="w-full max-w-sm mb-4 bg-red-500/[0.08] border-[0.3px] border-red-500/20 rounded-xl px-4 py-3">
    86	          <p className="text-[12px] text-red-400 leading-relaxed">{hashError}</p>
    87	        </div>
    88	      )}
    89	
    90	      {/* Card connexion */}
    91	      <div className="bg-white/[0.02] rounded-xl p-6 w-full max-w-sm">
    92	        <div className="mb-5">
    93	          <h2 className="text-[15px] font-bold text-white">{t('login.title')}</h2>
    94	          <p className="text-[12px] text-white/40 mt-1">
    95	            {t('login.subtitle')}
    96	          </p>
    97	        </div>
    98	
    99	        <form onSubmit={handleSubmit} className="flex flex-col gap-4">
   100	          <div>
   101	            <label className="block text-[10px] font-bold uppercase tracking-[0.18em] text-white/40 mb-1.5">
   102	              {t('login.email')}
   103	            </label>
   104	            <input
   105	              name="email"
   106	              type="email"
   107	              placeholder={t('login.placeholder.email')}
   108	              required
   109	              className="w-full h-[48px] rounded-xl bg-[#222222] px-4 text-[14px] font-medium text-white placeholder:text-white/20 outline-none  transition-colors"
   110	            />
   111	          </div>
   112	
   113	          <div>
   114	            <label className="block text-[10px] font-bold uppercase tracking-[0.18em] text-white/40 mb-1.5">
   115	              {t('login.password')}
   116	            </label>
   117	            <div className="relative">
   118	              <input
   119	                name="password"
   120	                type={showPassword ? 'text' : 'password'}
   121	                placeholder="••••••••"
   122	                required
   123	                className="w-full h-[48px] rounded-xl bg-[#222222] px-4 pr-11 text-[14px] font-medium text-white placeholder:text-white/20 outline-none  transition-colors"
   124	              />
   125	              <button
   126	                type="button"
   127	                onClick={() => setShowPassword(v => !v)}
   128	                className="absolute right-3 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 text-white/25 hover:text-white/60 transition-colors"
   129	              >
   130	                {showPassword ? <EyeOff size={15} /> : <Eye size={15} />}
   131	              </button>
   132	            </div>
   133	          </div>
   134	
   135	          {error && (
   136	            <div className="bg-red-500/[0.08] border-[0.3px] border-red-500/20 rounded-xl px-4 py-2.5">
   137	              <p className="text-[12px] text-red-400">{error}</p>
   138	            </div>
   139	          )}
   140	
   141	          <button
   142	            type="submit"
   143	            disabled={isPending}
   144	            className="mt-1 flex h-[48px] items-center justify-between rounded-xl bg-[#f2f2f2] pl-5 pr-2 transition-all hover:bg-[#ffffff] active:scale-[0.99] disabled:opacity-50"
   145	          >
   146	            <span className="text-[12px] font-bold uppercase tracking-[0.12em] text-[#080808]">
   147	              {isPending ? t('login.pending') : t('login.submit')}
   148	            </span>
   149	            <div className="flex h-9 w-9 items-center justify-center rounded-xl bg-black/[0.12]">
   150	              {isPending
   151	                ? <Loader2 size={15} className="animate-spin text-[#080808]" />
   152	                : <ArrowRight size={15} className="text-[#080808]" />
   153	              }
   154	            </div>
   155	          </button>
   156	
   157	          {demoLoginEnabled && (
   158	            <button
   159	              type="button"
   160	              onClick={handleDemoLogin}
   161	              disabled={isPending}
   162	              className="flex h-[44px] items-center justify-center rounded-xl border border-white/[0.08] bg-white/[0.03] px-4 text-[11px] font-bold uppercase tracking-[0.14em] text-white/72 transition-all hover:bg-white/[0.05] active:scale-[0.99] disabled:opacity-50"
   163	            >
   164	              {isPending ? t('login.pending') : t('login.demo')}
   165	            </button>
   166	          )}
   167	        </form>
   168	      </div>
   169	
   170	      <p className="mt-6 text-[11px] text-white/20 text-center">
   171	        {t('login.footer')}
   172	      </p>
   173	    </div>
   174	  )
   175	}

    77	      for (const option of prev) merged.set(option.key, option)
    78	      for (const option of nextOptions) merged.set(option.key, option)
    79	      return Array.from(merged.values())

    81	    const activePrepScenario = initialPreps.find((prep) => prep.is_active)?.scenario_key

    86

    99	  function commitRename() {
   100	    if (!renamingScenarioKey || !renameValue.trim()) {
   101	      setRenamingScenarioKey(null)
   102	      return
   103	    }
   104	    const newLabel = renameValue.trim()
   105	    setScenarioOptions(prev => prev.map(s =>

   116	      }).catch(err => console.error('[rename] PATCH prep failed', err))
   117	    })

   119	
   120	  const activeScenario = useMemo(
   121	    () => scenarioOptions.find((scenario) => scenario.key === activeScenarioKey) ?? scenarioOptions[0] ?? { key: 'default', label: "Scénario principal" },
   122	    [activeScenarioKey, scenarioOptions],

   124	  const isFutureDate = date > todayDate

   157	  async function handleSavePrep() {

   160	    if (ok) {
   161	      logRef.current?.clearDrafts()
   162	      setEditingPrep(null)

   164	      router.refresh()
   165	    } else {
   166	      showFlash('Erreur lors de la sauvegarde. Réessaie.', 'error')
   167	    }
   168	    setSaving(null)
   169	  }
   170	
   171	  async function handleSaveMeal() {

   174	    if (!mealOk) {
   175	      showFlash('Erreur lors de la validation. Réessaie.', 'error')
   176	      setSaving(null)
   177	      return
   178	    }
   179	    const prepLogResults = await Promise.allSettled(

   182	      )
   183	    )
   184	    const failedCount = prepLogResults.filter(
   185	      r => r.status === 'rejected' || (r.status === 'fulfilled' && !r.value.ok)
   186	    ).length
   187	    if (failedCount > 0) {
   188	      console.error(`[handleSaveMeal] ${failedCount} prep(s) failed to log`)
   189	    }
   190	    setSaving(null)
   191	    router.push('/client/nutrition')
   192	  }
   193	
   194	  function handleCancel() {

   196	    setEditingPrep(null)

   198	  }
   199	
   200	  const activePrepCount = simulation.activePreps.length

   202	
   203	  // Scenario comparison totals (all preps grouped by scenario, using is_active ones)

UI CANDIDATE: ./app/client/nutrition/compose/page.tsx
------------------------------------------------------------
     1	import { createClient } from '@/utils/supabase/server'
     2	import { createClient as createServiceClient } from '@supabase/supabase-js'
     3	import { resolveClientFromUser } from '@/lib/client/resolve-client'
     4	import { resolveClientTimezone } from '@/lib/client/checkin/resolveClientTimezone'
     5	import { computePhysiologicalDate } from '@/lib/nutrition/physiological-date'
     6	import { utcRangeForPhysiologicalDate } from '@/lib/client/checkin/timeWindows'
     7	import { resolveProtocolDayByDate, resolveRestProtocolDay } from '@/lib/nutrition/protocol-schedule'
     8	import { shiftIsoDate } from '@/lib/utils/date'
     9	import type { NutritionMacros } from '@/components/client/smart/SmartNutritionWidget'
    10	import type { SmartNutritionPrep } from '@/components/client/smart/SmartNutritionPrepList'
    11	import ComposeClientPage from './ComposeClientPage'
    12	
    13	function svc() {
    14	  return createServiceClient(
    15	    process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_URL!,
    16	    process.env.SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY!,
    17	  )
    18	}
    19	
    20	function clampComposeDate(candidate: string | null | undefined, todayIso: string): string {
    21	  if (!candidate || !/^\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2}$/.test(candidate)) return todayIso
    22	  const maxIso = shiftIsoDate(todayIso, 3)
    23	  if (candidate < todayIso) return todayIso
    24	  if (candidate > maxIso) return maxIso
    25	  return candidate
    26	}
    27	
    28	export default async function ClientNutritionComposePage({
    29	  searchParams,
    30	}: {
    31	  searchParams?: Promise<Record<string, string | string[] | undefined>> | Record<string, string | string[] | undefined>
    32	}) {
    33	  const supabase = createClient()
    34	  const { data: { user } } = await supabase.auth.getUser()
    35	  if (!user) return null
    36	
    37	  const client = await resolveClientFromUser(user.id, user.email, svc(), 'id, gender')
    38	  if (!client) return null
    39	  const clientRecord = client as { id: string; gender?: string | null }
    40	  const clientId = clientRecord.id
    41	  const timezone = await resolveClientTimezone(svc(), clientId)
    42	  const todayDate = computePhysiologicalDate(new Date(), timezone)
    43	  const resolvedSearchParams = searchParams ? await searchParams : {}
    44	  const rawDate = Array.isArray(resolvedSearchParams?.date) ? resolvedSearchParams.date[0] : resolvedSearchParams?.date
    45	  const date = clampComposeDate(rawDate, todayDate)
    46	  const { start, end } = utcRangeForPhysiologicalDate(date, timezone)
    47	
    48	  const [protoResult, mealsResult, prepsResult, waterResult, weightResult, checkinWeightResult] = await Promise.allSettled([
    49	    svc()
    50	      .from('nutrition_protocols')
    51	      .select('schedule_start_date, nutrition_protocol_days(position, calories, protein_g, carbs_g, fat_g, hydration_ml, carb_cycle_type), nutrition_protocol_schedule_slots(week_index, dow, protocol_day_position)')
    52	      .eq('client_id', clientId)
    53	      .eq('status', 'shared')
    54	      .order('updated_at', { ascending: false })
    55	      .limit(1)
    56	      .maybeSingle(),
    57	
    58	    svc()
    59	      .from('nutrition_meals')
    60	      .select('total_calories, total_protein_g, total_carbs_g, total_fat_g')
    61	      .eq('client_id', clientId)
    62	      .eq('physiological_date', date),
    63	
    64	    svc()
    65	      .from('client_nutrition_preps')
    66	      .select('id, physiological_date, title, meal_type, meal_slot, variant_group_id, scenario_key, scenario_label, is_active, status, entries, total_calories, total_protein_g, total_carbs_g, total_fat_g, total_fiber_g, planned_for, created_at, updated_at')
    67	      .eq('client_id', clientId)
    68	      .eq('physiological_date', date)
    69	      .eq('status', 'planned')
    70	      .order('created_at', { ascending: false }),
    71	
    72	    svc()
    73	      .from('client_water_logs')
    74	      .select('amount_ml, caffeine_mg')
    75	      .eq('client_id', clientId)
    76	      .gte('logged_at', start)
    77	      .lt('logged_at', end),
    78	
    79	    svc()
    80	      .from('assessment_responses')
    81	      .select('numeric_value')
    82	      .eq('client_id', clientId)
    83	      .eq('field_key', 'weight_kg')
    84	      .not('numeric_value', 'is', null)
    85	      .order('created_at', { ascending: false })
    86	      .limit(1)
    87	      .maybeSingle(),
    88	
    89	    svc()
    90	      .from('client_daily_checkins')
    91	      .select('weight_kg')
    92	      .eq('client_id', clientId)
    93	      .not('weight_kg', 'is', null)
    94	      .order('date', { ascending: false })
    95	      .limit(1)
    96	      .maybeSingle(),
    97	  ])
    98	
    99	  const protoData = protoResult.status === 'fulfilled' ? protoResult.value.data : null
   100	  const protocolDay = resolveProtocolDayByDate(
   101	    date,
   102	    (protoData as any)?.schedule_start_date ?? null,
   103	    (protoData?.nutrition_protocol_days as any) ?? [],
   104	    (protoData?.nutrition_protocol_schedule_slots as any) ?? [],
   105	  ) ?? resolveRestProtocolDay(((protoData?.nutrition_protocol_days as any[]) ?? []))
   106	
   107	  const target: NutritionMacros = {
   108	    kcal: Number(protocolDay?.calories ?? 2000),
   109	    protein_g: Number(protocolDay?.protein_g ?? 150),
   110	    carbs_g: Number(protocolDay?.carbs_g ?? 200),
   111	    fat_g: Number(protocolDay?.fat_g ?? 60),
   112	    water_ml: Number(protocolDay?.hydration_ml ?? 2500),
   113	  }
   114	
   115	  const meals = mealsResult.status === 'fulfilled' ? (mealsResult.value.data ?? []) : []
   116	  const rawPreps = prepsResult.status === 'fulfilled' ? (prepsResult.value.data ?? []) : []
   117	  const waterEntries = waterResult.status === 'fulfilled' ? (waterResult.value.data ?? []) : []
   118	  const bodyWeightRow = weightResult.status === 'fulfilled' ? weightResult.value.data : null
   119	  const checkinWeightRow = checkinWeightResult.status === 'fulfilled' ? checkinWeightResult.value.data : null
   120	  const bodyWeightKg = checkinWeightRow?.weight_kg != null
   121	    ? Number(checkinWeightRow.weight_kg)
   122	    : (bodyWeightRow?.numeric_value ? Number(bodyWeightRow.numeric_value) : null)
   123	
   124	  const preps: SmartNutritionPrep[] = (rawPreps as any[]).map((prep) => ({
   125	    ...prep,
   126	    meal_slot: prep.meal_slot ?? prep.meal_type ?? 'snack',
   127	    variant_group_id: prep.variant_group_id ?? prep.meal_slot ?? prep.meal_type ?? 'snack',
   128	    scenario_key: prep.scenario_key ?? 'default',
   129	    scenario_label: prep.scenario_label ?? "Scénario principal",
   130	    is_active: prep.is_active === true,
   131	    entries: Array.isArray(prep.entries) ? prep.entries : [],
   132	    total_calories: Number(prep.total_calories ?? 0),
   133	    total_protein_g: Number(prep.total_protein_g ?? 0),
   134	    total_carbs_g: Number(prep.total_carbs_g ?? 0),
   135	    total_fat_g: Number(prep.total_fat_g ?? 0),
   136	    total_fiber_g: Number(prep.total_fiber_g ?? 0),
   137	  }))
   138	
   139	  const consumed: NutritionMacros = {
   140	    kcal: meals.reduce((s, m) => s + Number(m.total_calories ?? 0), 0),
   141	    protein_g: meals.reduce((s, m) => s + Number(m.total_protein_g ?? 0), 0),
   142	    carbs_g: meals.reduce((s, m) => s + Number(m.total_carbs_g ?? 0), 0),
   143	    fat_g: meals.reduce((s, m) => s + Number(m.total_fat_g ?? 0), 0),
   144	    water_ml: waterEntries.reduce((s, w) => s + Number((w as any).amount_ml ?? 0), 0),
   145	    caffeine_mg: waterEntries.reduce((s, w) => s + Number((w as any).caffeine_mg ?? 0), 0),
   146	  }
   147	
   148	  return (
   149	    <ComposeClientPage
   150	      consumed={consumed}
   151	      target={target}
   152	      date={date}
   153	      todayDate={todayDate}
   154	      initialPreps={preps}
   155	      gender={clientRecord.gender ?? null}
   156	      bodyWeightKg={bodyWeightKg}
   157	    />
   158	  )
   159	}

     1	import { createClient } from '@/utils/supabase/server'

    23	type SearchParams = { date?: string }
