    25	function inferTrainingDay(protocolDay: Record<string, unknown> | null): boolean {
    26	  if (!protocolDay) return false
    27	  const name = String(protocolDay.name ?? '').toLowerCase()
    28	  const cycle = String(protocolDay.carb_cycle_type ?? '').toLowerCase()
    29	  return (
    30	    name.includes('entraînement') ||
    31	    name.includes('entrainement') ||
    32	    name.includes('training') ||
    33	    cycle.includes('high')
    34	  )
    35	}
    36	
    37	function svc() {
    38	  return createServiceClient(
    39	    process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_URL!,
    40	    process.env.SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY!,
    41	  )
    42	}
    43	
    44	export default async function ClientNutritionPage({ searchParams }: { searchParams: SearchParams }) {
    45	  const supabase = createClient()
    46	  const { data: { user } } = await supabase.auth.getUser()
    47	  if (!user) return null
    48	
    49	  const client = await resolveClientFromUser(user.id, user.email, svc(), 'id, gender')
    50	  if (!client) return null
    51	  const isFemale = (client as { gender?: string | null }).gender === 'female'
    52	  const timezone = await resolveClientTimezone(svc(), client.id)
    53	
    54	  const date = searchParams.date ?? computePhysiologicalDate(new Date(), timezone)
    55	  const { start: physiologicalStart, end: physiologicalEnd } = utcRangeForPhysiologicalDate(date, timezone)
    56	  const clientId = client.id
    57	
    58	  // ── Parallel fetches (all direct Supabase, no loopback HTTP) ──────────────
    59	  const [protoResult, mealsResult, prepsResult, waterResult, weightResult, checkinWeightResult, trendResult, streakResult, prefsResult, cycleResult, cycleLogsResult, dayOverrideResult] = await Promise.allSettled([
    60	    svc()
    61	      .from('nutrition_protocols')
    62	      .select('cycle_sync_enabled, tdee_adaptive, tdee_data_source, schedule_start_date, nutrition_protocol_days(position, name, calories, protein_g, carbs_g, fat_g, hydration_ml, carb_cycle_type, cycle_sync_phase, recommendations), nutrition_protocol_schedule_slots(week_index, dow, protocol_day_position)')
    63	      .eq('client_id', clientId)
    64	      .eq('status', 'shared')
    65	      .order('updated_at', { ascending: false })
    66	      .limit(1)
    67	      .maybeSingle(),
    68	
    69	    // Meals with full entries for the journal list
    70	    svc()
    71	      .from('nutrition_meals')
    72	      .select(`
    73	        id, meal_type, title, logged_at, physiological_date,
    74	        total_calories, total_protein_g, total_carbs_g, total_fat_g, total_fiber_g,
    75	        photo_urls, notes,
    76	        nutrition_entries (
    77	          id, quantity_g, calories_kcal, protein_g, carbs_g, fat_g, fiber_g,
    78	          input_mode, confidence_score,

   117	function buildInitialSets(exercises: Exercise[], goal: string): SetLog[] {
   118	  const sets: SetLog[] = []
   119	  for (const ex of exercises) {
   120	    const resolvedTempo = ex.tempo ?? getDefaultTempo(ex.movement_pattern ?? null, goal)
   121	    const plannedRows = Array.isArray(ex.set_prescriptions) && ex.set_prescriptions.length > 0
   122	      ? ex.set_prescriptions
   123	      : Array.from({ length: ex.sets }, (_, index) => ({
   124	          set_number: index + 1,
   125	          reps: ex.reps,
   126	          rest_sec: ex.rest_sec,
   127	          rir: ex.rir,
   128	          tempo: ex.tempo ?? null,
   129	          set_type: null as PlannedSetType,
   130	        }))
   131	
   132	    for (let i = 0; i < plannedRows.length; i++) {
   133	      const planned = plannedRows[i]
   134	      const plannedTempo = planned.tempo ?? resolvedTempo
   135	      const plannedType = planned.set_type ?? 'working'
   136	      if (ex.is_unilateral) {
   137	        for (const side of ['right', 'left'] as const) {
   138	          sets.push({
   139	            exercise_id: ex.id,
   140	            exercise_name: ex.name,
   141	            set_number: planned.set_number ?? i + 1,
   142	            side,
   143	            set_type: plannedType,
   144	            planned_reps: planned.reps ?? ex.reps,
   145	            actual_reps: '',
   146	            actual_weight_kg: ex.current_weight_kg !== null ? String(ex.current_weight_kg) : '',
   147	            completed: false,
   148	            rir_actual: '',
   149	            notes: '',
   150	            rest_sec_actual: null,
   151	            rest_sec: planned.rest_sec ?? ex.rest_sec,
   152	            primary_muscles: ex.primary_muscles ?? [],
   153	            secondary_muscles: ex.secondary_muscles ?? [],
   154	            tempo_used: plannedTempo,
   155	          })
   156	        }
   157	      } else {
   158	        sets.push({
   159	          exercise_id: ex.id,
   160	          exercise_name: ex.name,
   161	          set_number: planned.set_number ?? i + 1,
   162	          side: 'bilateral',
   163	          set_type: plannedType,
   164	          planned_reps: planned.reps ?? ex.reps,
   165	          actual_reps: '',
   166	          actual_weight_kg: ex.current_weight_kg !== null ? String(ex.current_weight_kg) : '',
   167	          completed: false,
   168	          rir_actual: '',
   169	          notes: '',
   170	          rest_sec_actual: null,
   171	          rest_sec: planned.rest_sec ?? ex.rest_sec,
   172	          primary_muscles: ex.primary_muscles ?? [],
   173	          secondary_muscles: ex.secondary_muscles ?? [],
   174	          tempo_used: plannedTempo,
   175	        })
   176	      }
   177	    }
   178	  }
   179	  return sets
   180	}
   181	
   182	function formatTime(sec: number) {
   183	  const abs = Math.abs(sec)
   184	  const m = Math.floor(abs / 60).toString().padStart(2, '0')
   185	  const s = (abs % 60).toString().padStart(2, '0')
   186	  return sec < 0 ? `-${m}:${s}` : `${m}:${s}`
   187	}
   188	
   189	function formatWeight(kg: number): string {
   190	  // Round to nearest 0.25 then display without trailing zeros
   191	  const snapped = Math.round(kg * 4) / 4
   192	  return parseFloat(snapped.toFixed(2)).toString()
   193	}
   194	
   195	function recKey(exerciseId: string, setNumber: number, side: string): string {
   196	  return `${exerciseId}_set${setNumber}_${side}`
   197	}
   198	
   199	function resolveReps(ex: Exercise): number {
   200	  const n = parseInt(ex.reps, 10)
   201	  if (!isNaN(n) && String(n) === ex.reps.trim()) return n
   202	  if (ex.rep_min !== null && ex.rep_min > 0) return ex.rep_min
   203	  return 8
   204	}
   205	
   206	function getCoachingCue(
   207	  rir: number | null,
   208	  setNumber: number,
   209	  totalSets: number,
   210	  isLastSet: boolean,
   211	  setType: SetType,
   212	  prescribedRir: number | null,
   213	  t: (k: string) => string,
   214	): string | null {
   215	  if (rir === null) return null
   216	  // Warmup and cooldown sets are not intensity work — intensity cues don't apply
   217	  if (setType === 'warmup' || setType === 'cooldown') return null
   218	  if (rir === 0) return isLastSet ? t('logger.coaching.maxLast') : t('logger.coaching.failure')
   219	  if (rir <= 1 && isLastSet) return t('logger.coaching.perfect')
   220	  if (rir <= 2) return t('logger.coaching.good')
   221	  // "Too easy" only fires when RIR is genuinely above the prescribed target.
   222	  // If the coach prescribed a high RIR (e.g. warmup-style working set at RIR 5)
   223	  // and the client hit it, they did exactly what was asked — no cue.
   224	  if (rir >= 5 && setNumber < totalSets && (prescribedRir === null || rir > prescribedRir + 1)) {
   225	    return t('logger.coaching.tooEasy')
   226	  }
   227	  if (rir >= 4 && isLastSet) return t('logger.coaching.comfortable')
   228	  return null
   229	}
   230	
   231	// Hydration formula for resistance training
   232	// Base rate: 10 ml/kg/hr — empirically calibrated on practical targets
   233	// (No peer-reviewed coefficients exist specifically for strength training;
   234	//  literature gap confirmed by Baker 2023 + ACSM 2007 which target cardio only)
   235	const BASE_ML_KG_HR = 10
   236	
   237	// Goal → metabolic demand coefficient
   238	const GOAL_HYDRATION_COEFF: Record<string, number> = {
   239	  strength: 0.85,   // heavy loads, long rest, lower sustained HR
   240	  hypertrophy: 1.00,
   241	  recomp: 1.05,
   242	  fat_loss: 1.15,
   243	  endurance: 1.30,
   244	}
   245	
   246	// Muscle group size → metabolic heat produced during resistance training
   247	// Lower body compound (quads/glutes/hamstrings) produces 1.5–2× more heat than isolation
   248	const LOWER_BODY_KEYWORDS = [
   249	  'quad', 'quadricep', 'hamstring', 'ischio', 'glute', 'fessier',
   250	  'hip flexor', 'fléchisseur', 'adductor', 'abducteur', 'adducteur', 'leg',
   251	]
   252	const UPPER_COMPOUND_KEYWORDS = [
   253	  'back', 'dos', 'lat', 'latissimus', 'grand dorsal', 'rhomboid', 'rhomboïde',
   254	  'trap', 'trapèze', 'chest', 'pectoral', 'shoulder', 'épaule', 'delt', 'deltoïde',
   255	]
   256	// isolation default: biceps, triceps, forearms, abs, calves, obliques, core
   257	
   258	function getMuscleCoefficient(muscle: string): number {
   259	  const m = muscle.toLowerCase()
   260	  if (LOWER_BODY_KEYWORDS.some(k => m.includes(k))) return 1.20

    36	export function WaterIntakeCalculator({ language: propLanguage }: WaterIntakeCalculatorProps = { language: undefined }) {
    37	  const [internalLanguage, setInternalLanguage] = useState<Language>('fr');
    38	  const language = propLanguage ?? internalLanguage;
    39	  const t = getTranslation(language);
    40	
    41	  const [weight, setWeight] = useState<string>('');

    51	    sedentary: 0,
    52	    moderate: 700,
    53	    active: 500,
    54	    veryActive: 700,
    55	  };
    56	
    57	  const climateBonus = {
    58	    temperate: 0,

    61	  };

    64	  const totalML = baseIntake + activityBonus[activity] + climateBonus[climate];
    65	  const totalLiters = totalML / 1000;
    66	  const glasses = Math.round(totalML / 250);
    67	
    68	  const handleCalculate = () => {
    69	    if (weightNum > 0) {

    71	    }
    72	  };
    73

    80	            {t.waterIntakeCalculator.title}
    81	          </h1>
    82	          <p className="text-base sm:text-lg text-white/70 mb-6">
    83	            {t.waterIntakeCalculator.subtitle}
    84	          </p>
    85	        </div>
    86

    91	              {/* Weight */}

    94	                  Votre poids ({t.macroCalculator.personalInfo.weightUnit})
    95	                </label>
    96	                <input
    97	                  type="text"
    98	                  inputMode="numeric"
    99	                  value={weight}
   100	                  onChange={(e) => {
   101	                    setWeight(e.target.value.replace(/[^0-9.]/g, ''));
   102	                    setShowResults(false);
   103	                  }}
   104	                  onFocus={(e) => {
   105	                    e.target.select();
   106	                  }}
   107	                  className="w-full min-h-[44px] px-4 py-3 bg-white/5 border border-white/20 rounded-card focus:border-[#19D4FF] focus:outline-none text-white placeholder:text-white/50 transition-all font-sans font-normal text-base"

UI CANDIDATE: ./components/client/CaffeineGlyph.tsx
------------------------------------------------------------
     1	"use client"
     2	
     3	import { DRINK_PRESETS, type DrinkType } from "@/lib/client/nutrition/drinks"
     4	
     5	type GlyphSize = "sm" | "md" | "lg"
     6	
     7	interface Props {
     8	  drinkType: DrinkType
     9	  active?: boolean
    10	  size?: GlyphSize
    11	  className?: string
    12	  color?: string
    13	}
    14	
    15	const SIZE_MAP: Record<GlyphSize, { glyph: number; gap: number; chip: string }> = {
    16	  sm: { glyph: 11, gap: 4, chip: "h-6 px-1.5" },
    17	  md: { glyph: 13, gap: 4, chip: "h-7 px-2" },
    18	  lg: { glyph: 15, gap: 5, chip: "h-8 px-2.5" },
    19	}
    20	
    21	function BeanGlyph({ size, color }: { size: number; color: string }) {
    22	  return (
    23	    <svg width={size} height={size} viewBox="0 0 16 16" aria-hidden="true">
    24	      <path
    25	        d="M8 1.5c2.9 0 5 2.2 5 5.5S10.9 14.5 8 14.5 3 12.3 3 9 5.1 1.5 8 1.5Z"
    26	        fill="none"
    27	        stroke={color}
    28	        strokeWidth="1.7"
    29	        strokeLinecap="round"
    30	        strokeLinejoin="round"
    31	      />
    32	      <path
    33	        d="M7.9 2.5c.7 1.2 1.1 2.6 1.1 4.2 0 2.3-.8 4.3-2.3 5.8"
    34	        fill="none"
    35	        stroke={color}
    36	        strokeWidth="1.4"
    37	        strokeLinecap="round"
    38	      />
    39	    </svg>
    40	  )
    41	}
    42	
    43	function LeafGlyph({ size, color }: { size: number; color: string }) {
    44	  return (
    45	    <svg width={size} height={size} viewBox="0 0 16 16" aria-hidden="true">
    46	      <path
    47	        d="M12.8 2.8c-3.6-.7-7 .9-8.8 4.4C2.6 10 2.8 12.5 3.2 13.7c1.2.4 3.7.6 6.5-.9 3.5-1.8 5.1-5.2 4.4-8.8-.1-.5-.7-.9-1.3-1Z"
    48	        fill="none"
    49	        stroke={color}
    50	        strokeWidth="1.7"
    51	        strokeLinecap="round"
    52	        strokeLinejoin="round"
    53	      />
    54	      <path
    55	        d="M4.8 11.2c1.9-2.4 4.3-4.3 7.2-5.6"
    56	        fill="none"
    57	        stroke={color}
    58	        strokeWidth="1.4"
    59	        strokeLinecap="round"
    60	      />
    61	    </svg>
    62	  )
    63	}
    64	
    65	export function CaffeineGlyph({ drinkType, active = false, size = "md", className = "", color }: Props) {
    66	  const preset = DRINK_PRESETS[drinkType]
    67	  const dims = SIZE_MAP[size]
    68	  const count = preset.cupCount
    69	  const iconColor = color ?? (active ? "#111111" : preset.accent)
    70	  const isTea = drinkType === "tea"
    71	
    72	  return (
    73	    <div
    74	      className={`inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-xl border ${dims.chip} ${className}`}
    75	      style={{
    76	        background: active ? preset.accent : "rgba(255,255,255,0.04)",
    77	        borderColor: active ? `${preset.accent}55` : "rgba(255,255,255,0.08)",
    78	        boxShadow: active ? `0 0 0 1px ${preset.accent}22 inset` : "none",
    79	      }}
    80	      aria-hidden="true"
    81	    >
    82	      <div className="flex items-center justify-center" style={{ gap: dims.gap }}>
    83	        {isTea ? (
    84	          <LeafGlyph size={dims.glyph + 2} color={iconColor} />
    85	        ) : (
    86	          Array.from({ length: count }).map((_, index) => (
    87	            <BeanGlyph
    88	              key={`${drinkType}-${index}`}
    89	              size={dims.glyph}
    90	              color={iconColor}
    91	            />
    92	          ))
    93	        )}
    94	      </div>
    95	    </div>
    96	  )
    97	}

UI CANDIDATE: ./components/client/cycle/CyclePhaseModal.tsx

     1	'use client'
     2	
     3	import { motion, AnimatePresence } from 'framer-motion'
     4	import { X } from 'lucide-react'
     5	import type { CyclePhase } from '@/lib/cycle/cycleEngine'
     6	import { PHASE_CONTENT, type CycleContext } from '@/lib/client/cycle/phaseContent'
     7	
     8	const PHASE_COLORS: Record<CyclePhase, string> = {
     9	  follicular: '#22c55e',
    10	  ovulatory:  '#fbbf24',
    11	  luteal:     '#a855f7',
    12	  menstrual:  '#ef4444',
    13	}
    14	
    15	interface Props {
    16	  open: boolean
    17	  phase: CyclePhase
    18	  cycleDay: number
    19	  avgCycleLength?: number
    20	  context: CycleContext
    21	  onClose: () => void
    22	}
    23	
    24	export default function CyclePhaseModal({
    25	  open,
    26	  phase,
    27	  cycleDay,
    28	  avgCycleLength = 28,
    29	  context,
    30	  onClose,
    31	}: Props) {
    32	  const content = PHASE_CONTENT[phase][context]
    33	  const color = PHASE_COLORS[phase]
    34	
    35	  return (
    36	    <AnimatePresence>
    37	      {open && (
    38	        <>
    39	          <motion.div
    40	            className="fixed inset-0 bg-black/60 z-[79]"
    41	            initial={{ opacity: 0 }}
    42	            animate={{ opacity: 1 }}
    43	            exit={{ opacity: 0 }}
    44	            onClick={onClose}
    45	          />
    46	
    47	          <motion.div
    48	            className="fixed bottom-0 left-0 right-0 z-[80] bg-[#161616] rounded-t-2xl px-5 pt-4 pb-8 space-y-4"
    49	            style={{ maxHeight: '88vh' }}
    50	            initial={{ y: '100%' }}
    51	            animate={{ y: 0 }}
    52	            exit={{ y: '100%' }}
    53	            transition={{ type: 'spring', damping: 28, stiffness: 320 }}
    54	          >
    55	            <div className="w-8 h-1 rounded-full bg-white/10 mx-auto" />
    56	
    57	            <div className="flex items-start justify-between">
    58	              <div className="space-y-0.5">
    59	                <p
    60	                  className="font-barlow-condensed font-bold uppercase tracking-[0.18em] text-[11px]"
    61	                  style={{ color }}
    62	                >
    63	                  {content.subtitle}
    64	                </p>
    65	                <p className="text-[20px] font-bold text-white leading-tight">{content.title}</p>
    66	                <p className="text-[11px] text-white/40">J{cycleDay} sur {avgCycleLength}</p>
    67	              </div>
    68	              <button
    69	                onClick={onClose}
    70	                className="w-7 h-7 rounded-full bg-white/[0.06] flex items-center justify-center shrink-0"
    71	              >
    72	                <X size={13} className="text-white/50" />
    73	              </button>
    74	            </div>
    75	
    76	            <div
    77	              className="rounded-xl px-3 py-2 border-[0.3px]"
    78	              style={{
    79	                background: `${color}10`,
    80	                borderColor: `${color}30`,
    81	              }}
    82	            >
    83	              <p className="text-[10px] font-semibold uppercase tracking-[0.14em] text-white/40 mb-0.5">
    84	                Impact {context === 'nutrition' ? 'nutritionnel' : 'entraînement'}
    85	              </p>
    86	              <p className="text-[11px] font-medium" style={{ color }}>{content.impact}</p>
    87	            </div>
    88	
    89	            <div className="space-y-3">
    90	              {content.bullets.map((bullet, i) => (
    91	                <div key={i} className="flex items-start gap-2.5">
    92	                  <div
    93	                    className="w-1.5 h-1.5 rounded-full shrink-0 mt-1.5"
    94	                    style={{ background: color }}
    95	                  />
    96	                  <p className="text-[13px] text-white/70 leading-relaxed">{bullet}</p>
    97	                </div>
    98	              ))}
    99	            </div>
   100	          </motion.div>
   101	        </>
   102	      )}
   103	    </AnimatePresence>
   104	  )
   105	}

UI CANDIDATE: ./components/client/nutrition/CycleSyncBanner.tsx

     1	"use client"
     2	
     3	import { Moon } from 'lucide-react'
     4	import type { CyclePhase, CycleSyncAdjustment } from '@/lib/nutrition/engine/cycleSync'
     5	
     6	const PHASE_LABELS: Record<CyclePhase, string> = {
     7	  menstrual: 'Menstruation',
     8	  follicular: 'Phase folliculaire',
     9	  ovulatory: 'Phase ovulatoire',
    10	  luteal: 'Phase lutéale',
    11	}
    12	
    13	const PHASE_COLORS: Record<CyclePhase, { bg: string; border: string; dot: string }> = {
    14	  menstrual:  { bg: 'rgba(239,68,68,0.06)',   border: 'rgba(239,68,68,0.18)',   dot: '#ef4444' },
    15	  follicular: { bg: 'rgba(34,197,94,0.06)',   border: 'rgba(34,197,94,0.18)',   dot: '#22c55e' },
    16	  ovulatory:  { bg: 'rgba(251,191,36,0.06)',  border: 'rgba(251,191,36,0.18)',  dot: '#fbbf24' },
    17	  luteal:     { bg: 'rgba(168,85,247,0.06)',  border: 'rgba(168,85,247,0.18)',  dot: '#a855f7' },
    18	}
    19	
    20	interface Props {
    21	  phase: CyclePhase
    22	  adjustment: CycleSyncAdjustment
    23	  cycleDay?: number
    24	}
    25	
    26	export default function CycleSyncBanner({ phase, adjustment, cycleDay }: Props) {
    27	  const colors = PHASE_COLORS[phase]
    28	  const label = PHASE_LABELS[phase]
    29	
    30	  return (
    31	    <div
    32	      className="rounded-2xl p-4 space-y-3"
    33	      style={{ background: colors.bg, border: `0.3px solid ${colors.border}` }}
    34	    >
    35	      {/* Header */}
    36	      <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
    37	        <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
    38	          <div className="w-5 h-5 rounded-full flex items-center justify-center" style={{ background: colors.border }}>
    39	            <Moon size={10} style={{ color: colors.dot }} />
    40	          </div>
    41	          <div>
    42	            <p className="text-[9px] font-barlow-condensed font-bold uppercase tracking-[0.18em] text-white/30">
    43	              Cycle Sync
    44	            </p>
    45	            <p className="text-[13px] font-semibold text-white/90">{label}</p>
    46	          </div>
    47	        </div>
    48	        {cycleDay && (
    49	          <span className="text-[10px] text-white/30 font-mono">J{cycleDay}</span>
    50	        )}
    51	      </div>
    52	
    53	      {/* Macro adjustments */}
    54	      {(adjustment.caloriesDelta !== 0 || adjustment.proteinDelta !== 0 || adjustment.carbsDelta !== 0) && (
    55	        <div className="grid grid-cols-3 gap-2">
    56	          {adjustment.caloriesDelta !== 0 && (
    57	            <div className="rounded-xl bg-white/[0.04] px-2 py-1.5 text-center">
    58	              <p className="text-[18px] font-bold" style={{ color: colors.dot }}>
    59	                {adjustment.caloriesDelta > 0 ? '+' : ''}{adjustment.caloriesDelta}
    60	              </p>
    61	              <p className="text-[9px] text-white/30 font-barlow-condensed uppercase tracking-[0.12em]">kcal</p>
    62	            </div>
    63	          )}
    64	          {adjustment.proteinDelta !== 0 && (
    65	            <div className="rounded-xl bg-white/[0.04] px-2 py-1.5 text-center">
    66	              <p className="text-[18px] font-bold text-[color:var(--data-copper)]">
    67	                {adjustment.proteinDelta > 0 ? '+' : ''}{adjustment.proteinDelta}g
    68	              </p>
    69	              <p className="text-[9px] text-white/30 font-barlow-condensed uppercase tracking-[0.12em]">protéines</p>
    70	            </div>
    71	          )}
    72	          {adjustment.carbsDelta !== 0 && (
    73	            <div className="rounded-xl bg-white/[0.04] px-2 py-1.5 text-center">
    74	              <p className="text-[18px] font-bold text-[color:var(--data-gold)]">
    75	                {adjustment.carbsDelta > 0 ? '+' : ''}{adjustment.carbsDelta}g
    76	              </p>
    77	              <p className="text-[9px] text-white/30 font-barlow-condensed uppercase tracking-[0.12em]">glucides</p>
    78	            </div>
    79	          )}
    80	        </div>
    81	      )}
    82	
    83	      {/* Optimal deficit badge */}
    84	      {adjustment.optimalForDeficit && (
    85	        <div className="flex items-center gap-1.5 px-2 py-1 rounded-lg bg-white/[0.04] w-fit">
    86	          <div className="w-1.5 h-1.5 rounded-full bg-[#22c55e]" />
    87	          <p className="text-[10px] text-white/50">Phase optimale pour le déficit</p>
    88	        </div>
    89	      )}
    90	
    91	      {/* First note */}
    92	      <p className="text-[11px] text-white/40 leading-relaxed">
    93	        {adjustment.notes[0]}
    94	      </p>
    95	    </div>
    96	  )
    97	}

     1	"use client"

     8	  /** When true, renders in the violet/indigo planning theme instead of neutral */
     9	  variant?: "neutral" | "violet"
    10	}
    11	
    12	function formatRemainingMacro(value: number): string {
    13	  if (value > 0) return `${Math.round(value)} g`
    14	  if (value === 0) return "déjà atteint"
    15	  return `déjà couvert (${Math.round(Math.abs(value))} g)`
    16	}
    17	
    18	function formatRemainingCalories(value: number): string {
    19	  if (value > 0) return `${Math.round(value)} kcal restantes`
    20	  if (value === 0) return "objectif atteint"
    21	  return `déjà couvert (${Math.round(Math.abs(value))} kcal)`
    22	}
    23	
    24	export default function RemainingNutritionSummary({ remaining, variant = "neutral" }: RemainingNutritionSummaryProps) {
    25	  const isViolet = variant === "violet"
    26	
    27	  const wrapperStyle = isViolet
    28	    ? { background: "rgba(129,140,248,0.07)", border: "0.3px solid rgba(129,140,248,0.14)" }
    29	    : { background: "rgba(255,255,255,0.04)" }
    30	
    31	  const titleColor = isViolet ? "rgba(129,140,248,0.7)" : "rgba(255,255,255,0.30)"
    32	  const subtitleColor = isViolet ? "rgba(255,255,255,0.40)" : "rgba(255,255,255,0.35)"
    33	  const cardBg = isViolet ? "rgba(129,140,248,0.06)" : "rgba(255,255,255,0.03)"
    34	
    35	  return (
    36	    <div className="rounded-2xl p-4 mb-3" style={wrapperStyle}>
    37	      <div className="flex items-center justify-between gap-3 mb-3">
    38	        <p
    39	          className="text-[10px] uppercase tracking-[0.16em] font-bold"
    40	          style={{ color: titleColor }}
    41	        >
    42	          Reste à consommer
    43	        </p>
    44	        <p className="text-[10px]" style={{ color: subtitleColor }}>
    45	          Suivez cette cible ajustée.
    46	        </p>
    47	      </div>
    48	      <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-2">
    49	        <div className="rounded-xl p-2.5" style={{ background: cardBg }}>
    50	          <p className="text-[10px] uppercase tracking-[0.12em] text-white/30 font-semibold">Protéines</p>
    51	          <p className="text-[14px] font-black mt-1" style={{ color: NUTRITION_UI_COLORS.protein }}>
    52	            {formatRemainingMacro(remaining.protein)}
    53	          </p>
    54	        </div>
    55	        <div className="rounded-xl p-2.5" style={{ background: cardBg }}>
    56	          <p className="text-[10px] uppercase tracking-[0.12em] text-white/30 font-semibold">Glucides</p>
    57	          <p className="text-[14px] font-black mt-1" style={{ color: NUTRITION_UI_COLORS.carbs }}>
    58	            {formatRemainingMacro(remaining.carbs)}
    59	          </p>
    60	        </div>
    61	        <div className="rounded-xl p-2.5" style={{ background: cardBg }}>
    62	          <p className="text-[10px] uppercase tracking-[0.12em] text-white/30 font-semibold">Lipides</p>
    63	          <p className="text-[14px] font-black mt-1" style={{ color: NUTRITION_UI_COLORS.fat }}>
    64	            {formatRemainingMacro(remaining.fat)}
    65	          </p>
    66	        </div>
    67	        <div className="rounded-xl p-2.5" style={{ background: cardBg }}>
    68	          <p className="text-[10px] uppercase tracking-[0.12em] text-white/30 font-semibold">Calories</p>
    69	          <p className="text-[14px] font-black mt-1" style={{ color: NUTRITION_UI_COLORS.calories }}>
    70	            {formatRemainingCalories(remaining.calories)}
    71	          </p>
    72	        </div>
    73	      </div>
    74	    </div>
    75	  )
    76	}

------------------------------------------------------------
UI CANDIDATE: ./components/client/QuickCaffeineModal.tsx
------------------------------------------------------------
     1	"use client"
     2	
     3	import { useEffect, useMemo, useState } from "react"
     4	import { useRouter } from "next/navigation"
     5	import { motion, AnimatePresence } from "framer-motion"
     6	import { Minus, Plus, Trash2, X } from "lucide-react"
     7	import { DRINK_PRESETS, estimateCaffeineMg, type DrinkType } from "@/lib/client/nutrition/drinks"
     8	import { CaffeineGlyph } from "@/components/client/CaffeineGlyph"
     9	
    10	type CaffeineLog = {
    11	  id: string
    12	  amount_ml: number
    13	  caffeine_mg: number
    14	  drink_type: DrinkType
    15	  logged_at: string
    16	}
    17	
    18	interface Props {
    19	  open: boolean
    20	  onClose: () => void
    21	  date?: string
    22	  onLogged?: (mg: number) => void
    23	  onDeleted?: (mg: number) => void
    24	}
    25	
    26	function formatTime(iso: string): string {
    27	  return new Date(iso).toLocaleTimeString("fr-FR", { hour: "2-digit", minute: "2-digit" })
    28	}
    29	
    30	export default function QuickCaffeineModal({ open, onClose, date, onLogged, onDeleted }: Props) {
    31	  const router = useRouter()
    32	  const [drinkType, setDrinkType] = useState<DrinkType>("coffee")
    33	  const [ml, setMl] = useState(DRINK_PRESETS.coffee.baseAmountMl)
    34	  const [saving, setSaving] = useState(false)
    35	  const [done, setDone] = useState(false)
    36	  const [error, setError] = useState<string | null>(null)
    37	  const [logs, setLogs] = useState<CaffeineLog[]>([])
    38	  const [deletingId, setDeletingId] = useState<string | null>(null)
    39	
    40	  useEffect(() => {
    41	    if (!open) return
    42	    const url = new URL("/api/client/water", window.location.origin)
    43	    url.searchParams.set("kind", "caffeine")
    44	    if (date) url.searchParams.set("date", date)
    45	    fetch(url)
    46	      .then(r => r.json())
    47	      .then(d => setLogs(d.logs ?? []))
    48	      .catch(() => {})
    49	  }, [open, date])
    50	
    51	  useEffect(() => {
    52	    if (!open) return
    53	    const preset = DRINK_PRESETS[drinkType]
    54	    setMl(preset.baseAmountMl)
    55	  }, [drinkType, open])
    56	
    57	  const caffeineMg = useMemo(() => estimateCaffeineMg(drinkType, ml), [drinkType, ml])
    58	  const totalMl = logs.reduce((s, l) => s + l.amount_ml, 0)
    59	  const totalMg = logs.reduce((s, l) => s + l.caffeine_mg, 0)
    60	
    61	  async function log() {
    62	    if (saving) return
    63	    setSaving(true)
    64	    setError(null)
    65	    onLogged?.(caffeineMg)
    66	
    67	    try {
    68	      const res = await fetch("/api/client/water", {
    69	        method: "POST",
    70	        headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
    71	        body: JSON.stringify({
    72	          amount_ml: ml,
    73	          caffeine_mg: caffeineMg,
    74	          drink_type: drinkType,
    75	          date,
    76	        }),
    77	      })
    78	
    79	      if (!res.ok) {
    80	        const json = await res.json().catch(() => ({}))
    81	        setError(json.error ?? "Impossible d'enregistrer la boisson.")
    82	        setSaving(false)
    83	        return
    84	      }
    85	
    86	      const payload = await res.json().catch(() => ({}))
    87	      const newLog: CaffeineLog = {
    88	        id: payload.id ?? crypto.randomUUID(),
    89	        amount_ml: ml,
    90	        caffeine_mg: caffeineMg,
    91	        drink_type: drinkType,
    92	        logged_at: payload.logged_at ?? new Date().toISOString(),
    93	      }
    94	      setLogs(prev => [...prev, newLog])
    95	      setDone(true)
    96	      setTimeout(() => {
    97	        setDone(false)
    98	        setSaving(false)
    99	        router.refresh()
   100	      }, 700)
   101	    } catch {
   102	      setError("Impossible d'enregistrer la boisson.")
   103	      setSaving(false)
   104	    }
   105	  }
   106	
   107	  async function deleteLog(log: CaffeineLog) {
   108	    setDeletingId(log.id)
   109	    try {
   110	      const res = await fetch(`/api/client/water/${log.id}`, { method: "DELETE" })
   111	      if (res.ok) {
   112	        setLogs(prev => prev.filter(l => l.id !== log.id))
   113	        onDeleted?.(log.caffeine_mg)
   114	        router.refresh()
   115	      }
   116	    } finally {
   117	      setDeletingId(null)
   118	    }
   119	  }
   120	
   121	  const options: DrinkType[] = ["espresso", "coffee", "lungo", "tea"]
   122	
   123	  return (
   124	    <AnimatePresence>
   125	      {open && (
   126	        <>
   127	          <motion.div
   128	            initial={{ opacity: 0 }}
   129	            animate={{ opacity: 1 }}
   130	            exit={{ opacity: 0 }}
   131	            onClick={onClose}
   132	            className="fixed inset-0 z-[80] bg-black/60 backdrop-blur-[2px]"
   133	          />
   134	          <motion.div
   135	            initial={{ y: "100%" }}
   136	            animate={{ y: 0, transition: { type: "spring", stiffness: 300, damping: 30 } }}
   137	            exit={{ y: "100%", transition: { duration: 0.2, ease: "easeIn" } }}
   138	            className="fixed bottom-0 left-0 right-0 z-[90] rounded-t-2xl"
   139	            style={{ background: "#0d0d0d", maxHeight: "88vh", display: "flex", flexDirection: "column" }}
   140	          >
   141	            <div className="relative flex items-center justify-between px-5 pt-5 pb-4 shrink-0">
   142	              <div className="absolute top-2.5 left-1/2 -translate-x-1/2 w-10 h-1 rounded-full bg-white/[0.10]" />
   143	              <p className="text-[15px] font-barlow-condensed font-bold uppercase tracking-[0.12em] text-white">
   144	                Café & thé
   145	              </p>
   146	              <button
   147	                onClick={onClose}
   148	                className="h-8 w-8 flex items-center justify-center rounded-xl bg-white/[0.06] text-white/40 hover:text-white/70 transition-colors"
   149	              >
   150	                <X size={14} />
   151	              </button>
   152	            </div>
   153	
   154	            <div className="flex-1 overflow-y-auto min-h-0 px-5 pb-8">
   155	              {logs.length > 0 && (
   156	                <div className="mb-4">
   157	                  <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-2">
   158	                    <p className="text-[9px] font-barlow-condensed font-bold uppercase tracking-[0.14em] text-white/30">Aujourd'hui</p>
   159	                    <p className="text-[11px] font-bold tabular-nums" style={{ color: DRINK_PRESETS[drinkType].accent }}>
   160	                      {totalMg}mg cumulés · {totalMl}ml
   161	                    </p>
   162	                  </div>
   163	                  <div className="space-y-1.5 max-h-[160px] overflow-y-auto">
   164	                    {logs.map(log => {
   165	                      const label = DRINK_PRESETS[log.drink_type]?.label ?? "Boisson"
   166	                      const entryUnit = log.drink_type === "tea" ? "théine" : "caféine"
   167	                      return (
   168	                        <div
   169	                          key={log.id}
   170	                          className="flex items-center justify-between bg-white/[0.03] rounded-xl px-3 py-2"
   171	                        >
   172	                          <div className="flex items-center gap-2 min-w-0">
   173	                            <CaffeineGlyph drinkType={log.drink_type} active={false} size="sm" color={DRINK_PRESETS[log.drink_type]?.accent ?? "#c08457"} className="shrink-0" />
   174	                            <span className="text-[13px] font-bold text-white tabular-nums">{log.amount_ml} ml</span>
   175	                            <span className="text-[10px] text-white/25 truncate">{label} · {log.caffeine_mg}mg {entryUnit}</span>
   176	                            <span className="text-[10px] text-white/20 shrink-0">{formatTime(log.logged_at)}</span>
   177	                          </div>
   178	                          <button
   179	                            onClick={() => deleteLog(log)}
   180	                            disabled={deletingId === log.id}
   181	                            className="h-7 w-7 flex items-center justify-center rounded-lg bg-white/[0.06] text-white/40 hover:text-white/70 active:scale-95 transition-all disabled:opacity-40"
   182	                          >
   183	                            <Trash2 size={12} />
   184	                          </button>
   185	                        </div>
   186	                      )
   187	                    })}
   188	                  </div>
   189	                  <div className="h-px bg-white/[0.06] mt-3 mb-4" />
   190	                </div>
   191	              )}
   192	
   193	              <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-2 mb-4">
   194	                {options.map((type) => {
   195	                  const preset = DRINK_PRESETS[type]
   196	                  const active = drinkType === type
   197	                  const density = Math.round((preset.baseCaffeineMg / preset.baseAmountMl) * 100)
   198	                  return (
   199	                    <button
   200	                      key={type}
   201	                      onClick={() => setDrinkType(type)}
   202	                      className={`rounded-2xl px-3 py-3 text-left transition-all active:scale-[0.98] ${
   203	                        active ? "bg-white/[0.08] border border-white/10" : "bg-white/[0.03]"
   204	                      }`}
   205	                      style={active ? { boxShadow: `0 0 0 1px ${preset.accent}22 inset` } : undefined}
   206	                    >
   207	                      <CaffeineGlyph drinkType={type} active={active} size="lg" className="mx-auto" color={active ? "#111111" : preset.accent} />
   208	                      <div className="mt-2 flex items-center justify-between">
   209	                        <span className="text-[12px] font-bold text-white">{preset.label}</span>
   210	                        <span className="text-[10px] text-white/30 tabular-nums">{preset.baseAmountMl}ml</span>
   211	                      </div>
   212	                      <p className="text-[10px] text-white/35 leading-tight mt-1">
   213	                        {preset.baseCaffeineMg}mg · {density}mg/100ml · {preset.strengthLabel}
   214	                      </p>
   215	                    </button>
   216	                  )
   217	                })}
   218	              </div>
   219	
   220	              <div className="flex items-center gap-3 mb-5">
   221	                <button
   222	                  onClick={() => setMl(m => Math.max(20, m - 20))}
   223	                  className="h-10 w-10 flex items-center justify-center bg-white/[0.06] rounded-xl text-white active:scale-95 shrink-0"
   224	                >
   225	                  <Minus size={15} />
   226	                </button>
   227	                <div className="flex-1 text-center">
   228	                  <p className="text-[28px] font-black text-white leading-none tabular-nums">{ml}</p>
   229	                  <p className="text-[10px] text-white/30 font-barlow-condensed uppercase tracking-wider mt-0.5">millilitres</p>
   230	                </div>
   231	                <button
   232	                  onClick={() => setMl(m => Math.min(600, m + 20))}
   233	                  className="h-10 w-10 flex items-center justify-center bg-white/[0.06] rounded-xl text-white active:scale-95 shrink-0"
   234	                >
   235	                  <Plus size={15} />
   236	                </button>
   237	              </div>
   238	
   239	              <div className="mb-4 rounded-2xl bg-white/[0.03] px-4 py-3">
   240	                <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
   241	                  <span className="text-[10px] uppercase tracking-[0.14em] text-white/35 font-bold">Charge active</span>
   242	                  <span className="text-[14px] font-black text-white tabular-nums">{caffeineMg} mg</span>
   243	                </div>
   244	                <div className="mt-2 h-1.5 bg-white/[0.06] rounded-full overflow-hidden">
   245	                  <div
   246	                    className="h-full rounded-full"
   247	                    style={{
   248	                      width: `${Math.min(100, (caffeineMg / 160) * 100)}%`,
   249	                      background: DRINK_PRESETS[drinkType].accent,
   250	                      transition: "width 0.25s ease",
   251	                    }}
   252	                  />
   253	                </div>
   254	                <p className="mt-2 text-[10px] text-white/30">
   255	                  {drinkType === "tea" ? "théine estimée" : "caféine estimée"} à partir du volume choisi.
   256	                </p>
   257	              </div>
   258	
   259	              {error && <p className="text-[11px] text-red-400 text-center mb-3">{error}</p>}
   260

UI CANDIDATE: ./components/client/QuickLogSheet.tsx

     1	"use client";
     2	
     3	import { useEffect, useState } from "react";
     4	import { motion, AnimatePresence } from "framer-motion";
     5	import { X, Drop, ForkKnife, Lightning } from "@phosphor-icons/react";
     6	import dynamic from "next/dynamic";
     7	import type { CycleState } from "@/lib/cycle/cycleEngine";
     8	import type { NutritionMacros } from "@/components/client/smart/SmartNutritionWidget";
     9	import { CaffeineGlyph } from "@/components/client/CaffeineGlyph";
    10	
    11	const QuickWaterModal   = dynamic(() => import("@/components/client/QuickWaterModal"),           { ssr: false });
    12	const QuickCaffeineModal = dynamic(() => import("@/components/client/QuickCaffeineModal"),       { ssr: false });
    13	const FreeActivitySheet = dynamic(() => import("@/components/client/smart/FreeActivitySheet"),   { ssr: false });
    14	const LogPeriodSheet    = dynamic(() => import("@/components/client/cycle/LogPeriodSheet"),      { ssr: false });
    15	const MealLogSheet      = dynamic(() => import("@/components/client/smart/MealLogSheet"),        { ssr: false });
    16	const VoiceLogSheet     = dynamic(() => import("@/components/client/smart/VoiceLogSheet"),       { ssr: false });
    17	
    18	interface Props {
    19	  open: boolean;
    20	  onClose: () => void;
    21	}
    22	
    23	type BalanceContext = {
    24	  consumed: NutritionMacros
    25	  target: NutritionMacros
    26	}
    27	
    28	type SubSheet = "water" | "caffeine" | "activity" | "cycle" | "meal" | "meal-voice" | null;
    29	
    30	const BASE_ACTIONS = [
    31	  {
    32	    key: "water" as const,
    33	    Icon: Drop,
    34	    label: "Eau",
    35	    sub: "Logger ma consommation d'eau",
    36	  },
    37	  {
    38	    key: "caffeine" as const,
    39	    Icon: Drop,
    40	    label: "Café & thé",
    41	    sub: "Espresso, normal, lungo",
    42	  },
    43	  {
    44	    key: "meal" as const,
    45	    Icon: ForkKnife,
    46	    label: "Repas",
    47	    sub: "Ajouter un repas ou aliment",
    48	  },
    49	  {
    50	    key: "activity" as const,
    51	    Icon: Lightning,
    52	    label: "Activité",
    53	    sub: "Course, marche, sport libre…",
    54	  },
    55	];
    56	
    57	export default function QuickLogSheet({ open, onClose }: Props) {
    58	  const [sub, setSub] = useState<SubSheet>(null);
    59	  const [cycleState, setCycleState] = useState<CycleState | null>(null);
    60	  const [balanceContext, setBalanceContext] = useState<BalanceContext | null>(null);
    61	
    62	  useEffect(() => {
    63	    if (!open) return;
    64	    // Cycle state
    65	    fetch("/api/client/cycle/status")
    66	      .then(r => r.ok ? r.json() : null)
    67	      .then(data => { if (data?.cycleState) setCycleState(data.cycleState); })
    68	      .catch(() => {});
    69	    // Nutrition balance du jour pour les jauges live
    70	    fetch("/api/client/nutrition/today-progress")
    71	      .then(r => r.ok ? r.json() : null)
    72	      .then(data => {
    73	        if (!data?.target) return;
    74	        const toMacros = (d: { calories: number; protein_g: number; carbs_g: number; fat_g: number }): NutritionMacros => ({
    75	          kcal: d.calories,
    76	          protein_g: d.protein_g,
    77	          carbs_g: d.carbs_g,
    78	          fat_g: d.fat_g,
    79	          water_ml: 0,
    80	        });
    81	        setBalanceContext({ consumed: toMacros(data.consumed), target: toMacros(data.target) });
    82	      })
    83	      .catch(() => {});
    84	  }, [open]);
    85	
    86	  function handleClose() {
    87	    setSub(null);
    88	    onClose();
    89	  }
    90	
    91	  function handleAction(key: string) {
    92	    if (key === "water")    { setSub("water"); return; }
    93	    if (key === "caffeine") { setSub("caffeine"); return; }
    94	    if (key === "activity") { setSub("activity"); return; }
    95	    if (key === "cycle")    { setSub("cycle"); return; }
    96	    // "meal" → ouvrir directement MealLogSheet standard, pas de sélecteur intermédiaire
    97	    if (key === "meal")     { setSub("meal"); return; }
    98	  }
    99	
   100	  const actions = [
   101	    ...BASE_ACTIONS,
   102	    ...(cycleState?.hasActiveCycle ? [{
   103	      key: "cycle" as const,
   104	      Icon: Drop,
   105	      label: "Cycle",
   106	      sub: "Début ou fin de règles",
   107	    }] : []),
   108	  ];
   109	
   110	  return (
   111	    <>
   112	      {/* Main quick-log sheet */}
   113	      <AnimatePresence>
   114	        {open && sub === null && (
   115	          <>
   116	            <motion.div
   117	              key="overlay"
   118	              className="fixed inset-0 z-[60] bg-black/60 backdrop-blur-[2px]"
   119	              initial={{ opacity: 0 }}
   120	              animate={{ opacity: 1 }}
   121	              exit={{ opacity: 0 }}
   122	              onClick={handleClose}
   123	            />
   124	            <motion.div
   125	              key="sheet"
   126	              className="fixed left-0 right-0 bottom-0 z-[70] rounded-t-2xl"
   127	              style={{ background: '#0d0d0d', maxHeight: '88vh', display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', paddingBottom: "max(env(safe-area-inset-bottom), 16px)" }}
   128	              initial={{ y: "100%" }}
   129	              animate={{ y: 0 }}
   130	              exit={{ y: "100%" }}
   131	              transition={{ type: "spring", stiffness: 300, damping: 30 }}
   132	            >
   133	              {/* Header */}
   134	              <div className="relative flex items-center justify-between px-5 pt-5 pb-4 shrink-0">
   135	                <div className="absolute top-2.5 left-1/2 -translate-x-1/2 w-10 h-1 rounded-full bg-white/[0.10]" />
   136	                <p className="text-[15px] font-barlow-condensed font-bold uppercase tracking-[0.12em] text-white">
   137	                  Logger
   138	                </p>
   139	                <button
   140	                  onClick={handleClose}
   141	                  className="w-8 h-8 flex items-center justify-center rounded-xl bg-white/[0.06] text-white/40 active:bg-white/[0.08]"
   142	                >
   143	                  <X size={15} />
   144	                </button>
   145	              </div>
   146	
   147	              {/* Actions */}
   148	              <div className="px-4 pb-4 flex flex-col gap-2">
   149	                <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-2">
   150	                  {actions.filter(action => action.key === "water" || action.key === "caffeine").map(({ key, Icon, label, sub: subLabel }) => (
   151	                    <button
   152	                      key={key}
   153	                      onClick={() => handleAction(key)}
   154	                      className="flex items-center gap-3 px-3 h-[64px] rounded-xl bg-white/[0.03] active:bg-white/[0.06] transition-colors text-left"
   155	                    >
   156	                      <div className="w-10 h-10 rounded-xl flex items-center justify-center shrink-0 bg-white/[0.06]">
   157	                        {key === "caffeine" ? <CaffeineGlyph drinkType="coffee" active size="sm" color="#111111" /> : <Icon size={18} className="text-white/70" />}
   158	                      </div>
   159	                      <div className="flex flex-col min-w-0">
   160	                        <span className="text-[13px] font-barlow font-semibold text-[#e0e0e0] leading-tight">
   161	                          {label}
   162	                        </span>
   163	                        <span className="text-[10px] font-barlow text-white/40 leading-tight truncate">
   164	                          {subLabel}
   165	                        </span>
   166	                      </div>
   167	                    </button>
   168	                  ))}
   169	                </div>
   170	                <div className="flex flex-col gap-2">
   171	                  {actions.filter(action => action.key !== "water" && action.key !== "caffeine").map(({ key, Icon, label, sub: subLabel }) => (
   172	                    <button
   173	                      key={key}
   174	                      onClick={() => handleAction(key)}
   175	                      className="flex items-center gap-4 px-4 h-[60px] rounded-xl bg-white/[0.03] active:bg-white/[0.06] transition-colors text-left"
   176	                    >
   177	                      <div className="w-9 h-9 rounded-lg flex items-center justify-center shrink-0 bg-white/[0.06]">
   178	                        <Icon size={18} className="text-white/70" />
   179	                      </div>
   180	                      <div className="flex flex-col min-w-0">
   181	                        <span className="text-[14px] font-barlow font-semibold text-[#e0e0e0] leading-tight">
   182	                          {label}
   183	                        </span>
   184	                        <span className="text-[11px] font-barlow text-white/40 leading-tight truncate">
   185	                          {subLabel}
   186	                        </span>
   187	                      </div>
   188	                    </button>
   189	                  ))}
   190	                </div>
   191	              </div>
   192	            </motion.div>
   193	          </>
   194	        )}
   195	      </AnimatePresence>
   196	
   197	      {/* Sub-sheets */}
   198	      <QuickWaterModal
   199	        open={sub === "water"}
   200	        onClose={() => { setSub(null); onClose(); }}
   201	      />
   202	      <QuickCaffeineModal
   203	        open={sub === "caffeine"}
   204	        onClose={() => { setSub(null); onClose(); }}
   205	      />
   206	      <FreeActivitySheet
   207	        open={sub === "activity"}
   208	        onClose={() => { setSub(null); onClose(); }}
   209	        onSaved={() => { setSub(null); onClose(); }}
   210	      />
   211	      <LogPeriodSheet
   212	        open={sub === "cycle"}
   213	        cycleState={cycleState}
   214	        onClose={() => { setSub(null); onClose(); }}
   215	        onUpdated={(newState) => { setCycleState(newState); setSub(null); onClose(); }}
   216	      />
   217	      {/* Repas → surface unifiée avec jauges live */}
   218	      <MealLogSheet
   219	        open={sub === "meal"}
   220	        composerMode="standard"
   221	        intent="track"
   222	        balanceContext={balanceContext ?? undefined}
   223	        onClose={() => { setSub(null); onClose(); }}
   224	        onSuccess={() => { setSub(null); onClose(); }}
   225	      />
   226	      <VoiceLogSheet
   227	        open={sub === "meal-voice"}
   228	        onClose={() => { setSub(null); onClose(); }}
   229	        onSuccess={() => { setSub(null); onClose(); }}
   230	        initialInputMode="voice"
   231	      />
   232	    </>
   233	  );
   234	}

------------------------------------------------------------
UI CANDIDATE: ./components/client/QuickWaterModal.tsx
------------------------------------------------------------
     1	'use client'
     2	
     3	import { useState, useEffect } from 'react'
     4	import { useRouter } from 'next/navigation'
     5	import { motion, AnimatePresence } from 'framer-motion'
     6	import { X, Droplets, Plus, Minus, Trash2 } from 'lucide-react'
     7	import { useClientT } from '@/components/client/ClientI18nProvider'
     8	import { NUTRITION_UI_COLORS } from '@/lib/nutrition/ui-colors'
     9	
    10	const QUICK_AMOUNTS = [150, 250, 330, 500]
    11	
    12	type WaterLog = { id: string; amount_ml: number; logged_at: string }
    13	
    14	interface Props {
    15	  open: boolean
    16	  onClose: () => void
    17	  onLogged?: (ml: number) => void
    18	  onDeleted?: (ml: number) => void
    19	  date?: string
    20	}
    21	
    22	function formatTime(iso: string): string {
    23	  return new Date(iso).toLocaleTimeString('fr-FR', { hour: '2-digit', minute: '2-digit' })
    24	}
    25	
    26	export default function QuickWaterModal({ open, onClose, onLogged, onDeleted, date }: Props) {
    27	  const { t } = useClientT()
    28	  const router = useRouter()
    29	  const [ml, setMl] = useState(250)
    30	  const [saving, setSaving] = useState(false)
    31	  const [done, setDone] = useState(false)
    32	  const [error, setError] = useState<string | null>(null)
    33	  const [logs, setLogs] = useState<WaterLog[]>([])
    34	  const [deletingId, setDeletingId] = useState<string | null>(null)
    35	
    36	  useEffect(() => {
    37	    if (!open) return
    38	    const url = new URL('/api/client/water', window.location.origin)
    39	    if (date) url.searchParams.set('date', date)
    40	    url.searchParams.set('kind', 'water')
    41	    fetch(url)
    42	      .then(r => r.json())
    43	      .then(d => setLogs(d.logs ?? []))
    44	      .catch(() => {})
    45	  }, [open, date])
    46	
    47	  async function log() {
    48	    if (saving) return
    49	    setSaving(true)
    50	    setError(null)
    51	    onLogged?.(ml)
    52	
    53	    try {
    54	      const res = await fetch('/api/client/water', {
    55	        method: 'POST',
    56	        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
    57	        body: JSON.stringify({ amount_ml: ml, date }),
    58	      })
    59	
    60	      if (!res.ok) {
    61	        const json = await res.json().catch(() => ({}))
    62	        setError(json.error ?? t('water.error'))
    63	        setSaving(false)
    64	        return
    65	      }
    66	
    67	      const payload = await res.json().catch(() => ({}))
    68	      const newLog: WaterLog = {
    69	        id: payload.id ?? crypto.randomUUID(),
    70	        amount_ml: ml,
    71	        logged_at: payload.logged_at ?? new Date().toISOString(),
    72	      }
    73	      setLogs(prev => [...prev, newLog])
    74	      setDone(true)
    75	      setTimeout(() => {
    76	        setDone(false)
    77	        setSaving(false)
    78	        router.refresh()
    79	      }, 700)
    80	    } catch {
    81	      setError(t('water.error'))
    82	      setSaving(false)
    83	    }
    84	  }
    85	
    86	  async function deleteLog(log: WaterLog) {
    87	    setDeletingId(log.id)
    88	    try {
    89	      const res = await fetch(`/api/client/water/${log.id}`, { method: 'DELETE' })
    90	      if (res.ok) {
    91	        setLogs(prev => prev.filter(l => l.id !== log.id))
    92	        onDeleted?.(log.amount_ml)
    93	        router.refresh()
    94	      }
    95	    } finally {
    96	      setDeletingId(null)
    97	    }
    98	  }
    99	
   100	  const totalMl = logs.reduce((s, l) => s + l.amount_ml, 0)
   101	
   102	  return (
   103	    <AnimatePresence>
   104	      {open && (
   105	        <>
   106	          <motion.div
   107	            initial={{ opacity: 0 }}
   108	            animate={{ opacity: 1 }}
   109	            exit={{ opacity: 0 }}
   110	            onClick={onClose}
   111	            className="fixed inset-0 z-[80] bg-black/60 backdrop-blur-[2px]"
   112	          />
   113	          <motion.div
   114	            initial={{ y: '100%' }}
   115	            animate={{ y: 0, transition: { type: 'spring', stiffness: 300, damping: 30 } }}
   116	            exit={{ y: '100%', transition: { duration: 0.2, ease: 'easeIn' } }}
   117	            className="fixed bottom-0 left-0 right-0 z-[90] rounded-t-2xl"
   118	            style={{ background: '#0d0d0d', maxHeight: '88vh', display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column' }}
   119	          >
   120	            {/* Header */}
   121	            <div className="relative flex items-center justify-between px-5 pt-5 pb-4 shrink-0">
   122	              <div className="absolute top-2.5 left-1/2 -translate-x-1/2 w-10 h-1 rounded-full bg-white/[0.10]" />
   123	              <p className="text-[15px] font-barlow-condensed font-bold uppercase tracking-[0.12em] text-white">
   124	                {t('water.title')}
   125	              </p>
   126	              <button
   127	                onClick={onClose}
   128	                className="h-8 w-8 flex items-center justify-center rounded-xl bg-white/[0.06] text-white/40 hover:text-white/70 transition-colors"
   129	              >
   130	                <X size={14} />
   131	              </button>
   132	            </div>
   133	
   134	            {/* Scrollable content */}
   135	            <div className="flex-1 overflow-y-auto min-h-0 px-5 pb-8">
   136	
   137	              {/* Log history */}
   138	              {logs.length > 0 && (
   139	                <div className="mb-4">
   140	                  <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-2">
   141	                    <p className="text-[9px] font-barlow-condensed font-bold uppercase tracking-[0.14em] text-white/30">Aujourd'hui</p>
   142	                    <p className="text-[11px] font-bold tabular-nums" style={{ color: NUTRITION_UI_COLORS.water }}>
   143	                      {(totalMl / 1000).toFixed(1)} L total
   144	                    </p>
   145	                  </div>
   146	                  <div className="space-y-1.5 max-h-[140px] overflow-y-auto">
   147	                    {logs.map(log => (
   148	                      <div
   149	                        key={log.id}
   150	                        className="flex items-center justify-between bg-white/[0.03] rounded-xl px-3 py-2"
   151	                      >
   152	                        <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
   153	                          <Droplets size={12} style={{ color: NUTRITION_UI_COLORS.water }} className="opacity-60" />
   154	                          <span className="text-[13px] font-bold text-white tabular-nums">{log.amount_ml} ml</span>
   155	                          <span className="text-[10px] text-white/25">{formatTime(log.logged_at)}</span>
   156	                        </div>
   157	                        <button
   158	                          onClick={() => deleteLog(log)}
   159	                          disabled={deletingId === log.id}
   160	                          className="h-7 w-7 flex items-center justify-center rounded-lg bg-white/[0.06] text-white/40 hover:text-white/70 active:scale-95 transition-all disabled:opacity-40"
   161	                        >
   162	                          <Trash2 size={12} />
   163	                        </button>
   164	                      </div>
   165	                    ))}
   166	                  </div>
   167	                  <div className="h-px bg-white/[0.06] mt-3 mb-4" />
   168	                </div>
   169	              )}
   170	
   171	              {/* Quick pills */}
   172	              <div className="grid grid-cols-4 gap-2 mb-4">
   173	                {QUICK_AMOUNTS.map(a => (
   174	                  <button
   175	                    key={a}
   176	                    onClick={() => setMl(a)}
   177	                    className={`h-10 rounded-xl text-[12px] font-bold transition-all active:scale-95 ${
   178	                      ml === a
   179	                        ? 'bg-white/[0.10] text-white'
   180	                        : 'bg-white/[0.04] text-white/40'
   181	                    }`}
   182	                  >
   183	                    {a}ml
   184	                  </button>
   185	                ))}
   186	              </div>
   187	
   188	              {/* Fine-tune */}
   189	              <div className="flex items-center gap-3 mb-5">
   190	                <button
   191	                  onClick={() => setMl(m => Math.max(50, m - 50))}
   192	                  className="h-10 w-10 flex items-center justify-center bg-white/[0.06] rounded-xl text-white active:scale-95 shrink-0"
   193	                >
   194	                  <Minus size={15} />
   195	                </button>
   196	                <div className="flex-1 text-center">
   197	                  <p className="text-[28px] font-black text-white leading-none tabular-nums">{ml}</p>
   198	                  <p className="text-[10px] text-white/30 font-barlow-condensed uppercase tracking-wider mt-0.5">millilitres</p>
   199	                </div>
   200	                <button
   201	                  onClick={() => setMl(m => Math.min(2000, m + 50))}
   202	                  className="h-10 w-10 flex items-center justify-center bg-white/[0.06] rounded-xl text-white active:scale-95 shrink-0"
   203	                >
   204	                  <Plus size={15} />
   205	                </button>
   206	              </div>
   207	
   208	              {error && (
   209	                <p className="text-[11px] text-red-400 text-center mb-3">{error}</p>
   210	              )}
   211	
   212	              <button
   213	                onClick={log}
   214	                disabled={saving && !done}
   215	                className={`w-full h-12 flex items-center justify-center gap-2 rounded-xl font-barlow-condensed font-bold uppercase tracking-[0.14em] text-[12px] transition-all active:scale-[0.98] ${
   216	                  done
   217	                    ? 'bg-white/[0.06] text-white/50'
   218	                    : 'disabled:opacity-60'
   219	                }`}
   220	                style={done ? undefined : { background: '#f2f2f2', color: '#080808' }}
   221	              >
   222	                <Droplets size={15} />
   223	                {done ? t('water.logged', { ml: String(ml) }) : saving ? t('water.saving') : t('water.log', { ml: String(ml) })}
   224	              </button>
   225	            </div>
   226	          </motion.div>
   227	        </>
   228	      )}
   229	    </AnimatePresence>
   230	  )
   231	}

------------------------------------------------------------
UI CANDIDATE: ./components/client/smart/FreeActivitySheet.tsx
------------------------------------------------------------
     1	'use client'
     2	
     3	import { useState } from 'react'
     4	import { motion, AnimatePresence } from 'framer-motion'
     5	import { X } from 'lucide-react'
     6	import { useClientT } from '../ClientI18nProvider'
     7	
     8	type ActivityType = 'running' | 'cycling' | 'swimming' | 'walking' | 'team_sport' | 'other'
     9	
    10	export type FreeActivitySheetProps = {
    11	  open: boolean
    12	  onClose: () => void
    13	  onSaved?: () => void
    14	}
    15	
    16	const TYPES: ActivityType[] = ['running', 'cycling', 'swimming', 'walking', 'team_sport', 'other']
    17	
    18	const formatDateTime = (iso: string) => {
    19	  const d = new Date(iso)
    20	  return (
    21	    d.toLocaleDateString('fr-FR', { day: 'numeric', month: 'long', year: 'numeric' }) +
    22	    ' à ' +
    23	    d.toLocaleTimeString('fr-FR', { hour: '2-digit', minute: '2-digit' })
    24	  )
    25	}
    26	
    27	export default function FreeActivitySheet({ open, onClose, onSaved }: FreeActivitySheetProps) {
    28	  const { t } = useClientT()
    29	  const [type, setType] = useState<ActivityType>('running')
    30	  const [customLabel, setCustomLabel] = useState('')
    31	  const [startedAt, setStartedAt] = useState(() => new Date().toISOString().slice(0, 16))
    32	  const [duration, setDuration] = useState(30)
    33	  const [intensity, setIntensity] = useState(5)
    34	  const [notes, setNotes] = useState('')
    35	  const [saving, setSaving] = useState(false)
    36	  const [error, setError] = useState('')
    37	
    38	  const submit = async () => {
    39	    setError('')
    40	    setSaving(true)
    41	    try {
    42	      const body: Record<string, unknown> = {
    43	        activity_type: type,
    44	        started_at: new Date(startedAt).toISOString(),
    45	        duration_min: duration,
    46	        intensity,
    47	      }
    48	      if (type === 'other' && customLabel.trim()) body.custom_label = customLabel.trim()
    49	      if (notes.trim()) body.notes = notes.trim()
    50	
    51	      const r = await fetch('/api/client/activity-logs', {
    52	        method: 'POST',
    53	        headers: { 'content-type': 'application/json' },
    54	        body: JSON.stringify(body),
    55	      })
    56	      if (!r.ok) {
    57	        const j = await r.json().catch(() => ({}))
    58	        throw new Error((j as any).error ?? 'Erreur')
    59	      }
    60	      onSaved?.()
    61	      onClose()
    62	    } catch (e: unknown) {
    63	      setError(e instanceof Error ? e.message : 'Erreur')
    64	    } finally {
    65	      setSaving(false)
    66	    }
    67	  }
    68	
    69	  const pct = ((intensity - 1) / 9) * 100
    70	
    71	  return (
    72	    <AnimatePresence>
    73	      {open && (
    74	        <>
    75	          <motion.div
    76	            className="fixed inset-0 z-[65] bg-black/60 backdrop-blur-[2px]"
    77	            onClick={onClose}
    78	            initial={{ opacity: 0 }} animate={{ opacity: 1 }} exit={{ opacity: 0 }}
    79	          />
    80	          <motion.div
    81	            className="fixed left-0 right-0 bottom-0 z-[70] rounded-t-2xl flex flex-col"
    82	            style={{ background: '#0d0d0d', maxHeight: '88vh' }}
    83	            initial={{ y: '100%' }} animate={{ y: 0 }} exit={{ y: '100%' }}
    84	            transition={{ type: 'spring', stiffness: 300, damping: 30 }}
    85	          >
    86	            <div className="relative px-5 pt-5 pb-4 shrink-0 flex items-center justify-between">
    87	              <div className="absolute top-2.5 left-1/2 -translate-x-1/2 w-10 h-1 rounded-full bg-white/[0.10]" />
    88	              <h3 className="font-barlow-condensed font-bold uppercase tracking-[0.12em] text-[15px] text-white">
    89	                {t('activity.logTitle')}
    90	              </h3>
    91	              <button onClick={onClose} className="h-8 w-8 rounded-xl bg-white/[0.06] flex items-center justify-center text-white/40">
    92	                <X size={15} />
    93	              </button>
    94	            </div>
    95	
    96	            <div className="overflow-y-auto flex-1 min-h-0 px-5 pb-8 space-y-4">
    97	              <div>
    98	                <label className="block text-[10px] font-bold uppercase tracking-[0.18em] text-white/55 mb-2">Type</label>
    99	                <div className="grid grid-cols-3 gap-2">
   100	                  {TYPES.map(tt => (
   101	                    <button
   102	                      key={tt}
   103	                      onClick={() => setType(tt)}
   104	                      className={`h-10 rounded-xl text-[11px] font-semibold transition-colors ${
   105	                        type === tt ? 'bg-white/[0.10] text-white' : 'bg-white/[0.03] text-white/40'
   106	                      }`}
   107	                    >
   108	                      {t(`smart.activity.type.${tt}` as any)}
   109	                    </button>
   110	                  ))}
   111	                </div>
   112	              </div>
   113	
   114	              {type === 'other' && (
   115	                <div>
   116	                  <label className="block text-[10px] font-bold uppercase tracking-[0.18em] text-white/55 mb-2">{t('activity.specify')}</label>
   117	                  <input
   118	                    value={customLabel}
   119	                    onChange={e => setCustomLabel(e.target.value)}
   120	                    maxLength={80}
   121	                    className="w-full min-w-0 h-11 px-3 rounded-xl bg-[#080808] text-white text-[14px] outline-none"
   122	                    placeholder="Ex: Tennis"
   123	                  />
   124	                </div>
   125	              )}
   126	
   127	              <div>
   128	                <label className="block text-[10px] font-bold uppercase tracking-[0.18em] text-white/55 mb-2">{t('activity.when')}</label>
   129	                <div className="relative w-full h-11">
   130	                  <div className="w-full h-full flex items-center px-3 rounded-xl bg-[#080808] text-white text-[14px] pointer-events-none select-none">
   131	                    {formatDateTime(startedAt)}
   132	                  </div>
   133	                  <input
   134	                    type="datetime-local"
   135	                    value={startedAt}
   136	                    onChange={e => setStartedAt(e.target.value)}
   137	                    className="absolute inset-0 w-full h-full opacity-0 cursor-pointer"
   138	                  />
   139	                </div>
   140	              </div>
   141	
   142	              <div>
   143	                <label className="block text-[10px] font-bold uppercase tracking-[0.18em] text-white/55 mb-2">{t('smart.activity.duration')}</label>
   144	                <input
   145	                  type="text"
   146	                  inputMode="decimal"
   147	                  min={1}
   148	                  max={360}
   149	                  value={duration}
   150	                  onFocus={e => e.target.select()}
   151	                  onChange={e => setDuration(parseInt(e.target.value) || 1)}
   152	                  className="w-full min-w-0 h-11 px-3 rounded-xl bg-[#080808] text-white text-[14px] outline-none"
   153	                />
   154	              </div>
   155	
   156	              <div>
   157	                <label className="block text-[10px] font-bold uppercase tracking-[0.18em] text-white/55 mb-2">
   158	                  {t('activity.intensityFull', { n: String(intensity) })}
   159	                </label>
   160	                <input
   161	                  type="range"
   162	                  min={1}
   163	                  max={10}
   164	                  step={1}
   165	                  value={intensity}
   166	                  onChange={e => setIntensity(parseInt(e.target.value))}
   167	                  className="w-full h-2 appearance-none rounded-full cursor-pointer slider-client"
   168	                  style={{
   169	                    background: `linear-gradient(to right, #f2f2f2 0%, #f2f2f2 ${pct}%, rgba(255,255,255,0.1) ${pct}%, rgba(255,255,255,0.1) 100%)`,
   170	                  }}
   171	                />
   172	              </div>
   173	
   174	              <div>
   175	                <label className="block text-[10px] font-bold uppercase tracking-[0.18em] text-white/55 mb-2">{t('activity.notesOpt')}</label>
   176	                <textarea
   177	                  value={notes}
   178	                  onChange={e => setNotes(e.target.value)}
   179	                  rows={3}
   180	                  maxLength={500}
   181	                  className="w-full min-w-0 px-3 py-2 rounded-xl bg-[#080808] text-white text-[14px] outline-none resize-none"
   182	                />
   183	              </div>
   184	
   185	              {error && <p className="text-[12px] text-red-400">{error}</p>}
   186	
   187	              <button
   188	                disabled={saving}
   189	                onClick={submit}
   190	                className="w-full h-12 rounded-xl bg-white/[0.10] text-white font-bold uppercase tracking-[0.1em] text-[12px] disabled:opacity-50 active:scale-[0.98] transition-transform"
   191	              >
   192	                {saving ? '...' : t('smart.activity.save')}
   193	              </button>
   194	            </div>
   195	          </motion.div>
   196	        </>
   197	      )}
   198	    </AnimatePresence>
   199	  )
   200	}

    26	  if (h < 10) return "breakfast"
    27	  if (h < 14) return "lunch"

    44	interface LiveMacroHeaderProps {
    45	  consumed: NutritionMacros
    46	  target: NutritionMacros

    48	  drafts: { calories: number; protein: number; carbs: number; fat: number; count: number }

    51	function MacroBar({ value, max, color }: { value: number; max: number; color: string }) {
    52	  const pct = max > 0 ? Math.min((value / max) * 100, 100) : 0
    53	  const over = max > 0 && value > max
    54	  return (
    55	    <div className="h-[3px] rounded-full overflow-hidden bg-white/[0.08] flex-1">
    56	      <div
    57	        className="h-full rounded-full transition-all duration-300"
    58	        style={{ width: `${pct}%`, backgroundColor: over ? "#ef4444" : color }}
    59	      />
    60	    </div>
    61	  )
    62	}
    63	
    64	function LiveMacroHeader({ consumed, target, drafts }: LiveMacroHeaderProps) {
    65	  // Total = déjà consommé + drafts en cours (simulation live)
    66	  const totalKcal   = consumed.kcal        + drafts.calories
    67	  const totalProt   = consumed.protein_g   + drafts.protein
    68	  const totalCarbs  = consumed.carbs_g     + drafts.carbs
    69	  const totalFat    = consumed.fat_g       + drafts.fat
    70	
    71	  const kcalPct = target.kcal > 0 ? Math.min((totalKcal / target.kcal) * 100, 100) : 0
    72	  const kcalOver = totalKcal > target.kcal
    73	
    74	  // Arc SVG — 200° arc, r=28
    75	  const r = 28
    76	  const cx = 36
    77	  const cy = 36
    78	  const startAngle = -200
    79	  const endAngle   = 20
    80	  const totalDeg   = endAngle - startAngle
    81	  const toRad = (d: number) => (d * Math.PI) / 180
    82	  const arcX = (a: number) => cx + r * Math.cos(toRad(a))
    83	  const arcY = (a: number) => cy + r * Math.sin(toRad(a))
    84	
    85	  function arcPath(fromDeg: number, toDeg: number) {
    86	    const large = toDeg - fromDeg > 180 ? 1 : 0
    87	    return `M ${arcX(fromDeg)} ${arcY(fromDeg)} A ${r} ${r} 0 ${large} 1 ${arcX(toDeg)} ${arcY(toDeg)}`
    88	  }
    89	
    90	  const fillDeg = startAngle + (totalDeg * kcalPct) / 100
    91	
    92	  return (
    93	    <div className="flex items-center gap-4 px-4 py-3 shrink-0" style={{ borderBottom: "0.3px solid rgba(129,140,248,0.14)" }}>
    94	      {/* Arc gauge kcal */}
    95	      <div className="shrink-0 relative w-[72px] h-[72px]">
    96	        <svg width="72" height="72" viewBox="0 0 72 72">
    97	          {/* Track */}
    98	          <path
    99	            d={arcPath(startAngle, endAngle)}
   100	            fill="none"
   101	            stroke="rgba(255,255,255,0.08)"
   102	            strokeWidth="5"
   103	            strokeLinecap="round"
   104	          />
   105	          {/* Fill */}
   106	          {kcalPct > 0 && (
   107	            <path
   108	              d={arcPath(startAngle, fillDeg)}
   109	              fill="none"
   110	              stroke={kcalOver ? "#ef4444" : NUTRITION_UI_COLORS.calories}
   111	              strokeWidth="5"
   112	              strokeLinecap="round"
   113	            />
   114	          )}
   115	        </svg>
   116	        {/* Center text */}
   117	        <div className="absolute inset-0 flex flex-col items-center justify-center">
   118	          <span className="text-[13px] font-black text-white leading-none tabular-nums">
   119	            {Math.round(totalKcal)}
   120	          </span>
   121	          <span className="text-[8px] text-white/30 uppercase tracking-[0.10em]">kcal</span>
   122	        </div>
   123	      </div>
   124	
   125	      {/* Macro bars */}
   126	      <div className="flex-1 flex flex-col gap-2.5">
   127	        {/* Protéines */}
   128	        <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
   129	          <span className="text-[9px] font-bold uppercase tracking-[0.10em] w-4" style={{ color: NUTRITION_UI_COLORS.protein }}>P</span>
   130	          <MacroBar value={totalProt} max={target.protein_g} color={NUTRITION_UI_COLORS.protein} />
   131	          <span className="text-[10px] tabular-nums text-white/40 w-14 text-right">
   132	            {Math.round(totalProt)}<span className="text-white/20">/{Math.round(target.protein_g)}g</span>
   133	          </span>
   134	        </div>
   135	        {/* Glucides */}
   136	        <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
   137	          <span className="text-[9px] font-bold uppercase tracking-[0.10em] w-4" style={{ color: NUTRITION_UI_COLORS.carbs }}>G</span>
   138	          <MacroBar value={totalCarbs} max={target.carbs_g} color={NUTRITION_UI_COLORS.carbs} />
   139	          <span className="text-[10px] tabular-nums text-white/40 w-14 text-right">
   140	            {Math.round(totalCarbs)}<span className="text-white/20">/{Math.round(target.carbs_g)}g</span>
   141	          </span>
   142	        </div>
   143	        {/* Lipides */}
   144	        <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
   145	          <span className="text-[9px] font-bold uppercase tracking-[0.10em] w-4" style={{ color: NUTRITION_UI_COLORS.fat }}>L</span>
   146	          <MacroBar value={totalFat} max={target.fat_g} color={NUTRITION_UI_COLORS.fat} />

   148	            {Math.round(totalFat)}<span className="text-white/20">/{Math.round(target.fat_g)}g</span>
   149	          </span>

   151	      </div>

   154	}

   232	          >
   233	            {/* Safe-area background fill — makes iOS status bar match the sheet bg */}
   234	            <div
   235	              className="shrink-0"
   236	              style={{
   237	                height: 'env(safe-area-inset-top, 0px)',
   238	                background: isGuideMode ? '#0a0a10' : '#0d0d0d',
   239	              }}

   241	            {/* ── Topbar fixe ── */}

   243	              className="flex items-center justify-between px-4 shrink-0"
   244	              style={{
   245	                paddingTop: "16px",
   246	                paddingBottom: "12px",

   260	                  </p>

    49	function MacroStrip({ p, g, f }: { p: number; g: number; f: number }) {
    50	  const pK = p * 4, gK = g * 4, fK = f * 9
    51	  const total = pK + gK + fK || 1
    52	  return (
    53	    <div className="flex h-[4px] rounded-full overflow-hidden gap-[2px]">
    54	      <div className="rounded-full" style={{ width: `${(pK / total) * 100}%`, backgroundColor: MC.prot }} />
    55	      <div className="rounded-full" style={{ width: `${(gK / total) * 100}%`, backgroundColor: MC.carb }} />
    56	      <div className="rounded-full" style={{ width: `${(fK / total) * 100}%`, backgroundColor: MC.fat }} />
    57	    </div>
