    63	function MealTypeChooser({ mealId, current, onChange }: { mealId: string; current: string; onChange: (t: string) => void }) {
    64	  const { t } = useClientT()
    65	  const [open, setOpen] = useState(false)
    66	  const types = ["breakfast", "lunch", "dinner", "snack"] as const
    67	
    68	  async function pick(type: string) {
    69	    setOpen(false)
    70	    onChange(type)
    71	    await fetch(`/api/client/nutrition/meals/${mealId}`, {
    72	      method: "PATCH",
    73	      headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
    74	      body: JSON.stringify({ meal_type: type }),
    75	    })
    76	  }
    77	
    78	  return (
    79	    <div className="relative">
    80	      <button onClick={(e) => { e.stopPropagation(); setOpen(o => !o) }} className="flex items-center gap-1.5 group">
    81	        {(() => { const Icon = MEAL_TYPE_ICON[current] ?? Coffee; return <Icon size={11} className="text-white/50 group-hover:text-white/80 transition-colors" /> })()}
    82	        <span className="text-[11px] font-bold text-white/70 group-hover:text-white transition-colors">
    83	          {MEAL_TYPE_KEYS[current] ? t(MEAL_TYPE_KEYS[current]) : current}
    84	        </span>
    85	        <svg width="8" height="8" viewBox="0 0 8 8" className="text-white/20 group-hover:text-white/50 transition-colors" fill="currentColor"><path d="M4 5L1 2h6L4 5z"/></svg>
    86	      </button>
    87	      <AnimatePresence>
    88	        {open && (
    89	          <>
    90	            <div className="fixed inset-0 z-40" onClick={() => setOpen(false)} />
    91	            <motion.div
    92	              initial={{ opacity: 0, y: -6, scale: 0.96 }}
    93	              animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0, scale: 1 }}
    94	              exit={{ opacity: 0, y: -4, scale: 0.97 }}
    95	              transition={{ duration: 0.15 }}
    96	              onClick={(e) => e.stopPropagation()}
    97	              className="absolute left-0 top-6 z-50 bg-[#111111] rounded-xl overflow-hidden shadow-[0_8px_32px_rgba(0,0,0,0.7)] min-w-[140px]"
    98	            >
    99	              {types.map(type => (
   100	                <button
   101	                  key={type}
   102	                  onClick={() => pick(type)}
   103	                  className={`w-full flex items-center gap-2 px-3 py-2.5 text-left text-[12px] transition-colors hover:bg-white/[0.06] ${
   104	                    type === current ? "text-[#f2f2f2] font-bold" : "text-white/70"
   105	                  }`}
   106	                >
   107	                  {(() => { const Icon = MEAL_TYPE_ICON[type] ?? Coffee; return <Icon size={12} className="text-white/40" /> })()}
   108	                  {MEAL_TYPE_KEYS[type] ? t(MEAL_TYPE_KEYS[type]) : type}

   110	                </button>
   111	              ))}
   112	            </motion.div>
   113	          </>
   114	        )}
   115	      </AnimatePresence>
   116	    </div>
   117	  )
   118	}

   120	function TimeEditor({ mealId, loggedAt, onUpdated }: { mealId: string; loggedAt: string; onUpdated: (iso: string) => void }) {
   121	  const [open, setOpen] = useState(false)
   122	  const [saving, setSaving] = useState(false)
   123	  const d = new Date(loggedAt)
   124	  const currentVal = `${String(d.getHours()).padStart(2,'0')}:${String(d.getMinutes()).padStart(2,'0')}`
   125	  const timeStr = d.toLocaleTimeString('fr-FR', { hour: '2-digit', minute: '2-digit' })
   126	
   127	  async function handleChange(e: React.ChangeEvent<HTMLInputElement>) {
   128	    const timeVal = e.target.value
   129	    if (!timeVal) return
   130	    setSaving(true)
   131	    setOpen(false)
   132	    const base = new Date(loggedAt)
   133	    const [h, m] = timeVal.split(':').map(Number)
   134	    base.setHours(h, m, 0, 0)
   135	    const iso = base.toISOString()
   136	    await fetch(`/api/client/nutrition/meals/${mealId}`, {
   137	      method: 'PATCH',
   138	      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
   139	      body: JSON.stringify({ logged_at: iso }),
   140	    })
   141	    onUpdated(iso)
   142	    setSaving(false)
   143	  }
   144	
   145	  return (
   146	    <div className="relative" onClick={e => e.stopPropagation()}>
   147	      <button onClick={() => setOpen(o => !o)} className="flex items-center gap-1 group mt-0.5">
   148	        <span className={`text-[10px] text-white/25 group-hover:text-white/50 transition-colors ${saving ? 'opacity-40' : ''}`}>
   149	          {saving ? '…' : timeStr}
   150	        </span>
   151	        <Pencil size={8} className="text-white/15 group-hover:text-white/40 transition-colors" />
   152	      </button>
   153	      <AnimatePresence>
   154	        {open && (
   155	          <>
   156	            <div className="fixed inset-0 z-40" onClick={() => setOpen(false)} />
   157	            <motion.div
   158	              initial={{ opacity: 0, y: -4, scale: 0.97 }}
   159	              animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0, scale: 1 }}
   160	              exit={{ opacity: 0, y: -3, scale: 0.97 }}
   161	              transition={{ duration: 0.13 }}
   162	              className="absolute left-0 top-6 z-50 bg-[#1a1a1a] border border-white/[0.08] rounded-xl px-3 py-2.5 shadow-[0_8px_32px_rgba(0,0,0,0.7)]"
   163	              onClick={e => e.stopPropagation()}
   164	            >
   165	              <p className="text-[9px] font-barlow-condensed font-bold uppercase tracking-[0.14em] text-white/30 mb-2">Heure</p>
   166	              <input
   167	                type="time"
   168	                defaultValue={currentVal}
   169	                onChange={handleChange}
   170	                className="bg-transparent text-white border-none outline-none"
   171	                style={{ fontSize: 16, colorScheme: 'dark' }}
   172	              />
   173	            </motion.div>
   174	          </>
   175	        )}
   176	      </AnimatePresence>
   177	    </div>
   178	  )
   179	}
   180	
   181	function EntryRow({
   182	  entry, mealId, onDeleted, onUpdated,
   183	}: {
   184	  entry: NutritionEntry & { food_items?: { name_fr?: string } }
   185	  mealId: string
   186	  onDeleted: (entryId: string) => void
   187	  onUpdated: (entryId: string, quantity_g: number, newMealTotals: Record<string, number>) => void
   188	}) {
   189	  const name = entry.food_items?.name_fr ?? (entry as any).food_item?.name_fr ?? "—"
   190	  const [editing, setEditing] = useState(false)
   191	  const [qty, setQty] = useState(String(entry.quantity_g))
   192	  const [saving, setSaving] = useState(false)
   193	  const [deleting, setDeleting] = useState(false)
   194	
   195	  async function saveQty(e: React.FormEvent) {
   196	    e.preventDefault()
   197	    const q = parseFloat(qty)
   198	    if (!q || q <= 0 || q === entry.quantity_g) { setEditing(false); return }
   199	    setSaving(true)
   200	    const res = await fetch(`/api/client/nutrition/entries/${entry.id}`, {
   201	      method: 'PATCH',
   202	      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
   203	      body: JSON.stringify({ quantity_g: q }),
   204	    })
   205	    if (res.ok) {
   206	      const json = await res.json()
   207	      onUpdated(entry.id, q, json.meal?.totals ?? {})
   208	    }
   209	    setSaving(false)
   210	    setEditing(false)
   211	  }
   212	
   213	  async function deleteEntry(e: React.MouseEvent) {
   214	    e.stopPropagation()
   215	    setDeleting(true)
   216	    const res = await fetch(`/api/client/nutrition/entries/${entry.id}`, { method: 'DELETE' })
   217	    if (res.ok) onDeleted(entry.id)
   218	    else setDeleting(false)
   219	  }
   220	
   221	  return (
   222	    <div className={`flex items-center gap-2 transition-opacity ${deleting ? 'opacity-30' : ''}`}>
   223	      <div className="w-1 h-1 rounded-full bg-white/20 shrink-0 mt-[1px]" />
   224	      <span className="text-[12px] text-white/65 truncate flex-1 min-w-0">{name}</span>
   225	      {editing ? (
   226	        <form onSubmit={saveQty} className="flex items-center gap-1.5 shrink-0" onClick={e => e.stopPropagation()}>
   227	          <input
   228	            autoFocus
   229	            type="number"
   230	            min={1}
   231	            max={5000}
   232	            step={1}
   233	            value={qty}
   234	            onChange={e => setQty(e.target.value)}
   235	            className="w-14 h-6 bg-white/[0.08] border border-white/[0.12] rounded-lg text-[11px] text-white text-center tabular-nums outline-none focus:border-white/30"
   236	          />
   237	          <span className="text-[10px] text-white/30">g</span>
   238	          <button type="submit" disabled={saving} className="h-6 px-2 bg-white/[0.1] rounded-lg text-[10px] text-white/70 hover:text-white active:scale-95 transition-all disabled:opacity-40">
   239	            {saving ? '…' : '✓'}
   240	          </button>
   241	          <button type="button" onClick={e => { e.stopPropagation(); setEditing(false) }} className="h-6 px-2 bg-white/[0.05] rounded-lg text-[10px] text-white/40 hover:text-white/70">
   242	            ✕
   243	          </button>
   244	        </form>
   245	      ) : (
   246	        <div className="flex items-center gap-2 shrink-0">
   247	          <button onClick={e => { e.stopPropagation(); setEditing(true) }} className="flex items-center gap-1 group">
   248	            <span className="text-[11px] text-white/30 group-hover:text-white/60 transition-colors tabular-nums">{entry.quantity_g}g</span>
   249	            <Pencil size={8} className="text-white/15 group-hover:text-white/40 transition-colors" />
   250	          </button>
   251	          <span className="text-[11px] text-white/40 font-semibold w-14 text-right tabular-nums">
   252	            {Math.round(entry.calories_kcal)} kcal
   253	          </span>
   254	          <button
   255	            onClick={deleteEntry}
   256	            disabled={deleting}
   257	            className="h-6 w-6 flex items-center justify-center rounded-lg bg-red-500/0 hover:bg-red-500/15 text-white/20 hover:text-red-400 active:scale-95 transition-all disabled:opacity-40"
   258	          >
   259	            <Trash2 size={10} />
   260	          </button>

    41	// ISO weekday: 1=Lun … 7=Dim

   106	function WeekSchedule({ slots, days }: { slots: ScheduleSlot[]; days: ProtocolDay[] }) {
   107	  if (slots.length === 0) return null
   108	
   109	  // Build a lookup: dayName → carbCycleType
   110	  const dayTypeByName = new Map(days.map(d => [d.name, d.carb_cycle_type ?? null]))
   111	  // Build a lookup: dow → slot
   112	  const slotByDow = new Map(slots.map(s => [s.dow, s]))
   113	
   114	  return (
   115	    <div className="bg-[#111111] rounded-2xl p-4 space-y-3">
   116	      <p className="font-barlow-condensed font-bold uppercase tracking-[0.14em] text-[9px] text-white/25">
   117	        Planning hebdomadaire
   118	      </p>
   119	      <div className="grid grid-cols-7 gap-1">
   120	        {DOW_DISPLAY_ORDER.map((dow, i) => {
   121	          const slot = slotByDow.get(dow)
   122	          const cct  = slot ? (dayTypeByName.get(slot.dayName) ?? slot.carbCycleType) : null
   123	          const color = cct ? CARB_CYCLE_COLOR[cct] : 'rgba(255,255,255,0.08)'
   124	          const label = cct === 'high' ? 'H' : cct === 'medium' ? 'M' : cct === 'low' ? 'B' : '—'
   125	          return (
   126	            <div key={dow} className="flex flex-col items-center gap-1.5">
   127	              <p className="text-[9px] text-white/30">{DOW_LABELS[i]}</p>
   128	              <div
   129	                className="w-full rounded-full"
   130	                style={{ height: 4, backgroundColor: color }}
   131	              />
   132	              <p className="text-[9px] font-bold" style={{ color: cct ? color : 'rgba(255,255,255,0.15)' }}>
   133	                {label}
   134	              </p>
   135	            </div>
   136	          )
   137	        })}
   138	      </div>
   139	      {/* Legend */}
   140	      <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-3">
   141	        {Object.entries(CARB_CYCLE_LABELS).map(([key, label]) => (
   142	          days.some(d => d.carb_cycle_type === key) && (
   143	            <div key={key} className="flex items-center gap-1.5">
   144	              <div className="w-2 h-2 rounded-full" style={{ backgroundColor: CARB_CYCLE_COLOR[key] }} />
   145	              <span className="text-[10px] text-white/35">{label}</span>
   146	            </div>
   147	          )
   148	        ))}
   149	      </div>
   150	    </div>
   151	  )
   152	}

   154	function DayAccordion({
   155	  day,
   156	  tdee,
   157	  tdeeSource,
   158	  bodyWeightKg,
   159	  cycleState,
   160	  cycleSyncEnabled,
   161	  defaultOpen,
   162	}: {
   163	  day: ProtocolDay
   164	  tdee: number | null
   165	  tdeeSource: string | null
   166	  bodyWeightKg?: number | null
   167	  cycleState?: CycleState | null
   168	  cycleSyncEnabled?: boolean
   169	  defaultOpen: boolean
   170	}) {
   171	  const { t } = useClientT()
   172	  const [open, setOpen] = useState(defaultOpen)
   173	
   174	  const delta     = tdee != null && tdee > 0 ? Math.round(day.kcal - tdee) : null
   175	  const deltaStr  = delta != null ? (delta >= 0 ? `+${delta}` : `${delta}`) + ' kcal vs TDEE' : null
   176	  const goalLabel =
   177	    delta == null ? null :
   178	    delta >  100  ? 'Surplus' :
   179	    delta < -100  ? t('goal.deficit_calorique') : t('goal.maintenance')
   180	
   181	  const gPerKg = bodyWeightKg && bodyWeightKg > 0
   182	    ? (day.protein_g / bodyWeightKg).toFixed(2)
   183	    : null
   184	
   185	  const tdeeSourceLabel = tdeeSource === 'formula_proxy'
   186	    ? 'Estimé (formule)'
   187	    : 'Adaptatif'
   188	
   189	  const cycleTypeLabel = day.carb_cycle_type ? CARB_CYCLE_LABELS[day.carb_cycle_type] : null
   190	  const cycleTypeColor = day.carb_cycle_type ? CARB_CYCLE_COLOR[day.carb_cycle_type] : undefined
   191	
   192	  const showCycle = !!(cycleSyncEnabled && cycleState?.hasActiveCycle && cycleState.currentPhase)
   193	  const cycleAdj  = showCycle ? getCycleSyncAdjustment(cycleState!.currentPhase!) : null
   194	
   195	  return (
   196	    <div className="bg-[#111111] rounded-2xl overflow-hidden">
   197	      {/* Header */}
   198	      <button
   199	        onClick={() => setOpen(v => !v)}
   200	        className="w-full flex items-center justify-between px-4 py-3 active:bg-white/[0.03] transition-colors"
   201	      >
   202	        <div className="text-left flex-1 min-w-0">
   203	          <div className="flex items-center gap-2 flex-wrap">
   204	            <p className="font-barlow-condensed font-bold uppercase tracking-[0.18em] text-[11px] text-white/70 truncate">
   205	              {day.name}
   206	            </p>
   207	            {cycleTypeLabel && (
   208	              <span
   209	                className="text-[9px] font-bold uppercase tracking-[0.1em] rounded-full px-2 py-0.5 shrink-0"
   210	                style={{ color: cycleTypeColor, backgroundColor: cycleTypeColor ? `${cycleTypeColor}18` : undefined }}
   211	              >
   212	                {cycleTypeLabel}
   213	              </span>
   214	            )}
   215	          </div>
   216	          <div className="flex items-baseline gap-2 mt-0.5">
   217	            <p className="text-[13px] font-semibold text-[#e0e0e0] tabular-nums">
   218	              {Math.round(day.kcal).toLocaleString('fr-FR')} kcal
   219	            </p>
   220	            {goalLabel && (
   221	              <p className="text-[11px] text-white/35">{goalLabel}</p>
   222	            )}
   223	          </div>
   224	        </div>
   225	        <motion.div animate={{ rotate: open ? 180 : 0 }} transition={{ duration: 0.2 }} className="shrink-0 ml-3">
   226	          <ChevronDown size={16} className="text-white/30" />
   227	        </motion.div>
   228	      </button>
   229	
   230	      {/* Expanded detail */}
   231	      <AnimatePresence initial={false}>
   232	        {open && (
   233	          <motion.div
   234	            initial={{ height: 0, opacity: 0 }}
   235	            animate={{ height: 'auto', opacity: 1 }}
   236	            exit={{ height: 0, opacity: 0 }}
   237	            transition={{ duration: 0.22, ease: 'easeOut' }}
   238	            className="overflow-hidden"
   239	          >
   240	            <div className="px-4 pb-4 border-t border-white/[0.05]">
   241	
   242	              {/* Notes coach */}
   243	              {day.recommendations && (
   244	                <>
   245	                  <SectionLabel>Notes de ton coach</SectionLabel>
   246	                  <p className="text-[12px] text-white/60 leading-relaxed whitespace-pre-wrap pb-1">
   247	                    {day.recommendations}
   248	                  </p>
   249	                </>
   250	              )}
   251	
   252	              {/* TDEE */}
   253	              {tdee != null && tdee > 0 && (
   254	                <>
   255	                  <SectionLabel>Dépense énergétique</SectionLabel>
   256	                  <Row
   257	                    label="TDEE"
   258	                    value={`${Math.round(tdee).toLocaleString('fr-FR')} kcal`}
   259	                    sub={tdeeSourceLabel}
   260	                    valueColor="#4a90e2"

UI CANDIDATE: ./components/client/smart/RemainingBreakdown.tsx
------------------------------------------------------------
     1	'use client'
     2	
     3	import type { NutritionMacros } from './SmartNutritionWidget'
     4	import { computeNutritionBalance } from '@/lib/nutrition/balance'
     5	import { computeActionableRemaining } from '@/lib/nutrition/actionable-remaining'
     6	import { NUTRITION_UI_COLORS } from '@/lib/nutrition/ui-colors'
     7	import { useClientT } from '../ClientI18nProvider'
     8	
     9	type DeltaCard = {
    10	  key: 'protein' | 'carbs' | 'fat' | 'water'
    11	  label: string
    12	  shortLabel: string
    13	  remaining: number
    14	  overflow: number
    15	  unit: 'g' | 'L'
    16	  accent: string
    17	}
    18	
    19	function formatValue(value: number, unit: 'g' | 'L'): string {
    20	  return unit === 'L' ? `${value.toFixed(1)} ${unit}` : `${Math.round(value)}${unit}`
    21	}
    22	
    23	function buildHeadline(cards: DeltaCard[], remainingCaloriesNet: number, t: (key: any) => string): string {
    24	  const activeRemaining = cards.filter(card => card.remaining > 0)
    25	  const activeOverflow = cards.filter(card => card.overflow > 0)
    26	
    27	  if (activeOverflow.length === 0 && activeRemaining.length === 0 && remainingCaloriesNet <= 0) {
    28	    return t("nutrition.goals.reached")
    29	  }
    30	
    31	  if (activeOverflow.length > 0) {
    32	    const names = activeOverflow.map(card => card.shortLabel.toLowerCase()).join(", ")
    33	    return t("nutrition.overflow.msg").replace("{names}", names)
    34	  }
    35	
    36	  const primary = activeRemaining.sort((a, b) => b.remaining - a.remaining)[0]
    37	  if (!primary) {
    38	    return remainingCaloriesNet > 0
    39	      ? t("nutrition.calories.available").replace("{n}", String(Math.round(remainingCaloriesNet)))
    40	      : t("nutrition.day.calibrated")
    41	  }
    42	
    43	  return t("nutrition.macro.priority").replace("{macro}", primary.label)
    44	}
    45	
    46	export default function RemainingBreakdown({
    47	  consumed,
    48	  target,
    49	  gender,
    50	  bodyWeightKg,
    51	}: {
    52	  consumed: NutritionMacros
    53	  target: NutritionMacros
    54	  gender?: string | null
    55	  bodyWeightKg?: number | null
    56	}) {
    57	  const { t } = useClientT()
    58	  const informativeBalance = computeNutritionBalance(consumed, target)
    59	  const actionable = computeActionableRemaining({
    60	    target,
    61	    consumed,
    62	    profile: { gender, weightKg: bodyWeightKg },
    63	  })
    64	  const { remainingCaloriesFromMacros } = informativeBalance
    65	  const remaining = {
    66	    protein_g: actionable.actionableRemaining.protein,
    67	    carbs_g: actionable.actionableRemaining.carbs,
    68	    fat_g: actionable.actionableRemaining.fat,
    69	    water_ml: Math.max(0, target.water_ml - consumed.water_ml),
    70	  }
    71	  const overflow = {
    72	    protein_g: actionable.overflow.protein_g,
    73	    carbs_g: actionable.overflow.carbs_g,
    74	    fat_g: actionable.overflow.fat_g,
    75	    water_ml: Math.max(0, consumed.water_ml - target.water_ml),
    76	  }
    77	  const cards: DeltaCard[] = [
    78	    {
    79	      key: 'protein',
    80	      label: t('nutrition.protein'),
    81	      shortLabel: t('nutrition.protein'),
    82	      remaining: remaining.protein_g,
    83	      overflow: overflow.protein_g,
    84	      unit: 'g',
    85	      accent: NUTRITION_UI_COLORS.protein,
    86	    },
    87	    {
    88	      key: 'carbs',
    89	      label: t('nutrition.carbs'),
    90	      shortLabel: t('nutrition.carbs'),
    91	      remaining: remaining.carbs_g,
    92	      overflow: overflow.carbs_g,
    93	      unit: 'g',
    94	      accent: NUTRITION_UI_COLORS.carbs,
    95	    },
    96	    {
    97	      key: 'fat',
    98	      label: t('nutrition.fat'),
    99	      shortLabel: t('nutrition.fat'),
   100	      remaining: remaining.fat_g,
   101	      overflow: overflow.fat_g,
   102	      unit: 'g',
   103	      accent: NUTRITION_UI_COLORS.fat,
   104	    },
   105	    {
   106	      key: 'water',
   107	      label: t('nutrition.hydration'),
   108	      shortLabel: t('nutrition.hydration'),
   109	      remaining: remaining.water_ml / 1000,
   110	      overflow: overflow.water_ml / 1000,
   111	      unit: 'L',
   112	      accent: NUTRITION_UI_COLORS.water,
   113	    },
   114	  ]
   115	
   116	  const activeCards = cards.filter(card => card.remaining > 0 || card.overflow > 0)
   117	  const remainingCards = activeCards
   118	    .filter(card => card.remaining > 0)
   119	    .sort((a, b) => b.remaining - a.remaining)
   120	  const overflowCards = activeCards
   121	    .filter(card => card.overflow > 0)
   122	    .sort((a, b) => b.overflow - a.overflow)
   123	  const headline = buildHeadline(cards, actionable.actionableRemaining.calories, t)
   124	
   125	  return (
   126	    <div className="bg-[#111111] rounded-2xl p-4">
   127	      <div className="flex items-start justify-between gap-3">
   128	        <div>
   129	          <div className="font-barlow-condensed font-bold uppercase tracking-[0.18em] text-[11px] text-white mb-1">
   130	            Reste à consommer
   131	          </div>
   132	          <p className="text-[13px] text-white/65 leading-relaxed max-w-[28ch]">
   133	            {headline}
   134	          </p>
   135	        </div>
   136	        <div className="shrink-0 rounded-2xl bg-white/[0.04] px-3 py-2 text-right">
   137	          <div className="text-[18px] font-black text-white tabular-nums">
   138	            {Math.round(actionable.actionableRemaining.calories)}
   139	          </div>
   140	          <div className="text-[9px] uppercase tracking-[0.12em] text-white/35">
   141	            kcal restantes
   142	          </div>
   143	        </div>
   144	      </div>
   145	
   146	      <div className="mt-3 grid grid-cols-2 gap-2">
   147	        {remainingCards.length > 0 ? (
   148	          remainingCards.map(card => (
   149	            <div key={card.key} className="rounded-2xl bg-white/[0.03] p-3">
   150	              <div className="text-[10px] uppercase tracking-[0.1em] text-white/40 font-bold">{card.label}</div>
   151	              <div className="mt-1 text-[20px] font-black tabular-nums" style={{ color: card.accent }}>
   152	                {formatValue(card.remaining, card.unit)}
   153	              </div>
   154	              <div className="text-[10px] text-white/35 mt-1">
   155	                encore utiles
   156	              </div>
   157	            </div>
   158	          ))
   159	        ) : (
   160	          <div className="col-span-2 rounded-2xl bg-[#111111] p-3">
   161	            <div className="text-[10px] uppercase tracking-[0.12em] text-[#e0e0e0] font-bold">Bonne zone</div>
   162	            <div className="mt-1 text-[13px] text-white/75 leading-relaxed">
   163	              {t("nutrition.nomacro.lag")}
   164	            </div>
   165	          </div>
   166	        )}
   167	      </div>
   168	
   169	      {overflowCards.length > 0 && (
   170	        <div className="mt-3 rounded-2xl bg-[#111111] p-3">
   171	          <div className="text-[10px] uppercase tracking-[0.12em] text-[#e0e0e0] font-bold">À freiner</div>
   172	          <div className="mt-2 flex flex-wrap gap-2">
   173	            {overflowCards.map(card => (
   174	              <div
   175	                key={card.key}
   176	                className="rounded-full bg-white/[0.06] px-2.5 py-1 text-[11px] font-bold tabular-nums text-[#b0b0b0]"
   177	              >
   178	                {card.label} +{formatValue(card.overflow, card.unit)}
   179	              </div>
   180	            ))}
   181	          </div>
   182	        </div>
   183	      )}
   184	
   185	      {remainingCaloriesFromMacros > 0 && (
   186	        <div className="mt-3 rounded-2xl bg-white/[0.025] px-3 py-2.5 flex items-center justify-between gap-3">
   187	          <span className="text-[11px] uppercase tracking-[0.1em] text-white/35 font-bold">
   188	            Protocole brut
   189	          </span>
   190	          <span className="text-[12px] text-white/60 tabular-nums">
   191	            {Math.round(remainingCaloriesFromMacros)} kcal avant compensation
   192	          </span>
   193	        </div>
   194	      )}
   195	
   196	    </div>
   197	  )
   198	}

UI CANDIDATE: ./components/client/smart/SmartNutritionHero.tsx

     1	'use client'
     2	
     3	import Link from 'next/link'
     4	import { ChevronLeft, ChevronRight } from 'lucide-react'
     5	import { shiftIsoDate } from '@/lib/utils/date'
     6	import { getNutritionProgressMeta, type NutritionProgressState } from '@/lib/nutrition/progress'
     7	import { computeNutritionBalance } from '@/lib/nutrition/balance'
     8	import { getRemainingNutritionTargets } from '@/lib/nutrition/remaining-targets'
     9	import { computeActionableRemaining } from '@/lib/nutrition/actionable-remaining'
    10	import type { NutritionMacros } from './SmartNutritionWidget'
    11	import { NUTRITION_UI_COLORS } from '@/lib/nutrition/ui-colors'
    12	import { useClientT } from '../ClientI18nProvider'
    13	
    14	type Props = {
    15	  date: string
    16	  consumed: NutritionMacros
    17	  target: NutritionMacros
    18	  onWaterClick?: () => void
    19	  simulationMode?: boolean
    20	  gender?: string | null
    21	  bodyWeightKg?: number | null
    22	  compact?: boolean
    23	  micro?: boolean
    24	  showSimulationBadge?: boolean
    25	}
    26	
    27	// ── Arc geometry — 240° gauge ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
    28	// Center (110,110), r=76, gap 120° at bottom, clockwise
    29	// Start (bottom-left): (44.2, 148) — End (bottom-right): (175.8, 148)
    30	// Arc length: 2π × 76 × (240/360) ≈ 319
    31	// Equator (y=110) sits at (110−15)/145 = 65.5 % from top of viewBox "20 15 180 145"
    32	const ARC_R   = 76
    33	const ARC_D   = `M 44.2,148 A ${ARC_R},${ARC_R} 0 1,1 175.8,148`
    34	const ARC_LEN = 2 * Math.PI * ARC_R * (240 / 360)  // ≈ 319
    35	
    36	const MACRO_KEYS = [
    37	  { key: 'protein_g' as const, iKey: 'nutrition.protein' as const, color: NUTRITION_UI_COLORS.protein },
    38	  { key: 'carbs_g'   as const, iKey: 'nutrition.carbs' as const,   color: NUTRITION_UI_COLORS.carbs   },
    39	  { key: 'fat_g'     as const, iKey: 'nutrition.fat' as const,     color: NUTRITION_UI_COLORS.fat     },
    40	]
    41	
    42	const SIMULATION_COLOR = '#818cf8'
    43	
    44	const shiftDate = shiftIsoDate
    45	
    46	function formatNav(iso: string): string {
    47	  const [y, m, d] = iso.split('-').map(Number)
    48	  return new Intl.DateTimeFormat('fr-FR', { weekday: 'short', day: 'numeric', month: 'short' })
    49	    .format(new Date(Date.UTC(y, m - 1, d)))
    50	}
    51	
    52	function formatOverflow(value: number, unit: 'g' | 'L'): string | null {
    53	  if (value <= 0) return null
    54	  return unit === 'L' ? `+${value.toFixed(1)} L au-dessus` : `+${Math.round(value)}g au-dessus`
    55	}
    56	
    57	function getStateColor(state: NutritionProgressState, base: string): string {
    58	  if (state === 'over')       return '#ef4444'
    59	  if (state === 'near_limit') return '#f59e0b'
    60	  return base
    61	}
    62	
    63	function formatRemainingLabel(value: number, unit: 'g' | 'L'): string {
    64	  if (value <= 0) return 'objectif atteint'
    65	  if (unit === 'L') return `${value.toFixed(1)} L restants`
    66	  return `${Math.round(value)}g restants`
    67	}
    68	
    69	export default function SmartNutritionHero({
    70	  date,
    71	  consumed,
    72	  target,
    73	  onWaterClick,
    74	  simulationMode = false,
    75	  gender,
    76	  bodyWeightKg,
    77	  compact = false,
    78	  micro = false,
    79	  showSimulationBadge = true,
    80	}: Props) {
    81	  const { t } = useClientT()
    82	  const prev = shiftDate(date, -1)
    83	  const next = shiftDate(date, 1)
    84	  const balance = computeNutritionBalance(consumed, target)
    85	  const MACROS = MACRO_KEYS.map(m => ({ ...m, label: t(m.iKey as any) }))
    86	  const rawRemaining = getRemainingNutritionTargets({
    87	    dailyTargets: target,
    88	    consumedToday: consumed,
    89	  })
    90	  const actionableRemaining = computeActionableRemaining({
    91	    target,
    92	    consumed,
    93	    profile: { gender, weightKg: bodyWeightKg },
    94	  })
    95	
    96	  const kcalMeta   = getNutritionProgressMeta(consumed.kcal, target.kcal)
    97	  const pct        = Math.min(kcalMeta.ratio, 1)
    98	  const arcOffset  = ARC_LEN * (1 - pct)
    99	  const kcalColor  = getStateColor(kcalMeta.state, NUTRITION_UI_COLORS.calories)
   100	  const kcalStroke = simulationMode ? SIMULATION_COLOR : kcalColor
   101	  const remaining  = Math.round(balance.remainingCaloriesNet)
   102	
   103	  const waterMeta          = getNutritionProgressMeta(consumed.water_ml, target.water_ml)
   104	  const waterOverflowLabel = formatOverflow((consumed.water_ml - target.water_ml) / 1000, 'L')
   105	  const cardPadding = micro ? '8px' : compact ? '12px' : '18px'
   106	  const arcHeight = micro ? 72 : compact ? 112 : 145
   107	  const consumedTextSize = micro ? 'text-[18px]' : compact ? 'text-[22px]' : 'text-[28px]'
   108	  const sideTextSize = micro ? 'text-[15px]' : compact ? 'text-[17px]' : 'text-[20px]'
   109	  const macroGapClass = micro ? 'gap-1.5 mt-0' : compact ? 'gap-2 mt-0.5' : 'gap-3 mt-2'
   110	  const showMacroHelpers = !micro
   111	
   112	  return (
   113	    <div
   114	      className="bg-[#111111] rounded-2xl"
   115	      style={simulationMode ? {
   116	        padding: cardPadding,
   117	        backgroundImage: 'radial-gradient(circle, rgba(129,140,248,0.07) 1px, transparent 1px)',
   118	        backgroundSize: '18px 18px',
   119	        backgroundColor: '#111111',
   120	      } : { padding: cardPadding }}
   121	    >
   122	
   123	      {/* ── Simulation badge ── */}
   124	      {simulationMode && showSimulationBadge && (
   125	        <div className={`flex items-center ${micro ? 'mb-1' : compact ? 'mb-1.5' : 'mb-3'}`}>
   126	          <div className="inline-flex items-center gap-1.5 px-2.5 py-1 rounded-full bg-[#818cf8]/10">
   127	            <div className="w-1.5 h-1.5 rounded-full bg-[#818cf8] animate-pulse" />
   128	            <span className="text-[9px] font-barlow-condensed font-bold uppercase tracking-[0.18em] text-[#818cf8]">Simulation</span>
   129	          </div>
   130	        </div>
   131	      )}
   132	
   133	      {/* ── Date nav — hidden in simulation ── */}
   134	      {!simulationMode && (
   135	        <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-1">
   136	          <Link href={`/client/nutrition?date=${prev}`} className="flex items-center gap-1 text-white/50 text-[11px]">
   137	            <ChevronLeft size={14} />{formatNav(prev)}
   138	          </Link>
   139	          <span className="text-[17px] font-black tracking-[-0.02em] text-white">{formatNav(date)}</span>
   140	          <Link href={`/client/nutrition?date=${next}`} className="flex items-center gap-1 text-white/50 text-[11px]">
   141	            {formatNav(next)}<ChevronRight size={14} />
   142	          </Link>
   143	        </div>
   144	      )}
   145	
   146	      {/* ── Arc + values overlay ──────────────────────────────────────────── */}
   147	      {/* viewBox "20 15 180 145" — equator y=110 sits at 65.5 % from top   */}
   148	      <div className="relative" style={{ height: arcHeight }}>
   149	        <svg
   150	          viewBox="20 15 180 145"
   151	          className="w-full h-full"
   152	          preserveAspectRatio="xMidYMid meet"
   153	        >
   154	          {/* Track */}
   155	          <path d={ARC_D} fill="none" stroke="rgba(255,255,255,0.07)" strokeWidth="7" strokeLinecap="round" />
   156	          {/* Progress */}
   157	          <path
   158	            d={ARC_D}
   159	            fill="none"
   160	            stroke={kcalStroke}
   161	            strokeWidth="7"
   162	            strokeLinecap="round"
   163	            strokeDasharray={ARC_LEN}
   164	            strokeDashoffset={arcOffset}
   165	            style={{ transition: 'stroke-dashoffset 0.6s ease, stroke 0.3s ease' }}
   166	          />
   167	        </svg>
   168	
   169	        {/* Values — floating at equator (65.5 % from top) */}
   170	        <div
   171	          className="absolute left-0 right-0 grid grid-cols-3 items-center px-1"
   172	          style={{ top: '65.5%', transform: 'translateY(-50%)' }}
   173	        >
   174	          {/* Restant */}
   175	          <div className="text-left">
   176	            <div className={`${sideTextSize} font-bold text-white tabular-nums leading-none`}>
   177	              {remaining}
   178	            </div>
   179	            <div className={`uppercase tracking-[0.14em] text-white/35 ${micro ? 'text-[8px] mt-0.5' : 'text-[9px] mt-1'}`}>
   180	              Restant
   181	            </div>
   182	          </div>
   183	
   184	          {/* Consommé — larger, colored */}
   185	          <div className="text-center">
   186	            <div
   187	              className={`${consumedTextSize} font-black tabular-nums leading-none`}
   188	              style={{ color: kcalStroke }}
   189	            >
   190	              {Math.round(consumed.kcal)}
   191	            </div>
   192	            <div className={`uppercase tracking-[0.14em] text-white/35 ${micro ? 'text-[8px] mt-0.5' : 'text-[9px] mt-1'}`}>
   193	              {simulationMode ? 'Simulé' : 'Consommé'}
   194	            </div>
   195	          </div>
   196	
   197	          {/* Objectif */}
   198	          <div className="text-right">
   199	            <div className={`${sideTextSize} font-bold text-white/50 tabular-nums leading-none`}>
   200	              {target.kcal}
   201	            </div>
   202	            <div className={`uppercase tracking-[0.14em] text-white/35 ${micro ? 'text-[8px] mt-0.5' : 'text-[9px] mt-1'}`}>
   203	              Objectif
   204	            </div>
   205	          </div>
   206	        </div>
   207	      </div>
   208	
   209	      {/* ── Macros: label → bar → Xg/Xg ── */}
   210	      <div className={`grid grid-cols-3 ${macroGapClass}`}>
   211	        {MACROS.map(m => {
   212	          const consumedValue = consumed[m.key] ?? 0
   213	          const rawTarget = target[m.key] ?? 0
   214	          const balanceKey = m.key as 'protein_g' | 'carbs_g' | 'fat_g'
   215	          const rawDelta =
   216	            simulationMode
   217	              ? balanceKey === 'protein_g'
   218	                ? actionableRemaining.actionableRemaining.protein
   219	                : balanceKey === 'carbs_g'
   220	                  ? actionableRemaining.actionableRemaining.carbs
   221	                  : actionableRemaining.actionableRemaining.fat
   222	              : balanceKey === 'protein_g'
   223	                ? rawRemaining.protein
   224	                : balanceKey === 'carbs_g'
   225	                  ? rawRemaining.carbs
   226	                  : rawRemaining.fat
   227	          const overflowValue = Math.max(0, -rawDelta)
   228	          const remainingValue = Math.max(0, rawDelta)
   229	          const displayTarget = rawTarget
   230	          const meta = getNutritionProgressMeta(consumedValue, Math.max(displayTarget, 0))
   231	          const fillColor = simulationMode
   232	            ? overflowValue > 0
   233	              ? '#ef4444'
   234	              : 'rgba(129,140,248,0.65)'
   235	            : getStateColor(
   236	                overflowValue > 0 ? 'over' : meta.state,
   237	                m.color,
   238	              )
   239	          const helperLabel =
   240	            overflowValue > 0
   241	              ? 'à freiner'
   242	              : formatRemainingLabel(remainingValue, 'g')
   243	          const overflow = formatOverflow(overflowValue, 'g')
   244	          return (
   245	            <div key={m.key}>
   246	              <div className={`text-white/40 uppercase font-bold tracking-[0.08em] ${micro ? 'text-[8px] mb-1' : 'text-[9px] mb-1.5'}`}>
   247	                {m.label}
   248	              </div>
   249	              <div className={`${micro ? 'h-1' : 'h-1.5'} bg-white/[0.06] rounded-full overflow-hidden`}>
   250	                <div
   251	                  className="h-full rounded-full transition-all duration-500"
   252	                  style={{ width: `${meta.clampedPercent}%`, background: fillColor }}
   253	                />
   254	              </div>
   255	              <div
   256	                className={`${micro ? 'mt-1 text-[10px]' : 'mt-1.5 text-[11px]'} font-bold tabular-nums`}
   257	                style={{ color: fillColor }}
   258	              >
   259	                {Math.round(consumedValue)}<span className="text-white/25 text-[9px] font-normal">/{Math.round(displayTarget)}g</span>
   260	              </div>

UI CANDIDATE: ./components/client/smart/SmartNutritionWidget.tsx

     1	'use client'
     2	
     3	import { useState } from 'react'
     4	import Link from 'next/link'
     5	import { Plus } from 'lucide-react'
     6	import QuickWaterModal from '../QuickWaterModal'
     7	import { useClientT } from '@/components/client/ClientI18nProvider'
     8	import { getNutritionProgressMeta, type NutritionProgressState } from '@/lib/nutrition/progress'
     9	import { NUTRITION_UI_COLORS } from '@/lib/nutrition/ui-colors'
    10	
    11	export type NutritionMacros = {
    12	  kcal: number
    13	  protein_g: number
    14	  carbs_g: number
    15	  fat_g: number
    16	  water_ml: number
    17	  caffeine_mg?: number
    18	}
    19	
    20	export type SmartNutritionWidgetProps = {
    21	  consumed: NutritionMacros
    22	  target: NutritionMacros
    23	  proteinStreakDays?: number
    24	}
    25	
    26	function formatOverflow(value: number, unit: 'g' | 'L'): string | null {
    27	  if (value <= 0) return null
    28	  return unit === 'L'
    29	    ? `+${value.toFixed(1)} ${unit} au-dessus`
    30	    : `+${Math.round(value)}${unit} au-dessus`
    31	}
    32	
    33	export default function SmartNutritionWidget({ consumed, target, proteinStreakDays }: SmartNutritionWidgetProps) {
    34	  const { t } = useClientT()
    35	  const MACROS = [
    36	    { key: 'protein_g' as const, label: t('smart.nutrition.protein'), color: NUTRITION_UI_COLORS.protein },
    37	    { key: 'carbs_g'   as const, label: t('smart.nutrition.carbs'),   color: NUTRITION_UI_COLORS.carbs },
    38	    { key: 'fat_g'     as const, label: t('smart.nutrition.fat'),     color: NUTRITION_UI_COLORS.fat },
    39	  ]
    40	  const [waterOpen, setWaterOpen] = useState(false)
    41	  const [waterDelta, setWaterDelta] = useState(0)
    42	  const effectiveWaterMl = consumed.water_ml + waterDelta
    43	
    44	  function getStateColor(state: NutritionProgressState, baseColor: string): string {
    45	    if (state === 'over')       return '#ef4444'
    46	    if (state === 'near_limit') return '#f59e0b'
    47	    return baseColor
    48	  }
    49	
    50	  const kcalMeta = getNutritionProgressMeta(consumed.kcal, target.kcal)
    51	  const waterMeta = getNutritionProgressMeta(effectiveWaterMl, target.water_ml)
    52	  const waterOverflowLabel = formatOverflow((effectiveWaterMl - target.water_ml) / 1000, 'L')
    53	  const kcalPct = Math.min(kcalMeta.ratio, 1)
    54	  const r = 80
    55	  const arcTotal = Math.PI * r
    56	  const arcOffset = arcTotal * (1 - kcalPct)
    57	  const kcalStroke = getStateColor(kcalMeta.state, NUTRITION_UI_COLORS.calories)
    58	
    59	  return (
    60	    <>
    61	      <QuickWaterModal
    62	        open={waterOpen}
    63	        onClose={() => setWaterOpen(false)}
    64	        onLogged={ml => setWaterDelta(d => d + ml)}
    65	        onDeleted={ml => setWaterDelta(d => d - ml)}
    66	      />
    67	      <Link
    68	        href="/client/nutrition"
    69	        className="block bg-[#111111] rounded-2xl p-5 active:scale-[0.99] transition-transform"
    70	      >
    71	        <div className="flex items-baseline justify-between mb-3">
    72	          <span className="font-barlow-condensed font-bold uppercase tracking-[0.18em] text-[11px] text-white/30">Nutrition</span>
    73	          <span className="text-[10px] font-semibold text-[#f2f2f2]">→</span>
    74	        </div>
    75	
    76	        {/* Arc demi-cercle */}
    77	        <div className="relative" style={{ height: 110 }}>
    78	          <svg viewBox="0 0 200 110" className="w-full h-full">
    79	            <path
    80	              d={`M ${100 - r} 100 A ${r} ${r} 0 0 1 ${100 + r} 100`}
    81	              fill="none"
    82	              stroke="rgba(255,255,255,0.08)"
    83	              strokeWidth={12}
    84	              strokeLinecap="round"
    85	            />
    86	            <path
    87	              d={`M ${100 - r} 100 A ${r} ${r} 0 0 1 ${100 + r} 100`}
    88	              fill="none"
    89	              stroke={kcalStroke}
    90	              strokeWidth={12}
    91	              strokeLinecap="round"
    92	              strokeDasharray={arcTotal}
    93	              strokeDashoffset={arcOffset}
    94	              style={{ transition: 'stroke-dashoffset 0.6s ease' }}
    95	            />
    96	          </svg>
    97	          <div className="absolute inset-0 flex flex-col items-center justify-end pb-1">
    98	            <div className="font-black leading-none text-white tabular-nums text-[28px]">
    99	              {Math.round(consumed.kcal)}
   100	            </div>
   101	            <div className="text-[9px] uppercase tracking-[0.12em] text-white/35 mt-1">Calories consommées</div>
   102	            <div className="text-[10px] text-white/50 tabular-nums">/ {target.kcal} kcal</div>
   103	          </div>
   104	        </div>
   105	
   106	        {/* Barres macros */}
   107	        <div className="flex flex-col gap-2 mt-3">
   108	          {MACROS.map(m => {
   109	            const c = (consumed[m.key] as number) ?? 0
   110	            const tg = (target[m.key] as number) ?? 0
   111	            const meta = getNutritionProgressMeta(c, tg)
   112	            const fillColor = getStateColor(meta.state, m.color)
   113	            const overflowLabel = formatOverflow(c - tg, 'g')
   114	            return (
   115	              <div key={m.key}>
   116	                <div className="flex justify-between text-[10px] mb-1">
   117	                  <span className="text-white/50 uppercase tracking-[0.1em] font-bold">{m.label}</span>
   118	                  <span className="font-bold tabular-nums" style={{ color: fillColor }}>
   119	                    {Math.round(c)}/{tg}g
   120	                  </span>
   121	                </div>
   122	                <div className="h-1.5 bg-white/[0.06] rounded-full overflow-hidden">
   123	                  <div
   124	                    className="h-full rounded-full"
   125	                    style={{
   126	                      width: `${meta.clampedPercent}%`,
   127	                      background: fillColor,
   128	                      transition: 'width 0.4s ease',
   129	                    }}
   130	                  />
   131	                </div>
   132	                <div className="mt-1 min-h-[14px] text-[9px] font-bold tabular-nums" style={{ color: meta.state === 'over' ? '#ef4444' : 'rgba(255,255,255,0.28)' }}>
   133	                  {overflowLabel ?? '\u00A0'}
   134	                </div>
   135	              </div>
   136	            )
   137	          })}
   138	        </div>
   139	
   140	        {/* Eau */}
   141	        <div className="flex items-center gap-3 mt-4 pt-3">
   142	          <div className="flex-1">
   143	            <div className="flex justify-between text-[10px] mb-1">
   144	              <span className="text-white/50 uppercase tracking-[0.1em] font-bold">Hydratation</span>
   145	              <span className="text-white font-bold tabular-nums">
   146	                {(effectiveWaterMl / 1000).toFixed(1)} / {(target.water_ml / 1000).toFixed(1)} L
   147	              </span>
   148	            </div>
   149	            <div className="h-1.5 bg-white/[0.06] rounded-full overflow-hidden">
   150	              <div
   151	                className="h-full rounded-full"
   152	                style={{
   153	                  width: `${waterMeta.clampedPercent}%`,
   154	                  background: getStateColor(waterMeta.state, NUTRITION_UI_COLORS.water),
   155	                  transition: 'width 0.4s ease',
   156	                }}
   157	              />
   158	            </div>
   159	            <div className="mt-1 min-h-[14px] text-[9px] font-bold tabular-nums" style={{ color: waterMeta.state === 'over' ? '#ef4444' : 'rgba(255,255,255,0.28)' }}>
   160	              {waterOverflowLabel ?? '\u00A0'}
   161	            </div>
   162	          </div>
   163	          <button
   164	            onClick={e => { e.preventDefault(); setWaterOpen(true) }}
   165	            className="w-9 h-9 rounded-xl bg-[#f2f2f2] flex items-center justify-center text-[#080808] active:scale-95 transition-transform shrink-0"
   166	          >
   167	            <Plus size={16} strokeWidth={2.5} />
   168	          </button>
   169	        </div>
   170	
   171	        {consumed.caffeine_mg != null && consumed.caffeine_mg > 0 && (
   172	          <div className="mt-2 flex items-center justify-between rounded-xl bg-white/[0.03] px-3 py-2 text-[10px]">
   173	            <span className="text-white/40 uppercase tracking-[0.1em] font-bold">Caféine / théine</span>
   174	            <span className="text-white font-bold tabular-nums">{Math.round(consumed.caffeine_mg)} mg</span>
   175	          </div>
   176	        )}
   177	
   178	        {/* Régularité protéines */}
   179	        {proteinStreakDays !== undefined && target.protein_g > 0 && (
   180	          <div className="mt-3 pt-3">
   181	            <div className="flex justify-between text-[10px] mb-1.5">
   182	              <span className="text-white/40 uppercase tracking-[0.1em] font-bold">{t('nutrition.consistency')}</span>
   183	              <span className="text-white/60 tabular-nums font-bold">{proteinStreakDays}/7j</span>
   184	            </div>
   185	            <div className="h-1 bg-white/[0.06] rounded-full overflow-hidden">
   186	              <div
   187	                className="h-full rounded-full bg-[#f2f2f2]"
   188	                style={{ width: `${(proteinStreakDays / 7) * 100}%`, transition: 'width 0.6s ease' }}
   189	              />
   190	            </div>
   191	          </div>
   192	        )}
   193	      </Link>
   194	    </>
   195	  )
   196	}

UI CANDIDATE: ./components/client/smart/TodayPrepsSection.tsx
------------------------------------------------------------
     1	"use client"
     2	
     3	import { useState } from "react"
     4	import { Coffee, Sun, Moon, Apple, Pencil, Sparkles } from "lucide-react"
     5	import { NUTRITION_UI_COLORS } from "@/lib/nutrition/ui-colors"
     6	import type { SmartNutritionPrep } from "@/components/client/smart/SmartNutritionPrepList"
     7	import type { SmartPrepSlot } from "@/lib/nutrition/simulation-state"
     8	
     9	const SLOT_ICON: Record<SmartPrepSlot, React.ElementType> = {
    10	  breakfast: Coffee,
    11	  lunch: Sun,
    12	  dinner: Moon,
    13	  snack: Apple,
    14	}
    15	
    16	const SLOT_LABEL: Record<SmartPrepSlot, string> = {
    17	  breakfast: "P.Déj",
    18	  lunch: "Déjeuner",
    19	  dinner: "Dîner",
    20	  snack: "Collation",
    21	}
    22	
    23	function MacroStrip({ p, g, f }: { p: number; g: number; f: number }) {
    24	  const pK = p * 4, gK = g * 4, fK = f * 9
    25	  const total = pK + gK + fK || 1
    26	  return (
    27	    <div className="flex h-[3px] rounded-full overflow-hidden gap-[2px]">
    28	      <div className="rounded-full" style={{ width: `${(pK / total) * 100}%`, backgroundColor: NUTRITION_UI_COLORS.protein }} />
    29	      <div className="rounded-full" style={{ width: `${(gK / total) * 100}%`, backgroundColor: NUTRITION_UI_COLORS.carbs }} />
    30	      <div className="rounded-full" style={{ width: `${(fK / total) * 100}%`, backgroundColor: NUTRITION_UI_COLORS.fat }} />
    31	    </div>
    32	  )
    33	}
    34	
    35	function PrepRow({
    36	  prep,
    37	  onEdit,
    38	  onValidated,
    39	}: {
    40	  prep: SmartNutritionPrep
    41	  onEdit: (prep: SmartNutritionPrep) => void
    42	  onValidated: () => void
    43	}) {
    44	  const [busy, setBusy] = useState(false)
    45	  const [error, setError] = useState<string | null>(null)
    46	  const Icon = SLOT_ICON[prep.meal_slot] ?? Apple
    47	
    48	  async function handleValidate() {
    49	    setBusy(true)
    50	    setError(null)
    51	    const res = await fetch(`/api/client/nutrition/preps/${prep.id}/log`, { method: "POST" })
    52	    if (res.ok) {
    53	      onValidated()
    54	    } else {
    55	      setError("Erreur — réessaie")
    56	      setBusy(false)
    57	    }
    58	  }
    59	
    60	  return (
    61	    <div className="flex flex-col gap-1.5 px-4 py-3 rounded-xl bg-white/[0.03] border border-white/[0.05]">
    62	      <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
    63	        {/* Slot icon */}
    64	        <div className="w-8 h-8 rounded-lg flex items-center justify-center bg-[#818cf8]/10 shrink-0">
    65	          <Icon size={14} className="text-[#818cf8]" />
    66	        </div>
    67	
    68	        {/* Title + slot */}
    69	        <div className="flex-1 min-w-0">
    70	          <p className="text-[13px] font-semibold text-white truncate leading-tight">
    71	            {prep.title || "Repas composé"}
    72	          </p>
    73	          <p className="text-[10px] text-white/35 uppercase tracking-[0.10em]">
    74	            {SLOT_LABEL[prep.meal_slot]} · {Math.round(prep.total_calories)} kcal
    75	          </p>
    76	        </div>
    77	
    78	        {/* Macro pills */}
    79	        <div className="flex items-center gap-1.5 shrink-0">
    80	          <span className="text-[10px] font-semibold" style={{ color: NUTRITION_UI_COLORS.protein }}>
    81	            P{Math.round(prep.total_protein_g)}
    82	          </span>
    83	          <span className="text-[10px] font-semibold" style={{ color: NUTRITION_UI_COLORS.carbs }}>
    84	            G{Math.round(prep.total_carbs_g)}
    85	          </span>
    86	          <span className="text-[10px] font-semibold" style={{ color: NUTRITION_UI_COLORS.fat }}>
    87	            L{Math.round(prep.total_fat_g)}
    88	          </span>
    89	        </div>
    90	
    91	        {/* Actions */}
    92	        <div className="flex items-center gap-1.5 shrink-0">
    93	          <button
    94	            onClick={() => onEdit(prep)}
    95	            className="w-7 h-7 flex items-center justify-center rounded-lg bg-white/[0.05] text-white/35 active:bg-white/[0.08] transition-colors"
    96	          >
    97	            <Pencil size={11} />
    98	          </button>
    99	          <button
   100	            onClick={handleValidate}
   101	            disabled={busy}
   102	            className="h-7 px-2.5 rounded-lg bg-[#f2f2f2] text-[#080808] text-[10px] font-barlow-condensed font-bold uppercase tracking-wide active:scale-[0.97] transition-all disabled:opacity-50"
   103	          >
   104	            {busy ? "…" : "Valider"}
   105	          </button>
   106	        </div>
   107	      </div>
   108	
   109	      <MacroStrip
   110	        p={prep.total_protein_g}
   111	        g={prep.total_carbs_g}
   112	        f={prep.total_fat_g}
   113	      />
   114	
   115	      {error && (
   116	        <p className="text-[10px] text-red-400">{error}</p>
   117	      )}
   118	    </div>
   119	  )
   120	}
   121	
   122	interface Props {
   123	  preps: SmartNutritionPrep[]
   124	  date: string
   125	  onEdit: (prep: SmartNutritionPrep) => void
   126	  onValidated: () => void
   127	}
   128	
   129	export default function TodayPrepsSection({ preps, date, onEdit, onValidated }: Props) {
   130	  const todayPreps = preps.filter(
   131	    p => p.status === "planned" && p.physiological_date === date
   132	  )
   133	
   134	  if (todayPreps.length === 0) return null
   135	
   136	  return (
   137	    <div className="flex flex-col gap-2">
   138	      {/* Section header */}
   139	      <div className="flex items-center gap-2 px-0.5">
   140	        <Sparkles size={12} className="text-[#818cf8]" />
   141	        <p className="text-[10px] font-barlow-condensed font-bold uppercase tracking-[0.16em] text-[#818cf8]">
   142	          Planifié aujourd&apos;hui
   143	        </p>
   144	        <span className="ml-auto text-[10px] text-white/25">{todayPreps.length} prep{todayPreps.length > 1 ? "s" : ""}</span>
   145	      </div>
   146	
   147	      {/* Prep rows */}
   148	      {todayPreps.map(prep => (
   149	        <PrepRow
   150	          key={prep.id}
   151	          prep={prep}
   152	          onEdit={onEdit}
   153	          onValidated={onValidated}
   154	        />
   155	      ))}
   156	    </div>
   157	  )
   158	}

    67	// Extends VoiceItem with per-gram nutritional bases for correct quantity recalculation
    68	type DisplayItem = VoiceItem & {
    69	  _kcal_per_g: number;
    70	  _protein_per_g: number;
    71	  _carbs_per_g: number;
    72	  _fat_per_g: number;
    73	  _fiber_per_g: number;
    74	};
    75	
    76	function withBases(item: VoiceItem): DisplayItem {
    77	  const q = item.quantity_g > 0 ? item.quantity_g : 1;
    78	  const guessedCategory =
    79	    item.category_l1 && item.category_l2
    80	      ? { category_l1: item.category_l1, category_l2: item.category_l2 }
    81	      : guessVoiceFoodCategory(item.name);
    82	  return {
    83	    ...item,
    84	    _kcal_per_g: item.kcal / q,
    85	    _protein_per_g: item.protein_g / q,
    86	    _carbs_per_g: item.carbs_g / q,
    87	    _fat_per_g: item.fat_g / q,
    88	    _fiber_per_g: item.fiber_g / q,
    89	    category_l1: item.category_l1 ?? guessedCategory?.category_l1,
    90	    category_l2: item.category_l2 ?? guessedCategory?.category_l2,
    91	  };
    92	}

    97	
    98	function calculateCyclePhase(dayOfCycle: number, cycleLength: number): CyclePhase {
    99	  if (dayOfCycle >= 1 && dayOfCycle <= 5) return 'menstrual'
   100	  if (dayOfCycle >= 6 && dayOfCycle <= Math.floor(cycleLength / 2) - 1) return 'follicular'
   101	  if (dayOfCycle >= Math.floor(cycleLength / 2) && dayOfCycle <= Math.floor(cycleLength / 2) + 1) return 'ovulatory'
   102	  return 'luteal'
   103	}

   111	function NumInput({ value, onChange, placeholder, step, min, max, className = '' }: {
   112	  value: string; onChange: (v: string) => void; placeholder?: string
   113	  step?: string; min?: string; max?: string; className?: string
   114	}) {
   115	  return (
   116	    <input
   117	      type="number" value={value} step={step} min={min} max={max}
   118	      onChange={e => onChange(e.target.value)} placeholder={placeholder}
   119	      className={`w-full h-8 rounded-lg bg-white/[0.04] border-[0.3px] border-white/[0.06] px-3 text-[12px] font-semibold text-white placeholder:text-white/20 outline-none focus:border-white/[0.12] transition-colors ${className}`}
   120	    />
   121	  )
   122	}

   124	function DSSelect<T extends string>({ value, onChange, options }: {
   125	  value: T; onChange: (v: T) => void; options: { value: T; label: string }[]
   126	}) {
   127	  return (
   128	    <select value={value} onChange={e => onChange(e.target.value as T)}
   129	      className="w-full h-8 rounded-lg bg-white/[0.04] border-[0.3px] border-white/[0.06] px-3 text-[12px] font-semibold text-white outline-none focus:border-white/[0.12] transition-colors appearance-none cursor-pointer"
   130	    >
   131	      {options.map(o => <option key={o.value} value={o.value} className="bg-[#181818]">{o.label}</option>)}
   132	    </select>
   133	  )
   134	}

   136	function SectionHeader({ children, icon: Icon }: { children: React.ReactNode; icon?: React.ElementType }) {
   137	  return (
   138	    <div className="flex items-center gap-2 mb-3">
   139	      {Icon && <Icon size={11} className="text-white/30" strokeWidth={1.75} />}
   140	      <p className="text-[9px] font-bold uppercase tracking-[0.18em] text-white/30">{children}</p>
   141	    </div>
   142	  )
   143	}

   145	function ModuleBlock({
   146	  title, icon: Icon, badge, defaultOpen = false, accent, children,
   147	}: {
   148	  title: string; icon?: React.ElementType; badge?: string; defaultOpen?: boolean
   149	  accent?: string; children: React.ReactNode
   150	}) {
   151	  const [open, setOpen] = useState(defaultOpen)
   152	  return (
   153	    <div className="bg-white/[0.02] border-[0.3px] border-white/[0.06] rounded-2xl overflow-hidden">
   154	      <button
   155	        onClick={() => setOpen(o => !o)}
   156	        className="w-full flex items-center justify-between px-4 py-3 hover:bg-white/[0.02] transition-colors"
   157	      >
   158	        <div className="flex items-center gap-2.5">
   159	          {Icon && <Icon size={13} className={accent ?? 'text-white/30'} strokeWidth={1.75} />}
   160	          <span className="text-[11px] font-semibold text-white/70">{title}</span>
   161	          {badge && (
   162	            <span className="px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full text-[9px] font-bold bg-white/[0.06] text-white/30">
   163	              {badge}
   164	            </span>
   165	          )}
   166	        </div>
   167	        {open ? <ChevronUp size={13} className="text-white/30" /> : <ChevronDown size={13} className="text-white/30" />}
   168	      </button>
   169	      {open && <div className="px-4 pb-4 border-t-[0.3px] border-white/[0.04] pt-3">{children}</div>}
   170	    </div>
   171	  )
   172	}

    80	function parseNumber(value: string) {
    81	  if (value.trim() === '') return null;
    82	  const parsed = Number(value);
    83	  return Number.isFinite(parsed) ? parsed : null;
    84	}
    85	
    86	function toStringValue(value: number | null | undefined) {
    87	  return value == null ? '' : String(value);
    88	}
    89	
    90	function useCopyState() {
    91	  const [copied, setCopied] = useState(false);
    92	
    93	  async function copy(text: string) {
    94	    await navigator.clipboard.writeText(text);
    95	    setCopied(true);
    96	    window.setTimeout(() => setCopied(false), 1500);
    97	  }
    98	
    99	  return { copied, copy };
   100	}

   104	}

   137	function SelectField<T extends string>({
   138	  value,
   139	  onChange,
   140	  options,
   141	}: {
   142	  value: T;
   143	  onChange: (value: T) => void;
   144	  options: Array<{ value: T; label: string }>;
   145	}) {
   146	  return (
   147	    <select
   148	      value={value}
   149	      onChange={(e) => onChange(e.target.value as T)}
   150	      className="h-9 w-full cursor-pointer appearance-none rounded-lg border-[0.3px] border-white/[0.06] bg-white/[0.04] px-3 text-[12px] font-semibold text-white outline-none transition-colors focus:border-white/[0.12]"
   151	    >
   152	      {options.map((option) => (
   153	        <option key={option.value} value={option.value} className="bg-[#181818]">
   154	          {option.label}
   155	        </option>
   156	      ))}
   157	    </select>
   158	  );
   159	}

   161	function MetricCard({
   162	  label,
   163	  value,
   164	  suffix,
   165	  tone = 'white',
   166	}: {
   167	  label: string;
   168	  value: string | number;
   169	  suffix?: string;
   170	  tone?: 'white' | 'green' | 'amber';
   171	}) {
   172	  const toneCls =
   173	    tone === 'green' ? 'text-[#1f8a65]' : tone === 'amber' ? 'text-amber-400' : 'text-white';
   174	
   175	  return (
   176	    <div className="rounded-2xl border border-white/[0.06] bg-white/[0.03] p-3">
   177	      <p className="text-[10px] uppercase tracking-[0.16em] text-white/35">{label}</p>
   178	      <div className="mt-2 flex items-end gap-1">
   179	        <span className={`text-[22px] font-semibold leading-none ${toneCls}`}>{value}</span>
   180	        {suffix && <span className="pb-0.5 text-[10px] text-white/35">{suffix}</span>}
   181	      </div>
   182	    </div>
   183	  );
   184	}

   186	function Disclosure({
   187	  title,
   188	  children,
   189	  defaultOpen = false,
   190	  icon: Icon,
   191	}: {
   192	  title: string;
   193	  children: React.ReactNode;
   194	  defaultOpen?: boolean;
   195	  icon?: React.ElementType;
   196	}) {
   197	  const [open, setOpen] = useState(defaultOpen);

   199	  return (
   200	    <div className="rounded-2xl border border-white/[0.06] bg-white/[0.02]">
   201	      <button
   202	        type="button"
   203	        onClick={() => setOpen((value) => !value)}
   204	        className="flex w-full items-center justify-between px-4 py-3 text-left"
   205	      >
   206	        <span className="flex items-center gap-2 text-[11px] font-semibold text-white/70">
   207	          {Icon && <Icon size={13} className="text-white/35" />}
   208	          {title}
   209	        </span>
   210	        {open ? (
   211	          <ChevronUp size={13} className="text-white/30" />
   212	        ) : (
   213	          <ChevronDown size={13} className="text-white/30" />
   214	        )}
   215	      </button>
   216	      {open && <div className="border-t border-white/[0.05] px-4 py-3">{children}</div>}
   217	    </div>
   218	  );
   219	}
   220	
   221	function parsePlanFromSearch(searchParams: ReturnType<typeof useSearchParams>) {
   222	  const gender = searchParams.get('gender');
   223	  const goal = searchParams.get('goal');
   224	  const age = parseNumber(searchParams.get('age') ?? '');
   225	  const height = parseNumber(searchParams.get('height') ?? '');
   226	  const weight = parseNumber(searchParams.get('weight') ?? '');
   227	
   228	  if (gender !== 'male' && gender !== 'female') return null;
   229	  if (goal !== 'deficit' && goal !== 'maintenance' && goal !== 'surplus') return null;
   230	  if (age == null || height == null || weight == null) return null;
   231	
   232	  const occupation = parseNumber(searchParams.get('occupation') ?? '');
   233	  const phase = searchParams.get('cycle');
   234	
   235	  return {
   236	    gender,
   237	    goal,
   238	    age,
   239	    height,
   240	    weight,
   241	    steps: parseNumber(searchParams.get('steps') ?? ''),
   242	    occupation,
   243	    workouts: parseNumber(searchParams.get('workouts') ?? ''),
   244	    duration: parseNumber(searchParams.get('duration') ?? ''),
   245	    cardio: parseNumber(searchParams.get('cardio') ?? ''),
   246	    cardioDuration: parseNumber(searchParams.get('cardioDuration') ?? ''),
   247	    bodyFat: parseNumber(searchParams.get('bodyFat') ?? ''),
   248	    bmr: parseNumber(searchParams.get('bmr') ?? ''),
   249	    sleep: parseNumber(searchParams.get('sleep') ?? ''),
   250	    stress: parseNumber(searchParams.get('stress') ?? ''),
   251	    caffeine: parseNumber(searchParams.get('caffeine') ?? ''),
   252	    alcohol: parseNumber(searchParams.get('alcohol') ?? ''),
   253	    phase: phase === 'follicular' || phase === 'luteal' ? phase : 'unknown',
   254	  };
   255	}
   256

   258	  const router = useRouter();
   259	  const searchParams = useSearchParams();
   260	  const hydratedFromQuery = useRef(false);

     1	"use client"

    10	
    11	const PHASES: CyclePhase[] = ["follicular", "ovulatory", "luteal", "menstrual"]
    12	
    13	const PHASE_LABELS: Record<CyclePhase, string> = {
    14	  follicular: "Phase folliculaire",
    15	  ovulatory:  "Phase ovulatoire",
    16	  luteal:     "Phase lutéale",
    17	  menstrual:  "Menstruation",
    18	}
    19	
    20	const PHASE_DAYS: Record<CyclePhase, string> = {
    21	  follicular: "J6–J13",
    22	  ovulatory:  "J14–J16",
    23	  luteal:     "J17–J28",
    24	  menstrual:  "J1–J5",
    25	}
    26	
    27	const PHASE_COLORS: Record<CyclePhase, { bg: string; border: string; dot: string; tag: string }> = {
    28	  follicular: { bg: "rgba(34,197,94,0.06)",   border: "rgba(34,197,94,0.18)",   dot: "#22c55e", tag: "bg-green-500/10 text-green-400" },
    29	  ovulatory:  { bg: "rgba(251,191,36,0.06)",  border: "rgba(251,191,36,0.18)",  dot: "#fbbf24", tag: "bg-amber-500/10 text-amber-400" },
    30	  luteal:     { bg: "rgba(168,85,247,0.06)",  border: "rgba(168,85,247,0.18)",  dot: "#a855f7", tag: "bg-purple-500/10 text-purple-400" },
    31	  menstrual:  { bg: "rgba(239,68,68,0.06)",   border: "rgba(239,68,68,0.18)",   dot: "#ef4444", tag: "bg-red-500/10 text-red-400"    },
    32	}
    33	
    34	function ResultRow({
    35	  label,
    36	  base,
    37	  delta,
    38	  unit,
    39	}: {
    40	  label: string
    41	  base: number
    42	  delta: number
    43	  unit: string
    44	}) {
    45	  if (delta === 0) return null
    46	  const result = Math.round(base + delta)
    47	  return (
    48	    <div className="flex items-center justify-between gap-1">
    49	      <span className="text-[9px] text-white/35 uppercase tracking-[0.12em] shrink-0">{label}</span>
    50	      <span className="text-[9px] font-mono text-right">
    51	        <span className="text-white/30">{Math.round(base)}</span>
    52	        <span className="text-white/45"> {delta > 0 ? "+" : ""}{delta}{unit}</span>
    53	        <span className="text-white/75 font-semibold"> = {result}{unit}</span>
    54	      </span>
    55	    </div>
    56	  )
    57	}
    58	
    59	function DeltaOnly({ value, unit, label }: { value: number; unit: string; label: string }) {
    60	  if (value === 0) return null
    61	  return (
    62	    <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
    63	      <span className="text-[9px] text-white/35 uppercase tracking-[0.12em]">{label}</span>
    64	      <span className={`text-[10px] font-semibold ${value > 0 ? "text-white/70" : "text-white/50"}`}>
    65	        {value > 0 ? "+" : ""}{value}{unit}
    66	      </span>
    67	    </div>
    68	  )
    69	}

    71	interface Props {
    72	  baseMacros?: NutritionMacros | null
    73	  currentCycleDay?: number | null
    74	}
    75	
    76	export default function CycleSyncPhaseGrid({ baseMacros, currentCycleDay }: Props) {
    77	  const currentPhase = currentCycleDay != null ? detectCurrentPhase(currentCycleDay) : null
    78	
    79	  return (
    80	    <div className="space-y-3">
    81	      <p className="text-[10px] text-white/40 leading-relaxed">
    82	        Ajustements macros automatiques selon la phase du cycle menstruel (Davidsen 2007, Oosthuyse &amp; Bosch 2010).
    83	        Les valeurs ci-dessous sont additives — elles s&apos;appliquent sur la base calculée.
    84	      </p>
    85	
    86	      <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-2">
    87	        {PHASES.map((phase) => {
    88	          const adj = getCycleSyncAdjustment(phase)
    89	          const colors = PHASE_COLORS[phase]
    90	          const isCurrent = phase === currentPhase
    91	          const isDimmed = currentPhase !== null && !isCurrent
    92	          const hasDeltas = adj.caloriesDelta !== 0 || adj.proteinDelta !== 0 || adj.carbsDelta !== 0 || adj.fatDelta !== 0
    93	
    94	          return (
    95	            <div
    96	              key={phase}
    97	              className={`rounded-xl p-3 space-y-2.5 transition-opacity ${isDimmed ? "opacity-35" : "opacity-100"}`}
    98	              style={{
    99	                background: isDimmed ? "rgba(255,255,255,0.02)" : colors.bg,
   100	                border: `0.3px solid ${isCurrent ? colors.dot : isDimmed ? "rgba(255,255,255,0.06)" : colors.border}`,
   101	                boxShadow: isCurrent ? `0 0 0 1px ${colors.dot}33` : undefined,
   102	              }}
   103	            >
   104	              {/* Header */}
   105	              <div className="flex items-start justify-between gap-1">
   106	                <div className="flex items-center gap-1.5">
   107	                  <div
   108	                    className="w-4 h-4 rounded-full flex items-center justify-center shrink-0"
   109	                    style={{ background: colors.border }}
   110	                  >
   111	                    <Moon size={8} style={{ color: colors.dot }} />
   112	                  </div>
   113	                  <div>
   114	                    <p className="text-[10px] font-semibold text-white/80 leading-tight">
   115	                      {PHASE_LABELS[phase]}
   116	                    </p>
   117	                    <p className="text-[8px] text-white/30">{PHASE_DAYS[phase]}</p>
   118	                  </div>
   119	                </div>
   120	                {isCurrent && (
   121	                  <span className={`text-[7px] font-bold uppercase tracking-wide px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded-full ${colors.tag}`}>
   122	                    Actuelle
   123	                  </span>
   124	                )}
   125	              </div>
   126	
   127	              {/* Macros: base + delta = result, or delta-only if no base */}
   128	              <div className="space-y-1">
   129	                {!hasDeltas ? (
   130	                  <p className="text-[9px] text-white/30 italic">Aucun ajustement</p>
   131	                ) : baseMacros ? (
   132	                  <>
   133	                    <ResultRow label="Calories"  base={baseMacros.kcal}      delta={adj.caloriesDelta}    unit=" kcal" />
   134	                    <ResultRow label="Protéines" base={baseMacros.protein_g} delta={adj.proteinDelta}     unit="g" />
   135	                    <ResultRow label="Glucides"  base={baseMacros.carbs_g}   delta={adj.carbsDelta}       unit="g" />
   136	                    <ResultRow label="Lipides"   base={baseMacros.fat_g}     delta={adj.fatDelta}         unit="g" />
   137	                    <DeltaOnly value={adj.hydrationDeltaMl} unit=" ml" label="Hydratation" />
   138	                  </>
   139	                ) : (
   140	                  <>
   141	                    <DeltaOnly value={adj.caloriesDelta}    unit=" kcal" label="Calories" />
   142	                    <DeltaOnly value={adj.proteinDelta}     unit="g"     label="Protéines" />
   143	                    <DeltaOnly value={adj.carbsDelta}       unit="g"     label="Glucides" />
   144	                    <DeltaOnly value={adj.fatDelta}         unit="g"     label="Lipides" />
   145	                    <DeltaOnly value={adj.hydrationDeltaMl} unit=" ml"  label="Hydratation" />
   146	                  </>
   147	                )}
   148	              </div>
   149	
   150	              {/* Optimal deficit badge */}
   151	              {adj.optimalForDeficit && (
   152	                <div className="flex items-center gap-1">
   153	                  <div className="w-1.5 h-1.5 rounded-full bg-green-500/70" />
   154	                  <p className="text-[8px] text-white/35">Phase optimale déficit</p>
   155	                </div>
   156	              )}
   157	
   158	              {/* First note */}
   159	              <p className="text-[9px] text-white/30 leading-relaxed line-clamp-2">
   160	                {adj.notes[0]}
   161	              </p>
   162	            </div>
   163	          )
   164	        })}
   165	      </div>
   166	    </div>
   167	  )
   168	}

    98	export default function ParameterAdjustmentPanel({
    99	  isOpen,
   100	  onClose,
   101	  clientData,
   102	  onUpdateTraining,
   103	  onUpdateLifestyle,
   104	  onUpdateBiometrics,
   105	  trainingConfig,
   106	  lifestyleConfig,
   107	  biometricsConfig,
   108	}: Props) {
   109	  const [showBMRCalculator, setShowBMRCalculator] = useState(false);
   110	  const [bmrFormula, setBMRFormula] = useState<
   111	    "katch-mcardle" | "mifflin-st-jeor"
   112	  >("katch-mcardle");
   113	  const [bmrResult, setBMRResult] = useState<number | null>(null);
   114	  const [saved, setSaved] = useState(false);
   115	  const [heightInput, setHeightInput] = useState<string>(
   116	    biometricsConfig.height_cm?.toString() ?? ""
   117	  );
   118	  const saveTimeoutRef = useRef<ReturnType<typeof setTimeout> | null>(null);
   119	
   120	  // Auto-save debounce 500ms
   121	  const triggerAutoSave = () => {
   122	    setSaved(false);
   123	    if (saveTimeoutRef.current) clearTimeout(saveTimeoutRef.current);
   124	    saveTimeoutRef.current = setTimeout(() => {
   125	      setSaved(true);
   126	      setTimeout(() => setSaved(false), 2000);
   127	    }, 500);
   128	  };
   129	
   130	  // Cleanup timeout on unmount
   131	  useEffect(() => {
   132	    return () => {
   133	      if (saveTimeoutRef.current) clearTimeout(saveTimeoutRef.current);
   134	    };
   135	  }, []);
   136	
   137	  // Update height input when biometricsConfig changes
   138	  useEffect(() => {
   139	    setHeightInput(biometricsConfig.height_cm?.toString() ?? "");
   140	  }, [biometricsConfig.height_cm]);
   141	
   142	  const handleCalculateBMR = () => {
   143	    let result: number | null = null;
   144	
   145	    if (
   146	      bmrFormula === "katch-mcardle" &&
   147	      biometricsConfig.weight_kg &&
   148	      biometricsConfig.body_fat_pct !== null
   149	    ) {
   150	      result = calculateBMRKatchMcArdle(
   151	        biometricsConfig.weight_kg,
   152	        biometricsConfig.body_fat_pct,
   153	      );
   154	    } else if (
   155	      bmrFormula === "mifflin-st-jeor" &&
   156	      biometricsConfig.weight_kg &&
   157	      biometricsConfig.height_cm &&
   158	      clientData?.age
   159	    ) {
   160	      result = calculateBMRMifflin(
   161	        biometricsConfig.weight_kg,
   162	        biometricsConfig.height_cm,
   163	        clientData.age,
   164	        clientData.gender === "female"
   165	          ? "F"
   166	          : clientData.gender === "male"
   167	            ? "M"
   168	            : null,
   169	      );
   170	    }
   171	
   172	    if (result) {
   173	      setBMRResult(result);
   174	    }
   175	  };
   176	
   177	  const handleApplyBMR = () => {
   178	    if (bmrResult) {
   179	      onUpdateBiometrics("bmr_kcal_measured", bmrResult.toString());
   180	      onUpdateBiometrics("bmr_source", "calculated");
   181	      setShowBMRCalculator(false);
   182	      setBMRResult(null);
   183	    }
   184	  };
   185	
   186	  return (
   187	    <AnimatePresence>
   188	      {isOpen && (
   189	        <>
   190	          {/* Backdrop */}
   191	          <motion.div
   192	            initial={{ opacity: 0 }}
   193	            animate={{ opacity: 1 }}
   194	            exit={{ opacity: 0 }}
   195	            onClick={onClose}
   196	            className="fixed inset-0 bg-black/50 z-40"
   197	          />
   198	
   199	          {/* Panel */}
   200	          <motion.div
   201	            initial={{ x: 400, opacity: 0 }}
   202	            animate={{ x: 0, opacity: 1 }}
   203	            exit={{ x: 400, opacity: 0 }}
   204	            transition={{ type: "spring", stiffness: 300, damping: 30 }}
   205	            className="fixed right-0 top-0 bottom-0 w-[400px] bg-[#181818] z-50 flex flex-col border-l border-white/[0.06]"
   206	          >
   207	            {/* Header */}
   208	            <div className="flex items-center justify-between p-4 border-b border-white/[0.06]">
   209	              <h3 className="text-[13px] font-semibold text-white">
   210	                Ajuster les paramètres
   211	              </h3>
   212	              <button
   213	                onClick={onClose}
   214	                className="text-white/40 hover:text-white/70 transition-colors"
   215	              >
   216	                <X size={16} />
   217	              </button>
   218	            </div>
   219	
   220	            {/* Scrollable content */}
   221	            <div className="flex-1 overflow-y-auto scrollbar-hide p-4 space-y-0">
   222	              {/* Height quick-add if missing */}
   223	              {!biometricsConfig.height_cm && (
   224	                <div className="bg-amber-500/15 border-[0.3px] border-amber-500/30 rounded-lg p-3 mb-4">
   225	                  <div className="flex items-start gap-2">
   226	                    <AlertTriangle size={14} className="text-amber-400 mt-0.5 shrink-0" />
   227	                    <div className="flex-1 min-w-0">
   228	                      <p className="text-[11px] font-semibold text-amber-300 mb-2">
   229	                        Taille manquante
   230	                      </p>
   231	                      <div className="flex items-center gap-1.5">
   232	                        <input
   233	                          type="number"
   234	                          value={heightInput}
   235	                          onChange={(e) => setHeightInput(e.target.value)}
   236	                          placeholder="170"
   237	                          className="flex-1 rounded-lg bg-white/[0.04] border-[0.3px] border-amber-500/40 px-2 py-1 text-[10px] text-white outline-none placeholder:text-white/20 focus:border-amber-500/60"
   238	                        />

    93	const ACTIVITY_STEPS: Record<ActivityLevel, number> = {
    94	  sedentary: 2000,
    95	  light: 4000,
    96	  moderate: 7000,
    97	  active: 11000,
    98	  veryActive: 15000,
    99	};
   100	
   101	const HYDRATION_ACTIVITY_MAP: Record<
   102	  ActivityLevel,
   103	  "sedentary" | "light" | "moderate" | "intense" | "athlete"
   104	> = {
   105	  sedentary: "sedentary",
   106	  light: "light",
   107	  moderate: "moderate",
   108	  active: "intense",
   109	  veryActive: "athlete",
