   111	
   112	function resolveStudioPhase(client: Pick<NutritionClientData, "transformation_phase" | "training_goal">) {
   113	  return resolveTransformationPhase({
   114	    transformationPhase: client.transformation_phase,
   115	    trainingGoal: client.training_goal,
   116	  });
   117	}
   118	
   119	function getActivityLevel(clientData: NutritionClientData): ActivityLevel {
   120	  const freq = clientData.weekly_frequency ?? 0;
   121	  if (freq === 0) return "sedentary";
   122	  if (freq <= 2) return "light";
   123	  if (freq <= 3) return "moderate";
   124	  if (freq <= 5) return "active";
   125	  return "veryActive";
   126	}

   135	  calories_source: 'logs' | 'protocol'
   136	  avg_intake_kcal: number
   137	  weight_delta_kg: number
   138	  protocol_updated: boolean
   139	  confidence?: 'high' | 'medium' | 'low'
   140	  confidence_score?: number
   141	  confidence_reasons?: string[]
   142	}

   173	export function useNutritionStudio(
   174	  clientId: string,
   175	  existingProtocol?: NutritionProtocol,
   176	) {
   177	  const debounceRef = useRef<ReturnType<typeof setTimeout> | null>(null);
   178	
   179	  const [clientData, setClientData] = useState<NutritionClientData | null>(
   180	    null,
   181	  );
   182	  const [clientLoading, setClientLoading] = useState(true);
   183	  const [protocolName, setProtocolName] = useState(
   184	    existingProtocol?.name ?? "Nouveau protocole",
   185	  );
   186	  const [goal, setGoal] = useState<MacroGoal>("surplus");
   187	  const [transformationPhase, setTransformationPhase] = useState<TransformationPhase>(
   188	    inferTransformationPhaseFromTrainingGoal("hypertrophy"),
   189	  );
   190	  const [calorieAdjustPct, setCalorieAdjustPct] = useState(0);
   191	
   192	  const [proteinOverride, setProteinOverride] = useState<number | null>(null);
   193	  const [trainingConfig, setTrainingConfig] = useState<TrainingConfig>({
   194	    weeklyFrequency: 3,
   195	    sessionDurationMin: 60,
   196	    cardioFrequency: 0,
   197	    cardioDurationMin: 0,
   198	    dailySteps: 0,
   199	    trainingCaloriesWeekly: null,
   200	  });
   201	  const [lifestyleConfig, setLifestyleConfig] = useState<LifestyleConfig>({
   202	    stressLevel: null,
   203	    sleepDurationH: null,
   204	    sleepQuality: null,
   205	    caffeineDailyMg: null,
   206	    alcoholWeekly: null,
   207	    workHoursPerWeek: null,
   208	  });
   209	  const [biometricsConfig, setBiometricsConfig] = useState<BiometricsConfig>({
   210	    weight_kg: null,
   211	    height_cm: null,
   212	    body_fat_pct: null,
   213	    lean_mass_kg: null,
   214	    muscle_mass_kg: null,
   215	    visceral_fat_level: null,
   216	    bmr_kcal_measured: null,
   217	    bmr_source: "estimated",
   218	  });
   219	
   220	  const setGoalWithPreset = useCallback(
   221	    (newGoal: MacroGoal) => {
   222	      setGoal(newGoal);
   223	      const bf =
   224	        biometricsConfig.body_fat_pct ?? clientData?.body_fat_pct ?? null;
   225	      setCalorieAdjustPct(
   226	        computeSmartPreset(newGoal, bf, trainingConfig.weeklyFrequency),
   227	      );
   228	    },
   229	    [
   230	      biometricsConfig.body_fat_pct,
   231	      clientData?.body_fat_pct,
   232	      trainingConfig.weeklyFrequency,
   233	    ],
   234	  );
   235	
   236	  const setTransformationPhaseWithPreset = useCallback(
   237	    (newPhase: TransformationPhase) => {
   238	      setTransformationPhase(newPhase);
   239	      const bf = biometricsConfig.body_fat_pct ?? clientData?.body_fat_pct ?? null;
   240	      const weeklyFrequency = trainingConfig.weeklyFrequency;
   241	      const mappedGoal = transformationPhaseToMacroGoal(newPhase);
   242	      setGoal(mappedGoal);
   243	      setCalorieAdjustPct(
   244	        computePhaseDrivenCalorieAdjustPct({
   245	          phase: newPhase,
   246	          bodyFat: bf,
   247	          weeklyFrequency,
   248	          basePreset: computeSmartPreset,
   249	        }),
   250	      );
   251	    },
   252	    [
   253	      biometricsConfig.body_fat_pct,
   254	      clientData?.body_fat_pct,
   255	      trainingConfig.weeklyFrequency,
   256	    ],
   257	  );
   258	
   259	  const [macroOverrides, setMacroOverrides] = useState<MacroOverrides>({
   260	    protein_g: null,

    36	export function WaterIntakeCalculator({ language: propLanguage }: WaterIntakeCalculatorProps = { language: undefined }) {
    37	  const [internalLanguage, setInternalLanguage] = useState<Language>('fr');
    38	  const language = propLanguage ?? internalLanguage;
    39	  const t = getTranslation(language);
    40	
    41	  const [weight, setWeight] = useState<string>('');
    42	  const [age, setAge] = useState<string>('');
    43	  const [activity, setActivity] = useState<'sedentary' | 'moderate' | 'active' | 'veryActive'>('moderate');
    44	  const [climate, setClimate] = useState<'temperate' | 'hot' | 'veryHot'>('temperate');
    45	  const [showResults, setShowResults] = useState(false);
    46

    48	  const ageNum = Number(age) || 0;
    49	
    50	  const activityBonus = {
    51	    sedentary: 0,
    52	    moderate: 700,
    53	    active: 500,
    54	    veryActive: 700,
    55	  };
    56	
    57	  const climateBonus = {
    58	    temperate: 0,
    59	    hot: 300,
    60	    veryHot: 500,
    61	  };
    62	
    63	  const baseIntake = weightNum > 0 ? weightNum * 35 : 0; // 35ml per kg
    64	  const totalML = baseIntake + activityBonus[activity] + climateBonus[climate];
    65	  const totalLiters = totalML / 1000;
    66	  const glasses = Math.round(totalML / 250);
    67	
    68	  const handleCalculate = () => {
    69	    if (weightNum > 0) {
    70	      setShowResults(true);
    71	    }
    72	  };
    73	
    74	  return (
    75	    <section className="relative py-12 md:py-16 lg:py-24">
    76	      <div className="max-w-6xl mx-auto px-4 sm:px-6 lg:px-8">

    78	        <div className="mb-8 md:mb-12">

    80	            {t.waterIntakeCalculator.title}
    81	          </h1>
    82	          <p className="text-base sm:text-lg text-white/70 mb-6">
    83	            {t.waterIntakeCalculator.subtitle}
    84	          </p>
    85	        </div>
    86	
    87	        {/* Input Form Card */}

    89	          <div className="space-y-6">
    90	            <div className="grid grid-cols-1 sm:grid-cols-2 gap-4">
    91	              {/* Weight */}
    92	              <div>
    93	                <label className="block text-sm text-white/70 mb-2 font-sans font-normal">

    95	                </label>

    97	                  type="text"
    98	                  inputMode="numeric"

   101	                    setWeight(e.target.value.replace(/[^0-9.]/g, ''));
   102	                    setShowResults(false);
   103	                  }}
   104	                  onFocus={(e) => {
   105	                    e.target.select();

   116	                </label>

   118	                  type="text"
   119	                  inputMode="numeric"

   121	                  onChange={(e) => {
   122	                    setAge(e.target.value.replace(/[^0-9]/g, ''));

UI CANDIDATE: ./lib/client/nutrition/drinks.ts

     1	export type DrinkType = "water" | "espresso" | "coffee" | "lungo" | "tea"
     2	export type DrinkLogKind = "all" | "water" | "caffeine"
     3	
     4	export type DrinkPreset = {
     5	  drinkType: DrinkType
     6	  label: string
     7	  shortLabel: string
     8	  baseAmountMl: number
     9	  baseCaffeineMg: number
    10	  accent: string
    11	  cupCount: 1 | 2 | 3
    12	  strengthLabel: string
    13	}
    14	
    15	export const DRINK_PRESETS: Record<DrinkType, DrinkPreset> = {
    16	  water: {
    17	    drinkType: "water",
    18	    label: "Eau",
    19	    shortLabel: "Eau",
    20	    baseAmountMl: 250,
    21	    baseCaffeineMg: 0,
    22	    accent: "#60a5fa",
    23	    cupCount: 1,
    24	    strengthLabel: "hydratation",
    25	  },
    26	  espresso: {
    27	    drinkType: "espresso",
    28	    label: "Espresso",
    29	    shortLabel: "Espresso",
    30	    baseAmountMl: 40,
    31	    baseCaffeineMg: 80,
    32	    accent: "#c08457",
    33	    cupCount: 1,
    34	    strengthLabel: "concentré",
    35	  },
    36	  coffee: {
    37	    drinkType: "coffee",
    38	    label: "Café",
    39	    shortLabel: "Café",
    40	    baseAmountMl: 180,
    41	    baseCaffeineMg: 95,
    42	    accent: "#c08457",
    43	    cupCount: 2,
    44	    strengthLabel: "classique",
    45	  },
    46	  lungo: {
    47	    drinkType: "lungo",
    48	    label: "Lungo",
    49	    shortLabel: "Lungo",
    50	    baseAmountMl: 120,
    51	    baseCaffeineMg: 110,
    52	    accent: "#c08457",
    53	    cupCount: 3,
    54	    strengthLabel: "allongé",
    55	  },
    56	  tea: {
    57	    drinkType: "tea",
    58	    label: "Thé",
    59	    shortLabel: "Thé",
    60	    baseAmountMl: 250,
    61	    baseCaffeineMg: 35,
    62	    accent: "#34d399",
    63	    cupCount: 1,
    64	    strengthLabel: "infusé",
    65	  },
    66	}
    67	
    68	const CAFFEINATED_TYPES: Exclude<DrinkType, "water">[] = ["espresso", "coffee", "lungo", "tea"]
    69	
    70	export function isCaffeinatedDrinkType(type: DrinkType): type is Exclude<DrinkType, "water"> {
    71	  return CAFFEINATED_TYPES.includes(type as Exclude<DrinkType, "water">)
    72	}
    73	
    74	export function getDrinkPreset(drinkType: DrinkType): DrinkPreset {
    75	  return DRINK_PRESETS[drinkType]
    76	}
    77	
    78	export function estimateCaffeineMg(drinkType: DrinkType, amountMl: number): number {
    79	  if (drinkType === "water") return 0
    80	  const preset = DRINK_PRESETS[drinkType]
    81	  const safeAmount = Math.max(1, amountMl)
    82	  return Math.max(0, Math.round(preset.baseCaffeineMg * (safeAmount / preset.baseAmountMl)))
    83	}
    84	
    85	export function inferDrinkTypeFromFoodItem(input: { name_fr: string; category_l1: string; category_l2: string | null }): DrinkType {
    86	  const name = input.name_fr.toLowerCase()
    87	  const category = `${input.category_l1 ?? ""} ${input.category_l2 ?? ""}`.toLowerCase()
    88	
    89	  if (input.category_l1 !== "drinks") return "water"
    90	  if (/espresso|expresso/.test(name)) return "espresso"
    91	  if (/lungo/.test(name)) return "lungo"
    92	  if (/(th[eé]|tisane|infusion|rooibos|camomille)/.test(name) || /(th[eé]|tisane|infusion|rooibos|camomille)/.test(category)) return "tea"
    93	  if (/cafe|coffee|cappuccino|latte|macchiato|ristretto/.test(name)) return "coffee"
    94	  if (/chauds?/.test(category)) return "coffee"
    95	  return "water"
    96	}

UI CANDIDATE: ./lib/client/smart/adherenceScore.ts
------------------------------------------------------------
     1	export type AdherenceInput = {
     2	  sessionDates: string[]
     3	  plannedDaysOfWeek: number[]
     4	  mealDates: string[]
     5	  waterByDate: Record<string, number>
     6	  waterTargetMl: number
     7	  checkinDates: string[]
     8	  referenceDate: string
     9	}
    10	
    11	export type AdherenceResult = {
    12	  score: number
    13	  scoreDelta: number
    14	  dimensions: {
    15	    sport: number
    16	    nutrition: number
    17	    hydration: number
    18	    checkins: number
    19	  }
    20	}
    21	
    22	function getWindow(referenceDate: string, daysBack: number): string[] {
    23	  const dates: string[] = []
    24	  const ref = new Date(referenceDate)
    25	  for (let i = daysBack - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
    26	    const d = new Date(ref)
    27	    d.setDate(ref.getDate() - i)
    28	    dates.push(d.toISOString().split('T')[0])
    29	  }
    30	  return dates
    31	}
    32	
    33	function getDayOfWeek(dateStr: string): number {
    34	  const jsDay = new Date(dateStr).getDay()
    35	  return jsDay === 0 ? 7 : jsDay
    36	}
    37	
    38	function computeDimensions(
    39	  window: string[],
    40	  sessionDates: string[],
    41	  plannedDaysOfWeek: number[],
    42	  mealDates: string[],
    43	  waterByDate: Record<string, number>,
    44	  waterTargetMl: number,
    45	  checkinDates: string[],
    46	): AdherenceResult['dimensions'] {
    47	  const sessionSet = new Set(sessionDates)
    48	  const mealSet = new Set(mealDates)
    49	  const checkinSet = new Set(checkinDates)
    50	
    51	  const plannedInWindow = window.filter(d => plannedDaysOfWeek.includes(getDayOfWeek(d)))
    52	  const sportDone = plannedInWindow.filter(d => sessionSet.has(d)).length
    53	  const sport = plannedInWindow.length > 0
    54	    ? Math.round((sportDone / plannedInWindow.length) * 25)
    55	    : 25
    56	
    57	  const nutritionDone = window.filter(d => mealSet.has(d)).length
    58	  const nutrition = Math.round((nutritionDone / window.length) * 25)
    59	
    60	  const hydrationDone = window.filter(d => (waterByDate[d] ?? 0) >= waterTargetMl * 0.8).length
    61	  const hydration = waterTargetMl > 0
    62	    ? Math.round((hydrationDone / window.length) * 25)
    63	    : 25
    64	
    65	  const checkinDone = window.filter(d => checkinSet.has(d)).length
    66	  const checkins = Math.round((checkinDone / window.length) * 25)
    67	
    68	  return { sport, nutrition, hydration, checkins }
    69	}
    70	
    71	export function computeAdherenceScore(input: AdherenceInput): AdherenceResult {
    72	  const { sessionDates, plannedDaysOfWeek, mealDates, waterByDate, waterTargetMl, checkinDates, referenceDate } = input
    73	
    74	  const todayWindow = getWindow(referenceDate, 7)
    75	  const dims = computeDimensions(todayWindow, sessionDates, plannedDaysOfWeek, mealDates, waterByDate, waterTargetMl, checkinDates)
    76	  const score = dims.sport + dims.nutrition + dims.hydration + dims.checkins
    77	
    78	  const ref = new Date(referenceDate)
    79	  ref.setDate(ref.getDate() - 1)
    80	  const yesterdayRef = ref.toISOString().split('T')[0]
    81	  const yesterdayWindow = getWindow(yesterdayRef, 7)
    82	  const yd = computeDimensions(yesterdayWindow, sessionDates, plannedDaysOfWeek, mealDates, waterByDate, waterTargetMl, checkinDates)
    83	  const yesterdayScore = yd.sport + yd.nutrition + yd.hydration + yd.checkins
    84	
    85	  return { score, scoreDelta: score - yesterdayScore, dimensions: dims }
    86	}

UI CANDIDATE: ./lib/client/smart/nutritionAlerts.ts
------------------------------------------------------------
     1	export type NutritionAlertCode =
     2	  | 'protein_low'
     3	  | 'carbs_limit'
     4	  | 'hydration_low'
     5	  | 'lunch_missing'
     6	
     7	export type NutritionAlertSeverity = 'info' | 'warning' | 'critical'
     8	
     9	export type NutritionAlert = {
    10	  code: NutritionAlertCode
    11	  severity: NutritionAlertSeverity
    12	  title: string
    13	  body?: string
    14	  delta?: number
    15	}
    16	
    17	export type NutritionConsumed = {
    18	  kcal: number
    19	  protein_g: number
    20	  carbs_g: number
    21	  fat_g: number
    22	  water_ml: number
    23	  caffeine_mg?: number
    24	}
    25	
    26	export type NutritionInput = {
    27	  consumed: NutritionConsumed
    28	  target: NutritionConsumed
    29	  currentHour: number
    30	  hasLunchLog: boolean
    31	}
    32	
    33	export function computeNutritionAlerts(input: NutritionInput): NutritionAlert[] {
    34	  const alerts: NutritionAlert[] = []
    35	  const { consumed, target, currentHour, hasLunchLog } = input
    36	
    37	  // Rule 1: protein_low (warning) — after 14h, behind schedule
    38	  if (currentHour >= 14) {
    39	    const expected = target.protein_g * (currentHour / 22)
    40	    const threshold = expected * 0.8
    41	    if (consumed.protein_g < threshold) {
    42	      const delta = Math.round(target.protein_g - consumed.protein_g)
    43	      alerts.push({
    44	        code: 'protein_low',
    45	        severity: 'warning',
    46	        title: 'PROTÉINES EN RETARD',
    47	        body: `il te reste ${delta}g pour atteindre ${target.protein_g}g`,
    48	        delta,
    49	      })
    50	    }
    51	  }
    52	
    53	  // Rule 2: carbs_limit (critical) — over target
    54	  if (consumed.carbs_g > target.carbs_g) {
    55	    const delta = Math.round(consumed.carbs_g - target.carbs_g)
    56	    alerts.push({
    57	      code: 'carbs_limit',
    58	      severity: 'critical',
    59	      title: 'LIMITE GLUCIDES ATTEINTE',
    60	      body: `-${delta}g sur ta cible`,
    61	      delta,
    62	    })
    63	  }
    64	
    65	  // Rule 3: hydration_low (warning) — after 14h, <50% of target
    66	  if (currentHour >= 14) {
    67	    const ratio = target.water_ml > 0 ? consumed.water_ml / target.water_ml : 1
    68	    if (ratio < 0.5) {
    69	      const deltaMl = target.water_ml - consumed.water_ml
    70	      const deltaL = (deltaMl / 1000).toFixed(1)
    71	      alerts.push({
    72	        code: 'hydration_low',
    73	        severity: 'warning',
    74	        title: 'HYDRATATION FAIBLE',
    75	        body: `il manque ${deltaL}L`,
    76	        delta: deltaMl,
    77	      })
    78	    }
    79	  }
    80	
    81	  // Rule 4: lunch_missing (info) — between 13-14h, no lunch log
    82	  if (currentHour >= 13 && currentHour < 15 && !hasLunchLog) {
    83	    alerts.push({
    84	      code: 'lunch_missing',
    85	      severity: 'info',
    86	      title: 'PAS DE DÉJEUNER LOGUÉ',
    87	    })
    88	  }
    89	
    90	  return alerts
    91	}

    73	}
    74	
    75	const SLOT_LABEL: Record<'morning' | 'midday' | 'afternoon' | 'evening', string> = {
    76	  morning: 'Hydratation matin',
    77	  midday: 'Hydratation midi',
    78	  afternoon: 'Hydratation après-midi',
    79	  evening: 'Hydratation soir',
    80	}
    81	
    82	export function buildTimeline(src: TimelineSource, tz: string = 'Europe/Paris'): TimelineEntry[] {
    83	  const entries: TimelineEntry[] = []
    84	
    85	  // Meals
    86	  for (const m of src.meals) {
    87	    entries.push({
    88	      id: m.id,
    89	      kind: 'meal',
    90	      start_iso: m.logged_at,
    91	      title: m.title,
    92	      subtitle: `${m.kcal} kcal · ${m.protein_g}P ${m.carbs_g}G ${m.fat_g}L`,
    93	      href: `/client/nutrition/journal#${m.id}`,
    94	    })
    95	  }
    96	
    97	  // Water aggregated by time of day
    98	  if (src.waterLogs.length > 0) {
    99	    const grouped = groupWaterByTimeOfDay(src.waterLogs, tz)
   100	    const dateRef = src.waterLogs[0].logged_at.slice(0, 10)
   101	    for (const slot of ['morning', 'midday', 'afternoon', 'evening'] as const) {
   102	      const ml = grouped[slot]
   103	      if (ml > 0) {
   104	        entries.push({
   105	          id: `water-${slot}`,
   106	          kind: 'water',
   107	          start_iso: `${dateRef}${SLOT_REPRESENTATIVE_SUFFIX[slot]}`,
   108	          title: SLOT_LABEL[slot],
   109	          subtitle: `${ml} ml`,
   110	        })
   111	      }
   112	    }
   113	  }
   114	
   115	  // Session
   116	  if (src.session) {
   117	    entries.push({
   118	      id: src.session.id,
   119	      kind: 'workout',
   120	      start_iso: src.session.completed_at,
   121	      title: src.session.title,
   122	      subtitle: `${src.session.exercises_count} exercices · ${src.session.duration_min} min`,
   123	      href: `/client/programme/recap/${src.session.id}`,
   124	    })
   125	  }
   126	
   127	  // Activities
   128	  for (const a of src.activities) {
   129	    entries.push({
   130	      id: a.id,
   131	      kind: 'activity',
   132	      start_iso: a.started_at,
   133	      title: a.custom_label?.trim() || ACTIVITY_LABEL[a.activity_type],
   134	      subtitle: `${a.duration_min} min · intensité ${a.intensity}/10`,
   135	    })
   136	  }
   137	
   138	  // Checkins
   139	  for (const c of src.checkins) {
   140	    const parts: string[] = []
   141	    if (c.sleep_h != null) parts.push(`${c.sleep_h}h sommeil`)
   142	    if (c.energy != null) parts.push(`énergie ${c.energy}/10`)
   143	    if (c.stress != null) parts.push(`stress ${c.stress}/10`)
   144	    entries.push({
   145	      id: c.id,
   146	      kind: 'checkin',
   147	      start_iso: c.logged_at,
   148	      title: 'Check-in',
   149	      subtitle: parts.join(' · '),
   150	    })
   151	  }
   152	
   153	  return entries.sort((a, b) => a.start_iso.localeCompare(b.start_iso))
   154	}

UI CANDIDATE: ./lib/client/smart/waterAggregation.ts
------------------------------------------------------------
     1	export type WaterLog = {
     2	  logged_at: string
     3	  amount_ml: number
     4	}
     5	
     6	export type WaterByTimeOfDay = {
     7	  morning: number
     8	  midday: number
     9	  afternoon: number
    10	  evening: number
    11	}
    12	
    13	function getHourInTz(iso: string, tz = 'Europe/Paris'): number {
    14	  const d = new Date(iso)
    15	  const fmt = new Intl.DateTimeFormat('en-US', {
    16	    timeZone: tz,
    17	    hour: 'numeric',
    18	    hour12: false,
    19	  })
    20	  const parts = fmt.formatToParts(d)
    21	  const h = parts.find(p => p.type === 'hour')?.value ?? '0'
    22	  return parseInt(h, 10)
    23	}
    24	
    25	export function groupWaterByTimeOfDay(
    26	  logs: WaterLog[],
    27	  tz: string = 'Europe/Paris'
    28	): WaterByTimeOfDay {
    29	  const out: WaterByTimeOfDay = { morning: 0, midday: 0, afternoon: 0, evening: 0 }
    30	  for (const log of logs) {
    31	    const hour = getHourInTz(log.logged_at, tz)
    32	    if (hour >= 5 && hour < 12) out.morning += log.amount_ml
    33	    else if (hour >= 12 && hour < 15) out.midday += log.amount_ml
    34	    else if (hour >= 15 && hour < 19) out.afternoon += log.amount_ml
    35	    else if (hour >= 19 && hour < 24) out.evening += log.amount_ml
    36	  }
    37	  return out
    38	}

------------------------------------------------------------
UI CANDIDATE: ./lib/nutrition/actionable-remaining.ts
------------------------------------------------------------
     1	import type { NutritionMacros } from '@/components/client/smart/SmartNutritionWidget'
     2	import { getRemainingNutritionTargets, type RemainingNutritionTargets } from './remaining-targets'
     3	
     4	type GenderLike = string | null | undefined
     5	
     6	export interface ActionableRemainingProfile {
     7	  gender?: GenderLike
     8	  weightKg?: number | null
     9	}
    10	
    11	export interface ActionableCompensationTrace {
    12	  overflowSource: Array<'protein' | 'carbs' | 'fat'>
    13	  overflowKcal: number
    14	  carbsReducedG: number
    15	  fatReducedG: number
    16	  proteinReducedG: number
    17	  fatFloorProtected: boolean
    18	}
    19	
    20	export interface ActionableRemainingResult {
    21	  informativeRemaining: RemainingNutritionTargets
    22	  actionableRemaining: RemainingNutritionTargets
    23	  overflow: {
    24	    protein_g: number
    25	    carbs_g: number
    26	    fat_g: number
    27	  }
    28	  fatFloorG: number
    29	  minActionableFatG: number
    30	  compensation: ActionableCompensationTrace
    31	  isExtremeCase: boolean
    32	}
    33	
    34	type MacroState = {
    35	  protein: number
    36	  carbs: number
    37	  fat: number
    38	}
    39	
    40	export function computeActionableRemaining({
    41	  target,
    42	  consumed,
    43	  profile,
    44	}: {
    45	  target: Pick<NutritionMacros, 'kcal' | 'protein_g' | 'carbs_g' | 'fat_g'>
    46	  consumed: Pick<NutritionMacros, 'kcal' | 'protein_g' | 'carbs_g' | 'fat_g'>
    47	  profile?: ActionableRemainingProfile
    48	}): ActionableRemainingResult {
    49	  const informativeRemaining = getRemainingNutritionTargets({
    50	    dailyTargets: target,
    51	    consumedToday: consumed,
    52	  })
    53	
    54	  const overflow = {
    55	    protein_g: Math.max(0, -informativeRemaining.protein),
    56	    carbs_g: Math.max(0, -informativeRemaining.carbs),
    57	    fat_g: Math.max(0, -informativeRemaining.fat),
    58	  }
    59	
    60	  const actionable: MacroState = {
    61	    protein: Math.max(0, informativeRemaining.protein),
    62	    carbs: Math.max(0, informativeRemaining.carbs),
    63	    fat: Math.max(0, informativeRemaining.fat),
    64	  }
    65	
    66	  // Cap fat floor at 85% of target so a low-fat protocol is never fully overridden
    67	  const rawFatFloorG = getFatFloorGrams(profile?.gender, profile?.weightKg)
    68	  const fatFloorG = target.fat_g > 0 ? Math.min(rawFatFloorG, round1(target.fat_g * 0.85)) : rawFatFloorG
    69	  const minActionableFatG = Math.max(0, round1(fatFloorG - consumed.fat_g))
    70	  const maxReducibleFatG = Math.max(0, round1(actionable.fat - minActionableFatG))
    71	
    72	  const overflowKcal = round1(
    73	    overflow.protein_g * 4 +
    74	    overflow.carbs_g * 4 +
    75	    overflow.fat_g * 9,
    76	  )
    77	
    78	  let remainingOverflowKcal = overflowKcal
    79	
    80	  const carbsReducedG = Math.min(actionable.carbs, round1(remainingOverflowKcal / 4))
    81	  actionable.carbs = round1(actionable.carbs - carbsReducedG)
    82	  remainingOverflowKcal = round1(Math.max(0, remainingOverflowKcal - carbsReducedG * 4))
    83	
    84	  const fatReducedG = Math.min(maxReducibleFatG, round1(remainingOverflowKcal / 9))
    85	  actionable.fat = round1(actionable.fat - fatReducedG)
    86	  remainingOverflowKcal = round1(Math.max(0, remainingOverflowKcal - fatReducedG * 9))
    87	
    88	  const proteinReducedG = Math.min(actionable.protein, round1(remainingOverflowKcal / 4))
    89	  actionable.protein = round1(actionable.protein - proteinReducedG)
    90	  remainingOverflowKcal = round1(Math.max(0, remainingOverflowKcal - proteinReducedG * 4))
    91	
    92	  const actionableRemaining: RemainingNutritionTargets = {
    93	    calories: round1(actionable.protein * 4 + actionable.carbs * 4 + actionable.fat * 9),
    94	    protein: actionable.protein,
    95	    carbs: actionable.carbs,
    96	    fat: actionable.fat,
    97	  }
    98	
    99	  const overflowSource: Array<'protein' | 'carbs' | 'fat'> = []
   100	  if (overflow.protein_g > 0) overflowSource.push('protein')
   101	  if (overflow.carbs_g > 0) overflowSource.push('carbs')
   102	  if (overflow.fat_g > 0) overflowSource.push('fat')
   103	
   104	  return {
   105	    informativeRemaining,
   106	    actionableRemaining,
   107	    overflow,
   108	    fatFloorG,
   109	    minActionableFatG,
   110	    compensation: {
   111	      overflowSource,
   112	      overflowKcal,
   113	      carbsReducedG,
   114	      fatReducedG,
   115	      proteinReducedG,
   116	      fatFloorProtected: fatReducedG < round1(overflowKcal / 9) || minActionableFatG > 0,
   117	    },
   118	    isExtremeCase: proteinReducedG > 0 || remainingOverflowKcal > 0.1,
   119	  }
   120	}
   121	
   122	function getFatFloorGrams(gender: GenderLike, weightKg?: number | null): number {
   123	  if (!weightKg || weightKg <= 0) return 0
   124	  const ratio = gender === 'female' ? 0.7 : 0.6
   125	  return round1(weightKg * ratio)
   126	}
   127	
   128	function round1(value: number): number {
   129	  return Math.round(value * 10) / 10
   130	}

UI CANDIDATE: ./lib/nutrition/adaptiveTdee.ts
------------------------------------------------------------
     1	export interface WeightSample {
     2	  date: string       // ISO date 'YYYY-MM-DD'
     3	  weight_kg: number
     4	}
     5	
     6	export interface AdaptiveTdeeInput {
     7	  weightSamples: WeightSample[]
     8	  avgIntakeKcal: number
     9	  caloriesSource: 'logs' | 'protocol'
    10	  windowDays: number
    11	  trackedDays?: number
    12	  // v2 signals
    13	  gender?: 'male' | 'female' | 'other' | 'prefer_not_to_say' | null
    14	  cyclePhases?: string[]        // cycle_phase per day in window (for female clients)
    15	  cycleConfidence?: 'estimated' | 'learning' | 'calibrated' | null
    16	  anchoredToProtocol?: boolean  // window starts at protocol share date
    17	}
    18	
    19	export interface AdaptiveTdeeResult {
    20	  tdeeAdaptive: number
    21	  weightDeltaKg: number
    22	  slopeKgPerDay: number
    23	  confidence: 'high' | 'medium' | 'low'
    24	  confidenceScore: number
    25	  confidenceReasons: string[]
    26	  // v2
    27	  appliedLutealCorrection: boolean
    28	  smoothedWeightUsed: boolean
    29	}
    30	
    31	export function linearRegression(samples: WeightSample[]): { slope: number; intercept: number } {
    32	  const sorted = [...samples].sort((a, b) => a.date.localeCompare(b.date))
    33	  const origin = new Date(sorted[0].date).getTime()
    34	  const points = sorted.map(s => ({
    35	    x: (new Date(s.date).getTime() - origin) / 86400000,
    36	    y: s.weight_kg,
    37	  }))
    38	  const n = points.length
    39	  const sumX = points.reduce((acc, p) => acc + p.x, 0)
    40	  const sumY = points.reduce((acc, p) => acc + p.y, 0)
    41	  const sumXY = points.reduce((acc, p) => acc + p.x * p.y, 0)
    42	  const sumX2 = points.reduce((acc, p) => acc + p.x * p.x, 0)
    43	  const denom = n * sumX2 - sumX * sumX
    44	  const slope = denom === 0 ? 0 : (n * sumXY - sumX * sumY) / denom
    45	  const intercept = (sumY - slope * sumX) / n
    46	  return { slope, intercept }
    47	}
    48	
    49	/**
    50	 * Apply 3-day centered moving average to smooth daily weight fluctuations.
    51	 * Reduces noise from water retention, glycogen, meal timing.
    52	 * Edge points use 2-day average (no center available).
    53	 */
    54	export function smoothWeightSamples(samples: WeightSample[]): WeightSample[] {
    55	  if (samples.length < 3) return samples
    56	  const sorted = [...samples].sort((a, b) => a.date.localeCompare(b.date))
    57	  return sorted.map((s, i) => {
    58	    const prev = i > 0 ? sorted[i - 1].weight_kg : null
    59	    const next = i < sorted.length - 1 ? sorted[i + 1].weight_kg : null
    60	    const vals = [prev, s.weight_kg, next].filter((v): v is number => v !== null)
    61	    return { date: s.date, weight_kg: parseFloat((vals.reduce((a, b) => a + b, 0) / vals.length).toFixed(3)) }
    62	  })
    63	}
    64	
    65	/**
    66	 * Detect if the majority of the window is in luteal phase.
    67	 * Luteal phase raises BMR ~5% via progesterone and causes 0.5–2 kg water retention.
    68	 * Reference: Davidsen et al. 2007, Oosthuyse & Bosch 2010.
    69	 */
    70	export function detectLutealMajority(cyclePhases: string[]): boolean {
    71	  if (cyclePhases.length === 0) return false
    72	  const lutealCount = cyclePhases.filter(p => p === 'luteal').length
    73	  return lutealCount / cyclePhases.length > 0.5
    74	}
    75	
    76	export function calcAdaptiveTdee(input: AdaptiveTdeeInput): AdaptiveTdeeResult {
    77	  if (input.weightSamples.length < 2) {
    78	    throw new Error('At least 2 weight samples required')
    79	  }
    80	
    81	  // v2 — smooth weights before regression to reduce daily noise
    82	  const smoothed = smoothWeightSamples(input.weightSamples)
    83	  const smoothedWeightUsed = smoothed.some((s, i) => s.weight_kg !== input.weightSamples[i]?.weight_kg)
    84	
    85	  // v2 — luteal correction for female clients
    86	  const isFemale = input.gender === 'female'
    87	  const lutealMajority = isFemale && input.cyclePhases
    88	    ? detectLutealMajority(input.cyclePhases)
    89	    : false
    90	  const appliedLutealCorrection = lutealMajority
    91	
    92	  // Adjust smoothed weights: subtract estimated water retention if luteal majority
    93	  // Luteal phase causes avg +0.8 kg water retention (Davidsen 2007)
    94	  const samplesForRegression = appliedLutealCorrection
    95	    ? smoothed.map(s => ({ ...s, weight_kg: s.weight_kg - 0.8 }))
    96	    : smoothed
    97	
    98	  const { slope } = linearRegression(samplesForRegression)
    99	
   100	  // MacroFactor method: TDEE = intake - (slope × 7700)
   101	  let rawTdee = input.avgIntakeKcal - slope * 7700
   102	
   103	  // v2 — luteal BMR correction: progesterone raises BMR ~5% (~+100 kcal on 2000 base)
   104	  // If majority of window is luteal, the avg intake was already elevated → add back
   105	  if (appliedLutealCorrection) {
   106	    rawTdee += 100
   107	  }
   108	
   109	  const tdeeAdaptive = Math.round(rawTdee / 10) * 10
   110	  const weightDeltaKg = parseFloat((slope * input.windowDays).toFixed(2))
   111	
   112	  // ── Confidence scoring ────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   113	  const confidenceReasons: string[] = []
   114	  let confidenceScore = 100
   115	
   116	  // Calorie source
   117	  if (input.caloriesSource === 'protocol') {
   118	    confidenceScore -= 45
   119	    confidenceReasons.push("Apports estimés depuis le protocole (pas les logs) — précision réduite")
   120	  } else {
   121	    confidenceReasons.push("Apports basés sur les repas loggés")
   122	  }
   123	
   124	  // Weight sample density
   125	  if (input.weightSamples.length < 4) {
   126	    confidenceScore -= 50
   127	    confidenceReasons.push(`Seulement ${input.weightSamples.length} pesée(s) — minimum 4 recommandées`)
   128	  } else if (input.weightSamples.length < 6) {
   129	    confidenceScore -= 10
   130	    confidenceReasons.push(`${input.weightSamples.length} pesées — couverture partielle`)
   131	  } else {
   132	    confidenceReasons.push(`${input.weightSamples.length} pesées — couverture solide`)
   133	  }
   134	
   135	  // Nutritional tracking compliance
   136	  if (typeof input.trackedDays === 'number') {
   137	    if (input.trackedDays < Math.max(5, Math.floor(input.windowDays / 2))) {
   138	      confidenceScore -= 20
   139	      confidenceReasons.push(`${input.trackedDays} jours nutritionnels suivis sur ${input.windowDays} — suivi insuffisant`)
   140	    } else {
   141	      confidenceReasons.push(`${input.trackedDays} jours nutritionnels suivis — suivi régulier`)
   142	    }
   143	  }
   144	
   145	  // v2 — window anchoring bonus
   146	  if (input.anchoredToProtocol) {
   147	    confidenceScore += 5
   148	    confidenceReasons.push("Fenêtre ancrée sur le début du protocole — données homogènes")
   149	  } else {
   150	    confidenceReasons.push("Fenêtre non ancrée — peut inclure des données pré-protocole")
   151	  }
   152	
   153	  // v2 — cycle signal quality for female clients
   154	  if (isFemale) {
   155	    if (!input.cyclePhases || input.cyclePhases.length === 0) {
   156	      confidenceScore -= 10
   157	      confidenceReasons.push("Pas de données cycle menstruel — correction lutéale impossible")
   158	    } else if (input.cycleConfidence === 'estimated') {
   159	      confidenceScore -= 10
   160	      confidenceReasons.push("Cycle menstruel estimé (pas de logs) — correction approximative")
   161	    } else if (appliedLutealCorrection) {
   162	      confidenceReasons.push("Phase lutéale majoritaire — correction rétention hydrique appliquée (+0.8 kg, +100 kcal)")
   163	    } else {
   164	      confidenceReasons.push("Phase non-lutéale — pas de correction nécessaire")
   165	    }
   166	  }
   167	
   168	  // v2 — window length signal
   169	  if (input.windowDays < 10) {
   170	    confidenceScore -= 15
   171	    confidenceReasons.push(`Fenêtre courte (${input.windowDays}j) — tendance moins fiable`)
   172	  } else if (input.windowDays >= 14) {
   173	    confidenceReasons.push(`Fenêtre ${input.windowDays}j — durée optimale`)
   174	  }
   175	
   176	  const confidence: 'high' | 'medium' | 'low' =
   177	    confidenceScore >= 80 ? 'high' : confidenceScore >= 55 ? 'medium' : 'low'
   178	
   179	  return {
   180	    tdeeAdaptive,
   181	    weightDeltaKg,
   182	    slopeKgPerDay: slope,
   183	    confidence,
   184	    confidenceScore: Math.max(0, Math.min(100, confidenceScore)),
   185	    confidenceReasons,
   186	    appliedLutealCorrection,
   187	    smoothedWeightUsed,
   188	  }
   189	}

UI CANDIDATE: ./lib/nutrition/engine/cycleSync.ts
------------------------------------------------------------
     1	// lib/nutrition/engine/cycleSync.ts
     2	// Cycle-phase macro adjustments — Davidsen 2007, Oosthuyse & Bosch 2010
     3	// Only applies when client gender === 'female'. Additive layer on top of base macros.
     4	
     5	import type { StryvrmMacros } from './types'
     6	
     7	export type CyclePhase = 'follicular' | 'ovulatory' | 'luteal' | 'menstrual'
     8	
     9	export interface CycleSyncAdjustment {
    10	  caloriesDelta: number       // kcal/day vs base
    11	  proteinDelta: number        // g/day
    12	  carbsDelta: number          // g/day
    13	  fatDelta: number            // g/day
    14	  hydrationDeltaMl: number    // ml/day
    15	  notes: string[]             // coach-facing guidance
    16	  optimalForDeficit: boolean  // true = favorable phase for caloric restriction
    17	}
    18	
    19	const ADJUSTMENTS: Record<CyclePhase, CycleSyncAdjustment> = {
    20	  follicular: {
    21	    caloriesDelta: 0,
    22	    proteinDelta: 0,
    23	    carbsDelta: 0,
    24	    fatDelta: 0,
    25	    hydrationDeltaMl: 0,
    26	    notes: [
    27	      "Phase optimale pour le déficit calorique — sensibilité à l'insuline élevée.",
    28	      "Glucides bien tolérés — privilégier les séances d'intensité haute.",
    29	      "Récupération rapide — idéal pour augmenter la fréquence d'entraînement.",
    30	    ],
    31	    optimalForDeficit: true,
    32	  },
    33	  ovulatory: {
    34	    caloriesDelta: 0,
    35	    proteinDelta: 0,
    36	    carbsDelta: 0,
    37	    fatDelta: 0,
    38	    hydrationDeltaMl: 0,
    39	    notes: [
    40	      "Pic de performance — force et endurance maximales.",
    41	      "Maintenir les calories cibles sans restriction supplémentaire.",
    42	      "Attention à la laxité ligamentaire accrue (oestrogène élevé).",
    43	    ],
    44	    optimalForDeficit: true,
    45	  },
    46	  luteal: {
    47	    // Progesterone increases BMR ~5% = +100 kcal sur base 2000 kcal
    48	    // Protein catabolism increases — +10g protein protective
    49	    // Serotonin drops → carb cravings — +20g carbs reduces cravings
    50	    caloriesDelta: 100,
    51	    proteinDelta: 10,
    52	    carbsDelta: 20,
    53	    fatDelta: 0,
    54	    hydrationDeltaMl: 250,   // rétention hydrique — compenser
    55	    notes: [
    56	      "Métabolisme augmenté (~5%) — ajouter 100 kcal pour soutenir la récupération.",
    57	      "Protéines supplémentaires anti-cataboliques (progestérone élève le turnover protéique).",
    58	      "Glucides complexes recommandés — soutiennent la sérotonine et réduisent les fringales.",
    59	      "Hydratation augmentée — compenser la rétention hydrique prémenstruelle.",
    60	      "Magnésium (400 mg/j) et oméga-3 — réduisent crampes et inflammation.",
    61	    ],
    62	    optimalForDeficit: false,
    63	  },
    64	  menstrual: {
    65	    caloriesDelta: 0,
    66	    proteinDelta: 5,         // soutien musculaire en période de perte de fer
    67	    carbsDelta: 0,
    68	    fatDelta: 5,             // oméga-3 anti-inflammatoires
    69	    hydrationDeltaMl: 250,
    70	    notes: [
    71	      "Maintenir les calories — ne pas couper en phase menstruelle.",
    72	      "Protéines et fer en priorité — aliments riches en fer hémique (viande rouge, légumineuses).",
    73	      "Lipides anti-inflammatoires (oméga-3) — réduisent dysménorrhée.",
    74	      "Hydratation augmentée — pertes physiologiques élevées.",
    75	      "Volume d'entraînement réduit si énergie basse — ne pas forcer.",
    76	    ],
    77	    optimalForDeficit: false,
    78	  },
    79	}
    80	
    81	export function getCycleSyncAdjustment(phase: CyclePhase): CycleSyncAdjustment {
    82	  return ADJUSTMENTS[phase]
    83	}
    84	
    85	export function adjustMacrosForPhase(
    86	  base: StryvrmMacros,
    87	  phase: CyclePhase,
    88	): StryvrmMacros & { hydrationDeltaMl: number } {
    89	  const adj = ADJUSTMENTS[phase]
    90	  const protein_g = Math.max(0, Math.round(base.protein_g + adj.proteinDelta))
    91	  const carbs_g = Math.max(0, Math.round(base.carbs_g + adj.carbsDelta))
    92	  const fat_g = Math.max(0, Math.round(base.fat_g + adj.fatDelta))
    93	  const calories = protein_g * 4 + carbs_g * 4 + fat_g * 9
    94	  return { protein_g, carbs_g, fat_g, calories, hydrationDeltaMl: adj.hydrationDeltaMl }
    95	}
    96	
    97	// Standard 28-day cycle phase boundaries (Davidsen et al.)
    98	// Day 1-5: menstrual, 6-13: follicular, 14-16: ovulatory, 17-28: luteal
    99	export function detectCurrentPhase(cycleDay: number): CyclePhase {
   100	  const day = ((cycleDay - 1) % 28) + 1  // normalize to 1-28
   101	  if (day <= 5) return 'menstrual'
   102	  if (day <= 13) return 'follicular'
   103	  if (day <= 16) return 'ovulatory'
   104	  return 'luteal'
   105	}

    71	/** Profil pour scaling portions anatomiques */
    72	export interface PortionScalingProfile {

    74	  height_cm?: number | null
    75	}

    77	export interface PortionSize {

    80	  baseG: number
    81	  /** 'hand' = scale avec longueur main user, 'fixed' = ustensile/unité produit, taille constante */
    82	  scales: "hand" | "fixed"

    84	}

    86	/**

    89	 * Anatomique (paume/poing/pouce) → scale × (handCm / 18).
    90	 * Fixed (cuillère/verre/œuf) → constant.

   112	/** Référence adulte (longueur main poignet → majeur, cm) */
   113	export const REFERENCE_HAND_CM = 18.0
   114	/** Ratio Pheasant 2003 — longueur main ≈ taille × 0.108 */
   115	export const HEIGHT_TO_HAND_RATIO = 0.108
   116	/** Multiplicateurs disponibles dans l'UI (×1 à ×5) */
   117	export const PORTION_MULTIPLIERS = [1, 1.5, 2, 2.5, 3, 4, 5] as const
   118	
   119	/**
   120	 * Retourne longueur main estimée (cm) : override user → dérivée taille → défaut 18.
   121	 */
   122	export function resolveHandLengthCm(profile: PortionScalingProfile | null | undefined): number {
   123	  if (!profile) return REFERENCE_HAND_CM
   124	  if (profile.hand_length_cm && profile.hand_length_cm > 0) return profile.hand_length_cm
   125	  if (profile.height_cm && profile.height_cm > 0) return profile.height_cm * HEIGHT_TO_HAND_RATIO
   126	  return REFERENCE_HAND_CM
   127	}
   128	
   129	/**
   130	 * Calcule grammes scalés d'une portion selon profil + multiplicateur.
   131	 * Multiplicateur appliqué après scaling main (×2 = deux fois la portion).
   132	 */
   133	export function getScaledPortionG(
   134	  portion: PortionSize,
   135	  profile: PortionScalingProfile | null | undefined,
   136	  multiplier: number = 1
   137	): number {
   138	  const mult = Math.max(0.5, Math.min(multiplier, 10))
   139	  if (portion.scales === "fixed") return Math.round(portion.baseG * mult)
   140	  const handCm = resolveHandLengthCm(profile)
   141	  const factor = handCm / REFERENCE_HAND_CM
   142	  return Math.round(portion.baseG * factor * mult)
   143	}
   144	
   145	/** True si profil a override main explicite (badge UI "ajusté à ta main") */
   146	export function isHandOverrideSet(profile: PortionScalingProfile | null | undefined): boolean {
   147	  return !!(profile?.hand_length_cm && profile.hand_length_cm > 0)
   148	}

   183	  "snacks-sucres": "Snacks & Sucreries",
   184	  "fast-food": "Fast-food",
   185	  // drinks subcategories
   186	  eau: "Eau & Hydratation",
   187	  chauds: "Boissons chaudes",
   188	  "jus-smoothies": "Jus & Smoothies",
   189	  "laits-vegetaux": "Laits végétaux",
   190	  "sports-drinks": "Boissons sportives",
   191	  alcools: "Alcools",
   192	}
   193	
   194	/** Calcule les macros d'une entrée depuis food_item + quantité */
   195	export function calcEntryMacros(
   196	  item: FoodItem,
   197	  quantity_g: number
   198	): Pick<NutritionEntry, "calories_kcal" | "protein_g" | "carbs_g" | "fat_g" | "fiber_g"> {
   199	  const factor = quantity_g / 100
   200	  const protein_g = Math.round(item.protein_per_100g * factor * 10) / 10
   201	  const carbs_g = Math.round(item.carbs_per_100g * factor * 10) / 10
   202	  const fat_g = Math.round(item.fat_per_100g * factor * 10) / 10
   203	  const fiber_g = Math.round(item.fiber_per_100g * factor * 10) / 10
   204	  return {
   205	    calories_kcal: computeMacroEnergy({ protein_g, carbs_g, fat_g, fiber_g }),
   206	    protein_g,
   207	    carbs_g,
   208	    fat_g,
   209	    fiber_g,
   210	  }
   211	}
   212	
   213	/** Somme les macros d'une liste d'entrées draft */
   214	export function sumDraftMacros(entries: EntryDraft[]): {
   215	  calories: number
   216	  protein: number
   217	  carbs: number
   218	  fat: number
   219	  fiber: number
   220	} {
   221	  return entries.reduce(
   222	    (acc, e) => {
   223	      const m = calcEntryMacros(e.food_item, e.quantity_g)
   224	      return {
   225	        calories: Math.round((acc.calories + m.calories_kcal) * 10) / 10,
   226	        protein: Math.round((acc.protein + m.protein_g) * 10) / 10,
   227	        carbs: Math.round((acc.carbs + m.carbs_g) * 10) / 10,
   228	        fat: Math.round((acc.fat + m.fat_g) * 10) / 10,
   229	        fiber: Math.round((acc.fiber + m.fiber_g) * 10) / 10,
   230	      }
   231	    },
   232	    { calories: 0, protein: 0, carbs: 0, fat: 0, fiber: 0 }
   233	  )
   234	}

UI CANDIDATE: ./lib/nutrition/food-taxonomy.ts

   114	function normalizeText(value: string): string {
   115	  return value
   116	    .toLowerCase()
   117	    .normalize("NFD")
   118	    .replace(/[̀-ͯ]/g, "")
   119	    .replace(/œ/g, "oe")
   120	    .replace(/æ/g, "ae")
   121	}
   122	
   123	function nameHasAny(item: Pick<FoodItem, "name_fr">, keywords: string[]): boolean {
   124	  const name = normalizeText(item.name_fr)
   125	  return keywords.some((keyword) => name.includes(normalizeText(keyword)))
   126	}
   127	
   128	function hasAnyText(value: string, keywords: string[]): boolean {
   129	  const text = normalizeText(value)
   130	  return keywords.some((keyword) => text.includes(normalizeText(keyword)))
   131	}
   132	
   133	function hasWordText(value: string, keywords: string[]): boolean {
   134	  const text = ` ${normalizeText(value)} `
   135	  return keywords.some((keyword) => {
   136	    const normalized = normalizeText(keyword)
   137	    return normalized ? text.includes(` ${normalized} `) : false
   138	  })
   139	}
   140	
   141	function hasWordPrefixText(value: string, keywords: string[]): boolean {
   142	  const text = normalizeText(value)
   143	  return keywords.some((keyword) => {
   144	    const normalized = normalizeText(keyword)
   145	    return normalized ? text === normalized || text.startsWith(`${normalized} `) || text.includes(` ${normalized} `) : false
   146	  })
   147	}
   148

     1	import { calculateMacros, type MacroGoal, type MacroGender } from "@/lib/formulas/macros";
     2	
     3	export type PublicTdeeMenstrualPhase = "follicular" | "luteal" | "unknown";
     4	
     5	export interface PublicTdeeInput {
     6	  gender: MacroGender;
     7	  age: number;
     8	  heightCm: number;
     9	  weightKg: number;
    10	  goal: MacroGoal;
    11	  dailySteps?: number;
    12	  occupationMultiplier?: number;
    13	  workoutsPerWeek?: number;
    14	  sessionDurationMin?: number;
    15	  cardioSessionsPerWeek?: number;
    16	  cardioDurationMin?: number;
    17	  bodyFatPct?: number;
    18	  bmrMeasuredKcal?: number;
    19	  sleepHours?: number;
    20	  stressLevel?: number;
    21	  caffeineDailyMg?: number;
    22	  alcoholWeekly?: number;
    23	  menstrualPhase?: PublicTdeeMenstrualPhase;
    24	}
    25	
    26	export interface PublicTdeeMacros {
    27	  calories: number;
    28	  protein_g: number;
    29	  carbs_g: number;
    30	  fat_g: number;
    31	}
    32	
    33	export interface PublicTdeeDaySplit {
    34	  trainingDays: number;
    35	  restDays: number;
    36	  spreadKcal: number;
    37	  trainingDayCalories: number;
    38	  restDayCalories: number;
    39	  averageCalories: number;
    40	  weeklyCalories: number;
    41	  trainingMacros: PublicTdeeMacros;
    42	  restMacros: PublicTdeeMacros;
    43	}
    44	
    45	export interface PublicTdeePlan {
    46	  input: PublicTdeeInput;
    47	  result: ReturnType<typeof calculateMacros>;
    48	  split: PublicTdeeDaySplit;
    49	  confidence: {
    50	    score: number;
    51	    label: "high" | "medium" | "low";
    52	  };
    53	  assumptions: string[];
    54	  guardrails: string[];
    55	  premiumSummary: string[];
    56	  exportText: string;
    57	  shareQuery: string;
    58	}

    60	export interface PublicTdeeValidationIssue {
    61	  field: keyof PublicTdeeInput | "unknown";
    62	  message: string;
    63	}
    64	
    65	function clamp(value: number, min: number, max: number) {
    66	  return Math.min(max, Math.max(min, value));
    67	}
    68	
    69	function round(value: number) {
    70	  return Math.round(value);
    71	}
    72	
    73	function buildMacros(calories: number, protein: number, fat: number): PublicTdeeMacros {
    74	  const proteinCalories = round(protein * 4);
    75	  const maxFatCalories = Math.max(0, calories - proteinCalories);
    76	  const cappedFatCalories = Math.min(round(fat * 9), maxFatCalories);
    77	  const carbs = Math.max(0, round((calories - proteinCalories - cappedFatCalories) / 4));
    78	  return {
    79	    calories: round(proteinCalories + cappedFatCalories + carbs * 4),
    80	    protein_g: round(protein),
    81	    carbs_g: carbs,
    82	    fat_g: round(cappedFatCalories / 9),
    83	  };
    84	}
    85	
    86	export function validatePublicTdeeInput(input: Partial<PublicTdeeInput>): PublicTdeeValidationIssue[] {
    87	  const issues: PublicTdeeValidationIssue[] = [];
    88	
    89	  if (input.gender !== "male" && input.gender !== "female") {
    90	    issues.push({ field: "gender", message: "Le sexe est requis." });
    91	  }
    92	
    93	  if (input.age == null || Number.isNaN(input.age) || input.age < 15 || input.age > 85) {
    94	    issues.push({ field: "age", message: "L'âge doit être compris entre 15 et 85 ans." });
    95	  }
    96	
    97	  if (input.heightCm == null || Number.isNaN(input.heightCm) || input.heightCm < 140 || input.heightCm > 220) {
    98	    issues.push({ field: "heightCm", message: "La taille doit être comprise entre 140 et 220 cm." });
    99	  }
   100	
   101	  if (input.weightKg == null || Number.isNaN(input.weightKg) || input.weightKg < 40 || input.weightKg > 250) {
   102	    issues.push({ field: "weightKg", message: "Le poids doit être compris entre 40 et 250 kg." });
   103	  }
   104	
   105	  if (input.goal !== "deficit" && input.goal !== "maintenance" && input.goal !== "surplus") {
   106	    issues.push({ field: "goal", message: "L'objectif est requis." });
   107	  }
   108	
   109	  return issues;
   110	}
   111	
   112	function buildConfidenceScore(input: PublicTdeeInput, result: ReturnType<typeof calculateMacros>) {
   113	  let score = 45;
   114	
   115	  if (input.bodyFatPct != null) score += 10;
   116	  if (input.bmrMeasuredKcal != null) score += 15;
   117	  if ((input.dailySteps ?? 0) > 0) score += 8;
   118	  if ((input.workoutsPerWeek ?? 0) > 0) score += 8;
   119	  if ((input.sessionDurationMin ?? 0) > 0) score += 4;
   120	  if ((input.cardioSessionsPerWeek ?? 0) > 0 && (input.cardioDurationMin ?? 0) > 0) score += 4;
   121	  if (input.sleepHours != null) score += 3;
   122	  if (input.stressLevel != null) score += 3;
   123	  if (input.caffeineDailyMg != null || input.alcoholWeekly != null) score += 2;
   124	  if (input.gender === "female" && input.menstrualPhase && input.menstrualPhase !== "unknown") score += 3;
   125	  if ((input.occupationMultiplier ?? 1) !== 1) score += 2;
   126	  if (result.dataProvenance.bmrSource === "measured") score += 3;
   127	
   128	  const capped = clamp(score, 0, 100);
   129	  return {
   130	    score: capped,
   131	    label: capped >= 80 ? "high" : capped >= 60 ? "medium" : "low",
   132	  } as const;
   133	}
   134	
   135	function buildAssumptions(input: PublicTdeeInput, result: ReturnType<typeof calculateMacros>) {
   136	  const assumptions: string[] = [];
   137	
   138	  if (result.dataProvenance.bmrSource !== "measured") {
   139	    assumptions.push("BMR estimé par formule plutôt que mesuré.");
   140	  }
   141	  if (result.dataProvenance.lbmSource === "boer") {
   142	    assumptions.push("Masse maigre estimée via Boer faute de body fat ou de masse maigre mesurée.");
   143	  }
   144	  if ((input.cardioSessionsPerWeek ?? 0) === 0 || (input.cardioDurationMin ?? 0) === 0) {
   145	    assumptions.push("Le cardio n'est pas détaillé séparément.");
   146	  }
   147	  if ((input.workoutsPerWeek ?? 0) === 0) {
   148	    assumptions.push("Pas de différenciation training/rest si aucune séance n'est renseignée.");
   149	  }
   150	  if (input.gender === "female" && (!input.menstrualPhase || input.menstrualPhase === "unknown")) {
   151	    assumptions.push("Aucun ajustement cycle menstruel appliqué.");
   152	  }
   153	  if (input.sleepHours == null && input.stressLevel == null) {
   154	    assumptions.push("Aucun module récupération n'a été appliqué.");
   155	  }
   156	
   157	  return assumptions;
   158	}
   159	
   160	function buildGuardrails(input: PublicTdeeInput, result: ReturnType<typeof calculateMacros>) {
   161	  const guardrails: string[] = [];
   162	
   163	  guardrails.push(...result.warnings.map((warning) => warning.replace(/^⚠️\s*/, "")));
   164	
   165	  if (result.breakdown.bmr < 1300) {
   166	    guardrails.push("BMR très bas, prudence sur les déficits agressifs.");
   167	  }
   168	  if (input.goal === "surplus" && result.estimatedBF > (input.gender === "male" ? 18 : 28)) {
   169	    guardrails.push("Surplus peu pertinent si le taux de masse grasse reste élevé.");
   170	  }
   171	  if (input.goal === "deficit" && result.recoveryAdaptation) {
   172	    guardrails.push("Le déficit est modulé à la hausse si récupération trop faible.");
   173	  }
   174	
   175	  if (guardrails.length === 0) {
   176	    guardrails.push("Plan conservateur construit à partir des données disponibles.");
   177	  }
   178	
   179	  return Array.from(new Set(guardrails)).slice(0, 6);
   180	}
   181	
   182	function buildSplit(input: PublicTdeeInput, result: ReturnType<typeof calculateMacros>): PublicTdeeDaySplit {
   183	  const trainingDays = clamp(Math.round(input.workoutsPerWeek ?? 0), 0, 7);
   184	  const restDays = 7 - trainingDays;
   185	  const baseCalories = round(result.calories);
   186	  const exerciseLoad = round(result.breakdown.eat + result.breakdown.eatCardio);
   187	
   188	  const spreadKcal =
   189	    trainingDays > 0 && restDays > 0
   190	      ? clamp(round(Math.max(80, exerciseLoad * 0.8 + (result.breakdown.neat * 0.05))), 80, 320)
   191	      : 0;
   192	
   193	  const trainingOffset = restDays > 0 ? round((spreadKcal * restDays) / 7) : 0;
   194	  const restOffset = trainingDays > 0 ? round((spreadKcal * trainingDays) / 7) : 0;
   195	
   196	  const trainingDayCalories = baseCalories + trainingOffset;
   197	  const restDayCalories = baseCalories - restOffset;
   198	  const averageCalories = baseCalories;
   199	  const weeklyCalories = baseCalories * 7;
   200	
   201	  const trainingMacros = buildMacros(trainingDayCalories, result.macros.p, result.macros.f);
   202	  const restMacros = buildMacros(restDayCalories, result.macros.p, result.macros.f);
   203	
   204	  return {
   205	    trainingDays,
   206	    restDays,
   207	    spreadKcal,
   208	    trainingDayCalories,
   209	    restDayCalories,
   210	    averageCalories,
   211	    weeklyCalories,
   212	    trainingMacros,
   213	    restMacros,
   214	  };
   215	}
   216	
   217	function buildPremiumSummary(input: PublicTdeeInput, result: ReturnType<typeof calculateMacros>, confidence: PublicTdeePlan["confidence"]) {
   218	  return [
   219	    `BMR ${result.dataProvenance.bmrSource === "measured" ? "mesuré" : "estimé"} · confiance ${confidence.score}/100`,
   220	    `NEAT piloté par ${((input.dailySteps ?? 0) > 0 ? "les pas" : "un niveau neutre")} et le contexte pro.`,
   221	    `EAT basé sur ${input.workoutsPerWeek ?? 0} séance${(input.workoutsPerWeek ?? 0) > 1 ? "s" : ""} / semaine.`,
   222	    `TEF conservé comme couche stable à partir du BMR.`,
   223	  ];
   224	}
   225	
   226	function buildShareQuery(input: PublicTdeeInput) {
   227	  const params = new URLSearchParams();
   228	  params.set("gender", input.gender);
   229	  params.set("age", String(input.age));
   230	  params.set("height", String(input.heightCm));
   231	  params.set("weight", String(input.weightKg));
   232	  params.set("goal", input.goal);
   233	
   234	  if (input.dailySteps != null) params.set("steps", String(input.dailySteps));
   235	  if (input.occupationMultiplier != null) params.set("occupation", String(input.occupationMultiplier));
   236	  if (input.workoutsPerWeek != null) params.set("workouts", String(input.workoutsPerWeek));
   237	  if (input.sessionDurationMin != null) params.set("duration", String(input.sessionDurationMin));
   238	  if (input.cardioSessionsPerWeek != null) params.set("cardio", String(input.cardioSessionsPerWeek));
   239	  if (input.cardioDurationMin != null) params.set("cardioDuration", String(input.cardioDurationMin));
   240	  if (input.bodyFatPct != null) params.set("bodyFat", String(input.bodyFatPct));
   241	  if (input.bmrMeasuredKcal != null) params.set("bmr", String(input.bmrMeasuredKcal));
   242	  if (input.sleepHours != null) params.set("sleep", String(input.sleepHours));
   243	  if (input.stressLevel != null) params.set("stress", String(input.stressLevel));
   244	  if (input.caffeineDailyMg != null) params.set("caffeine", String(input.caffeineDailyMg));
   245	  if (input.alcoholWeekly != null) params.set("alcohol", String(input.alcoholWeekly));
   246	  if (input.menstrualPhase && input.menstrualPhase !== "unknown") params.set("cycle", input.menstrualPhase);
   247	
   248	  return params.toString();
   249	}
   250	
   251	export function computePublicTdeePlan(input: PublicTdeeInput): PublicTdeePlan {
   252	  const issues = validatePublicTdeeInput(input);
   253	  if (issues.length > 0) {
   254	    const error = issues.map((issue) => issue.message).join(" ");
   255	    throw new Error(error);
   256	  }
   257	
   258	  const result = calculateMacros({
   259	    gender: input.gender,
   260	    age: input.age,

    48	// Local state for a day being edited in the tool (includes unsaved changes)
    49	export interface DayDraft {
    50	  localId: string        // temp id for new days not yet saved
    51	  dbId?: string          // undefined until saved
    52	  name: string
    53	  calories: string       // string for input binding
    54	  protein_g: string
    55	  carbs_g: string
    56	  fat_g: string
    57	  hydration_ml: string
    58	  carb_cycle_type: 'high' | 'medium' | 'low' | ''
    59	  cycle_sync_phase: 'follicular' | 'ovulatory' | 'luteal' | 'menstrual' | ''
    60	  recommendations: string
    61	}
    62	
    63	export function emptyDayDraft(name = 'Nouveau jour'): DayDraft {
    64	  return {
    65	    localId: crypto.randomUUID(),
    66	    name,
    67	    calories: '',
    68	    protein_g: '',
    69	    carbs_g: '',
    70	    fat_g: '',
    71	    hydration_ml: '',
    72	    carb_cycle_type: '',
    73	    cycle_sync_phase: '',
    74	    recommendations: '',
    75	  }
    76	}
    77	
    78	export function dayDraftFromDb(day: NutritionProtocolDay): DayDraft {
    79	  return {
    80	    localId: day.id,
    81	    dbId: day.id,
    82	    name: day.name,
    83	    calories: day.calories != null ? String(day.calories) : '',
    84	    protein_g: day.protein_g != null ? String(day.protein_g) : '',
    85	    carbs_g: day.carbs_g != null ? String(day.carbs_g) : '',
    86	    fat_g: day.fat_g != null ? String(day.fat_g) : '',
    87	    hydration_ml: day.hydration_ml != null ? String(day.hydration_ml) : '',
    88	    carb_cycle_type: day.carb_cycle_type ?? '',
    89	    cycle_sync_phase: day.cycle_sync_phase ?? '',
    90	    recommendations: day.recommendations ?? '',
    91	  }
    92	}

UI CANDIDATE: ./lib/nutrition/voice.ts

     1	import type { CategoryL1, MealType } from './food-items'
     2	
     3	export type VoiceConfidence = 'high' | 'medium' | 'low'
     4	
     5	export interface VoiceItem {
     6	  name: string
     7	  quantity_g: number
     8	  kcal: number
     9	  protein_g: number
    10	  carbs_g: number
    11	  fat_g: number
    12	  fiber_g: number
    13	  confidence: VoiceConfidence
    14	  food_item_id?: string
    15	  is_new: boolean
    16	  category_l1?: CategoryL1
    17	  category_l2?: string
    18	}
    19	
    20	export interface VoiceParseResult {
    21	  items: VoiceItem[]
    22	  meal_type: MealType
    23	  raw_transcript: string
    24	  clean_transcript: string
    25	}
    26	
    27	// ── Filler word maps ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    28	const FILLERS: Record<string, RegExp> = {
    29	  // Use (?:^|\s) / (?=\s|$) for accented words that break \b word boundaries
    30	  fr: /(?:^|\s)(?:euh|donc|voil[aà]|en fait|genre|alors|bon|ben)(?=\s|$)/gi,
    31	  en: /\b(um|uh|so|like|well|you know)\b/gi,
    32	  es: /(?:^|\s)(?:eh|bueno|pues|o sea)(?=\s|$)/gi,
    33	}
    34	
    35	// ── Written numbers → digits (French) ───────────────────────────────────────
    36	const FR_NUMBERS: Array<[RegExp, string]> = [
    37	  [/\bmille\b/gi, '1000'],
    38	  [/\bcinq cents\b/gi, '500'],
    39	  [/\bquatre cents\b/gi, '400'],
    40	  [/\btrois cents\b/gi, '300'],
    41	  [/\bdeux cents\b/gi, '200'],
    42	  [/\bcent cinquante\b/gi, '150'],
    43	  [/\bcent\b/gi, '100'],
    44	  [/\bquatre-vingt-dix\b/gi, '90'],
    45	  [/\bquatre-vingts?\b/gi, '80'],
    46	  [/\bsoixante-dix\b/gi, '70'],
    47	  [/\bsoixante\b/gi, '60'],
    48	  [/\bciquante\b/gi, '50'],
    49	  [/\bquarante\b/gi, '40'],
    50	  [/\btrente\b/gi, '30'],
    51	  [/\bvingt\b/gi, '20'],
    52	  [/\bdix\b/gi, '10'],
    53	  [/\bneuf\b/gi, '9'],
    54	  [/\bhuit\b/gi, '8'],
    55	  [/\bsept\b/gi, '7'],
    56	  [/\bsix\b/gi, '6'],
    57	  [/\bcinq\b/gi, '5'],
    58	  [/\bquatre\b/gi, '4'],
    59	  [/\btrois\b/gi, '3'],
    60	  [/\bdeux\b/gi, '2'],
    61	  [/\bun\b/gi, '1'],
    62	  [/\bune demi\b/gi, '0.5'],
    63	  [/\bun quart\b/gi, '0.25'],
    64	]
    65	
    66	// ── Unit normalizations ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    67	const UNITS: Array<[RegExp, string]> = [
    68	  [/\bkilogrammes?\b/gi, 'kg'],
    69	  [/\bgrammes?\b/gi, 'g'],
    70	  [/\bmillilitres?\b/gi, 'ml'],
    71	  [/\bcentilitres?\b/gi, 'cl'],
    72	  [/\blitres?\b/gi, 'L'],
    73	]
    74	
    75	export function cleanTranscript(raw: string, lang: string): string {
    76	  let text = raw.toLowerCase()
    77	
    78	  const fillerRe = FILLERS[lang] ?? FILLERS['fr']
    79	  text = text.replace(fillerRe, '')
    80	
    81	  if (lang === 'fr') {
    82	    for (const [re, digit] of FR_NUMBERS) {
    83	      text = text.replace(re, digit)
    84	    }
    85	  }
    86	
    87	  for (const [re, abbr] of UNITS) {
    88	    text = text.replace(re, abbr)
    89	  }
    90	
    91	  return text.replace(/\s+/g, ' ').trim()
    92	}

   193	  },
   194	  {
   195	    category_l1: "fats",
   196	    category_l2: "autres-lipides",
   197	    patterns: [/\bavocat\b/i, /\bbeurre\b/i, /\bpur[eé]e d'amande\b/i, /\bpeanut butter\b/i],
   198	  },
   199	]
   200	
   201	export function guessVoiceFoodCategory(name: string): VoiceCategorySuggestion | null {
   202	  const label = name.trim().toLowerCase()
   203	  if (!label) return null
   204	
   205	  for (const group of VOICE_CATEGORY_PATTERNS) {
   206	    if (group.patterns.some((pattern) => pattern.test(label))) {
   207	      return {
   208	        category_l1: group.category_l1,
   209	        category_l2: group.category_l2,
   210	      }
   211	    }
   212	  }
   213	
   214	  return null
   215	}

------------------------------------------------------------
UI CANDIDATE: ./lib/nutrition/weightSamples.ts
------------------------------------------------------------
     1	import type { SupabaseClient } from '@supabase/supabase-js'
     2	import type { WeightSample } from './adaptiveTdee'
     3	
     4	const MIN_WINDOW_DAYS = 7  // below this, regression is unreliable
     5	
     6	/**
     7	 * Find the date when the current protocol was shared with the client.
     8	 * Uses metric_annotations (label LIKE 'Protocole nutritionnel%') as the
     9	 * most reliable signal — this is written automatically when coach shares.
    10	 * Falls back to null if not found.
    11	 */
    12	export async function resolveProtocolStartDate(
    13	  db: SupabaseClient,
    14	  clientId: string,
    15	  protocolName: string,
    16	): Promise<string | null> {
    17	  const { data } = await db
    18	    .from('metric_annotations')
    19	    .select('event_date')
    20	    .eq('client_id', clientId)
    21	    .eq('event_type', 'nutrition')
    22	    .ilike('label', `Protocole nutritionnel%${protocolName}%`)
    23	    .order('event_date', { ascending: false })
    24	    .limit(1)
    25	    .maybeSingle()
    26	
    27	  return (data as any)?.event_date ?? null
    28	}
    29	
    30	/**
    31	 * Collect weight samples from all available sources, deduplicated by date.
    32	 *
    33	 * Window anchoring (priority order):
    34	 *   1. Since protocol share date (metric_annotations) — avoids mixing pre/post diet data
    35	 *   2. Adaptive fallback: tries targetWindowDays → 21d → 30d if not enough samples
    36	 *
    37	 * If the anchored window is < MIN_WINDOW_DAYS, returns empty samples with
    38	 * a tooShort flag so the caller can surface a meaningful error instead of
    39	 * computing a nonsense TDEE.
    40	 *
    41	 * Weight source priority (highest → lowest):
    42	 *   1. client_daily_checkins.weight_kg  (daily, real-time)
    43	 *   2. assessment_responses field_key='weight_kg'  (bilans)
    44	 *   3. coach_client_nutrition_manual_data.weight_kg  (coach override)
    45	 */
    46	export async function collectWeightSamples(
    47	  db: SupabaseClient,
    48	  clientId: string,
    49	  targetWindowDays = 14,
    50	  minSamples = 4,
    51	  protocolName?: string,
    52	): Promise<{ samples: WeightSample[]; windowDays: number; anchoredToProtocol: boolean; tooShort: boolean }> {
    53	
    54	  // Try to anchor to protocol start date first
    55	  let anchorDate: string | null = null
    56	  if (protocolName) {
    57	    anchorDate = await resolveProtocolStartDate(db, clientId, protocolName)
    58	  }
    59	
    60	  const today = new Date().toISOString().slice(0, 10)
    61	
    62	  if (anchorDate) {
    63	    const daysSinceAnchor = Math.floor(
    64	      (new Date(today).getTime() - new Date(anchorDate).getTime()) / 86400000
    65	    )
    66	
    67	    if (daysSinceAnchor < MIN_WINDOW_DAYS) {
    68	      // Too soon since protocol start — don't compute, signal tooShort
    69	      return { samples: [], windowDays: daysSinceAnchor, anchoredToProtocol: true, tooShort: true }
    70	    }
    71	
    72	    // Collect samples since anchor date
    73	    const samples = await fetchWeightSamples(db, clientId, anchorDate)
    74	    if (samples.length >= 2) {
    75	      return { samples, windowDays: daysSinceAnchor, anchoredToProtocol: true, tooShort: false }
    76	    }
    77	    // Not enough samples since anchor — fall through to adaptive window
    78	  }
    79	
    80	  // Adaptive window fallback (no anchor or insufficient anchored samples)
    81	  const windows = [targetWindowDays, 21, 30].filter((w, i, arr) => w > arr[i - 1] || i === 0)
    82	
    83	  for (const windowDays of windows) {
    84	    const cutoff = new Date()
    85	    cutoff.setDate(cutoff.getDate() - windowDays)
    86	    const cutoffDate = cutoff.toISOString().slice(0, 10)
    87	
    88	    const samples = await fetchWeightSamples(db, clientId, cutoffDate)
    89	
    90	    if (samples.length >= minSamples || windowDays === windows[windows.length - 1]) {
    91	      return { samples, windowDays, anchoredToProtocol: false, tooShort: false }
    92	    }
    93	  }
    94	
    95	  return { samples: [], windowDays: targetWindowDays, anchoredToProtocol: false, tooShort: false }
    96	}
    97	
    98	async function fetchWeightSamples(
    99	  db: SupabaseClient,
   100	  clientId: string,
   101	  cutoffDate: string,
   102	): Promise<WeightSample[]> {
   103	  const map = new Map<string, number>()
   104	
   105	  // Source 3 (lowest priority) — coach manual data
   106	  const { data: manual } = await db
   107	    .from('coach_client_nutrition_manual_data')
   108	    .select('weight_kg, updated_at')
   109	    .eq('client_id', clientId)
   110	    .not('weight_kg', 'is', null)
   111	    .order('updated_at', { ascending: false })
   112	    .limit(1)
   113	    .maybeSingle()
   114	
   115	  if (manual?.weight_kg != null) {
   116	    const d = String(manual.updated_at ?? '').slice(0, 10)
   117	    if (d >= cutoffDate) map.set(d, Number(manual.weight_kg))
   118	  }
   119	
   120	  // Source 2 — assessment bilans
   121	  const { data: assessmentRows } = await db
   122	    .from('assessment_responses')
   123	    .select('value_number, assessment_submissions!inner(submitted_at, client_id, bilan_date)')
   124	    .eq('field_key', 'weight_kg')
   125	    .eq('assessment_submissions.client_id', clientId)
   126	    .gte('assessment_submissions.submitted_at', cutoffDate)
   127	    .not('value_number', 'is', null)
   128	
   129	  for (const row of assessmentRows ?? []) {
   130	    const sub = (row as any).assessment_submissions
   131	    const d: string = (sub?.bilan_date ?? String(sub?.submitted_at ?? '').slice(0, 10)) as string
   132	    if (d >= cutoffDate && row.value_number != null) {
   133	      map.set(d, Number(row.value_number))
   134	    }
   135	  }
   136	
   137	  // Source 1 (highest priority) — daily check-ins
   138	  const { data: checkins } = await db
   139	    .from('client_daily_checkins')
   140	    .select('date, weight_kg')
   141	    .eq('client_id', clientId)
   142	    .gte('date', cutoffDate)
   143	    .not('weight_kg', 'is', null)
   144	    .order('date', { ascending: true })
   145	
   146	  for (const c of checkins ?? []) {
   147	    if (c.weight_kg != null) {
   148	      map.set(String(c.date), Number(c.weight_kg))
   149	    }
   150	  }
   151	
   152	  return Array.from(map.entries())
   153	    .map(([date, weight_kg]) => ({ date, weight_kg }))
   154	    .sort((a, b) => a.date.localeCompare(b.date))
   155	}
   156	
   157	/**
   158	 * Compute average daily kcal intake from nutrition_meals over the window.
   159	 * Falls back to protocol day 1 calories if insufficient logs.
   160	 */
   161	export async function collectAvgIntake(
   162	  db: SupabaseClient,
   163	  clientId: string,
   164	  windowDays: number,
   165	  protocolFallbackKcal: number,
   166	  anchorDate?: string,
   167	): Promise<{ avgIntakeKcal: number; caloriesSource: 'logs' | 'protocol'; trackedDays: number }> {
   168	  const cutoffDate = anchorDate ?? (() => {
   169	    const d = new Date()
   170	    d.setDate(d.getDate() - windowDays)
   171	    return d.toISOString().slice(0, 10)
   172	  })()
   173	
   174	  const { data: meals } = await db
   175	    .from('nutrition_meals')
   176	    .select('physiological_date, total_protein_g, total_carbs_g, total_fat_g, total_fiber_g')
   177	    .eq('client_id', clientId)
   178	    .gte('physiological_date', cutoffDate)
   179	
   180	  if (!meals || meals.length === 0) {
   181	    return { avgIntakeKcal: protocolFallbackKcal, caloriesSource: 'protocol', trackedDays: 0 }
   182	  }
   183	
   184	  const byDate = new Map<string, number>()
   185	  for (const m of meals) {
   186	    const kcal =
   187	      Number(m.total_protein_g ?? 0) * 4 +
   188	      Number(m.total_carbs_g ?? 0) * 4 +
   189	      Number(m.total_fat_g ?? 0) * 9 +
   190	      Number(m.total_fiber_g ?? 0) * 2
   191	    byDate.set(m.physiological_date, (byDate.get(m.physiological_date) ?? 0) + kcal)
   192	  }
   193	
   194	  const trackedEntries = Array.from(byDate.values()).filter(v => v >= 800)
   195	  const trackedDays = trackedEntries.length
   196	
   197	  if (trackedDays === 0) {
   198	    return { avgIntakeKcal: protocolFallbackKcal, caloriesSource: 'protocol', trackedDays: 0 }
   199	  }
   200	
   201	  const avgIntakeKcal = Math.round(trackedEntries.reduce((s, v) => s + v, 0) / trackedDays)
   202	  return { avgIntakeKcal, caloriesSource: 'logs', trackedDays }
   203	}
   204	
   205	/**
   206	 * Collect client signals needed for v2 adaptive TDEE:
   207	 * - gender (for luteal correction gate)
   208	 * - cycle_phase per day in the window (for female clients)
   209	 * - cycle confidence level
   210	 */
   211	export async function collectClientSignals(
   212	  db: SupabaseClient,
   213	  clientId: string,
   214	  cutoffDate: string,
   215	): Promise<{
   216	  gender: string | null
   217	  cyclePhases: string[]
   218	  cycleConfidence: 'estimated' | 'learning' | 'calibrated' | null
   219	}> {
   220	  // Gender from coach_clients
   221	  const { data: cc } = await db
   222	    .from('coach_clients')
   223	    .select('gender')
   224	    .eq('id', clientId)
   225	    .single()
   226	
   227	  const gender = (cc as any)?.gender ?? null
   228	
   229	  if (gender !== 'female') {
   230	    return { gender, cyclePhases: [], cycleConfidence: null }
   231	  }
   232	
   233	  // Cycle phases from daily checkins over the window
   234	  const { data: checkins } = await db
   235	    .from('client_daily_checkins')
   236	    .select('date, cycle_phase')
   237	    .eq('client_id', clientId)
   238	    .gte('date', cutoffDate)
   239	    .not('cycle_phase', 'is', null)
   240	    .order('date', { ascending: true })
   241	
   242	  const cyclePhases = (checkins ?? [])
   243	    .map((c: any) => c.cycle_phase as string)
   244	    .filter(Boolean)
   245	
   246	  // Cycle confidence from menstrual_cycle_logs count
   247	  const { count } = await db
   248	    .from('menstrual_cycle_logs')
   249	    .select('id', { count: 'exact', head: true })
   250	    .eq('client_id', clientId)
   251	
   252	  const logsCount = count ?? 0
   253	  const cycleConfidence: 'estimated' | 'learning' | 'calibrated' =
   254	    logsCount >= 4 ? 'calibrated' : logsCount >= 1 ? 'learning' : 'estimated'
   255	
   256	  return { gender, cyclePhases, cycleConfidence }
   257	}

UI CANDIDATE: ./tests/lib/client/smart/adherenceScore.test.ts
------------------------------------------------------------
     1	import { describe, it, expect } from 'vitest'
     2	import { computeAdherenceScore } from '@/lib/client/smart/adherenceScore'
     3	
     4	const BASE = {
     5	  sessionDates: [],
     6	  plannedDaysOfWeek: [1, 3, 5],
     7	  mealDates: [],
     8	  waterByDate: {},
     9	  waterTargetMl: 2500,
    10	  checkinDates: [],
    11	  referenceDate: '2026-05-20',
    12	}
    13	
    14	describe('computeAdherenceScore', () => {
    15	  it('returns 0 when no data', () => {
    16	    const r = computeAdherenceScore(BASE)
    17	    expect(r.score).toBe(0)
    18	    expect(r.dimensions.sport).toBe(0)
    19	    expect(r.dimensions.nutrition).toBe(0)
    20	    expect(r.dimensions.hydration).toBe(0)
    21	    expect(r.dimensions.checkins).toBe(0)
    22	  })
    23	
    24	  it('full sport score when all planned sessions done', () => {
    25	    // Window 2026-05-14 to 2026-05-20: Mon=18, Wed=20, Fri=15
    26	    const sessionDates = ['2026-05-15', '2026-05-18', '2026-05-20']
    27	    const r = computeAdherenceScore({ ...BASE, sessionDates, plannedDaysOfWeek: [1, 3, 5] })
    28	    expect(r.dimensions.sport).toBe(25)
    29	  })
    30	
    31	  it('full nutrition score when meals logged every day', () => {
    32	    const mealDates = ['2026-05-14','2026-05-15','2026-05-16','2026-05-17','2026-05-18','2026-05-19','2026-05-20']
    33	    const r = computeAdherenceScore({ ...BASE, mealDates })
    34	    expect(r.dimensions.nutrition).toBe(25)
    35	  })
    36	
    37	  it('full hydration score when water >= 80% target every day', () => {
    38	    const waterByDate: Record<string, number> = {
    39	      '2026-05-14': 2200, '2026-05-15': 2200, '2026-05-16': 2200,
    40	      '2026-05-17': 2200, '2026-05-18': 2200, '2026-05-19': 2200, '2026-05-20': 2200,
    41	    }
    42	    const r = computeAdherenceScore({ ...BASE, waterByDate, waterTargetMl: 2500 })
    43	    expect(r.dimensions.hydration).toBe(25)
    44	  })
    45	
    46	  it('full checkins score when checkin every day', () => {
    47	    const checkinDates = ['2026-05-14','2026-05-15','2026-05-16','2026-05-17','2026-05-18','2026-05-19','2026-05-20']
    48	    const r = computeAdherenceScore({ ...BASE, checkinDates })
    49	    expect(r.dimensions.checkins).toBe(25)
    50	  })
    51	
    52	  it('score sums dimensions correctly', () => {
    53	    const mealDates = ['2026-05-14','2026-05-15','2026-05-16','2026-05-17','2026-05-18','2026-05-19','2026-05-20']
    54	    const checkinDates = ['2026-05-14','2026-05-15','2026-05-16','2026-05-17','2026-05-18','2026-05-19','2026-05-20']
    55	    const r = computeAdherenceScore({ ...BASE, mealDates, checkinDates })
    56	    expect(r.score).toBe(r.dimensions.sport + r.dimensions.nutrition + r.dimensions.hydration + r.dimensions.checkins)
    57	  })
    58	
    59	  it('scoreDelta non-negative when today has more data', () => {
    60	    const mealDates = ['2026-05-17','2026-05-18','2026-05-19','2026-05-20']
    61	    const r = computeAdherenceScore({ ...BASE, mealDates })
    62	    expect(r.scoreDelta).toBeGreaterThanOrEqual(0)
    63	  })
    64	
    65	  it('partial sport score proportional to sessions done', () => {
    66	    // Only Mon done out of Mon/Wed/Fri → 1/3
    67	    const r = computeAdherenceScore({ ...BASE, sessionDates: ['2026-05-18'], plannedDaysOfWeek: [1, 3, 5] })
    68	    expect(r.dimensions.sport).toBeGreaterThan(0)
    69	    expect(r.dimensions.sport).toBeLessThan(25)
    70	  })
    71	})

     6	
     7	  it('returns empty array when no data', () => {

    10	  })

    36	      activities: [],
    37	      checkins: [],
    38	    }

    40	    const water = r.filter(e => e.kind === 'water')
    41	    expect(water.length).toBe(1) // morning bucket aggregated

    43	    expect(water[0].subtitle).toContain('750')
    44	  })
    45

    53	        title: 'Push Force',
    54	        duration_min: 58,
    55	        exercises_count: 8,
    56	      },
    57	      activities: [],
    58	      checkins: [],
    59	    }
    60	    const r = buildTimeline(src)
    61	    expect(r.find(e => e.kind === 'workout')?.title).toBe('Push Force')
    62	  })
    63

    66	      meals: [],

    71	        duration_min: 60, intensity: 6,
    72	      }],
    73	      checkins: [],
    74	    }
