    18	      mk('2026-05-17T09:30:00Z', 500),
    19	      mk('2026-05-17T13:00:00Z', 250),
    20	      mk('2026-05-17T16:00:00Z', 300),
    21	      mk('2026-05-17T20:00:00Z', 250),
    22	    ]
    23	    const r = groupWaterByTimeOfDay(logs, 'UTC')
    24	    expect(r.morning).toBe(750)
    25	    expect(r.midday).toBe(250)
    26	    expect(r.afternoon).toBe(300)
    27	    expect(r.evening).toBe(250)
    28	  })
    29	
    30	  it('ignores logs before 5h or after 24h boundary', () => {
    31	    const logs = [mk('2026-05-17T03:00:00Z', 100), mk('2026-05-17T07:00:00Z', 250)]
    32	    const r = groupWaterByTimeOfDay(logs, 'UTC')
    33	    expect(r.morning).toBe(250)
    34	  })
    35	})

UI CANDIDATE: ./tests/lib/nutrition/actionable-remaining.test.ts
------------------------------------------------------------
     1	import { describe, expect, it } from 'vitest'
     2	import { computeActionableRemaining } from '@/lib/nutrition/actionable-remaining'
     3	
     4	describe('computeActionableRemaining', () => {
     5	  it('keeps informative and actionable layers identical when there is no overflow', () => {
     6	    const result = computeActionableRemaining({
     7	      target: { kcal: 2237, protein_g: 153, carbs_g: 260, fat_g: 65 },
     8	      consumed: { kcal: 1000, protein_g: 80, carbs_g: 100, fat_g: 20 },
     9	      profile: { gender: 'male', weightKg: 90 },
    10	    })
    11	
    12	    expect(result.informativeRemaining).toEqual({
    13	      calories: 1237,
    14	      protein: 73,
    15	      carbs: 160,
    16	      fat: 45,
    17	    })
    18	    expect(result.actionableRemaining).toEqual({
    19	      calories: 1337,
    20	      protein: 73,
    21	      carbs: 160,
    22	      fat: 45,
    23	    })
    24	    expect(result.isExtremeCase).toBe(false)
    25	  })
    26	
    27	  it('compensates fat overflow on carbs first', () => {
    28	    const result = computeActionableRemaining({
    29	      target: { kcal: 2337, protein_g: 153, carbs_g: 260, fat_g: 65 },
    30	      consumed: { kcal: 1749, protein_g: 94, carbs_g: 145, fat_g: 88 },
    31	      profile: { gender: 'male', weightKg: 90 },
    32	    })
    33	
    34	    expect(result.informativeRemaining).toEqual({
    35	      calories: 588,
    36	      protein: 59,
    37	      carbs: 115,
    38	      fat: -23,
    39	    })
    40	    expect(result.actionableRemaining.protein).toBe(59)
    41	    expect(result.actionableRemaining.carbs).toBe(63.2)
    42	    expect(result.actionableRemaining.fat).toBe(0)
    43	    expect(result.actionableRemaining.calories).toBe(488.8)
    44	    expect(result.compensation.carbsReducedG).toBe(51.8)
    45	    expect(result.compensation.fatReducedG).toBe(0)
    46	  })
    47	
    48	  it('protects the fat floor when carbs overflow must be compensated', () => {
    49	    const result = computeActionableRemaining({
    50	      target: { kcal: 2200, protein_g: 160, carbs_g: 200, fat_g: 70 },
    51	      consumed: { kcal: 2100, protein_g: 120, carbs_g: 235, fat_g: 20 },
    52	      profile: { gender: 'male', weightKg: 90 },
    53	    })
    54	
    55	    expect(result.fatFloorG).toBe(54)
    56	    expect(result.minActionableFatG).toBe(34)
    57	    expect(result.informativeRemaining.fat).toBe(50)
    58	    expect(result.actionableRemaining.fat).toBe(34.4)
    59	    expect(result.compensation.fatReducedG).toBe(15.6)
    60	    expect(result.isExtremeCase).toBe(false)
    61	  })
    62	
    63	  it('enters extreme mode only when carbs and reducible fats are exhausted', () => {
    64	    const result = computeActionableRemaining({
    65	      target: { kcal: 2100, protein_g: 160, carbs_g: 50, fat_g: 55 },
    66	      consumed: { kcal: 2400, protein_g: 90, carbs_g: 180, fat_g: 54 },
    67	      profile: { gender: 'male', weightKg: 90 },
    68	    })
    69	
    70	    expect(result.actionableRemaining.carbs).toBe(0)
    71	    expect(result.actionableRemaining.fat).toBe(0)
    72	    expect(result.compensation.proteinReducedG).toBeGreaterThan(0)
    73	    expect(result.isExtremeCase).toBe(true)
    74	  })
    75	})

UI CANDIDATE: ./tests/lib/nutrition/adaptiveTdee.test.ts
------------------------------------------------------------
     1	import { describe, it, expect } from 'vitest'
     2	import { calcAdaptiveTdee, linearRegression } from '@/lib/nutrition/adaptiveTdee'
     3	
     4	const DAY = (offset: number, weight: number) => ({
     5	  date: new Date(Date.UTC(2026, 4, offset + 1)).toISOString().slice(0, 10),
     6	  weight_kg: weight,
     7	})
     8	
     9	describe('linearRegression', () => {
    10	  it('returns correct slope for steady weight loss', () => {
    11	    const samples = [DAY(0, 80), DAY(7, 79.3), DAY(14, 78.6)]
    12	    const { slope } = linearRegression(samples)
    13	    expect(slope).toBeCloseTo(-0.1, 1)
    14	  })
    15	
    16	  it('returns near-zero slope for stable weight', () => {
    17	    const samples = [DAY(0, 75), DAY(7, 75.1), DAY(14, 74.9)]
    18	    const { slope } = linearRegression(samples)
    19	    expect(Math.abs(slope)).toBeLessThan(0.02)
    20	  })
    21	
    22	  it('handles unsorted samples correctly', () => {
    23	    const sorted = [DAY(0, 80), DAY(7, 79.3)]
    24	    const unsorted = [DAY(7, 79.3), DAY(0, 80)]
    25	    const r1 = linearRegression(sorted)
    26	    const r2 = linearRegression(unsorted)
    27	    expect(r1.slope).toBeCloseTo(r2.slope, 4)
    28	  })
    29	})
    30	
    31	describe('calcAdaptiveTdee', () => {
    32	  it('TDEE > intake when losing weight', () => {
    33	    const result = calcAdaptiveTdee({
    34	      weightSamples: [DAY(0, 80), DAY(7, 79.5), DAY(14, 79.0)],
    35	      avgIntakeKcal: 2000,
    36	      caloriesSource: 'logs',
    37	      windowDays: 14,
    38	    })
    39	    expect(result.tdeeAdaptive).toBeGreaterThan(2000)
    40	  })
    41	
    42	  it('TDEE < intake when gaining weight', () => {
    43	    const result = calcAdaptiveTdee({
    44	      weightSamples: [DAY(0, 75), DAY(7, 75.4), DAY(14, 75.8)],
    45	      avgIntakeKcal: 2500,
    46	      caloriesSource: 'logs',
    47	      windowDays: 14,
    48	    })
    49	    expect(result.tdeeAdaptive).toBeLessThan(2500)
    50	  })
    51	
    52	  it('TDEE ≈ intake when weight stable', () => {
    53	    const result = calcAdaptiveTdee({
    54	      weightSamples: [DAY(0, 70), DAY(7, 70.05), DAY(14, 69.95)],
    55	      avgIntakeKcal: 2200,
    56	      caloriesSource: 'logs',
    57	      windowDays: 14,
    58	    })
    59	    expect(Math.abs(result.tdeeAdaptive - 2200)).toBeLessThan(100)
    60	  })
    61	
    62	  it('throws when fewer than 2 samples', () => {
    63	    expect(() => calcAdaptiveTdee({
    64	      weightSamples: [DAY(0, 80)],
    65	      avgIntakeKcal: 2000,
    66	      caloriesSource: 'logs',
    67	      windowDays: 14,
    68	    })).toThrow('At least 2 weight samples required')
    69	  })
    70	
    71	  it('rounds result to nearest 10 kcal', () => {
    72	    const result = calcAdaptiveTdee({
    73	      weightSamples: [DAY(0, 80), DAY(14, 79.0)],
    74	      avgIntakeKcal: 2000,
    75	      caloriesSource: 'logs',
    76	      windowDays: 14,
    77	    })
    78	    expect(result.tdeeAdaptive % 10).toBe(0)
    79	  })
    80	
    81	  it('confidence = low when source is protocol', () => {
    82	    const result = calcAdaptiveTdee({
    83	      weightSamples: [DAY(0, 80), DAY(7, 79.5), DAY(14, 79.0), DAY(10, 79.2)],
    84	      avgIntakeKcal: 2000,
    85	      caloriesSource: 'protocol',
    86	      windowDays: 14,
    87	    })
    88	    expect(result.confidence).toBe('low')
    89	    expect(result.confidenceReasons.length).toBeGreaterThan(0)
    90	  })
    91	
    92	  it('confidence = low when fewer than 4 samples', () => {
    93	    const result = calcAdaptiveTdee({
    94	      weightSamples: [DAY(0, 80), DAY(14, 79.0)],
    95	      avgIntakeKcal: 2000,
    96	      caloriesSource: 'logs',
    97	      windowDays: 14,
    98	    })
    99	    expect(result.confidence).toBe('low')
   100	  })
   101	
   102	  it('confidence = high when ≥4 samples + logs source', () => {
   103	    const result = calcAdaptiveTdee({
   104	      weightSamples: [DAY(0, 80), DAY(4, 79.7), DAY(8, 79.4), DAY(14, 79.0)],
   105	      avgIntakeKcal: 2000,
   106	      caloriesSource: 'logs',
   107	      windowDays: 14,
   108	      trackedDays: 10,
   109	    })
   110	    expect(result.confidence).toBe('high')
   111	  })
   112	
   113	  it('confidence drops to medium with partial tracked days', () => {
   114	    const result = calcAdaptiveTdee({
   115	      weightSamples: [DAY(0, 80), DAY(4, 79.8), DAY(8, 79.5), DAY(14, 79.2)],
   116	      avgIntakeKcal: 2100,
   117	      caloriesSource: 'logs',
   118	      windowDays: 14,
   119	      trackedDays: 5,
   120	    })
   121	    expect(result.confidence).toBe('medium')
   122	    expect(result.confidenceScore).toBeLessThan(80)
   123	  })
   124	
   125	  it('weightDeltaKg = slope × windowDays', () => {
   126	    const samples = [DAY(0, 80), DAY(7, 79.5), DAY(14, 79.0)]
   127	    const result = calcAdaptiveTdee({
   128	      weightSamples: samples,
   129	      avgIntakeKcal: 2000,
   130	      caloriesSource: 'logs',
   131	      windowDays: 14,
   132	    })
   133	    const { slope } = linearRegression(samples)
   134	    expect(result.weightDeltaKg).toBeCloseTo(slope * 14, 2)
   135	  })
   136	
   137	  it('handles rapid weight loss (1 kg/week)', () => {
   138	    const result = calcAdaptiveTdee({
   139	      weightSamples: [DAY(0, 85), DAY(7, 84), DAY(14, 83)],
   140	      avgIntakeKcal: 1800,
   141	      caloriesSource: 'logs',
   142	      windowDays: 14,
   143	    })
   144	    expect(result.tdeeAdaptive).toBeGreaterThan(2500)
   145	  })
   146	
   147	  it('formula: tdee = avgIntake - slope * 7700', () => {
   148	    const samples = [DAY(0, 80), DAY(14, 78.6)]
   149	    const { slope } = linearRegression(samples)
   150	    const expected = Math.round((2000 - slope * 7700) / 10) * 10
   151	    const result = calcAdaptiveTdee({
   152	      weightSamples: samples,
   153	      avgIntakeKcal: 2000,
   154	      caloriesSource: 'logs',
   155	      windowDays: 14,
   156	    })
   157	    expect(result.tdeeAdaptive).toBe(expected)
   158	  })
   159	})

UI CANDIDATE: ./tests/lib/nutrition/ciqual-classifier.test.ts
------------------------------------------------------------
     1	import { describe, expect, it } from 'vitest'
     2	import { classifyCiqualRow } from '@/lib/nutrition/ciqual-classifier.mjs'
     3	
     4	function mkRow(partial: {
     5	  alim_ssgrp_nom_fr?: string
     6	  alim_ssssgrp_nom_fr?: string
     7	  Aliments?: string
     8	}) {
     9	  return {
    10	    alim_ssgrp_nom_fr: partial.alim_ssgrp_nom_fr ?? '',
    11	    alim_ssssgrp_nom_fr: partial.alim_ssssgrp_nom_fr ?? '',
    12	    Aliments: partial.Aliments ?? '',
    13	  }
    14	}
    15	
    16	describe('ciqual classifier', () => {
    17	  it('keeps rice items in carbs', () => {
    18	    expect(classifyCiqualRow(mkRow({
    19	      alim_ssgrp_nom_fr: 'pâtes, riz et céréales',
    20	      alim_ssssgrp_nom_fr: 'pâtes, riz et céréales crus',
    21	      Aliments: 'Riz blanc, cru',
    22	    }))).toEqual({ category_l1: 'carbs', category_l2: 'cereales' })
    23	  })
    24	
    25	  it('routes fruits-only groups to fruits and ignores fruit words in snacks', () => {
    26	    expect(classifyCiqualRow(mkRow({
    27	      alim_ssgrp_nom_fr: 'fruits',
    28	      alim_ssssgrp_nom_fr: 'fruits crus',
    29	      Aliments: 'Abricot, cru',
    30	    }))).toEqual({ category_l1: 'fruits', category_l2: 'frais' })
    31	
    32	    expect(classifyCiqualRow(mkRow({
    33	      alim_ssgrp_nom_fr: 'fruits',
    34	      alim_ssssgrp_nom_fr: 'desserts de fruits',
    35	      Aliments: 'Biscuit sec fourré aux fruits',
    36	    }))).toEqual({ category_l1: 'extras', category_l2: 'snacks-sucres' })
    37	  })
    38	
    39	  it('splits oils from butter and margarine', () => {
    40	    expect(classifyCiqualRow(mkRow({
    41	      alim_ssgrp_nom_fr: 'huiles et graisses végétales',
    42	      alim_ssssgrp_nom_fr: '',
    43	      Aliments: 'Huile de son de riz',
    44	    }))).toEqual({ category_l1: 'fats', category_l2: 'huiles' })
    45	
    46	    expect(classifyCiqualRow(mkRow({
    47	      alim_ssgrp_nom_fr: 'huiles et graisses végétales',
    48	      alim_ssssgrp_nom_fr: '',
    49	      Aliments: 'Beurre allégé 39% MG',
    50	    }))).toEqual({ category_l1: 'fats', category_l2: 'autres-lipides' })
    51	  })
    52	
    53	  it('promotes obvious meat, egg and rice names even when the group is broad', () => {
    54	    expect(classifyCiqualRow(mkRow({
    55	      alim_ssgrp_nom_fr: 'plats composés',
    56	      alim_ssssgrp_nom_fr: '',
    57	      Aliments: 'Bœuf bourguignon',
    58	    }))).toEqual({ category_l1: 'proteins', category_l2: 'viandes' })
    59	
    60	    expect(classifyCiqualRow(mkRow({
    61	      alim_ssgrp_nom_fr: 'plats composés',
    62	      alim_ssssgrp_nom_fr: '',
    63	      Aliments: "Blanc d'œuf",
    64	    }))).toEqual({ category_l1: 'proteins', category_l2: 'oeufs' })
    65	
    66	    expect(classifyCiqualRow(mkRow({
    67	      alim_ssgrp_nom_fr: 'plats composés',
    68	      alim_ssssgrp_nom_fr: '',
    69	      Aliments: 'Galette de riz soufflé',
    70	    }))).toEqual({ category_l1: 'carbs', category_l2: 'cereales' })
    71	  })
    72	
    73	  it('routes composite meals to fast-food instead of ingredient families', () => {
    74	    expect(classifyCiqualRow(mkRow({
    75	      alim_ssgrp_nom_fr: 'plats composés',
    76	      alim_ssssgrp_nom_fr: '',
    77	      Aliments: 'Salade de pâtes, végétarienne',
    78	    }))).toEqual({ category_l1: 'extras', category_l2: 'fast-food' })
    79	
    80	    expect(classifyCiqualRow(mkRow({
    81	      alim_ssgrp_nom_fr: 'plats composés',
    82	      alim_ssssgrp_nom_fr: '',
    83	      Aliments: 'Bouillon de volaille',
    84	    }))).toEqual({ category_l1: 'extras', category_l2: 'fast-food' })
    85	
    86	    expect(classifyCiqualRow(mkRow({
    87	      alim_ssgrp_nom_fr: 'plats composés',
    88	      alim_ssssgrp_nom_fr: '',
    89	      Aliments: 'Pizza au chorizo ou salami',
    90	    }))).toEqual({ category_l1: 'extras', category_l2: 'fast-food' })
    91	  })
    92	})

UI CANDIDATE: ./tests/lib/nutrition/engine/cycleSync.test.ts
------------------------------------------------------------
     1	import { describe, it, expect } from 'vitest'
     2	import {
     3	  getCycleSyncAdjustment,
     4	  adjustMacrosForPhase,
     5	  detectCurrentPhase,
     6	} from '@/lib/nutrition/engine/cycleSync'
     7	import type { StryvrmMacros } from '@/lib/nutrition/engine/types'
     8	
     9	const BASE: StryvrmMacros = {
    10	  protein_g: 160,
    11	  fat_g: 64,
    12	  carbs_g: 200,
    13	  calories: 2000,
    14	}
    15	
    16	describe('getCycleSyncAdjustment', () => {
    17	  it('luteal → positive calorie delta (thermogenic)', () => {
    18	    const adj = getCycleSyncAdjustment('luteal')
    19	    expect(adj.caloriesDelta).toBeGreaterThan(0)
    20	    expect(adj.caloriesDelta).toBeLessThanOrEqual(200)
    21	  })
    22	
    23	  it('luteal → positive carbs delta (serotonin/cravings)', () => {
    24	    const adj = getCycleSyncAdjustment('luteal')
    25	    expect(adj.carbsDelta).toBeGreaterThan(0)
    26	  })
    27	
    28	  it('luteal → positive protein delta (anti-catabolic)', () => {
    29	    const adj = getCycleSyncAdjustment('luteal')
    30	    expect(adj.proteinDelta).toBeGreaterThan(0)
    31	  })
    32	
    33	  it('luteal → increased hydration', () => {
    34	    const adj = getCycleSyncAdjustment('luteal')
    35	    expect(adj.hydrationDeltaMl).toBeGreaterThan(0)
    36	  })
    37	
    38	  it('follicular → optimalForDeficit true (best phase for cut)', () => {
    39	    const adj = getCycleSyncAdjustment('follicular')
    40	    expect(adj.optimalForDeficit).toBe(true)
    41	  })
    42	
    43	  it('ovulatory → optimalForDeficit true (peak performance)', () => {
    44	    const adj = getCycleSyncAdjustment('ovulatory')
    45	    expect(adj.optimalForDeficit).toBe(true)
    46	  })
    47	
    48	  it('luteal → optimalForDeficit false (cravings/metabolism up)', () => {
    49	    expect(getCycleSyncAdjustment('luteal').optimalForDeficit).toBe(false)
    50	  })
    51	
    52	  it('menstrual → optimalForDeficit false', () => {
    53	    expect(getCycleSyncAdjustment('menstrual').optimalForDeficit).toBe(false)
    54	  })
    55	
    56	  it('all phases return non-empty notes', () => {
    57	    const phases = ['follicular', 'ovulatory', 'luteal', 'menstrual'] as const
    58	    for (const p of phases) {
    59	      expect(getCycleSyncAdjustment(p).notes.length).toBeGreaterThan(0)
    60	    }
    61	  })
    62	})
    63	
    64	describe('adjustMacrosForPhase', () => {
    65	  it('luteal → higher calories than base', () => {
    66	    const adj = adjustMacrosForPhase(BASE, 'luteal')
    67	    expect(adj.calories).toBeGreaterThan(BASE.calories)
    68	  })
    69	
    70	  it('luteal → higher protein than base', () => {
    71	    const adj = adjustMacrosForPhase(BASE, 'luteal')
    72	    expect(adj.protein_g).toBeGreaterThan(BASE.protein_g)
    73	  })
    74	
    75	  it('follicular → calories equal or within 50 of base', () => {
    76	    const adj = adjustMacrosForPhase(BASE, 'follicular')
    77	    expect(Math.abs(adj.calories - BASE.calories)).toBeLessThanOrEqual(50)
    78	  })
    79	
    80	  it('calories always match macro math (P×4 + C×4 + F×9)', () => {
    81	    const phases = ['follicular', 'ovulatory', 'luteal', 'menstrual'] as const
    82	    for (const p of phases) {
    83	      const adj = adjustMacrosForPhase(BASE, p)
    84	      const computed = adj.protein_g * 4 + adj.carbs_g * 4 + adj.fat_g * 9
    85	      expect(Math.abs(computed - adj.calories)).toBeLessThanOrEqual(10)
    86	    }
    87	  })
    88	
    89	  it('no negative macro values', () => {
    90	    const phases = ['follicular', 'ovulatory', 'luteal', 'menstrual'] as const
    91	    for (const p of phases) {
    92	      const adj = adjustMacrosForPhase(BASE, p)
    93	      expect(adj.protein_g).toBeGreaterThanOrEqual(0)
    94	      expect(adj.carbs_g).toBeGreaterThanOrEqual(0)
    95	      expect(adj.fat_g).toBeGreaterThanOrEqual(0)
    96	    }
    97	  })
    98	})
    99	
   100	describe('detectCurrentPhase', () => {
   101	  it('day 1 → menstrual', () => {
   102	    expect(detectCurrentPhase(1)).toBe('menstrual')
   103	  })
   104	
   105	  it('day 6 → follicular', () => {
   106	    expect(detectCurrentPhase(6)).toBe('follicular')
   107	  })
   108	
   109	  it('day 14 → ovulatory', () => {
   110	    expect(detectCurrentPhase(14)).toBe('ovulatory')
   111	  })
   112	
   113	  it('day 20 → luteal', () => {
   114	    expect(detectCurrentPhase(20)).toBe('luteal')
   115	  })
   116	
   117	  it('day 28 → luteal', () => {
   118	    expect(detectCurrentPhase(28)).toBe('luteal')
   119	  })
   120	
   121	  it('wraps correctly for day 30 (irregular cycle)', () => {
   122	    const phase = detectCurrentPhase(30)
   123	    expect(['follicular', 'ovulatory', 'luteal', 'menstrual']).toContain(phase)
   124	  })
   125	})
